Na'e fua tu‘u kehckehe ‘i he Makasini,
ka ko hono toki fakama'obo'obo mai eni
ki ha takafi be taha.
J. E. M. (ji i),


KOE TALATEU.
‘Oku toko lahi ‘ae kakai kuo hobo hake ‘i mamani:
koe ni‘ihi ko ‘onau boto, koe ni‘ihi ko ‘enau to‘a ‘i he
tau, koe ni'ihi ko ‘enau ma‘oluga, koe ni‘ihi ko ‘enau
lava me‘a lahi: ka koe ogoogo ‘o Jisu Kalaisi ‘oku
taha ‘ana ; ne ogo koe boto, ka na‘e ‘ikai fa'ahiga
moe boto ‘ae kakai koe; koe to‘a —ka koe to‘a ‘i ho
kataki be; koe ma'oluga mo‘oni—kae ha ki mamani
koe ma'ulalo ; bea ne ogo ‘ene lava me‘a lalahi, ka
tala'ehai na‘a ne hamu ha kolo, be ikuna ha fonua,
be fai ha taha ‘oe g. me‘a koia ‘oku fakahikihiki'i ai
‘ae kakai. Bea ‘oku taha ‘ana foki hono biokalafi.
‘Oku mo'oni koe fakamatala ki he mo‘ui ‘ae kakai
ogoogo koe me a ia ke lotaki'aki ‘ae lotovaivai, bea
ke o‘i ‘ae fakabikobiko, mo ta‘ofi mei he g. me‘a ‘oku
mahino hono kovi : ka koe fakamatala ‘o Jisu koe Ma
mo'oni ‘oe Mo‘wi, koe me‘a ‘oku ne fakamo‘ui ‘ae
laumalie ‘oe tagata na‘e mate, mo ne kilala hake ‘ae
o J »
mama ne goto. ‘I he te'eki ke hoko mai a Jisu koe
'aga'aga be ‘a mamani—lau koa kakai, ka kuo mole
‘ae mo‘ui na‘e ‘iloga ai koe tagata, ‘o toe be ‘ae aga
kelekele : ka ‘i he ogoogo ki ai ‘o Jisu mo ‘ene mo‘ui,
bea kamata foki mai hono mafana, hono faka‘ofo‘ofa,


hono malohi; bea talu aibe moe ‘a hono mata ke ‘ilo
me‘a, bea gaue hono nima ‘o ne lava me‘a, bea ne
tu‘u totonu, bea ne hala ata ‘o tau mo ha taha ‘oku
kauga ki he Lagi.
Koe faigata‘a‘ia‘aga ‘oe kakal ‘oku nofo ki he
fakamatala ki he mo‘ui ‘a Jisu, kabau te nau a‘au
hono kotoa mo hono g. ‘uhiga, bea ‘oku mo'oni be ‘a
Jione —tierilo ki mamani ha‘ane hao ai ‘ae g. tohi ‘e
fai. Bea kabau ‘e gata ‘i he g. me‘a lalahi mo hono
g. ‘uhiga ‘oku fu‘u e‘a, ka ‘e kei loloa fau, ‘o ‘ikai
fekitegaki ‘ae gata‘aga moe kamata'aga. Kane ogo
hono faigata‘a, mo hono matamata ta'elava ‘oe aga
koia ‘e ua, ka ko hono hala totonu ia ke ma‘u ai ‘ae
‘aoga ‘oe mo'ui mana koia. He, hage ‘oku ‘ikai loko
‘aoga ‘ae kai 'oku folofua, ka ‘oku toki lelei ‘oka
fakaeve hono kotoa ‘i hono lamulamu, behe ‘oku ma‘u
‘ae malohi ‘oe Folofola ‘i he sivi hakili mo fakafo‘ime‘a.
Ka ‘oku ‘i ai hano kovi ‘oe me‘a koia, he ‘oku fa‘a
mole ai ‘ae fekau'nkai ‘oe g. me‘a, bea toe fakaji‘iji‘i
ai ki hono ‘aoga. Ko hono lelei ke a‘au kotoa ‘ae fo‘i
kubu, kae buko aibe hono kauga ‘i he jino. Koe
haohaoa ia, bea ko hono ‘uhiga ia ‘oe Tohi Kinihini
ni—ke fakaha fakanounou ki he g. me‘a ‘oe mo'ui
koia, ‘o behe ke ala kuku ‘e he ‘atamai hono kotoa, ‘o
jio ki ho gata‘aga mei he kamata'aga: koe'uhi, ‘oka
fakamatala fakafo‘ime‘a ki he g. Kosibeli, bea mahino
aibe ‘ae tu'uga moe hokohoko ‘oe g. me‘a ‘i he mo‘ui
katoa ‘a Jisu.
Ko hono ‘uhiga ia ‘oe Tohi Kinikini ni; bea ‘oku
ha leva hono faigata'a o‘ona ‘i he lea kuo toki fai, ‘o
behe, ‘ ‘ae hokohoko ‘oe g. me‘a.’ He ne ogo ‘ae ‘ofa
‘ae Kau Abosetolo kia Jisu, bea ne ogo koe gaue na‘e
vahe‘i kinautolu ki ai koe ogoogoa. ‘o ‘ene mo'ui, ka


na‘e ‘ikai ha Id ha taha ke tohi ‘ae fakamatala, kae oua
ke hili ‘ae g. ta‘u lahi. Bea ne ogo na‘e faifai bea tohi,
ka na’e hage aibe ‘ae tohi ‘oe g. me‘a ‘oku to maheni
ai; ‘oku to li'aki ha g. me'a, bea ‘oku ‘ikai te te ‘ai
ke mahu'igamalie ko ‘ete behe ‘e mahino ki he kakai,
‘o hage ko ‘ene mahino kia kita. Koia, ‘oku meimei
‘ikai ha lau ta‘u ‘i he Kosibeli; bea ‘oku hoko moe
fakamatala ‘oe ‘aho ni ha ‘aho mama‘o atu : ‘oku ‘ai
fakataha foki ‘i he botu ni‘ihi ‘ae g, me'a ‘oku alaaga,
ne ogo na‘e fai ‘i he g. taimi kehekehe ; kae'uma'a e
me‘a tebu, ko ‘ene kogokoga be, kae li'aki fua ‘ae g.
me‘a na‘e fakahoko'aki ‘ae g. koga koia. Ko hono
fakatiita totonu—‘oku ‘ikai koe fo‘i ma na‘e to‘o ‘e
Jisu, ‘o fafaga'aki ‘ae kakai, ka koe g. mabakihaki'i ma
na‘e tanaki ‘e be Kau Abosetolo ; bea koe ‘etau gaiie,
ke hokohoko ‘ao g. koga koia ke fo‘i ma. Bea ‘oku
mo‘oni, ‘e faigofua ‘ae g. me‘a lahi—‘e fe'uga ‘ae
makoko koe moe tebu koe, bea ‘iloga hono tu‘uga ‘i
he fo‘i ma —ka koe me‘a ni‘ihi ‘e tatau be, ‘o ‘ikai
mahino be na‘e tu‘u ‘i fe. Koia ‘e lava lelei ‘ae
hokohoko ‘oe g. me'a lahi ‘i he‘etau fakamatala, ka
koe ni‘ihi ‘e fakahokogata'a. Kane ogo e me‘a ke
fefe, he koe Tohi Kinikini be: kehe be ke mahino ‘ae
fouga; ka koe tokatamaki moe luo moe alame‘a behe
tuku ia ke gaohia ‘e he g. tohi fakamatala.

KOE TOHI KINIKINI
MO‘UI ‘A JISU KALAISI.
KOE YAHE I.
KOE ‘ULUAKI KUOGA.
Na‘e alea ‘ae Jiaji ‘i mu‘a ke tauhi ‘a h. 25 ‘o Tisema
koe ‘aho fakamanatu ki he ‘alo‘i ‘o Jisu Kalaisi : ka
‘oku ‘ikai ke mahino na‘a nau ‘ilo ko hano ‘aho
totonu ia; ka ‘oku matamata koe taimi ia na‘e fai ai
ha fu‘u katoaga hiteni, ‘o nau ‘ai behe ko hono hiki
ki ha me‘a fakalotu. Ka ‘oku ‘i ai ha g. me‘a ‘oku
tuku ki he mahina ko Ebeleli ko honomahina totonu.
Ko hono ta‘u foki na‘e hala; he, ‘i he ta‘u koia,
na‘e lau ki ai ‘e he Jiaji i mu‘a kuo loa ‘ae bekia ‘a
Helota, ‘aia ‘oku tau ‘ilo na‘e kei laumalie ‘i he hoko
mai ‘ae Fakamo‘ui ‘o Mamani. Koia te tau lau na‘e
‘alo‘i ‘a Jisu Kalaisi ‘i h. 5 ‘o Ebeleli ‘i h. 4 ‘oe ta‘u
K. M.
Ko ‘ene fa‘e ko Mele koe toko taha ‘i he ha'atu'i
mu‘a, bea behe foki mo Jiosifa, koe tagata na‘a na
nonofo, ‘aia na‘e maholo ‘e mamani ko ‘ene tamai
mo‘oni, koe ‘ikai te nau ‘ilo ki hono aga totonu. Ka
ne ogo ia ka na‘e majiva ‘ae ogo me‘a, mo tae‘iloa ;


bea na‘a na nonofo ‘i ha kolo fakatu‘a ‘i he tukuhita
‘o Kaleli, ko Nasaleti hono higoa; bea na‘e ma‘u
ji'ona tauhi ‘i he gaue fakatufuga ‘a Jiosifa.
Lolotoga ia na‘e hoko mai ‘ae tu'utu'uni mei he
Tu‘i Fakaleveleva ‘o mamani, koe Akosito Sisa, ke
tohi-kakai ‘ae g. fonua : bea fanogonogo ‘e Helota ke
‘alu ‘ae kakai ki he g. ‘abi na‘e tauhi ai honau g. tohi
hohoko, ke nau tohi ai. Koia na‘e toki fonoga atu ‘a
Jiosifa mo Mele ki Betelihema, koe kolo ‘o hona
tubu‘aga ko Tevita; bea na‘a na tu‘utu‘uni, nai, ka
hili hona tohi bea na o ki Selusalema ki he Basova.
Ka na‘e ‘ikai lava ia, he koe bo koia na‘e ‘alo‘i mai ‘i
Betelihema ‘ae Basova Mo'oni, ‘ae Lami ‘ae ‘Otua,
‘aia ka hao ai ‘ae g. fa'ahiga kehekehe ‘o mamani ‘i
he'enau gaue'aki hono ta‘ata‘a.
‘Oku ‘ikai koe tohi ‘eni ke fakamatala lahi ki he g.
me‘a na‘e fai—he'ena a‘u atu ki he faletalifonoga na‘e
tu‘u ‘i hetofi'a totonu ‘o Tevita—‘ene fonu ‘aeg. loki,
moe bau ke na 6 ki he falemanu—hono ‘alo‘i ‘o Jisu
‘o hage koe ha tamajih kehe, ‘o kofu fakatamajhi
valevale—‘ae ha ‘ae agelo ki he kau tauhi sibi &c.
Ka ‘oku mahino, ka ne tae‘oua ‘ae fakamatala ‘ae kau
tauhi sibi koia, na‘o ‘ikai ha me‘a ke ha ai koe toko
taha kehe ia ; ka na‘e gaohi ia ‘o tatau tofu be mo
kitautolu. Koia na‘e fai ki ai ‘ae g. tu‘utu‘uni ‘oe kuoga
koia : na‘e kamu ia ‘i hono ‘aho valu, ‘o fakahigoa ko
Jisu, ‘aia koe aga o'enau ‘ai ‘ae higoa ko Jiosiua
kimui. Ko hono ‘uhiga foki ia na‘e ‘ave ai ki he
Temibale, ‘i hono ‘aho fagoi'ulu, ke fai hono fakama'a ;
ne ogo na‘e ‘ikai ha momo'i kovi ‘e taha ‘iate ia :
bea, ‘i hono ‘oatu koia, na‘e ‘ilo ia ‘e he ogo matu‘a
lotu, ko Simione mo Ana, ‘o na fakababau koe toko
taha ia kuo hoko mai ke fakamo‘ui ‘a Isileli.


Ka ‘oku hage na‘e ‘ikai tokaga ki ai ! e ha taha: ka
ko hono ‘uhiga, nai, kuo vaivai honau loto ‘i he g.
tautea ‘a Helota kuo toki fai ki ha ni'ihi na‘e o‘i ‘ae
me‘a faka-Jiu ; bea na‘e hage ha muna ‘ae lau ki
ha'anau mo‘ui ‘i ha tamaji‘i. ‘Oku tau ofo, foki, ‘i he
nofo ‘a Jiosifa mo Mele ‘i Betelihema; he ‘oku vaofi
‘aubito mo Selusalema, hage, nai, ko Eukunuku mo
Nukualofa : ka kuo na ogo‘i, nai, koe Misaia ‘eni, bea
‘oku tau ke ne tubu ‘i he kolo ‘o Tevita, ‘o hage koe
lau ‘ae kau Balofita.
‘Oku ‘ikai to tau ‘ilo ki he fuoloa ‘oe nofo koia ‘i
Betelihema ; ka koe mahina, nai, ko Jiulai be ko
Aokosi na‘e ha‘u ai ha fonoga ki Selusalema mei
Mesobotemia koe a‘ahi, tokua, ‘ae hou‘eiki ni‘ihi ‘i he
ha‘a Maid ki he Tu‘i Jiu kuo toki tubu ni. Koe
fa‘ahiga ia na‘e kilukilua honau tubu‘aga, bea na‘e
lahi ‘ae tokaga ki ai ko ‘enau boto ; he kuo ‘iate
kinautolu ‘ae g. fakakaukau ‘oe g. kuoga tukufaka-
holo. ‘I he taimi ‘o Nobukanesa mo Kolesi ko honau
tu‘ukimu‘a ‘a Taniela, bea na‘a nau ma‘u meiate ia
ha fakamatala ki he Misaia; ‘ae taimi te ne hoko ai,
‘ae g. fakahloga ‘e fakamelomelo kiate ia, moe gaue
te ne fai. Bea ‘i hono 7 ‘oe ta‘u K, M., kae‘uma‘a ‘i
hono 6, kuo nau vakai ‘i he feitu‘u koia ‘oe lagi na‘e
tuku ki he fonua koia ko Jiutea ‘ae fakataha ‘ae g.
balanite, bea moe ha, nai, ha fetu‘u fo‘ou. Koia na‘a
nau behe kuo ‘alo‘i mai ‘ae tu‘i na‘e tala; bea nau
behe ke fai ha a'ahi kiate ia.
Koe me‘a kehe ‘ae gaue ‘a Selusalema ‘i he hoko
mai ‘ae tala koeni. ‘Oku fakaha ‘e he Kosibeli na‘e
‘ikai ha fiefia ka koe bubutu‘u be: bea ne‘ine‘i, he
koe ‘eiki lototagia ‘a Helota, bea ko ‘ene aga ke
tamate noabe, ‘oka ne ka mahalo ‘oku ai ha lau


ki ha tu‘i kehe. Kuo mole behe hono naifi mo hono
kaiga, ‘io, mo ‘ene fanau totonu a‘ana: bea kola
na‘e manavahe ‘ae kakai ‘i he ha‘u ‘ae kau Maki, na‘a
tu'uganaki ia ‘e Helota, ‘o fai ha fu‘u fakabo ; kae-
‘uma‘a na‘e fakautuutu ‘ene lotofita'a ‘i he mahaki
na‘a ne buke ai, he na‘e keina ia ‘e he ‘uaga. Ka
na‘e fufu ‘e Helota ‘ene ‘ita, ‘o ne tala ke nan 6 ki
Betelihema, ‘o kumi ki he tamaji'i ‘eiki, ka ne toki
muimui atu.
Koe ‘aho lahi ki mamani ‘aia na‘o hoko ai ‘ae kau
Maki ki Betelihema; he koe taki kinautolu ‘oe
Senitaile : bea na‘e kamata ai ‘ae tukulolo ‘ae g.
fa'ahiga kia Jisu ; ‘aia kuo bau ke fai atu kae'oua ke
‘i hono lalova'e ‘ae g. me‘a kotoabe.
Ka koe aga aibe ‘oe mo‘ui ‘a Jisu na‘e tauhoa ‘ae
hakeaki‘i moe mamahi. Koia, ‘i he jitu'a leva ‘ae kau
Maki, na‘e bau ke holataki ia ki Ijibite telia ‘a
Helota; ‘aia kuo ne tu‘utu‘uni ke fakabogi ‘ae
tamaiki kotoabe na‘e mataraata to‘ume‘a moe Tu‘i Jiu.
‘Oku ‘ikai ‘ilo be na‘e fuoloa fefe ‘ene nofo ‘i he fonua
koia —hei'ilo ki ha mahina ‘e ono —kakoe me‘a ki he
feitu'u ‘o Ijibite, ‘oku matamata mo‘oni ‘ae talatubu'a,
ko Oni, tokua, koe kolo na‘e kau ki ai ‘a Jiosifa, bea
ako ai ‘a Mosese. ‘Okuhage na'ema'u ‘ae tu‘utu‘uni
‘ae matu‘a ‘a Jisu ke nofo ‘i Betelihema ; bea, ‘i he
bekia ‘a Helota na‘a na foki hake leva ke ‘alu ki ai.
Ka ‘i he'ena fanogo talanoa ki he aga ‘o Akileosi, ‘aia
kuo ne fetogi ‘ene tamai ko Helota, mo ‘ene kamata
‘ene bule ‘aki ‘ene fakabogi ha kakai laui afe, na‘a na
manavahe ‘o na mei foki: ka ka taki kinaua ‘e he
‘Eiki ki hona nofo‘aga mu‘a ko Nasaleti.
Koe botu koia na‘e tubu ‘ai hotau Fakamo'ui: bea
kohai ‘oku ‘ikai ke faka'amu ke ‘ilo ki he'ene g. me‘a


ua‘e fai ? Ka kuo fufu ia ‘e he ‘Eiki meiate kitautolu ;
bea koe g. fakakaukau ‘ae kakai kuo nau £ ahi‘ahi ke
fakaha ia ‘oku ‘ikai ‘aubito jiva‘u. ‘Oku nau lau ki
ha g. mana na‘a ne fai ‘i he‘ene kei tamajih, ‘a ‘ene
takao ‘ae faga ki‘i miji ‘umea, kae toki fakabuna, moe
mamate ‘ae nima ‘oe failautohi ‘i he‘ene ofa ke ta‘i
ia : ka oku mahino mei he folofola na‘e ‘ikai ha‘ane
mana ‘e fai, ka na‘a ne nofo be ‘o hage ha tamaji'i
kehe, gata be ‘i he ‘ikai ha‘ane kovi ‘e fai, bea moe
ogo‘i ‘e he kakai kotoabe koe toko taha ia ‘oku
‘ofeina mei lagi. ‘Oku fakaha mai na‘a ne tubu ‘i he
boto ; ‘aia ko hono ‘uhiga na‘e ai ‘ae g. me‘a ‘oku ‘ikai
te ne ‘ilo ki ai he ‘aho ni, ka ne toki ‘ilo ki ai
‘abogibogi ; bea ‘oku mahino mei ai, ta, kuo ne tuku
mo‘oni hono aga fakalagi. Kuo bau na‘a ne ‘alu ki
ha uanitu, he na‘e ‘ikai ha tamajhi ‘e nofo ‘i he taimi
koia ; bea ‘oku ha na‘a ne ako ki he lau ‘oe tohi faka-
Hebelu, bea koe me‘a ‘i he‘ene boto ai na‘e fili ia ke
lau ‘ae lesoni ‘i he falelotu ‘i he ‘Aho Tabu,
Koe taimi mamafa ki he tama Jiu a‘ene hoko ki
he hogofulu ma ua ta‘u. ‘I he'one kei tamaji'i na‘e
lau koe hoboate be, bea na‘e gofua hono fakatau ki
ha taha ‘e he'ene matu'a. Na‘e lau ‘e he kau Labai
hi‘ihi koe manu be ‘o a‘u ki hono ta‘u koia, ka, hili ia,
kuo ‘iate ia ‘ae laumalie ‘oe tagata. Ka‘a ne kamata
mo'ua ai ki he Lao, ‘o ne ‘ai ‘ae faildketeli, bea na‘e
fakakau ia ki he falelotu. Koia, ‘i he hoko ‘ae taimi
mamafa koia, na‘e ‘ave ’a Jisu ‘e Jiosifa mo Mele ‘i
he'ena 6 ki he Basova, koe‘uhi, ‘abe, ke na fakatabu ia
kia Jihova, he koe ‘uluaki ia. ‘Oku lau ‘e he ni‘ihi
na‘e ‘ave ha tamaji'i behe kine Temibale, bea lau ‘e
he'ene matu'a ‘oku na tukuage ia ki he ‘Eiki, he ko
‘Ene me‘a. Kabau koia, bea ‘oku ‘uhiga leva ‘ae


me‘a na’e hoko. He ‘oku ‘i ai ‘ae g. me‘a ‘i he lotu,
‘aia ‘oku fai koe kehe ke fai—hage koe babitaiso —
bea ‘oku tatataha ‘ae kakai ‘oku ogo‘i mo'oni hone
‘uhiga: behe, koe fakatabu'i ‘oe ‘uluaki kuo hoko
koe ge'eji me‘a, koe lau be. Ka koe loto ‘o Jisu koe
koto mo‘oni, bea, ‘i he'ene fanogo ki he g. lea mamafa
a‘ene matu'a, na‘a ne behe ko hono tukuage mo'oni
ki he gaue ‘ae ‘Eiki; koia na‘e ‘ikai te ne ‘alu moe
fonoga ‘i he'enau foki hake ki Kaleli; ka ka ‘alu be
ia ki he Temibale, ki he fale na‘e fakataha ai ‘ae kau
Labai, ‘o ne akoako atu ‘i he g. me‘a ‘oe lotu.
Na‘e ‘ikai hoha‘a ‘a Jiosifa mo Mele ‘i he ‘ikai ‘iloa
‘ae tamaji'i, he na‘a na behe ‘oku ne ‘i he kaiga be,
he koe tamaji'i ‘ofeina. Ka, ‘i he ‘ikai te ne ha‘u
kiate kinaua ‘i Jieliko (be koefe ha botu na‘a na
malolo ai), na‘a na fekumi hake ki ai ‘i he hala, ‘o a‘u
ki Selusalema, ‘o na toki ‘ilo ki he Temibale. Bea, ‘i
he kamata gaohi ia ‘e Mele, na‘a ne ofo bake, be
koeha na‘a na toe kumi ai kiate ia, kae‘uma‘a ‘ena
tae'ilo ki he botu na‘a ne ‘i ai. Hage na‘a ne behe :
“ Ikai na‘a mo tukuage au ki he ‘Eiki 1 bea lau ‘eau
te mo ‘ilo teu mo'ua ‘i He'ene gaue.’ Bea toki hoko
kiate ia ‘ae me‘a fakamamahi ‘oku fa‘a hoko ki he
fanau, a'enau ogo'i ‘oku ‘ikai mo‘oni ‘ae g. me‘a
kotoabe ‘oku fai ; bea na‘a moe kaiga ofi ‘e ‘ikai ala
fai ha falala ki he'enau lea kotoabe. He koe aga ‘a
tamaiki ‘oku nau tubu falala be, bea koe lea kotoabe
‘ae kakai ‘oku hage koe folofola kiate kinautolu ; bea
koe toki me‘a fakamamahi ‘enau ‘a hake ‘o ‘ilo, ta,
koe Mama kaka mo launoa. Na‘e behe, nai, ‘a Jisu ‘i
he'ene haga hake kia Mele mo Jiosifa : hage na‘e
kite leva kiate ia, ta, ko ‘ena g. lau mamafa kuo ne
fanogo ki ai koe ge‘eji lea be, bea ko hono tukuage


koe tukuage lau be. Ka na‘e ‘ikai te ne haga ‘o
valoki kinaua, ‘o hage ko ha tama Toga ; ka na‘a ne
tu‘u ‘o ‘alu mo kinaua ki Kasaleti, ‘o ne nofo tala-
gofua ki ai ‘o hogofulu ma valu ta‘u.
Ka tala'ehai koe me‘a faigofua kiate ia ke li'aki
‘ae fakataha ‘ae kau Labai, moe kau boto ‘o hono
fonua, ke alu ‘o gauo ‘i Kasaleti ; he ‘oku ha ‘ene
manako ki he boto : ka ko ‘ene gauo totonu ‘i he
taimi koia ke ako ha faiva hage ko mamani, bea ke
kakava hono fofoga ‘i he kumi hano tauhi, moe tokoni
ki hono famili. ‘Oku ha mei he tohi ‘a Maake (vi. 3)
na‘a ne gaue fakatufuga hage ko Jiosifa ; bea kohai
‘oku ‘ikai ke fakafeta‘i ‘i he'ene haunoa behe 1 Ho
ka ne fili ha faiva faka‘ei‘eiki ke ne mo‘ua ai, ‘ikai
kuo fakame‘avale‘i leva hotau toko lain. Ka koeni,
‘iloga ha faiva ‘oku matamata ta‘etoka‘i, bea mo'ua
ai ‘ae hou'eiki lalahi ‘o hotau fa'ahiga: ko Atama
mo Koa na‘e keli, ko Tevita na‘e tauhisibi, bea ko
Jisu na‘e tufuga.
Bea na‘e ‘ikai koia be. ‘Oku hage na‘e toko lahi
‘ae fanau ‘a Melc : ‘oku tau fanogo ki ha tamaiki
tagata ‘e toko fa, mo ha tamaiki fefme ‘e toko ua, nai;
bea ‘oku ha leva ‘ae gagau ‘a Jisu ‘e fai, he koe ta-
‘okete ia, bea kuo bau te ne mo'ua lahi ki honau
tauhi. Ka ‘oku tau behe ko ha ki‘i hevani ‘ae fale
koia ‘i Nasaleti ‘i he aga'ofa moe lea boto ‘a ji‘i Jisu.
‘Oku matamata mo'oni ‘ae lau, foki, ki he bekia ‘a
Jiosifa ‘i he te‘eki ke ne a‘u ki he uofulu ta‘u: bea
kabau koia bea, ta, koe ta‘u ‘e hogofulu tubu ‘ene fua
‘ae kavega mamafa koia koe tauhi ‘o ha fu‘u famili;
bea ne ‘ilo mo'oni ai ki ha taha ‘oe g. faigata'a lahi
‘oe mo'ui ni. Ka na‘e ma‘ama‘a ko ‘ene lotu. Koe
lotulotu ma'ube na‘e fai ‘e Jisu ‘i he‘ene me‘a fauo ‘i


Jiutea na‘e ‘ikai koe me'a tnlm fakafokifa be. ‘lkai
koe me‘a ia kuo tubu moia. Xc ogo ‘oku ‘ikai ha
fakamatala ki ai, ka ‘oku tau jio kiate ia ‘oku ne feohi
mo ‘ene Tamai ‘i hevani ‘i he‘ene kei tamaji‘i, hage
ko Samiuela; bea, ‘i he'ene talavou mo tagata, na‘a
ne li ‘atu ‘ene g. kavega ki he ‘Otua. Bea kuo bau
na‘e ai mo ‘ene me‘a ‘e taha ‘i he g. ta‘u koia. Tala-
‘ehai na‘e buli kiate ia koe Bilinisi ia ‘o Isileli; kae-
‘uma‘a ‘e fakaha ‘e Mele ‘ae tala ‘ae agelo, ‘o behe
koe tu‘utu‘uni ‘ae ‘Eiki ke ne ma‘u ‘ae taloni o‘ene
kui ko Tevita. Bea koe behe koa na‘e ikai gaiie ai
hono loto ! ‘A, kuo bau na‘e jio ma‘u ki ai hono
loto ; bea te ne me'a mo ‘alu hake ki he fu‘u mouga
‘oku tu‘u ai, ‘o ne vakai ‘ae g, feitu‘u ogoogo ‘o
Kenani na‘e ha ki ai, mo ne fakalaulauloto ki he g.
gaue na‘e fai ai ‘e he kau to‘a ‘o hono fonua, ‘o ne
fakatu‘otu‘a ki ha taimi ‘e toe tu'umalie ai ‘ae bule-
‘aga. Kane hage koe toko lahi kuo ne ‘oho ‘o kau
mo kinautolu na‘e ‘i be Kautaha-mamahi‘i-fonua ; ka
koe aga aibe ‘o Jisu ke ‘oua be ke tofa hano hala ‘e
he'ene Tamai ‘oku ‘i he lagi: koia na‘a ne fakama‘u-
ma‘u ‘o toe ‘alu hifo ki he'ene gaue ‘i Kasaleti.
(‘Oku kei toe be.)


KOE YAHE 11.
KOE KUOGA ‘O JIONE BABITAISO.
Na‘e fou belie ‘ae mo‘ui ‘a Jisu ‘o tolugofulu ta‘u.
Lolotoga ia, kuo bekia ‘ae Tu‘i Loma ko Akosito,
bea boko ‘a Taibilio Sisa; kao‘uma‘a kuo mole mei
Jiutea hono lau koe bule'aga, bea kuo matu'aki
fakaboko ia ki he Bule'aga ‘o Loma, bea na‘e nofo ‘a
Bonito Bailato ko hono Kovana. Fe'uga moia na‘e
boko ha me‘a, ‘aia na‘e gatfe ai ‘ae fonua mei Tani ki
Beasiba—toku a kuo ‘ofa ‘ae Eiki, ‘o ‘omi hanau
balofita. Na‘e ogo hake ki he g. feitu'u ‘oku ne nofo
‘i he fonua mamate ofi ki Jioatani moe Taha Mate,
bea ‘oku ne babitaiso ‘ae kakai ‘oku loto ki ai ke
nau hoko ki he lahi ‘oe Misaia, ‘aia tokua ‘oku ne
fakamelomelo ki ai.
Koe me‘a kehe ‘ae ga‘uta ‘ae fonua, moe ‘aukau
mai ‘ae g. kolo ke a‘ahi kiate ia. Koe taimi koia
na‘e fakafa‘afa‘ahiga ‘a Jiutea; ka na‘e tuku ‘ae
fakavafcavaha‘a, kae ‘alu fakataha ‘ae Falesi moe
Satusi, ‘ae Labai moe Tuku'uta, ‘o nofo ki he va‘e
‘oe balofita fo‘ou ni. Bea na‘e to hono geia kiate
kinautolu: kae fefe ! he ko ‘ene tubu koe mana, koe
tama ‘a ha ogo a‘ua‘u, na‘e tala'ekina hono fanau'i ‘e
ha agelo, bea talu ‘ene tamaji'i mo ‘ene nofo ‘i he
lala ‘o feohi mo lagi : bea na‘e fakaofo mo ‘ene ha


ni, he ko hono kofu na ! e hage koe kakai hehegi na‘e
hahamolofia ‘i he g. vaha ‘one'one ‘o hahake, bea
na‘e taube hifo hono lau ki he kolekele, ‘o hage koe
talanoa kia Samiuela moe kau balofita mu'a. Koia
‘i he‘enau jio ki hono aga koia, mo fanogo ki he'one
lea aji, na‘a nau behe ko Ilaijia tofu be, ‘aia kuo ne
hoko mai ‘o hage koe folofola ‘ae ‘Eiki ke teuteu ‘ae
kakai ki he Misaia.
Bea kabau na‘e ue‘ia ‘ae g. fa‘ahiga kovi ‘i he gaue
‘ae balofita ni, huanoa ha fai lelei hage ko Jisu; koia
na‘a ne tu‘u ‘o ‘alu atu moe kakai ke babitaiso ‘ia
Jione. ‘Oku mo'oni na‘e ‘ikai ha‘ane agahala ke
fakatomala ia, ka koe tu‘utu‘uni ‘oe lotu ; bea hage
na‘e kamu ia, ‘o fakakau ai ki he lotu faka-Jiu, behe
na‘a ne fakavaivai'i ia ki he tu‘utu‘uni ‘oe babitaiso
ko hono fakahoko ki ho akega fo‘ou. Na‘e fie ta'ofi
‘e Jione ‘i he‘ene mamata ki ai, he, ne ogo na‘e ‘ikai
te ne ‘ilo koe Misaia, ka kuo ogo ki hono loto ‘one
mo'ui ma‘oni‘oni, bea ‘oku ta'etau moia ke babitaiso
ha taha behe. Na‘e ‘ikai faka‘ikai‘i ‘e Jisu ki he'ene
lau koia, he na‘a ne ‘ilo ‘oku ‘ikai ha‘ane agahala;
kae hage na‘a ne behe, ‘ Koia aibe he koe tu‘utu‘uni
fakalotu, bea ‘iloga ha ni‘ihi ‘oku takimu'a ai hage ko
kitaua ‘oku tau ke nau fai hono g. tu‘utu‘uni kotoa.’
Bea toki ‘alu hifo ‘a Jisu ki Jioatani, bea fai hono
babitaiso ‘e Jione ‘o hage koe kakai kehe. Bea ‘oku
ha mai na‘e ‘ikai koe me‘a ma‘ama‘a kia Jisu, bea
na‘e ‘ikai te ne fai koe kehe ke fai, ho na‘a ne
mo‘utu‘u be ‘o lotu; bea, ‘i he'ene kamata hake ki
‘uta, na‘e vakai ‘e Jione ‘oku mahaeua ‘ae lagi, bea
‘oku ‘alu hifo mei loto hevani ha me‘a hage koe lube,
‘aia na‘e hifo tonu ‘o tu‘u ‘ia Jisu ; bea ogo mai foki
ha lea mei he Ta'ehamai, ‘o behe, “ Ko hoku ‘Alo


Bole ‘ena, ‘aia kuou hoifua ai.” Na‘e ‘ilo leva ‘e
Jione koe Misaia ‘a Jisu; he na‘e belie hono fakaha
kiate ia ‘i he‘ene kei ‘i he toafa, ‘o behe, tokua, ‘e ‘iloga
! ae Misaia koe ha'ele hifo ‘ae Laumalie Ma‘oni [ oni ‘o
nofo ki ai ; bea talu mei mu [ a moe lau koe vaka ‘oe
Laumalie ! ae Lube.
Kuo Kalaisi mo'oni ‘cni ‘a Jisu he kuo “ bani; ” ‘o
‘ikai ‘aki ‘ae 1010 fakamama, ka ‘aki ‘ae 1010 tobutabu
koe Laumalie Ma‘oni‘oni: bea ne ogo‘i leva ‘ene gaue
‘i hono loto, he na‘e hage kuo fakaoma ia ke ‘alu ki
he Toafa. Bea fai leva ‘e Jisu ki hono ue‘i koia, ‘o
ne fonoga atu aibe, ‘o meimoi uike ono ‘o ‘ikai te ne
kai ha me‘a. ‘Oku ‘ikai ke fakababau mai ‘e he
Folofola be koefe ‘ae toafa na‘a ne he fano ai, ka ‘oku
matamata koe Toafa ‘o Belana mo Sainai, ‘aia na‘e
mo‘ui ai ‘ae kakai Isileli ‘i mu‘a; he ‘oku ha koe
finagalo ‘oe ‘Otua ke fakatatau ‘ae mo‘ui ‘a hono ‘Alo,
ko Jisu, bea moe nofo ‘a hono fale‘alo ‘e taha, koe
kakai Isileli.
‘Oku ‘ikai ke fakaha mai ‘ae g. ‘ahi'ahi na‘e tau
mai ‘i he g. ‘aho koia. Mo‘oni ‘oku lau na‘a ne ‘i he
faga manu fekai, ka 'oku ‘ikai mahino koe ‘ahi'ahi ia :
na‘a kuo nau agalelei mai. Koe mana ‘ae tauhi ‘oe
mo‘ui ‘ae kakai Isileli ‘i he‘enau ‘alu fano ‘i he botu
koia, bea na‘e behe rnoe mo‘ui ‘a Jisu ; na‘e boubou
be mei Lagi; koia, ne ogo na‘e ‘ikai te ne tokoni'aki
ha me‘a, ka na‘a ne mo‘ui be. Ka, ‘i hono ‘aho
fagofulu, na‘e toki to‘o ‘ae tokoni koia, ‘o tuku ‘a Jisu
ke faka'eia be, bea ne halofia leva; bea ‘ikai'ia koia,
ka ‘oku matamata na‘a ne vaivai ‘aubito ; bea na‘e
ha ki he Fili ko hono ava ‘eni ke ‘ohofia.
‘Oku tau behe na‘e ‘ikai te ne ha ‘i hono aga totonu,
kae hage, uai, ko ha motu'a na‘a ne tu‘u ‘i he ve‘e


Jioatani ‘o mamata ki hono babitaiso, moe g. me'a
fakaofo na‘e boko ai. Bea koia ‘i he huhuage, nai, ‘e
Jisu be ‘oku ‘ikai ha'ane me‘a tokoni, na‘e ne lea mai
‘o hage ko ha ofo, ‘ Kabau koe ‘Alo koe ‘oe ‘Otua,
koeha ‘oku ‘ikai te ke gaohi ai ‘ae g. maka ni ke fo‘i
ma 1 Koe fu‘u fakatauvele ‘eni, ka tala‘ehai koe ‘ai
ke ne agahala—tabu mo Jisu—ka kce o‘i ke ne fai
‘ae me‘a ‘oku totonu ‘aubito ‘eta fai, koe ta‘ofi ‘ete
mo‘ui mei he mate. Koe malohi ia ‘oe ‘ahi‘ahi, koe
‘ikai te ne febaki mo ha lao ‘e taha ‘i he Polofola. Ka
‘oka ne fai ki ai ‘e Jisu, kuo mele leva ‘ae gaue kuo
ne ha‘u ai ki mamani; he, ‘ikai ko hono tu‘utu‘uni ‘e
taha ke ne faigata‘a‘ia ‘i he'etau g. faigata‘a, bea
‘ahi‘ahi‘i ‘o hage ko kitautolu, koe‘uhi ke mahino koe
tagata haohaoa? Bea lava fefe ia ‘o kabau te ne
hufaga ki he‘ene mafai mana, bea kalo ai mei he g.
faigata‘a t Koe tatau ia koa mo kitautolu 1 Koia
‘oku hage kuo ne tu‘utu‘uni ke ‘oua te ne fai ha
mana ma'ana, bea koe eginaki ‘a Setane na‘e febaki
moe tu‘utu‘uni koia. Bea koe akonaki ‘oku tau
ma‘u mei ai, a‘eni, Na‘a moe g. me'a ‘oku gofua, ka
‘oku ‘ikai gofua ki he kakai katoa ; ka ‘oku hage ‘oku
tau taki taha hano tabu ke tauhi.
Ko hono ua ‘oe ‘ahi‘ahi na‘e tau tonu ki he g.
‘ulugaaga ‘oe loto, kae‘uma‘a ‘ae ‘ulugaaga koia ‘oku
‘iate kitautolu kotoabe, bea ‘oku totonu—koe
mamahi'i kita. Bea ‘oku ha ai ‘ae boto ‘a Setane ‘i
he'ene fai ki hono ‘ulugaaga koia ; he ne ogo koe koto
totonu ‘iate ia, ka koe toki me‘a ‘oku ue‘igofua ki he
kovi. ‘Oku tatataha ‘ae tagata ‘iate kitautolu tubu
agahala ‘oku ‘ilo, ‘oka ne ka fai ha me‘a behe, be ko
‘ene mamahi'i totonu ia, be ko ‘ene fai ‘i he
‘afugi moe meheka. ‘Oku ta'efa'alaua ‘ae kakai,


kae‘uma‘a ‘ae hou'eiki, kuo lava‘i ‘e Setane ‘i he'ene
fai ki he ‘ulugaaga koia, bea lalii ‘ae gaue kovi kuo
nau fai ‘i he manumanu moe ‘afugi, ka nau lau koe
mamahhi kinautolu. Koia na‘a ne ‘ave ‘a Jisu ki he
tu'ahivi ‘oe Temibale ‘i Seluaalema, ‘o ne eginaki
ke ne hobo ki lalo, koe'uhi ke ha ki he kakai
hono aga totonu, ‘o nau fakaabaaba kiate ia. Na‘a
ne mounu‘aki foki ‘ae tauhele ha kubu‘i Folofola.
Tokua, kuo tohi, “‘E kouna ‘eia ‘ene kau agelo ke
aokavakai koe; bea te nau fataki nima koe na‘a
bakia ho ya‘e ‘i ha maka.” Na‘e boto ‘aubito ‘ae teu
‘oe tauhele, bea, ka ne fai ki ha taha ‘oku vale ‘i he
failelei, kuo ne mo'ua ai. Ka kuo boto ‘a Jisu koe
me‘a ‘i he'ene nofo ki he folofola : bea kuo mahino ki
hono loto ‘ae fa‘a fai hala ‘a Isileli ‘i he'enau ala'aki
ki he ‘Otua; koia na‘a no tali mei he folofola ‘a
Mosese ki he kakai k jia, ‘o behe, “ ‘E ‘ikai te ke ha'aki
‘ahi‘ahi ‘ae ‘Eiki ko ho ‘Otua.”
‘Oku meimei ‘ilogata'a ‘a hono tolu ‘oe ‘ahi‘ahi, bea
‘oku lahi ‘ae fifili ki ai. He koe behe koa ke
‘amanaki ‘e Setane ‘e bunou ‘ae ‘Alo ‘oe ‘Otua ‘o
lotu kiate ia! ‘Oku hage koe fai ‘a ha sesele. Ka
‘oku lelei ke tau manatu na‘e ‘i ai ha loto ‘o Setane,
‘o ‘ikai koe ‘atamai be ; bea ko kitautolu ‘oku fa‘a
‘oho hotau loto, ‘o tau fai ‘ae g. me‘a ‘oku ‘ikai ha
lelei ki hotau ‘atamai. Bea ‘oku hage kuo ‘ita ‘a
Setane, ‘i he kalofi ‘e J isu ‘ene g. velo, koia na‘a ne
tu‘utu‘uni ke ‘oho fakamalohi. ‘Oku lau'ilo kotoabe
ki he me'a na‘a ne fai. Na‘a ne ‘ave ia ki he fu‘u
mo‘uga, koe mataga, nai, na‘e tu‘u ai ‘a Mosese ‘o
mamata ki Kenani, bea ne fakaha ai ki he ‘Eiki ‘ae
g. bule'aga ‘o Kenani, ‘o ne tuhu atu, nai, ki he
mama'o ki Loma ‘i hihifo mo Batia ‘i hahake, ‘o ne


fakaha te ne ‘age kotoa kiafce ia, ‘o kabau te ne
bunou ‘o lotu kiate ia. Kuo ‘oji ‘etau fakaha koe
me‘a ia ‘e matu'aki ogo ki he loto ‘o Jisu, ‘ae manat u
ki hono fonua kuo to ki he kakai kehe ; kae‘uma‘a
koe me‘a ia ke ne faka‘amu ki ai, ‘a ‘ene hoko koe
tu‘i lahi, koe'uhi koe fu‘u lelei te ne lava ma‘ae
kakai. Ka koe behe koa ke ne lotu ki ha taha kehe,
‘o ‘ikai koe ‘Otua ! Talu mei mu‘a ‘i mu‘a koe toki
ofi e ‘ae agahala kiate ‘ia, bea mahiuo leva ko Setane;
he ‘oku ‘ikai mo ha taha ‘e behe fau ‘ene fiematamu'a.
Bea teki ‘ae laumalie ‘o Jisu, ‘o ne behe, “ Pei mo ‘alu
Setane ! ” Ka na‘a moe taimi koia na‘e ‘ikai te ne
falala ki hono malohi fakatagata, ka na‘a ne heleta
‘aki ‘ae folofola, he‘ene behe, “He kuo tohi, Koe
‘Otua be te ke lotu ki ai, bea koia be toko taha te ke
‘otua‘aki.”
Kuo ‘oji ‘eni ‘ae ‘ahi'ahi, bea na‘e bau ke ‘alu ‘a
Setane ‘i he lea koia; bea hage ko kitautolu ‘i he ‘oji
ha fekuki lahi na‘a ne ogo‘i vaivai hono jino. Ka
koia aibe, he kuo tau ‘ae tau, bea kuo toka ‘ae fili:
kuo lava ‘ene ‘uluaki gaue, bea kuo ne ma‘u ha ivi
fakalaumalie ke fai'aki ‘ene g. me‘a ‘oku kei toe :
kae‘uma‘a na‘e hifo mai ‘ae kau agelo mei lagi, ‘o
‘omi ‘ae tokoni ki hono jino.
‘Oku hage na‘a ne foki hake leva ki he botu na‘e
fai babitaiso ai ‘a Jione, ‘o ne fanogo malaga ai ; he
koe kuoga ‘o Jione Babitaiso ‘eni. Kuo te‘eki ke
mahino ‘ae feitu'u koia, ka koe ‘uhiga ‘o hono higoa
Betani, koe alafolau; bea, ta, koe taha ‘i he g. botu
na‘e fokotu'u ai ‘ae kakai mei he kauvai ki he kauvai
‘o Jioatani. Kuo ha mai na‘e ‘ikai koe loto ‘o Jisu
ke fa‘ao ‘ae lakaga ‘o Jione : ka koe tagata fai totonu
‘a Jione, bea, ‘i he'ene mamata ki he nofo mai ‘a Jisu


‘i he kau fanogo, na‘e mahino leva kuo hoko hono
taimi ke auauto hifo; hage ko ‘ene lea ki he kau ako,
“ Kuo bau ke fakaaau ia ki mu‘a kau fakaaau au ki
mui.” Koia na‘a ne kamata tuhu kia Jisu, ‘o fakaha
ki he'ene kau ako koe Lanii ia ‘ae ‘Otua, koe'uhi ke
hu‘ihu‘i kinautolu ke nofo ki he Misaia. Bea faifai
bea muimui atu ki ai ha ogo me‘a ‘e toko ua, ko
Anitelu mo Jione ; bea ‘ave kinaua ‘e Jisu ki hono
‘abi, ‘o ne ako kinaua ‘i he folofola, ‘o ne fakamo'oni
koe Misaia ia. Bea ‘i he'ena ‘ata leva, na c a na felelei
ki hona kaiga, ‘o na ‘omi kia Jisu ha toko ua, ‘a
Saimone bea mo Semisi koe foha ‘o Sebeti. Na‘e ‘ilo
leva ‘e Jisu ‘ae aga ‘o Saimone, ‘o ne fakahigoa ia ko
Kifasi ‘aia ko Maka, ka ko hono ‘ai faka-Kalisi ko
Bita ; bea koia ia na‘e fa‘a takimu‘a ‘i he kau ako.
Bea koeni kuo kamata nofo atu kia Jisu ha kau
ako, ‘o hage ko Jione moe kau Labai; bea ne manatu
ki ha taha na‘a na fa‘a fe'iloaki mu‘a, ‘aia na‘e tau
moe tu'uga koia. Ko Filibe ‘ae higoa ‘oe tagata
koia ; bea ‘i hono tala ki ai na‘a ne tali leva, bea nau
toki tu‘utu‘uni ke foki ki honau fonua ko Kaleli, ke
tala ‘ae me‘a ki honau kaiga mo honau kakai. Bea
fai: bea, ‘i he'ene ‘alu, na‘e ului mai mo ha taha ko
Nataniela, ‘aia ‘oku fa‘a lau na‘e ui ki mui ko
Batolomiu. Na‘e fakaofo ‘ae aga o‘ene hoko mai,
bea ‘oku ha ai ‘ae ivi fo‘ou kuo to kia Jisu. Tokua,
kuo ne ‘alu ki ha 1010 fiki ke fai ‘ene fefa'uhi moe
‘Otua, ‘o hage ko Sekobe, ke ma‘u ha tabuaki
fakalaumalie. Bea ne lava ; bea ‘oku ne foki fiefia,
‘o hage ko Isileli, moe ui age ‘e Filibe ke ne ‘alu ‘o
kau ‘i he lahi ‘oe Misaia. Bea, ‘i he faifai bea na a‘u
kia Jisu, na‘e folofola mai ‘ae ‘Eiki, ‘ Ko ha Isileli
mo'oni ‘eni ‘oku ha‘u; kuo ne lava ‘ae loto ma‘a.’


Bea ‘oho leva ‘a Nataniela be ko ‘ene ‘ilo mei fe ‘ae
me‘a kuo hoko. Bea inalimaliage ‘a Jisu ‘o ne behe,
‘Na'aku ‘ilo be ho‘o ‘alu ki he 1010 fiki, moe me‘a na‘a
ke fai.’ Bea ha leva kia Nataniela ‘ae ‘aga ‘o Jisu,
he kohai moe‘Otua te ne ‘afio ‘i hefufu? bea laka
atu leva ‘ene tui, ‘o mama‘o ‘i he kau ako kotoa ‘i
he‘ene behe, “ Ko koe ia ‘ae ‘Alo ‘oe ‘Otua, koe Tub
Isileli koe.”
‘Oku mahalo ‘e he ni'ihi na‘e tala ‘e Nataniela ke
nau ‘alu ki hono ‘abi, bea ko hono ‘abi koia na‘e tu‘u
‘i Kena. Heiblo ki ai, ka ko Kena ‘ae botu na‘a
nau hoko ki ai. Ta, ‘oku ‘i ai ‘ae fa‘e ‘a Jisu, ko ‘ene
ha‘u ki ha ta‘ane na‘a ne kau ai : bea, ‘i he'enau
fanogo kuo ha‘u ‘a Jisu, na‘e tala ‘ae katoaga kiate
ia; bea, ‘i he‘ene ‘alu ki ai, na‘e ‘alu moia ‘ene kau
ako, he koe aga ia ‘oe g. fonua na. Na‘e ‘ikai te navi
‘amanaki te nau toko lahi behe, bea ko hono ‘uhiga,
nai, ia ‘oe ‘oji vave ‘ae uaine ; bea koia na‘e lea ‘a
Mele ki he ‘Eiki ke ne fakaai ‘ae majiva, ‘aia te ne
lava noabe ‘o kabau te ne loto ki ai. ‘Oku te behe
na‘e ‘ikai ko ‘ene toki lulu behe kia Jisu, koia na‘e
‘ai ‘eia ‘ene ki‘i valoki, koe‘uhi ke ne ‘ilo, ne ogo ko
‘ene fa‘e, ka ‘oku ‘i ai ‘ae g. me‘a ‘oku ‘ikai ke kau ai
‘ae tamai be koe fa‘e, ka ‘oku ‘i he tagata be moe
‘Otua. Ka na‘a ne fai be ‘ae loto ‘o Mele ‘i he taimi
koia, ‘o ne liliu ha fu‘u vai, koe kalani ‘e teau tubu,
ke hoko koe uaine fugani lelei. Koe me‘a kehe ‘ae
‘ofo ‘ae kakai: kae fefe, he koe mana ka ko ha mana !
ka ko kitautolu ‘oku lahi ‘etau fakafeta‘l; he ko ‘ene
fai behe ‘ene ‘uluaki mana ko ‘ene hakeaki‘l ‘ae mali,
koe me‘a fakafiefia mo‘oni, mo ‘ene fakatonuhia ‘ae
fai katoaga ; ‘o ha ai koe mo‘ui koeni ‘oku ‘ikai ke
fakabalataha ki he gaue, ka ko hono tu‘utu‘uni ‘e


taha koe fai katoaga : kae‘uma‘a na‘a ne fakamahino
ai koe kava koe taha ‘ia ‘oe g. tabuaki ‘ae ‘Eiki, bea
ko hono inu ‘oku ‘ikai koe agahala, ‘o hage koe lau
‘ae ni‘ihi, ka koe me‘a ke gaue‘aki ke ‘aoga.
Kuo ofi ‘eni ‘ae Basova, bea koia na‘a nau o hifo,
‘a Jisu mo hono famili mo ‘ene Kau Ako, ki Kaban-
eume, ke nau toki tuku fakataha atu moe fu‘u fonoga
na‘e fa‘a ‘alu mei ai ki he katoaga. Ko ‘ene ‘alu
koia koe me‘a mamafa, he na‘e kik'te ki ai ‘e he
balofita ko Malakai, Tokua, ‘e ha‘u fakafokifa ‘ae
‘Eiki ki he Temibale, bea te ne fakama‘a ‘ae kau
gaue. Bea tala'ehai koe fait u'ubake, he koe faka-
lielia ka ko ha fakalielia ‘ae to‘oga ‘ae kau tu‘ukimu‘a
‘i he lotu. Ko ba‘aga be na‘a nau jio ki ai mei he
kau taula‘eiki ‘o fai hifo : na‘a moe tu'uga tobutabu
koe Taula‘eiki-Lahi ka na‘e ma‘u fakatau be, koe tuku
fufu ha ba‘aga ki he hou‘eiki Loma.
Koe g. me‘a koia na‘e mama'o, bea ‘e toki lava
hono faito‘o ‘i he liliu ‘oe aga : ka na‘e ai ‘ae g. me‘a
na‘e ofi, ‘aia na‘e balaku‘ia ai ‘ae kakai lotu mo‘oni
‘i he ‘aho kotoabe. Koe me‘a ‘e taha kuo tuku ‘ae
botu ‘e taha ‘i he Temibale ki he fakatau. Koe
feitu‘u koia na‘e ui koe Bale ‘o Senitaile, he koe botu
ia na‘e gata ai ‘ae hu ‘ae kakai na‘e ‘ikai Jiu, ‘o nau
nofo ‘o fai ai ‘enau lotu, kae laka atu ‘ae Jiu ki he
Pale ‘o Eefine, bea toki hu ai ki he Pale ‘o Isileli,
‘aia na‘e ha ki ai ‘ae olita moe fale tabu. Koe fugani
‘i he Fale masani ‘ae Fale ‘o Senitaile, he koe teau
hono hono loloa; bea na‘e ua ‘ae ‘otu bou ‘i loto fale,
‘o vahevahe hage koe fale ‘e tolu. Koe g. bou koia
koe maka mahuhga bea na‘e fe‘uga moe toko tolu
hono kubuji, bea koe ma‘oluga ‘oe to‘ufufu koe
tekumi ma ono. ‘E ‘ikai te tau fa‘a fakamatala ki


he fonofono me‘a ‘i he kanofale moo ‘aofi :ka na‘e
laui kilu hono ba‘aga, bea na‘e ji‘i ‘ae fale ‘i mamani
na‘a nau tatau.
Koe fale ‘eni ia na‘e tuku ki he fakatau ; bea, ‘i he
hu ki ai ‘a Jisu, na‘a ne vakai kuo fonu ia ‘i he sibi,
moe bulu, moe manu kehekehe. Bea tu‘u ai ‘ae kau
tagata mei he fonua kotoabe, ‘oku nau alea lalahi,
mo fakakikihi ki he totogi ‘oe g. me‘a ke fai'aki ‘ae
feilaulau. Koe mahaki aibe ‘oe Jiu koe manumanu ;
bea, ‘i he taimi koia, ne ‘oho ia ‘o fu‘u lahi; bea ke
faka'uta mu‘a ki he tau'aki kakii mo loi na‘e ogo ki
he finagalo ‘o Jisu ‘i he fale koia, he koe fai ‘ae Jiu
moe Jiu. Bea koe botu ia ke fai ai ha lotu ; tagi ‘ae
faga manu, fehohoaki ‘ae kakai, hage ha ‘abuaka ‘ae
namuku 1 Ne‘ine‘i mamahi ‘a Jisu ‘i he gaohi behe‘i
‘ae faletabu o‘ene Tamai. Tokua, na‘e gaiie hono
finagalo, ‘o ne gaohi ha uibi aki ‘ae g. afo na‘e
no'otaki ‘aki ‘ae faga manu, ‘o ne ‘unu'unu atu ki he
kakai, ‘o ne fekau ke nau hiki kitu‘a. Bea ofo hake
‘ae kakai, bea, ‘i he'enau mamata ki hono fofoga, moe
fiji kitu'a ‘ae houhau ‘a Totonu, na‘e to honau
manaya ‘o nau ga'unu ke ‘alu. Tala atu, koe ofa ‘ae
nima koia moe uibi na‘e ha kiate kinaufcolu ‘oku hage
koe heleta ‘ae Agelo Faka'auha. Bea kohai na‘e kei
manatu ki ha'ane manu, be na‘e fakato‘oto‘a ke tu‘u !
Ka na‘a nau hola kotoabe ‘o hage koe lau ‘ae balofita,
“ Kohai ‘e tu‘u ‘oka ke ka fotu mai.” Toki yete ‘e
Jisu ‘ae faga manu ‘o fakateka mo kinautolu kitua'a.
Hili ia, na‘a ne ‘alu ki he botu fale na‘e nofo ai ‘ae
kau fetogi ba‘aga. Koena ‘ae faga ki‘i tebile, moe
g. fokotu'uga ba‘aga tabu. Na‘e nofo ai taki taha
ha jiana Isileli ke fetogi ‘aki ia ‘ae ba‘aga kuo ha‘u
mo kinautolu mei he mama'o, he na‘e gata ‘i he


ba'aga tabu na‘e hu. Bea, ‘i he vakai ‘e Jisu ki
he'enau nofo hage ha faga hina ke bo ‘enau kai, kuo
fiji ‘ae kaka ‘i honau mata, na‘a ne haga ‘o tulaki ‘ae
tebile moe tebile, kae febunobunaki ‘ae ba'aga ki he
botu kotoabe. Ka mou vakaiii ki he faka‘atu‘i o'ene
fai: na‘e ‘ikai te ne laiki ‘ae g. finaki lube, he koeha
‘anautolu kuo fai 1 ka ne fekau be ke nau ‘ave, kae
ma‘a ‘ae fale o'ene Tamai, ke tau moe gaue na‘e laga
ki ai.
Ne ogo ‘e toko lahi ‘ae kakai, na‘e ‘ikai ha taha
‘e ala ke ta'ofi ‘ae gaue ‘a Jisu : kae fefe, he ‘oku fo‘i
aibe ‘ae konisenisi kovi, ‘o hage koe lau ‘ae mail.
Bea ‘ajiii he‘enau behe, “ Na‘a koe balofita ia ” : he koe
fa'ahiga ia na‘e matu'aki faka‘aba‘aba ki ai ‘e he kakai
Jiu : bea na‘e totonu aibe ‘ae me‘a na‘a ne fai. Koia
na‘e fehu'i kiate ‘ia ‘e he hou‘eiki be koeha ‘ae
faka‘iloga o'ene balofita : he koe aga ‘oe kau balofita
na‘a nau ha‘u mo kinautolu ha me‘a ke ‘iloga ai
‘enau lakaga. Bea tali ‘e Jisu “Holoki ‘ae fale tabu
ni, bea teu toe fokotu'u ‘i ha ‘aho ‘e tolu.” ‘Oku te
behe na‘a ne tuhu, nai, ki hono jino : bea kabau na‘e
‘ikai, ka na‘e tau ke nau ‘ilo koe lea fakatata be.
Ka nau ‘ehe'ehe ‘i he'ene lau ke laga ‘i ha ‘aho ‘e tolu
‘ae me‘a kuo fai ki ai ‘i he ta‘u ‘e 40 tubu ‘o ‘ikai
lava. Ka ‘oku ha mai na‘e ogo mamafa ki honau
loto ‘ene lea; he koe me‘a ia na‘a nau fakamanatu
hake hili ‘ae g. ta‘u, ‘o lau ki ai ‘i hono fakamau'i.
Koeni kuo ma‘a ‘ae fale ‘o Jihova, bea ‘oku hage
na‘e ma'uganofo ki ai ‘a Jisu, ‘o fai ‘ene ako ki he
kakai, bea lahi moe g. mana na‘a ne faka‘iloga‘aki
hono tu'uga. ‘Oku tau ‘ilo mei he g. botu kehekehe
‘ae aga o‘ene g. malaga, bea ‘oku ‘ikai te tau ofo ‘i he
fu‘u gaue ai ‘ae kau Labai; he na‘e matu‘aki febaki


mo ‘enau g. akonaki ‘anautolu ; koia ‘oku hage na‘a
nau o‘i ‘ae hou'eiki ke ta‘ofi; he na‘e mahino kiate
kinautolu kabau ‘e tu‘u ‘a Jisu te nau to kinautolu.
Na‘e tefito ‘ae bule ‘oe kakai Jiu ki he Sanetalimi,
‘aia koe fakataha o'enau kau tu‘ukimu‘a. Na‘e sea
ai ha toko tolu. Koe Taula‘eiki-lahi na‘e mu‘omu‘a,
bea hoko ai ‘ae Tokoni-bule, bea hoko moe toko taha
‘aia na‘e ui koe Akonaki Lahi; bea ko ‘ene gaue,
tokua, ke tokaga ki he g. malaga ‘oku fai ‘e he kau-
gaue ke hoa moe Lao. ‘Oku ha mei he g. tohi faka-
Jiu, na‘e ma‘u ‘ae lakaga koia ‘i he kuoga ‘o Jisu ‘e
he matabule na‘e higoa ko Nikotimasi; bea ‘oku ha
kiate kitautolu, na‘e lahi ‘ae lulu ki he toko taha
koia ke ne ta‘ofi ‘ae malaga ‘ae balofita fo‘ou. Ka
na‘e ‘ikai tilu mo ha toko taha behe ke ‘oho; koia
na‘a ne tuli hake kia Jisu ‘i ha ‘aho ‘e taha, ‘i he‘ene
‘alu, nai, mei Selusalema ki Betani, ke ‘eke ke mahu-
‘is;amalie ‘ae tokateline ‘oku ne fai‘aki. Koe atra
O O
aibe ‘o Jisu ke faka‘aba‘aba ki he kakai na‘e ma‘u
tu'uga ‘i he jiaji, bea ne a‘au leva kia Nikotimasi ‘ae
g. misiteli ‘oe lotu —‘ae fanau‘ifo‘ou, ‘ae aga ‘oe gaue
‘ae Laumalie, ‘ae kalusefai ‘oe Fanautama ‘a Tagata,
&c. Koe aga ‘o Nikotimasi koe loto to‘ohi, koia
na‘e ‘ikai te ne ‘ohofua ‘o biki ki he Misaia: kae
mole ke mama'o ha‘ane ta‘ofi, bea na‘e fai atu ‘e Jisu
‘ene gaue, ‘o ne ma‘u ha kau ako toko lahi.
Na‘a ne fai gaue foki ‘i he tuku'uta, ‘o ne ‘alu holo
‘i he g. kolo ‘o malaga : bea, ka loto ha kakai ke nofo
kiate ia, na‘e babitaiso kinautolu. ‘Oku hage koe
me‘a ia na‘e fokotu‘u ‘e he'ene kau ako, ko ‘enau
maheni, ‘abe, moe me‘a ‘a Jione : bea na‘e tuku ‘e
Jisu ke nau fai, he koe kuoga ‘o Jione ‘eni. Faifai
bea nau a‘u ki he botu ko Selemi, ‘aia ‘oku ‘i he


feitu'u saute ‘o Jiutea ‘o ofi ki Alati. Ta, koe botu
ia ‘oku gaue ai ‘a Jione : bea ne ogo koe tagata lelei
‘a Jione, bea ne ogo ‘e to'oa ‘ae loto ‘oe kakai ‘iate ia,
ka na‘e mahino leva ‘ae hnlu atu ‘a Jisu ‘i he me‘a
kotoa; bea, hage koe lau ‘ae kau ako ‘a Jione, “ JSTa'e
tafe taha ‘a mamani ki ai.” Koe me‘a fakamamahi
kia Jione ke mamata ki he hiki ‘ae kakai meiate ia :
ka na‘e ha ai hono lelei; he tala‘ehai na‘a ne moino'i
meheka, ka na‘a ne fiefia ‘i he toka ‘ae loto ‘oe kakai
ki hanau Misaia.
Kuo bau ke houga ha gaue behe ki he finagalo ‘o
Jisu : kae‘uma‘a na‘e faka'au ke lahi fau hono ogoogo,
‘aia koe me‘a na'a ne fa‘a hola mei ai: koia na‘a ne
tu‘utu‘uni ke tuku ‘ae feitu'u koia kia Jione ka ne
hiki ki Kaleli, ‘aia koe fonua na‘e bau ke ji‘i ai hono
tokaga‘i, he ko hono fonua o‘ona. Koe hala ki ai
na‘e fou ‘i he loto fonua ko Samelia, bea ‘i he‘ene
‘alu atu ai, na‘e hoko ai ‘ene talanoa ki he fefine
Samelia, ‘aia ‘oku utua mei ai ‘ae aga o‘ene gaue ‘i
mamani, bea mahino ai, ta, koe faka‘ofo‘ofa ‘i he faka-
‘ofo'ofaage fau ‘ene to‘oga kotoabe, mo ‘ene boto ‘i
he tohoaki mai ‘ae kakai ki he lotu. Ne‘ine‘i ofo ai
‘ae fefine, bea ne‘ine‘i ogo ki ji‘i kau Samelia koe
Misaia mo'oni ia, koe Fakamo‘ui ‘o mamani.
Bea koeni, ‘oku hage ka toe tubu hake hono ogoogo,
‘aia koe me‘a kuo ne toki hola mei ai: koia na‘a ne
fakavave ki Kaleli, heifilo ‘e toki mate ai, ‘o hage ko
‘ene fa‘a lau, tokua, ‘oku ‘ikai faka‘aba‘aba‘ia ha
balofita ‘i hono fonua o‘ona. Ka na‘e hage ka ‘ajili
ai ‘i he kamata‘aga; bea ne‘ine‘i he koe koto mo‘ui
ia, bea, ka ofi mai ha mahaki be ha tu‘utamaki, kuo
bau ke taba atu hono ivi, ‘o fai ha fu‘u fakamo‘ui.
Ka na‘e fai; he na‘e fakafetaulaki kiate ia ‘i Kena


‘ae mu‘a ‘ae tu‘i ko Helota—ko Kusa, ‘abe, liono higoa
—‘o ne fakamatala ki ji'ono foha kuo tei bekia.
Tuaiekemo kuo buna atu ‘ae folofola ‘a Jisu, ‘Alu, he
kuo mo‘ui ho foha : bea ne ogo ‘ae vamama‘o ‘o Kena
mo Kabaneume, ka na‘e a‘u ki he mahaki ‘o ne mo'ui
leva. Koe ivi ka ko ha ivi! bea na‘e ma‘u, foki, mo
Jisu ha fu‘u fiemalie ‘i he tui malohi ‘ae matabule ;
‘aia na‘e ha ‘i he'eue faifaimalie ‘ene foki ki ‘abi, koe
mahino ki hono loto kuo lelei hono foha.
Bea fai ‘e Jisu ‘i Kaleli ‘o hage ko ‘ene fai ‘i Jiutea,
‘o ne ‘alu holo. ‘o faiako ‘i he feitu'u kehekehe. Na'e
‘ikai te ne fokotu'u ha aga fo‘ou, ka ne fou be ‘i he g.
fouga mu‘a, ‘o ne fai ‘ene g. malaga ‘i he g. sinakoke,
‘aia koe g. falelotu ‘oe kuoga koia. Koe me‘a be
na‘e fo‘ou ko ‘ene akonaki, he na‘e matu'aki faike-
hekehe moe g. lau ‘ae kau Labai; bea hage ha
hu‘avai momoko ki he kakai na‘e fanogo, ko ‘ene
huluhulu ‘ae g. me‘a ‘oe mo‘ui ni, mo ‘aji tonu ‘i
he‘enau g. faigata‘a, mo hiki me‘a mamafa mei honau
loto.
Faifai bea ne a‘u ki Nasaleti, ‘ae kolo kuo ne tubu
ai; ‘o ne hu aibe ki he falelotu ‘i he ‘aho sabate, ‘o
ne kau ‘i hono gaue, ‘o ne lau ‘ae lesoni. Kuo
maheni ‘ae kakai mo ‘ene fai behe, he koe me‘a ‘i
he‘ene hulu atu ‘i he boto na‘e tili ia ki he lakaga
koia : ka koe me‘a na‘e fo‘ou kiate kinautolu, he hili
‘ene lau Folofola, na‘a ne nofo hifo ‘i he botu na‘e fa‘a
fai mei ai ‘ae malaga. Bea nau ofo ai, “ Ta, ‘e malaga
‘e he jiana ni kiate kitautolu ! ” bea kamata hogohogo
honau loto. Na‘e lolomi ‘i he kamata'aga ‘i he malie
o‘ene lea : ka, ‘i he'enau vakai ki he fakamatabule
o‘ene fai, ‘o hage kuo ta hono uho ki he aga koia,
kae‘uma‘a ‘ene fakahoko kiate ia ‘ae balofisai koia ‘a


Aisea, na‘e kamata gaiie hake honau loto. Koeha
‘ae me‘a ‘oku lau ‘e he jiana tufuga na ! koe behe koa
‘oku a'ana ke egina kitautolu 1 bea kabau koe balofita,
koeha kuo ne hakcaki'i ai ‘a Kena mo Kabaneume
kae tuku hono kolo o'onal Ka ka fai atu ‘e Jisu, ‘o
ne fakatatau ia ki he ogo balofita lalahi ‘oe kuoga
mu‘a, ‘aia na‘a nau gaue ‘i he me‘a ni‘ihi ki ha kakai
na‘e matu'aki Senitaile, ‘o tuku ‘a Isileli. Koe me‘a
koia na‘e fakagata ai ‘enau fakama‘uma‘u. Koe behe
koa ke fili mu‘a ‘ae Senitaile bate kinautolu ! bea koe
fai ia ‘e ho jiana tufuga kuo nau ‘ilo talu ‘ene
tamaji‘i! Na‘a nau ‘oho leva ‘o buke ‘o tohoaki ki
he lilifa, bea na‘e toe ji‘i ‘aubito bea nau fai ‘ae
agahala taubotu koe tamate'i ‘oe Fakamo'ui, ka ne
tae'oua ‘ae mahomo raai ‘a Jisu ‘o ne moulu mai, ‘o
hiki mei ai ki Kabaneume. Na‘e ‘ikai, nai, koe mana :
he kuo ‘i ai ha ni‘ihi kuo nau hao behe, koe ‘i ai ha
me‘a ‘i honau fofoga kuo ogo ki he loto ‘oe kakai, ‘o
faigata'a ai ‘enau ala.
Ka koia aibe. Kuo ‘oji ‘eni ‘ae ‘uluaki kuoga
o‘ene gaue, bea kuo mahino hono lakaga. ‘Oku ‘ikai
te ne kei ma‘u ha fo‘i feitu'u ; ka koe balofita ia ‘oe
fonua, ‘io, mo mamani; koia ‘oku tau ke ne hiki mei
ha kolo tuku'uta, hage ko Nasaleti, ki Kabaneume,
‘aia na‘e tu‘u ki tahi, koe fehokotaki'aga ‘oe g. feitu'u.
Na‘e kei tu‘u, foki, ‘ae kuoga ‘o Jione, bea koe gaiie ‘a
Jisu kuo fai na‘e hage ko ha ‘ahi'ahi be; bea ne ogo
kuo lava, ka koe aga aibe ‘o Natula ke ‘ai atu bea
toki malold : bea ko hono ‘uhiga, nai, ia na‘e tala ‘e
Jisu ke tutuku ji‘i ‘ene Kau Ako, mo nenofohifo ia ‘i
Kabaneume, ‘o talitali ki ha toe agi ‘e fai mei Lagi.
{‘Oku kei toe be.)


KOE VAHE TIT.
KOE ‘ULUAKI FOLI.
Koe ‘eiki ‘e Kaleli ‘i he kuoga koia ko Helota
Anitibasa, koe foha ‘o Helota Lahi. Na‘a ne ma‘u,
foki, mo ha fu‘u forma ‘i Tu‘a Jioataui, bea kuo mail
mo ha ‘ofefine ‘oe Tu‘i ‘o Alebea Bita mo Tamasi-
kusi; koia na‘e fa‘a ui ia koe tu‘i, ka na‘e ‘ikai ko
hono higoa totonu, he kuo ne ma‘u ‘ae bule mei he
Tu‘i Loma. Koia na‘a ne fa‘a a‘abi ki Loma ke fai
‘ene fakananivi ki he tu‘i lahi koia, ‘o ne nofo ! i he
abi o hono tehina ko Helota Eilibe. Kuo mali ‘ae
Helota koia mo Helotiasi koe ‘ofefine ‘o hono tehina
‘e taha —koe melo ia ‘oe kau Helota, na‘a nau holoki
‘ae ‘avahevahe ‘oe nofo ‘aunofo—bea koe ta'ahine
koia koe feline kakaba, ‘o ne hoha'a ‘i he ‘ikai ha
koga fonua ‘e bule ki ai ‘e hono husebaniti. Koia
na‘a ne faka'amu ke tokaga ‘a Helota Anitibasa kiate
ia, ka ne liaki hono husebaniti koe, ‘o na mali. Bea
fai: bea ha‘u ‘a Helotiasi ki Kaleli koe kuini ‘oe
fonua.
Kane ogo na‘e faka‘aba‘aba ‘ae toko lahi kiate ia,
ka na‘e ‘i ai ha toko taha na‘e ‘ikai, he na‘e valoki
ma‘ube ‘e Jione Babitaise ‘a Helota ‘i he‘ene mali
moe uaifl ‘o hono tehina, ‘o ne fakaha ‘oku tabu ‘i he


lao ‘ae ‘Otua moe tagata. Koe me‘a gei ‘ae ‘ita ‘a
Helotiasi, ‘o ne o‘i tu‘u hono husebaniti ke fai ha
me‘a ki he balofita. Na‘e manavaho, foki, ‘a Helota
na‘a faifai bea gauekovi ‘ae g. lea ‘a Jione ki he loto
‘oe kakai; koia na‘a ne buke ‘a Jione ‘o li ki he bili-
sone ‘i he kolo ko Makailo,
Na‘e mahino ‘eni kia Jisu kuo ‘oji ‘ae lakaga ‘a
Jione, bea kuo to ‘ae gaue kiate ia ; koia na‘a ne
kamata leva ke tanaki ‘ene kau ako, ‘aia kuo nau
tutuku ji‘i, nai, ke kumi ba'aga, mo gaue ki honau
famili. Na‘e ‘ikai te ne fiu‘a kumi ki ha ni‘ihi, he
koe kau toutai: bea, ‘i he‘ene ‘alu ki tahi, na‘a ne
‘ilo leva ‘a Saimone mo ‘Anitelu mo Somisi mo Jione
‘oku nau mo‘ua ‘i honau g. kubega; bea ne ui
kinautolu, bea nau tuku leva ‘enau gaue koia, ‘o nau
muimui kiate ia. Ko hono toe, nai, na‘e ‘i ‘uta, bea
ne behe ke fakakau mai kinautolu ‘i he‘ene malasra
atu ki honau g. ‘abi.
Na‘a nau kamata ‘enau gaue ‘i Kabaneume ‘i he
Sabate na‘e hoko, bea na‘e ha leva ki he kakai kuo
hoko kia Jisu ha ivi fo'ou, bea na‘e to‘oa honau loto
‘i he aga o‘ene fai. He na‘e lea tala'a aibe ‘ae kau
faifekau Jiu, ‘o boubou ‘enau g. fakaraatala ‘aki ‘ae
lau ‘a ha Labai ‘i mu‘a : ka ka lea fakababau be ‘a
Jisu, mo faka'eia, ‘o hage tofu be koe folofola ‘a ha
tu‘i ‘oku tafataha.
Koe aga aibe ‘o mamani ke tauhoa hono g. me‘a;
bea, ka malohi ‘ae me‘a ‘e taha, kuo bau ke gaue hake
mo hono fili. Bea koeni kuo oli ‘ae bule'aga ‘o
Hevani, bea ha leva kuo ofi moe malohi ‘o Heli. Koe
misiteli ‘ae me‘a koia, ka ‘oku hage kuo fakamaluluage
‘e he ‘Eiki ‘ae seini ‘oe kau tevolo, ‘o ne fakagofua
‘enau hu ki ha kakai ni‘ihi: ‘o ‘ikai, nai, te nau fai


noabe, ka koe ni‘ihi be kuo ‘aufuato ki he agahala.
Na‘a moe g. ‘aho ni ‘oku tau vakai ‘ae aga ‘ae ni'ihi
kuo matu'aki tukuage kinautolu ki he fai agahala,
‘oku hage tofu be koe toko taha mei heli; bea ‘oku
tau behe, be ko ha mama ia, be ko ha fa'ahikehe.
Bea ‘oku ha leva ‘e ‘ikai faigata'a ki ha tevolo ke
nofo‘ia ha taha behe.
Koe kovi ‘oe me‘a koia he na‘e ‘ikai kei fa'iteliha
ji‘i tagata ki hono g. kubu. Ko hotau jino ‘oku hage
ko ha fu‘u mesini, bea ko hotau g. memiba kotoabe
‘oku ‘i p.i hono me'a ue‘i taki taha; bea ko ‘ete ‘alu,
nofo, tu‘u, be koeha ha gaue ‘oku te fai, koe fua be
‘oe ala ‘e hoto loto ki he me'a ue'i ‘o hoto va‘e be
nima be ha. Bea ke fakakaukau age ki he kovi ‘o
ha toko taha, ‘aia ‘oku nofo toko ua mo hono loto ha
tevolo, ‘o ala ki he g. me'a ue‘i ‘o hono jino ko ‘ene
fa‘iteliha be, ‘o gaue ai hono g. kubu ta'ekau ai ‘ae
tagata ! Koe mala'ia ka ko ha mala‘ia !
Ka‘e ai ha taha na‘e ulujino behe na‘e nofo ‘i he
falelotu ‘i Kabaneume ‘i he Sabate koia, ‘o fanogo ki
he malaga ‘a Jisu. Bea faifai, bea ‘ikai kataki ‘e he
tevolo —hei‘ilo be ko ‘ene fehi'a ki ho lelei ‘oku
fakaha ni, be ko ‘ene vakai ‘oku tokagaage ‘ene
tagata ki ai—koia na‘a ne fakalea ‘ae jiana ‘o behe.
“Ko ho ha kimaua, ‘e Jisu mei Nasaleti? Kuo ke
ha‘u ke faka'auha kimaua 1 ‘Oku ou ‘ilo koe, koe
Toko Taha Tabu ‘oe ‘Otua.” Bea ha leva ha aga
fo‘ou ‘ia Jisu. ‘I he'ene fai mu‘a mo ha tevolo, na‘a
ne gaue‘aki ‘ae Folofola, ‘o hage koe fakakikihi ‘a ha
toko ua ‘oku tatau : ka koe fai ia ma‘ana, bea ‘aki
‘ene malohi fakatagata be. Ka kuo e‘a ‘eni hono
‘otua, bea koe fai, foki, ma‘a ha toko taha ‘i hono kakai
kuo fakamalohia; koia, na‘a ne lea ‘o hage koe Tu’i


Univesi, ‘aia ‘oku vaivai ki ai ‘ae Ta'ehamai, ‘o ne
folofola malohi atu, “ Tuku ho‘o lea, bea mahu‘l
meiate ia ! ” Ka‘e bau ke fai ‘e he fa ‘ahikehe, ka, ‘i
he‘ene matalili, na‘a ne fu‘u ha'aki ‘ae tagata, bea
kaila fakamanavahe bea mole. Ne‘ine‘i ofo ‘ae
kakai na‘e mamata ki he febaki behe ‘a Hevani mo
Hell: koe me‘a ‘oku tan ofo ai ‘ae ‘ikai te nan hoko
leva kotoabe ki be lahi ‘o Jisu.
‘I he tutuku ‘ae lotu na‘a ne ‘alu ki he fale ‘o Bita
ke malolo, hebilo ko ‘ene ofi mai, be koe‘uhi ke nan
alea ki he fonoga ‘oku ‘amanaki fai, he na‘e ai, foki,
moe fale ‘o Jisu ‘i Kabaneume. Bea na‘e faifai bea
ha‘u ha toko taba ‘o fakaba ‘oku ‘i ai ha feline ‘i be
fale ‘oku mahaki lahi. Bea tu‘u leva ‘a Jisu ‘o ‘alu
ki ai, ta, kuo bukea ‘i ha mahaki lahi, fa‘ahiga moe
misele. Bea haga leva ‘ae ‘Eiki, ‘o ala ki hono nima,
‘o fokotu‘u, bea tuaiekemo kuo mole ‘ae mahaki, bea
mole moe vaivai na‘e tubu ai, bea na‘a ne tu‘u leva ‘o
tokoni ‘i he taubi ‘o Jisu, he ko ‘ene ta'ahine koe uaifi
‘o Bita.
Na‘e ‘ikai fuoloa ‘ae malolo ‘a Jisu : ‘io, ka ne tae-
‘oua koe Sabate, kuo loa ‘ene mo‘ua ‘i he gaue. Kuo
talanoa'ia holo ‘ae me‘a na‘a ne fai ki he ‘avea, bea
kuo ha ki he tagata Kabaneume kotoabe ko hono ava
eni ke fakamo'ui ‘ene mahaki. Ka koe Sabate, bea
koe taimi koia na‘e fakamamafa ‘aubito ‘ae g. tibutu-
uni ‘oe ‘aho koia ; bea ne ogo na‘e ai ha kau Labai
ni‘ihi na‘e lau ‘oku gofua ke kumi faito‘o ‘i he ‘aho
Sabate, ka ka eginaki ‘e he ni‘ihi ke ‘oua. Koia na‘a
nau nofo ‘o vakai ‘ae la‘a, ‘o nau faka'amu ke vave
‘ene to, he ko ‘ene to leva bea gofua. Bea, ‘i he'ene
buli leva, na‘e holo ‘ae kolo ki he fale ‘o Bita, koe
‘omi ‘o ‘enau kau mahaki. Koe toki me‘a ‘oku ogo


ki he loto ko ‘ete jio ki ha kau mahaki ‘oku nofo
fakataha : bea ‘oku ha mai na‘e fu‘u gaiie ‘ae finagalo
‘o Jisu ‘i he'ene tu‘u mai mei fale, ‘o mamata ki he
fu‘u kau mahaki ‘oku fola ‘i tu‘a. Bea ‘ajili he koe
taha ‘i he g. ‘ulugaaga tu‘ukimu‘a ‘o Jisu koe
faka‘atu‘i ; bea, ‘i he'ene vakai ‘ae mamahi'ia ‘a ha
toko taha ‘i ha mahaki, na‘a ne mamahi ai moia. Bea
manatu ‘e Matiu ‘i he‘ene jio ki ai ki he kikite ‘a
Aisea ki he Misaia,
“ Na‘e to‘o ‘eia ‘etau g. vaivai,
‘0 ne fua ‘etau g. mamahi.”
Ka koe me‘a fakaogojia ‘aubito ‘ae me’a koia,
kae‘uma‘a na‘e tuai ‘ae gaue ko ‘ene ‘alu ki ai taki
taha, ‘o vakai ‘ae aga o‘ene maliaki, bea toki hilifaki
hono nima ki ai, ‘o fakamo‘ui. Koia na‘e faifai bea
vaivai hono jino o‘ona, kaeuma'a na‘e to ‘ae bo'uli ‘i
he te'eki ‘oji ‘ae g. mahaki. Koia, na‘a ne toe hu ki
fale, bea hoko ‘ae me‘a fakaofo koia, koe foki ha ni‘ihi
meia Jisu kuo ‘ikai fakamo'ui.
Na‘e fefe, nai, ‘ae loto ‘oe kakai Kabaneume ‘i
he'ene nofo ‘o mamata ki he me‘a koia —‘ae ‘alu ‘a
Jisu ki ha ‘avea, ‘aelea mai ‘ae tevolo mei he loto ‘oe
tagata, ‘aekounake ne ‘alu, ‘ae tekelili ji‘i tagata moe
kaikaila ‘ae fa'ahikehe, moe ba mai ‘ae haleluia ‘i he
‘iloage kuo mole : ‘ae tebitebi mai, foki, ‘a ji‘i mamatea
na‘e lubei atu ‘anenai, moe foki mo‘ui mai ‘ae kakai
kuo loa ‘enau hage ha ‘aga‘aga. Ne‘ine‘i ‘a ‘ae kau
Kabaneume ‘i he bo koia, ‘o lamalama ha‘ane ma'a ‘ae
‘aho ke nau faka'oji mai ‘enau g. mahaki.
Ka na‘e ‘ikai koe finagalo ‘o Jisu ia. Kuo ‘i ai
‘ene fu‘u gaue ke fai, kae‘uma‘ii kuo ma‘u ‘e he kau
Kabaneume honau ‘inaji. Koia na‘a ne mole ki he


vao kei bo'uli ke fai ‘ene lotu he ko ‘ene aga aibe
ia, ka tu'unuku mai ha gaue lahi, na‘a ne teuteu ki,
ai he fakalahi ‘ene lotu. ‘Oku mo‘oni koe ‘Otua ‘a
Jisu, ka na‘a ne tagata foki, bea na‘a ne fou ‘i he
fouga kuo tu'utu'uni mo‘oe tagata : bea, hage na‘e
malohi hono jino ko ‘ene kai, behe na‘e malohi hono
laumalie ko ‘ene lotu. Lolotoga ia kuo ha‘u ‘ae kakai
mo ‘enau g. mahaki, ‘o nau fafagu ‘ae kau abosetolo :
bea, ‘i he tu'u mai ‘a Bita mo kinautolu, ‘o mamata
ki he hage ha neveneve ‘ae kakai kuo ha‘u, na‘e hiki
honau loto ‘i he'enau kau ki ha toko taha ‘oku behe
hono tokaga'i; koia na‘e tala ‘e Bita ke nau tatali be,
ka nau ‘alu ‘o kumi ‘ae Tagata'eiki. Ka‘a nau kei
fo'ou ki he aga ‘o Jisu, he na‘a nau ‘amanaki te ne
foki leva ‘i he‘cnau tala kiate ia ‘oku tali mai ‘ae kolo
kotoa. Ka na‘e ‘ikai; kae kehe, na‘e fekau ‘e Jisu ke
nau kamata leva ‘enau fonoga; bea na‘a nau ‘alu atu
aibe mei he vao koia ke foli ‘ae g. fonua.
Koe fu‘u foli fakamanavahe ia na‘a nau fai, bea ne
ogo ‘oku ‘ikai ke fakaha ‘i he Kosibeli be na‘e fefe
hono fuoloa, ka kuo bau na‘e mahina lahi; ‘io, ‘oku te
meimei mahalo na‘e laka ‘i he ta‘u, bea na‘e hoko ai
‘ae Basova koia ‘oku ‘ikai ha fakamatala ki ai: he
‘oku ha mai, na‘a ne ‘alu ki Selusalema ‘i he foli koenn
‘Oku hage na‘a ne fuofua fai ki he botu tokelau ‘o
Kaleli, ‘o fai mei ai ki hihifo, ‘o fakaholo mai ‘i he
toga ‘o a‘u ki Jioatani. ‘Oku ha meia Matiu, na‘a ne
toki fou atu ‘i Tikabolusi. Koe g. koga lahi ‘oe
feitu‘u koia na‘e tu'u ki he botu hahake ‘oe Tahi ‘o
Kaleli ; ka na‘e ai hono feitu‘u ‘e taha ‘i hihifo, ‘aia
‘oku ‘iloga, koe kolo ko Betesani, bea ‘oku galigali
koia ia na‘a ne malaga ai ‘i he taimi ni, bea ne toki
hifo ‘i he Tele‘a ‘o Jioatani ki Jiutea ; he ‘oku tau


behe, na‘e ‘ikai te ne ‘alu ‘i Samelia, he ‘oku fakaha
na‘e gata ‘i he kakai Isileli na‘e ne fakamo'ui. ‘Oku
hage na‘a ne ‘alu leva Id Selusalema, he kuo bau na‘e
ofi ‘ae Basova; bea hill ia na‘a ne foil ‘a Jiutea, bea
ne a‘a ‘i Jioatani ki he kauvai, ‘o ne malaga holo ‘i
Tu‘a-Jioatani, ‘o a‘u ki he Tahi ‘o Kaleli, bea toki
foki ki hono ‘abi ‘o malolo ai.
Koe toki me‘a fakaofo koe ‘ikai ha talanoa ki he g.
me‘a na‘e fai. ‘Oku ‘ikai te tau ofo ‘i he ‘ikai ha
fakamatala ‘a Matiu, he na‘o tokaage be ha ‘aho te
ne lele atu ‘o kau ai, ka na‘e lahi bo ‘ene mo'ua ‘i
Kabaneume ‘i he‘ene gaue. Ka kuo bau na‘e ‘i ai ‘a
Bita, bea ko loto ke ‘i ai ha lau ‘a Maake ki ai, ka
‘oku ‘ikai, gata be he‘ene fai ke ‘oji ‘a Kaleli, bea mo
efiie kabuji tevolo. Bea ‘oku ha foki meia Matiu,
na‘a ne fakamo'ui ‘ae g. mahaki faigata‘a ‘aubito, ‘o
hage koe buke fakamahiua, moe mamatea ‘aia ‘oku
‘ikai mei ‘i ai hano faito‘o ‘i mamani. Ka koe gaue
lahi ‘oe ‘Uluaki Foli koia, koe tanaki mai ha kau ako,
bea koe me‘a toko lahi ‘ae fu‘u kakai na‘e foki moia ki
Kabaneume. Kuo lava ‘ene ‘uluaki gaue, ‘aia koe
ui, koe me‘a na‘e tu‘unuku mai kiate ia ke ne fai,
koe fili: bea, lolotoga ‘ene teuteu ki ai, na‘e toe tutuku
‘ae ‘uluaki kau ako, ‘o gaue ki honau g. ‘abi.
‘Oku tau behe na‘e ‘ikai ke fuoloa ‘ae tutuku,
koe'uhi ‘e faigata'a ke nofo mama‘o ha fu‘u kakai
behe ‘o fuoloa ; kae‘uma‘a na‘e mahino ‘aubito ‘ae
kau ako ni‘ihi : koia, na‘e vave ‘ene tu‘utu‘uni ke
fokotu'u ha tu‘uga fo‘ou, ‘o hiki kinautolu ki ai.
Koe faigamalie ‘ae me‘a kotoabe kia Jisu. Koe
‘aho ‘e taha na‘e feta‘ota‘omi mai ‘ae kakai ko ‘enau
fie fanogo malaga, bea vakai ‘e Jisu kia Saimone ‘oku
ne gaohi hono kubega, bea ne tala ke ‘omi hono vaka,


‘o ne heka ai. Tokua, ‘oku ‘i ai ha ki‘i komaki ‘o ofi
ki Kabaneume, ‘aia ‘e lava ai ha taha ke nofo ‘i he
vaka kae ogo ‘ene lea ki ha toko lahi. ‘Oku galigali
koe botu ia na‘e fai ai ‘e Jisu ‘ene malaga koeni : bea,
hili ia, na‘a ne fekau ke tuku atu ‘ae vaka ki he moana
koe'uhi ke ne totogi kia Bita ‘i hono gaiie'aki; he koe
‘Otua ‘oku ne fai gali tu‘i ‘ene me‘a, ‘o ne totogi ‘ae
gaue kotoabe ‘oku fai ma'ana. ‘Oku lau'ilo kotoabe
‘ae me‘a na‘e hoko, ‘ae a‘au ‘ae kubega ‘i he fekau ‘a
Jisu, ‘ae ha‘o ‘ae fu‘u takaga ika, ‘ae ogo leva kia Bita
‘ene ta'etau, moe tala te ne kamata leva ‘ae toutai
lelei hake, koe toutai laumalie. Ka koe me‘a ‘e ua
‘oku tau tokaga'i lahi, ‘ae ma ‘a Bita ke ofi atu ‘i he
fiji kitu'a ‘ae ‘otua ‘o Jisu—hage tofu be ko Mosese
mo Jiobemoekau agelo ‘i he Lagi—bea moe ‘ahi‘ahi‘i
behe ‘o Bita ‘e he ‘Eiki. He koe toutai ika ‘a Bita,
bea koe toki mana eni na‘e ogo ki hono loto, bea koe
va‘iga ‘ae siliva moe koula ‘i he fu‘u ika ‘oku fola na,
bea koe me‘a faigata'a .‘ae ‘omi ‘6 he ‘Eiki hono
manako, bea ke toki behe, Li'aki kotoa. Ka na‘e
fe'uga be ‘a Bita, ‘o ‘ikai ji‘i ha'ane talakitu'a, ka
na‘a ne tuku leva hono kotoa, ‘o muimui ki hono
‘Eiki.
Bea hiki ‘a Jisu mei Kabaneume, ‘o fonoga mo ‘ene
Kau Ako ki ha mo'uga na‘e tu‘u ofi mai. Talu mei
mu‘a moe lau ko Hotini ia, bea ‘oku hoa hono aga
moe g. me‘a na‘e fai. ‘Oku tokalelei ‘ae fuga mo'uga
koia, ‘o hage koe fakamatala ‘a Luke, ka ‘oku hobo
hake ha tumutumu ‘e ua, bea koe botu ia na‘e ‘alu
hake ki ai ‘a Jisu, ‘0 fai ai ‘ene lotu, kae nofo ‘ae kau
ako moe kakai ‘i he botu na‘e tokalelei.
Lolotoga ‘ae g. houa ‘oe bo koia moe lotu ‘a Jisu ki
he‘ene Tamai. Bea bogibogi hake na‘a ne ‘alu hifo


ki he lauua, ‘aia na‘e tatali mei ai hono kakai: ka
na‘e ‘ikai te ne ‘alu kiate kinautolu, ka ne nofo kehe
be. Bea ‘iloage na‘e ogo atu ‘ae folofola, “ Saimone
Bita, ha‘u kiheni.” Beaofo ia be koehahono ‘ubiga,
‘o ne tu‘u be, ‘o nofo atu. Kuo ban na‘e ogo kiate
kinautolu koe me‘a mamafa ‘oku fai : ka tala‘ebai
na‘e ‘alo‘alo‘iloa ‘e ha tabahono iku‘aga—‘ae behe te
nau boko koe g. makatu‘uga ‘oe Jiaji. Bea fai atu
‘ae fili. Koe toko ono na‘e fua nofo kiate ia ‘i he ka-
mata'aga na‘a nau ‘i ai katoa. Ko Matiu koe
bobilikane, ne ogo koe febi'anekina, ka na‘a ne ‘i ai,
bea ai foki mo bono tokoua vaivai ko Tomasi. ‘Oku
tau beho na‘e figofigo, nai, ‘ae ni‘ihi, ‘i he fili kinaua,
be kuo te‘eki ke ‘ata ki bonau loto ‘ae ‘ulugaaga koia
‘ae ‘Eiki, ‘a ‘ene gaue'aki ‘ae me‘a ta‘etoka‘i ‘o mam-
ani ke lava'aki ‘ene g. me‘a. Hoko ai moe Semisi
‘e taha, mo hono foha, ko Jiutasi, ‘aia na‘a na mata-
mata kau, foki, ‘i be famili ‘o Matiu ; bea fakamuimui
‘a Saimone Mamabbi-fonuaj bea mo Jiutasi Isikaliote.
Koe toki me‘a ‘eni ‘oku ha ai ‘ae fai totonu ‘a Jisu,
‘o ‘ikai te ne momou ko ba‘ane manavahe; be na‘e
ban ke taukovi ki be kakai Jiu ‘ene fili ‘a Matiu, bea
ki be bou'eiki ‘ene fili ‘a Saimone Mamahi‘i-fonua.
Kae‘uma‘a ‘e lau ‘e he toko lahi ‘oku ne ‘atamai uou-
nou ‘i he ‘ikai te ne vakai ki mu‘a ‘o ‘ilo ‘ae kovi ‘a
Jiutasi. Ka ‘oku mahino meia Luke na‘e lelei ‘a
Jiutasi ‘i he taimi koia, bea ko hono ‘ulugaaga koia,
‘aia na‘e hoko ki mui koe manumanu, ‘o tubu ai ‘ene
lavaki'i ‘a J isu, na‘e kei fou ‘i bala ia, koe ‘ulugaaga
lelei mo ‘aoga, be koe tokaga lelei ki he ba'aga moe
koloa ke ‘oua na‘a maumau noabe ha me‘a.
Bea koeni kuo lava leva ‘ae gaiie lahi, kuo fokotu'u
‘ae Bule‘aga ‘oe Lagi, bea fakanofo bono bou‘eiki: bea


toki haga ai ‘a Jisu ‘o fai fouo ke ‘ilo ‘c he hou'eiki
koia moe kakai ‘ae lao ‘oe Bule‘aga moe aga ‘oe nofo.
Oiau ! koe malaga ka ko ha malaga ! Te tau ‘ilo ‘i
fe hano tuha ‘ihemalie hono lea, mo ‘ene ‘aji ‘i he
tefito ‘oe totonu, mo ‘ene a'ujia ‘ae me‘a kotoabe
o'etau nofo ! ‘ Oku fa‘a ui koe Malaga ‘i he Mo‘uga ;
ka ko hono totonu koe Malaga‘alei ‘oe Bale‘aga ; he
‘oku ne fuofua fakamatala ‘ae g. ‘ulugaaga ‘oe kakai
‘oe Bule‘aga, bea, hili ia, koe aga ‘o hono lao, moe tu‘u-
tu‘uni ki he lotu moe nofo, bea moe g. faka'iloga ‘oe
kakai ‘oku ‘ikai kau ai. Kane ogo ia, ka koe malaga
faka-Jiu be, bea, hage koe lotu koia, koe koto ta‘elava
be, he ‘oku ‘ikai ha ai ‘ae mo‘ui‘aga moe fakamalohiga
‘oe lotu fo‘ou, koe Itolosi. Ka kuo te'eki hoko hono
kuoga o‘ona—‘e ‘ikai kataki ‘e he‘ene Kau Ako ha lau
behe ; bea na‘e ‘ikai koe ‘oho ‘a Jisu, ka na‘e ne gaue
‘o hage ko ‘ene Tamai, ‘o fai ‘ae me‘a kotoabe ‘i hono
taimi totonu.
{'Oku kei toe be.)


KOE YAHE IV.
KO lIONO UA ‘OE POLL
Hei'ilo be ‘oku ha lelei kiate kitautolu ‘ae mamafa
‘oe gaue koia ‘a Jisu, a‘ene fili ‘ae Kau Abosetolo.
‘I he te‘eki ke fai, na‘e tu‘u ‘ae lotu moe ‘amanaki
lelei ‘a mamani ‘ia Jisu toko taha be; bea, ka ne
bekia, kuo mate ‘ene gaue. Ka, ‘i he'enevavahe mai
‘ae Kau Abosetolo, kuo taha kehe leva. Ke ogo ‘e
hoko ha me‘a kiate ia, ka ‘oku ‘i ai ha ni‘ihi ke
mamahi'i ‘ae lotu fo‘ou, bea ke fakamo‘ui ‘ene gaue.
Koia ne ogo na‘e kei malaga ‘a Jisu ki he kakai, mo
ne kei fai mana, ka ‘oku hago ko ‘ene gaue lain koe
kau Abosetolo, honau ako'i, moe gaohi honau loto ke
tui bikitai kiate ia kae faka‘ehi‘ehi mei mamani.
Koe me‘a koia ‘oku ‘iloga ai hono ua ‘oe foli, bea
‘oku tau ‘ilo na‘e fai kehekehe ‘ae loto ‘oe Kau
Abosetolo ‘i he ‘alu koeni bea moe ‘alu mu‘a, he kuo
nau ma‘u tu‘uga ; bea koe toki me‘a ia ‘oku ne o‘i
‘ae loto ke tokaga. Ko hono ‘uhiga, nai, ia ‘oku lahi
ai ‘ae talanoa ki he g. me‘a na‘e fai: ka, koe me‘a ki
he ‘uluaki foli, ‘oku gata be ‘enau fakamatala ‘i he
higoa ‘oe g. feitu'u na‘a nau ‘i ai.
Na‘o foki leva ‘a Jisu mo ‘ene kau Abosetolo ki
Eabaneume, kae muimui aibe ha fu‘u kakai, kae'uma-


‘a ‘ene Kau Ako a‘ana. ‘lloage na‘e hoko ha me‘a,
‘aia na‘e lahi ‘ene ogo ki he kakai ‘i he mana kotoabe
kuo ne fai. Tokua, na‘e lele mai kiate ia ‘i he hala
ha motu'a kilia, koe fa'ahiga na‘e keheage, he na‘e
tofu hono jino, ‘o ‘ikai hano feitu'u ‘e ta‘ema‘u ai.
Koe mahaki koia na‘e ‘ikai hano faito‘o, kae‘uma‘a
na‘e lau koe mala, koe tautea mei he lagi, bea na‘e
hage koe tauluab ‘oe ‘Otua ‘ae ‘ahi'ahi ha me‘a ki ai.
Na‘e ‘ikai ha toe nofo kovi ‘i mamani ka koe nofo ‘ae
kilia ‘i Kenani: na‘e kabuji kitua‘a, na‘e tabu ‘ene
ofi mai kia kita, bea, ka ai ha'ane ‘alu fano ‘i he bo‘uli,
na‘e ban he ne toutou kaila, “ Tabu ! Tabu ! ” koe'uhi
ke ‘ilo ‘e he kakai, ‘o afe. Ka ko hono me‘a kona
o‘ete kilia koe ‘ikai ha‘ate ‘amanaki. Tokua, koe
me‘a e na‘e mafajia ai hono loto : ne ogo ‘oku ‘i ai ha
fakamo‘ui ‘i he mahaki koe moe, ka ‘oku ‘ikai ha
faito'o ma'ata: ko hoto ha‘i ‘e ‘ikai vete, ko hoto
mala ‘e ‘ikai hiki.
Koia ‘oku tau ofo be na‘e ma‘u fakafefe ‘e he kilia
koeni ‘ene tui malohi, he na‘a ne lele mai kia Jisu, ‘o
kalaga, “ ‘Eiki, ka ne ke loto ke fai, te ke lava ke
fakama'a an.” Bea na‘e hage ha hikuhikule‘o ‘ae tali
vave mai ‘a Jisu, “ ‘Oku ou loto be; ke ke ma‘a koe.”
Kae‘uma‘a na‘a ne fai ‘ae me‘a na‘e tobutabu, na‘a
ne ala ki he jiana ; bea matafi leva ‘ae kilia, ‘o fiji
kitu'a ‘ae mou‘i ‘i hono jino. Kane hoko ha mofuike,
‘o mafahi ‘ae kelekele ‘i honau ‘ao, ‘e ji‘i be ‘ae ofo
‘ae kakai ‘i he me‘a koeni kuo fai. Heiblo be koefe
‘ae me‘a na‘e lahi, he'enau ofo ‘i he mo‘ui ‘ae kilia,
be ko ‘enau teteki ‘i he ala ‘e Jisu ki ai. Bea ‘oku
hage na‘e fu‘u gaue moe finagalo ‘oe ‘Eiki, he koe Jiu,
foki, moia, bea ‘oku balotoloto bate ia a'enau g. aga,
bea kuo ne ogo‘i moia ‘ae teteki ‘i he mamata ki ha


kilia. Bea ‘oku tau ‘ilo ‘ekitautolu, ka ‘iloage kuo
tau ikuna hotau aga, ‘o fai ha me‘a ‘oku febaki moe
to'oga kuo tubu mo kitautolu, hage ‘oku foki leva
hotau loto, ‘o tau ‘ajili mamahi'i ‘ae me‘a mu‘a. Ko
hono ‘uhiga, nai, ia ‘oe na‘ina‘i mamafa belie ‘e Jisu
ki he jiana kuo fakamo'ui, ke ne feimo buna ke vave,
‘o fai ‘ae me‘a kuo tu‘utu‘uni ‘e he Lao. Kuo ikuna ‘e
he'ene ‘ofafaka'otua a'ens aga fakatagata, bea kuo ne
alaki he tagata he'ene fakaatu'i hono fakalili‘a‘ia : ka,
‘i he ‘oji hono fai, na‘e ‘oho ki mui hono ‘ulugaaga mu‘a,
‘o gaue lahi, bea tubu ai ‘ene teke'i ‘ae tagata ke ‘alu.
Koe taha ‘eni ‘i he g. mo‘a lahi ‘i he mo‘ui ‘a
Kalaisi. Tuku kehe hono fakaofo, ‘aia kuo tau
fakamatala ki ai, ka koe fu‘u malaga foki kiate
kitautolu. Na‘e lau'ilo ‘e he Jiu fulibe, koe kilia koe
taibe ‘oe agahala, Kuo fili ia ‘e he ‘Otua ke utua
mei ai hono fakalielia ‘oe agahala ‘i he'ene ‘afio, moe
tabu ha lave ki ai ha gaue ‘a lagi. Bea koe ala koia
‘a Jisu ki ai koe faka'iloga ‘oe fatogia kuo ne ha‘u ke
fai, koe lave ki he kau agahala. ‘lkai ko ‘ene mo‘ui
katoa koe ala be ki he kau kilia fakalaumalie 1 He
toe ai mo ha me‘a ‘e lauga ai ‘ae kau Falesi, ka ko
‘ene lata ki he kau agahala 1 Koia ko ‘ene fahu koia
‘ae tabu ‘i he'ene ala ki he tagata kilia, koe me‘a ia
ke ‘ilo ai ‘e mamani kuo mate ‘ae tabu ‘oe gaue mai
‘a lagi ki he kakai agahala.
Na‘e ha leva koe kuogafo'ou ni ‘oku taha ‘ana ; bea
ne‘ine‘i balotoloto ‘i he ‘atamai ‘oe Kau Abosetolo ‘ae
g. me‘a na‘e fai. Na‘e hoko ofi ki Kabaneume ‘ae
mana kuo tau lea ki ai, bea, ‘i he'ene hu leva ki he
kolo koia, na‘e fakafetaulaki mai kiate ia ‘ae kau
matabule ni'ihi na‘e tu‘ukimu‘a ‘i he jiaji, ko ‘enau
fai ‘ae kole ‘ae ‘eiki ‘oe vahegatau Loma na‘e le‘o ‘i


honau kolo. Koe aga ‘oe hou'eiki Loma na‘e ‘ikai te
nau momo'i toka'i ‘ae kakai Jiu, ‘o nau niatu'aki
fehi‘a ki he‘enan lotu. Ka na‘e taha kehe ‘ao mata-
bule koeni, he na‘a ne matu'aki ‘ofa ki ai, bea kuo ne
laga ‘eia honau falelotu. Kabau koe fale ia na‘e toki
keli ‘i Kabaneume, ta, koe me‘a lahi hono ba‘aga, he
na‘e laga‘aki ‘ae maka mahu'iga, koe mabeli. Koia,
na‘e fakamamafa ‘e he hou'eiki Jiu ki he‘ene kole :
bea na‘e tali ‘e Jisu ‘o ne behe te ne ‘alu atu ‘o faito'o
‘ae mahaki ‘oku lau ki ai. Ka, ‘i he fanogo ki ai ‘ae
senitulio, na‘a ne manavahe. Kuo ne fa‘a fanogo ki
he malaga ‘a Jisu, bea kuo ne mamata ki he gaiie
na‘a ne fai, bea kuo mahino kiate ia ‘oku ‘ikai koe
tagata noa ‘eni, be ko ha ‘eiki fakamama, ka ko ha
toko taha ‘i he fa'ahiga tabu, ‘aia ‘oku vaivai ki ai
‘ae Ta'ehamai. Koia, na‘e to hono manava ‘i he‘ene
fanogo ‘oku me‘a mai ‘a Jisu, ‘o ne fekau atu ha ni‘hi
ke ta‘ofi ; he ‘oku ‘ikai te ne tau ke tali ha ‘eiki behe.
Bea koe‘uma‘a, foki, ‘ene ogojia mai, ka ‘oku talitali
mai ha ni‘ihi mei he Ta'ehamai ke fai ‘ene fekau, kehe
be ke ne fai mai ha fo‘i folofola, bea ‘e lahi noabe ia.
Na‘a mo Jisu na‘a ne fu‘u ofo ‘i he lea koia, bea
ne‘ine‘i, he kuo te'eki ha Jiu te ne a‘ujia ha tui behe.
Bea ne fai leva ki hono loto, bea bunakaki ‘e he'ene
fo‘i lea ‘ae fakamo'ui ki he fale ‘oe senitulio. Bea ne
toki fakaha, koa ha‘a senitaile te nau fai behe te nau
fa‘ao ‘ae tu‘uga ‘oe kakai Jiu, bea, ‘i he Mama ‘e taha,
te nau ‘i he ‘alofi tonu : ka koe kakai Jiu na‘e
fuataki honau tu‘uga, ‘e kabuji kitua‘s, ke nofo aibe ‘i
he bo‘uli. Bea ne toki ‘ai ‘ae lea mamafa koia ‘aia
na‘e fa‘a fanogo ‘e he kakai mei hono fofoga, “ Koe
botu ia ‘e toki hoko ai ‘ae tagi moe fegai'itaki ‘oe nifo.”
Koe aga ia ‘e taha ‘o Jisu, bea ‘oku ‘iate kitautolu,


fold, ke taugalea'aki ha fo‘i lea ni'ihi. Koe taha
‘eni ‘i he g. lea kola, bea ‘oku ogo mai hage tofu be
kuo mamata tonu ‘e Jisu ki he botu ‘oe mala'ia, hea
kuo mahino kiate ia ‘ae matolu ‘oe mamahi ‘oku fai
ai, mo ‘ene hage ha va‘iga ‘ae g. mamahi ‘oe mo‘ui
koeni. Bea koia, ‘i he ‘iloage ‘oku kau ha'ane lea ki
Heli, na‘e ma‘ubu‘ubu hake ai ‘ae lea koia, ‘o hage
‘oku ogo mai kiate ia ‘ae tagi ‘ae kau mala'ia.
Kuo lahi ‘eni ‘ae me‘a fakaofo kuo fai ‘e Jisu ‘i
Kabaneume ; ka ne ogo ia, ka kuo te‘eki ke mahino
kiate kinautolu hono aga. Bea koia, ‘i he'enau fanogo
kuo ne ala ki ha kilia, na‘a nau faka'ehi'ehi mei ai,
‘io, ‘oku matamata hage na‘a nau fakaji‘iji‘i kiate ia
ke ne liiki kitua'a. Ko hono ‘uhiga, nai, ia o ‘ene
kamata leva ‘ene foli ‘a Kaleli, ‘o ‘ikai te ne malolo
ji‘i hifo mu‘a ‘i Kabaneume. He koe ‘aho ‘abogibogi,
‘oku ha mei he Folofola, kuo ne mama'o atu ki he
tuku'uta ; kae‘uma‘s, ‘oku hage kuo fanogonogo ‘oku
tabu ‘ene hu ki kolo, bea na‘a ne taka tua'a be. Ka
ne ogo ‘e faka'ehi'ehi ‘a hou‘eiki, ka tala'ehai na‘e
tokaga ki ai ‘e he kakai, ka koe mo‘a be na‘a nau
ogo‘i koe fiemo‘ui, bea na‘a nau ‘alu atu kitua'ii ke
fanogo ki he‘ene g. malaga, mo mamata ki he'ene g.
gaue. Bea ne ogo kuo hage a Jisu koe fakahed ki
motu, ka tala‘ehai na‘e tuku ai ‘ene gaue.
‘Io, koe ‘uluaki ‘aho o‘ene fonoga, ‘i he'ene fanogo
ki ha tagi ‘oku fai, na‘a ne ‘alu age ke vakai be
te ne ‘aoga ha me‘a ki ai. Ta koe butu. Ko ji‘i
fefine uitou kuo bekia ‘ene tama, ko ‘ene me'a
be taha. Bea ‘ofa ai ‘ae kolo—he koe mamahi
ka ko ha mamahi ! —boa kuo ‘aukau mai kitua'a ‘a
Keini katoa, ‘onau tagi mo ‘oiaue he'ene tukuhiiujia.
Bea koe behe ke nau ogo‘i, kae ‘ikai ogo‘i ‘e Jisu !


Koia na‘a ne ‘alu atu, ‘o ala ki he fata, ‘o hage ko
‘ene ala ki he kilia ‘aneafi; bea ne toki lea ki he
bekia ke ne tu‘u, bea nofo hake leva ‘ae ‘aga'aga, ‘o
ne kamata lea. Ne‘ine‘i fakaha ‘e he folofola na‘e
mo'u ilifia ‘ae kakai kotoabe, he na‘a moe Kau Abose-
tolo kuo te'eki te nan mamata ki ha me‘a behe, bea
koe fu‘u laka ia ‘i he mo‘ui ‘a Jisu : ka na‘e iku lelei
‘ae ilifia, ‘o liliu koe tui malohi, bea na‘e behe ‘e he
ni‘ihi, “ Ta, kuo a‘ahi ‘e he ‘Otua ki hono kakai.”
Ko hotau aga, nai, be koe mala, ‘ae hoko aibe moe
hu‘a ‘ae tahi a‘ene fono hifo; he na‘e feholoi moe
kuoga tui malohi ni, ha fu‘u fakata‘eta‘etui. Koe
me‘a ‘oku tau ofo ai a‘ene kamata ‘ia Jione Babi-
taiso. Kae ‘oua na‘a tau fakaaga ki ai, he kuo
fuoloa ‘ene nofo bilisone ‘i he g. ‘ana ‘i Makailo, ‘o
feagai moe fakabo‘uli, moe mo'ui faigata‘a. Kae-
‘uma‘a koe tama taka vao ia, bea ne ogo koe fale
lelei, ka ‘e hage ko ha bilisone kiate ia; huanoa ‘ae
faga ki‘i loki hage ha buha na‘a ne nofo ha'ijia ai.
Bea te tau ofo koii ‘i he gaue kovi ‘ae nofo koia ki
hono jino, moe mafajia ai hono loto 1 Bea ‘ajili, he
kuo mole ‘eni ‘ae mahina ‘e fiha moe ‘ikai fai ‘e Jisu
ha me‘a mono fakahaofi; ka ko hono kaiga fakajino

bea tala‘ehai ‘e faigata'a ha‘ane hamuji ia mei ke
kovi ‘oku ne ‘i ai. Bea hage na‘e gaue ‘ae Icabaw koia
‘i hono loto, bea fakatubu ‘ae tala‘a ; he kabau koe
Misaia, bea, ta, ‘oku ‘ikai ‘ofa—ka koe‘uma‘a ke faka-
matala, he koe tagata be ‘a Jione, bea kuo meimei
‘ikai ha taha ka kuo tukia hono vaka ‘i he hakau koia,
koe fai kehekehe ‘ae gaue ‘ae ‘Otua mo ha‘a tagata.

Koia na‘e fekau atu ‘e Jione ha toko ua ‘i he‘ene
Kau Ako ke fehu‘i kia Jisu be koe Misaia ia, be ko ha

‘o fakaha kia Jione ‘ae g. mo‘a ‘oku nau fanogo mo
mamata ki ai ; ‘ae fakahake mei he mate ‘ae tama ‘ae
uitou ‘o Keini, ‘aia na‘e fai ‘aneafi, ‘ae faka‘a ‘oe kui
moe fakaha'ele ‘oe bibiki, moe g. alame'a behe.
Bea koe'uhi ke ‘oua na‘a mahalo ‘e he kakai kuo
tuka ‘a Jione, koia na‘a ne haga ‘o fai ha fu‘u faka-
malo kiate ia. ‘Oku ‘ikai ko ha limutu‘u‘i‘au, bea
‘oku ‘ikai ko ha fakananivi, ka koe hoko tonu ‘o
Ilaijia, ‘aia na‘e ‘ikai te ne toka‘i ha toko taha.
Na‘a ne gaue'aki ‘ae me‘a, foki, ke valoki‘aki ‘ae
kakai ‘i he ta‘emau honau loto. Na‘a nau fakaaga
kia Jione koe'uhi, tokua, ko ‘ene aga fakaono'aho ; ka,
‘i he‘ene ha‘u ‘ana, ‘o fai'aki ‘ae aga ‘o onoboni, bea
nau toe aga‘i moia. Na‘a ne gaohi, foki, moe g. kolo
ni‘ihi, ‘aia kuo muimui atu honau kakai kiate ia, ka
kuo te‘eki ke nau tafoki: ko Kabaneume na‘a ne fa‘a
nofo ki ai, mo Kolesini mo Betesaita, ‘aia na‘a ne
fa‘a ‘eve'eva ki ai. Ke ‘oua te nau mahalo te nau
tu'umalie ‘amui koe'uhi ko ‘enau ofi kiate ia, he ‘oku
hage ka hulu atu ‘ae g. kolo na‘e hiteni ‘ata, ‘a Taia
mo Saitoni, ‘io, mo Sotoma mo Komola.
‘Oku tau behe na‘e loloa ‘ae malaga, bea hei'ilo be
koeha ‘ae me‘a na‘e hoko lolotoga ‘ene fai; ha lea, nai,
mei lagi, be ha ; he, 'iloage, na‘e tagaki hake ‘e Jisu


hono fofoga, ‘o ne fakatau folofola ki he ‘Otua. Bea,

kuo tuku kiate ia ‘ae me‘a kotoabe ki he‘ene fa'iteliha.
Bea lolotoga ‘oku nau mo‘utafu‘ua ‘i he fakaha ha
fu‘u me‘a behe, na‘e ogo mai ‘ae lea tuku ‘oe malaga,
“Ha‘u kiate au ‘akimoutolu kotoabe ‘oku fakaogojia
mo mafajia, bea teu fakamalolo kimoutolu. ‘Ai ‘eku
ioke kiate kimoutolu, bea mou ako ‘iate au : he ‘oku
ou fa‘a kataki mo agafakatu'a, bea te mou ‘ilo ha
malolo ‘i homou laumalie. He koe ioke a‘aku ‘oku
molu, bea koe kavega a‘aku ‘oku ma'ama'a.
Koe toki lea malie ia kuo ha‘u mei he fofoga ‘oe
tagata; bea, na‘a mo Jisu, hei'ilo be na‘e toe ai mo
ha‘ane lea ‘e tatau moia. Bea koe kakai na‘e fanogo
ki ai kuo nau maheni moe g. ioke ‘a Jisu, ‘aia na‘a
ne gaohi ma‘a ‘enau faga manu lolotoga ‘ene nofo koe
tufuga ‘o Nasaleti. ‘Oku tau tui na‘a ne gaohi ‘ae
g. ioke koia ke ma‘ama‘a mo molu, ke ji‘iji‘i ‘ae
mamahi ‘ae faga manu : bea, ‘i he‘ene mamata ki he
gaobe ‘a mamani, ‘o vaivai ‘i he gaiie, ne ogo na‘a ne
‘ilo kuo bau ke ai ha ioke mo ha fua kavega, ka na‘a
ne faka'amu ke ha‘u kotoabe kiate ia ke ne gaohi
ke faigofua, mo ne fakamalolo ji‘i laumalie fu‘u hoha'a.
Tokua, na‘e tu‘u ai ‘o fanogo ha fefine, koe toko
taha kuo ne li'aki ia ki he fai fakalielia. Bea na‘e
tautaugamalie ‘ae lea koia bea mo hono loto ; he kuo

agahala kae ‘ikai lava. Ka, ‘i he to mai ‘ae lea ‘ofa
koia, na‘e ofo hono laumalie—“ ‘O ha koa? Keu ‘alu
atu koa kiate ia, bea te ne fakamalolo hoku laumalie 1
Seuke, teu ‘alu leva.” Bea ‘i he'ene kamata laka
atu na‘a ne ogo‘i ‘i hono loto kuo fai; kuo fakamolemole
‘ene g. hia, bea kuo to ki hono loto ha noga lahi.


Fe‘uga moia, kuo fakaafe ‘a Jisu ‘e he matabule ‘oe
feitu'u, koe Falesi na‘e higoa ko Saimone. Na‘e ‘ikai
ko ‘ene ‘ofa ai, ka kohai moia na‘e tiiu ke tali ha
balofita belie 1 Kane ogo ia, kae mo'umuia atu aibe
‘e he feline kuo mafana hono loto ‘i he ‘ofa kuo fai;
‘o ne hu moe kakai ki fale, ‘o tu‘u mei he takafalu ‘o
Jisu, ‘aia kuo ne tokoto ‘i he sofa ‘o haga ki he tebile.
Ka, ‘i he'eno mamata kia Jisu, mo manatu ki he gaue
kuo fai, na‘e ‘ikai te ne mafakama‘uma‘u, bea na‘e
tafe hifo hono lo‘imata ‘o hage ha ‘uha. ‘lloage na‘a
ne vakai ‘oku viku ai hono to'ukubu kelekelea ‘o
Jisu, ‘o ne tu'ulutui leva, ‘o kamata holoholo'aki

ha me‘a lahi behe ma'ana, na‘e gaue hono loto feline,
‘o ne haga ‘o ‘uma ki ai, mo ne takai‘aki ‘ae 1010.
Lolotoga ia, ‘oku kevekeva tonu ‘ae motu'a Falesi,
‘o ne ligofigo kia Jisu ‘i he‘ene kataki ha me‘a belie ;
‘o ne tuku ‘i hono loto ha me‘a ‘e ua : Kabau koe
balofita ‘a Jisu, te ne ‘ilo ‘ae aga ‘oe feline, bea ‘oku
matamata kovi ‘ene fai behe ; bea, kabau ‘oku ‘ikai to
ne ‘ilo ki ai, bea, ta, ‘oku ‘ikai koe balofita ia. Ka ka
mea'i ‘e Jisu ‘ae aga ‘o hono loto ; ‘o ne tali‘aki ha taha
‘oe g. fakatata koia, ‘aia na‘a ne fa‘a huluhulu'aki ‘ae
loto na‘e fakabo'uli; ‘o ne gaue'aki ‘ae feline ke faka-
halaia ‘a Saimone—“ Neu hu mai ki ho fale, bea hoke
‘omi ha vai ki hoku va‘e ? ka koe feline ni kuo ne faka-
viviku hoku va‘e ‘aki hono lo'imata, bea holoholo'aki
hono lau.” Bea ne toki me‘a ki he feline, ‘o ne fakama-
lolo hono laumalie ‘o hage ko ‘ene tala'ofa, he‘ene behe,
“ Kuo fakamo'ui koe ‘e ho‘o tui; ‘alu, ‘o liemaliebea.
Koe‘uma‘a ke toe fakamatala ki he aga ‘o Jisu ‘i
he taimi ni; he kuo mahino mei he g, talanoa kuo
fai ‘ene aga gutuhua mo masani age fan. Bea ‘oku


hage na‘e ha belie ki he Kau Abosetolo, he ‘oku ‘ikai
mo h‘a‘anau toe fakamatala ki ha me‘a na‘e hoko ‘i
he foli ni, gata be ‘enau o moe kau feline koloa'ia,
‘aia na‘a nau tauhi ‘a Jisu mo ‘ene Kau Ako. Ta, koe
fonoga fakamanavahe mo ‘eikijia na‘a nau fai. Koe
ni'ihi ‘i he Kau Ako ‘oku nau mn'omu'a ke fakamelo-
melo, hoko ai mo Jisu moe Kau Abosetolo ‘oku nau
ha'ele atu be mo talanoa; hoko ai, nai, ‘ae hou'eiki
fafine ‘oku heka taki taha ki he‘ene asi, bea muimui
mai ‘ae g. kakai toko lahi —koe fonoga e mei
Kabaneume, koe fonoga 6 mei Betesaita, koe fonoga
e mei Neini, koe fonoga e mei Kena; ‘ae taga'ta, ‘ae
feline, bea koe ni'ihi ‘oku nau fua ‘enau tamaiki.
Ne‘ine‘i gaue ‘ae fatu ‘o Jisu ‘i he ‘ofa ki ai. Ka
kohai ‘oku ofo ‘i he‘enau muimui atu, ‘o kabau na‘a
nau fanogo mo mamata ki he g. me‘a kuo tau toki
fakamatala ki ai. Mo‘oni be ‘a Jisu, Kabau na‘e
‘ikai te nau fakatomala, ‘oku tau mo kimoutolu ‘ae
“bo'uli ‘o tua‘a.”
Ka ‘oku matamata hage na‘e ‘ikai loko tui ha toko
lahi: koia, ‘i he'enau foki ki Kabaneume, na‘a ne
tu‘utu‘uni ke liliu ‘ae aga o‘ene malaga, ‘o fou ‘i he
febale moe fakatata. Hei'ilo te nau tali ha me‘a kuo
hu‘i‘aki ha talanoa malie, ne ogo te nau tekaki ha
akonaki ‘oku tau tonu mai. ‘Oku tau vakai kuo
kofu ‘e he ‘Eiki ‘ae tega ‘oe ‘akau ni'ihi ‘aki ha
kakano melie, hage koe tava moe vi, koe'uhi ke ‘are
*e he faga manu moe kakai ko ‘ene hu'amelie, bea
fetuku ai ‘ae tega, ‘o to ‘i ho botu kehekehe. Koia
na‘e behe ‘e Jisu ke kofu‘aki ‘ene g. akonaki ‘ae g,
fakatata, koe'uhia ke nau manatu fuoloa ki ai, hei'ilo
‘e faifai bea ogo ki honau loto hono ‘uhiga ‘o nau tali ;
bea ka ‘ikai, bea fakaji‘iji‘i ai ki he'enau mala'ia.


Koia, koe ‘alio ‘e taha, na‘e heka ‘c Jisu ki ha vaka
‘i he ki‘i komaki, nai, kuo tau lea ki ai, bea ne fai ki
he fu‘u kakai na‘e tutu‘u ‘i ‘uta ‘ae Malaga Falcatdid.
Na‘e ‘ikai te ne fiu‘a kumi ki ha me‘a ke fai‘aki, he
na‘e ha, nai, kiate ia, ‘i he‘ene nofo ‘i he vaka, ‘ae jiana
‘oku fai ‘ene tutu‘i, moe malaga mai ‘ae faga manu-
buna ke kai, moe to ‘e he kau toutai honau uloa ‘i
tahi. He koe aga aibe ‘o Jisu ke gaue'aki ‘ae g. me‘a
ofi mai, koe g. me‘a na‘e matu'aki maheni ai ‘ae
kakai, ke tu‘uga ki ai ‘ene g. akonaki. Koe me‘a
‘oku tau ofo ai a‘ene lava ke fa‘u‘aki ‘ae g. me‘a
vale koeni ha malaga ‘oku motu taha ‘i hono malie
mo masani fau—koe tagata tutu‘i, koe uite moe tea,
koe tega‘i musita, koe levani moe mahoa'a, koe koloa
na‘e fufu, koe mata'itofe mahu‘iga lahi, moe uloa.
Lolotoga ‘oku tau lea ki ai ‘oku tau ogo‘i koe taha ia
‘oe g. me‘a malie ‘o mamani. ‘Oku ha hage ha
bubuga fetu‘u, be ha tuiga makakoloa, koe me‘a ke
malie‘ia ai ‘ae g. to'utagata. Kohai ‘oku fiu‘a lau 1
kohai ‘oku bahia ‘i he fanogo? ka kohai, foki, te ne
fakamatala be ‘oku tu‘u ‘i he ha hono malie koia ?
‘Oku hage ko ha me‘a fakato'ufeiva ia.
Ka tau ka nofo hifo ‘o sivi ‘ae Malaga Fakatdtd ui,
‘oku ha koe me‘a na‘e fa‘u ma‘ae Kau Abosetolo. ‘Oku
mo‘oni na‘e ‘aoga ki he kakai, kae ji‘i be, bea na‘a
nau tali fakaofo be, ‘o nau ogo‘i hono malie, kae ‘ikai
‘ilo‘i hono ‘uhiga. Ka na‘e tuha tonu moe Kau Abo-
setolo, ‘aia na‘e toe ji‘i bea nau motu atu ke malaga'aki
‘ae Kosibeli. Bea ‘oku ha mahino mei ai ‘ae aga ‘oe
gaue. He hala koa, ‘o kabau na‘a nau ‘amanaki ‘e
‘ohofua ‘a mamani ‘o tui leva ? ka ‘oku na‘ina‘i ‘e
Jisu ‘i he Tagata Tutu‘i, koe toko ji‘i be ‘e mo'ui
mo‘oni, bea na‘a mo kinautolu, ka ‘oku ha ‘i he Uite


moe Tea ‘e fiofio kovi: ‘o behe. Bea koe me‘a ‘oku
tau ofo ai koe ‘ikai mahino leva ‘ae me'a kola ki he
Kau Ako. ‘Oku hage na‘e ofo mo Jisu ‘i he'enau
fehu‘i kiate ia, bea na‘a ne ogo‘i ‘ae maraahi kola, ‘aia
‘oku kau ai ‘ene kau faifekau kotoa, koe kona hoto
loto ‘i he'ete vakai ne ogo kuo fuoloa ‘ete fai mo fai,
bea te ‘amanaki kuo ma‘u bau ‘e he kakai, ‘iloage,
‘oku ha ‘oku ‘ikai.
Kuo ‘oji ‘eni ‘a Kaleli ‘i he‘enau foli, bea na‘e
fcu‘utu‘uni ‘e Jisu ke ‘alu ki he kauvai. Bea, ‘i
he'enau o hifo ki tahi, na‘e hoko ha me'a ‘aia ‘oku ha
ai ‘ae aga ‘oe fai ‘a Jisu mo ‘ene Kau Ako. Tokua,
na‘e tebitebi mai ha fu‘u faifekau faka-Jiu, ‘o ne
behe ke kau ‘i hono lahi. ‘Oku te behe na‘e ogo
lelei ki he kakai ‘ene lau mateaki kia Jisu, “ Tagata-
‘eiki, teu muimui kiate koe, ne ogo be koefe ha botu
te ke me'a ki ai.” Ka ka ‘ilo ‘e Jisu hono loto : bea
ne ogo na‘e ‘ikai te ne fakafiji, ka na‘a ne faka-
mahino kiate ia koe gaixe ‘ae ‘Eiki ‘oku ‘ikai koe

moe faga manubuna ‘oe ‘ata hanau hunuga, ka koe
Fanautama ‘a Tagata ‘oku ‘ikai ji‘a botu ke ‘oluga ki
ai hono ‘ulu.” Koe loto fe ‘oku ‘ikai ke ogo ki ai ‘ae
fakamatala koia ki he nofo majiva ‘a Jisu. Bea ne
ogo kuo mo'oni tu‘o lahi, nai, ‘i he foli koeni kuo toki
fai—he na‘a ne fa‘a taka tua‘a—ka ‘oku hage ko
hono ‘uhiga lahi koe ‘ikai ke fai hano ‘abi ‘o hage
koe kakai kehe. Malo ‘o kabau ‘e fakaafe ia ‘e ha
ni'ihi, ka, ‘oka ‘ikai, bea koe toka ‘i vao ‘e fai.
‘Oku hage na‘e to ‘ae manava ‘oe Kau Abosetolo ‘i
he‘enau fanogo ki he lea koia, ‘o nau ‘amanaki leva
‘oku tu'unuku mai ha fu‘u faigata'a. Koia na‘e


boaki ‘e he toko ua ke nofo, koe taha, koe fie a‘ahi
mu‘a ki ‘abi, koe taha, koe bekia ‘ene tamai. Ka no
ko ha taimi kehe ‘oku te behe ‘e tukuage be ‘e Jisu ;
ka koe faka'oji ‘eni honau ako‘i, bea ‘oku ofi ‘enau
tutuku ke gaue : koia, ua‘a ne fakafiji ki he‘ena kole ;
‘o ne fakaji‘iji‘i ke na tuku ‘ae g. me‘a fakamama ki
he kakai kehe, he kuo mavahe kinautolu, kuo nau
mo'ua ‘i he gaue fakalaumalie.
Na‘a ne heka vaka, ka na‘e ‘ikai te ne lava ke ‘alu
leva. Kuo ‘ikai ‘aubito tuku ‘e he kakai ‘enau muimui
kiate ia, ko ‘enau malie'ia ‘i he'ene g. lau. Koia,
‘oku hage na‘a ne ta‘ofi ji‘i, ‘o toe malaga kiate
kinautolu, bea nau toki folau. Bea na‘a moia, ka
na‘e ‘ikai te nau fie mahu'i meiate ia, ka nau kumi
vaka be, ‘o tuli atu.
Koe aga ‘oe Tahi ‘o Kaleli ‘oku matagi to; bea to
moe ha‘aha‘a ‘ae g. taufa. Ka ‘oku tau behe, koe
matagi koia na‘e hoko na‘e ‘ikai koe gaue ‘ata ‘a
Katula, ka koe laga‘i ‘e Setane, koe “ ‘eiki ‘oe bule-
‘aga ‘oe ‘ata.” He kuo ogojia ‘a Jisu ‘i he gaue, bea
kuo ne tokoto, ‘o ‘oluga'aki ‘ae me‘a fakamolu, ‘o
mohe. Bea, ‘i he vakai ki ai ‘e Setane, na‘a ne behe
ko hono ava e ke lomaki ‘ae tagata fakaofo ni, ‘aia
na‘e ui koe ‘Alo ‘oe ‘Otua. Koia na‘a ne takai ba
fu‘u ‘ahiohio, ‘o velo mai ki he vaha : bea tuaiekemo
‘ene hou ‘ae tahi, bea kamata ke goto ‘ae vaka.
Tala'ehai na‘e fo'ou ‘ae Kau Abosetolo ki he me‘a
koia, he koe kau toutai ‘a honau ni‘ihi; ka, na‘a mo
kinautolu, na‘a nau manavahe ‘aubito, bea, ‘i he‘enau
vakai ki he fakabulou ‘ae vaka ‘e he beau, na‘a
nau fe'ohofi ki he taumuli, ‘o fekalaga‘l ae moe
ke fafagu ‘a Jisu. Bea koe me‘a na‘e ‘ikai mafai ‘e
he logoa'a ‘oe ‘ahiohio moe malohi ‘oe beau, na‘e lava


leva ‘e he tagi tautaba ‘ae tu'utamaki ; he na‘e ‘a ‘a
Jisu. Te tau ‘amanaki te ne fu‘u ‘oho ‘i he ‘iloage
na‘a ne ‘a ‘o vakai ki he vaka kuo mei goto, moe
viligia hono kofu, ‘ae heka mai ‘ae g. beau, kae'uma'a
‘ae fu‘u logoa'a. Ka na‘e ‘ikai ‘aubito. Na‘a ne
ki‘i malaga hake hono ‘ulu ‘o haga kiate kinautolu, ‘o
ofogi kinautolu ‘i he'enau loto ji‘i; bea ne toki tu‘u
ki oluga, ‘o haga ki he tahi hou moe ha‘aha‘a ‘oe
taufa, ‘o ne velo atu ‘ene fekau ‘o tau moe Tu‘i ‘o
Katula, “ Logoa, ‘oua ‘e momo'i gu.” Na‘e ‘ilo ‘e he
tahi moe matagi ‘ae le‘o koia, ‘o nau momou leva; ‘o
‘ikai ha beau ‘e bubula hake, be ha tu‘oni matagi ‘e
‘alu atu : bea ofo ‘ae kau tagata ‘i he fu‘u tofu na‘e
hoko, bea hage koe miji kiate kinautolu ‘ae tu‘utamaki
na‘a nau ‘i ai. Bea ne‘ine‘i ‘ikai fie haga hake ha
taha ‘i he tafoki mai ‘a Jisu ‘o ‘eke be na‘e ‘i fe
‘enau tui. ‘lkai na‘a nau mamata ki he'ene fakama'a
‘ae kilia, mo fakaake ‘ae mate 1 He, ka ne nau
fakakaukau ki ai, tenau ‘utagi'i ‘e ‘ikai lava ‘e he g.
beau kotoabe ‘oe tahi ke lomekina ha toko taha behe.
Ka koe me‘a fo'ou ‘eni, bea kuo ha ‘ae ivi kuo te‘eki
‘ilo ki ai ‘e mamani, bea nau ofo aibe he'enau behe,
“ Koe tagata ha ‘eni ! he na‘a moe tahi moe matagi
‘oku na fakaogo kiate ia ! ”
‘Oku te meimei fakatonuhia ‘ae Kau Abosetolo ‘i
he'enau ta'etui koia, he, ne ogo kuo lahi ‘ae g. mana
kuo ne fai, ka koe takataka faito'o be, bea kuo ‘i ai
‘ae kau tagata, kae'uma'a ‘ae kau balofita, kuo nau
mafai ‘ae g. alame‘a behe. Ka koe me‘a ‘oku ou
lauga ai kiate kinautolu, he'enau ta'etui kiate ia
kimui; he kohai moe ‘Otua ‘oku ne kuku ‘ae matagi,
bea fakatali ‘ae tahi ‘aki hono ‘aofinima ? Kae‘uma‘ii
‘oku te faka‘atu‘i ‘ae mamahi ‘a Jisu ‘i he ji‘i ‘ae


falala a'ene Kau Ako kiato ia. Ko loto ke nau
kataki ji‘i atu, ‘o ‘oua ‘e fafagu leva, ka nau febou-
bou ki honau loto ‘aki ‘ae lau o'ene g. mana. Bea
kovi koa ‘oka ne nau toe talia atu, ‘o luki ki he g.
beau ke faji mai ‘o fai honau tukuigata ki he Tagata-
‘eiki? Hono ‘ikai kuo ma‘u ai ‘e Jisu ha fu‘u
