fiemalie lahi ! Kae ‘oua na‘a tau fakaaga ua‘a aga‘ia
kitautolu. He ‘i he‘otau g. folau mo Kalaisi, ‘oku
fa‘a hoko behe, ‘oku to ha‘aha‘a mai ‘ae taufa kae
matamata ta‘etokaga ‘a ho tau ‘Eiki : bea kabau ‘oku
tau fie fakahoifua hono finagalo, tau fiemalie be mu‘a,
‘o ‘oua ‘e ha'aki fafagu ‘i ha'atau oho fakaetagata
atu; ka tau tuku be ‘ae kovi kiate ia ke ne lolomi
‘i hono taimi.
Koia koe fu‘u ako ki he Kau Abosetolo 'ae folau
kola. Bea koeni, hage kuo nau ‘i he bule'aga ‘o
Setane, bea kuo ne fakate ‘ene g. matatau ke ta'ofi
kinautolu. Koe botu na‘a nau tu‘uta ki ai koe tele‘a,
‘aia ‘oku hifo ai ha vaitafe mei he g. mo'uga ‘o
Besani. Na‘e bau ke tu‘u ha kolo ‘i ha botu behe,
ka ‘oku hage na‘e tu‘u ki ‘uta ‘a Kekesa (be Kelasa,
be kohai fua hono higoa ?); ka kuo nau foa ‘i he kau
tele‘a moe kau tele‘a honau g. fonualoto. Kuo ‘oji
‘etau fakamatala koe kuoga ia na‘e maluluage ‘ae
seini ‘oe kau tevolo, bea na‘e tuku ke nau nofo'ia ‘ae
jino ‘oe kakai ni'ihi. Koe aga ‘oe fa‘ahiga koia na‘e
‘ikai te nau kei hage ko ha kakai: koe toko lahi na‘a
nau ‘alu telefua, bea na‘a nau manako ke nofo ‘i he
g. fafitoka, ‘o fafale ki he ‘aga‘aga ‘oe hekia. Na‘e
‘i ai ha toko ua behe ‘i Kekesa, na‘e nofo ‘i he g.
fonualoto ‘i he kautele'a. Koe ogo maim fekai tofu be
kinaua, bea kuo li‘aki ‘aubito ‘ae hala ki tahi, koe me‘a
‘i he'ena fa‘a ‘oho mai ki he kakai ‘o gaohikovia.


Koia, ‘i he tau afcu ‘ae vaka ‘o Jisu, na‘a nau ‘oho
mai leva ki ai, kae‘uma‘a ‘ae toko taha, ‘aia koe jiana
kaukaua mo aga fita‘a ‘aubito. Ka, ‘i he‘ene ofi mai,
na‘e mea‘i ‘e Jisu hono ‘uhiga, ‘o ne kamata fekau ke
mahu‘i ‘ae fa'ahikehe meiate ia : ka, ‘i he tagitautau
hifo ‘ae kau tevolo, na‘a ne tuku ji‘i ‘o fai ‘ene fehu'i
ki he tagata. ‘Oiaue, hoto fakabo ! toki ai ha
mala'ia be koe nofo ‘ae tagata koia! Kuo tau
mamata ki ha tauga beka, hage koia ‘i Kolovai; ka,
ta, koe tauga tevolo ‘ae Jino ‘oe tagata ni. Na'e behe
‘enau toko lahi na‘a ne fakatatau ia ki he kogakau
Loma, koe fu‘u tau laui afe kuo ne mamata ki he‘enau
fakate ‘i Taibiliase be Kabaneume. Ne‘ine‘i ‘ofa
mamahi ‘e Jisu ki ha toko taha kuo behe‘i, ka, ‘i
he‘ene ene ke fai ha me‘a, na‘e nafui mai ‘e he kau
tevolo ‘enau kole, ke ‘oua te ne fakafoki kinautolu
ki heli. ‘Oku teki hotau loto ‘i he lea na‘e fai.
‘Oku hage ko ha ki‘i fakaava ‘eni ‘oe mataba ‘o
Hetesi, koe ogo mai ha ki‘i to‘e mei he luo ta'ehano-
takele. Be koeha na‘a nau fie hu ai ki he buaka,
bea moeha honau taimi kuo te‘eki hoko 1 Koe g.
misiteli kotoabe : ka ‘oku hage na‘e mahino kia Jisu ;
bea na‘a ne fakagofua ‘enau hu ki ha fu‘u faga buaka
toko lahi na'e kaikai mei he mama'o ‘i he tahifohifo
‘oe mo‘uga. Hei'ilo be na‘a ha fefe ki he Kau
Abosetolo —be na‘e ogo mai ha me‘a ‘o hage ha
tu‘oni matagi ‘oku ‘alu atu —ka na'e mahino leva
‘oku ‘ikai koe ge‘eji me‘a ‘ae folofola ‘a Jisu, bea
fakafokifa na'e ‘ai ‘e he faga buaka laui afe koia
‘enau fu‘u mofuta, ‘o nau ‘oho vale hifo mei he
mo'uga, ‘o to ki tahi ‘o melemo.
‘Oku te behe na'e hage ha miji ki he Kau Abose-
tolo ‘ae me‘a kuo nau mamata ki ai—‘ae lea ‘ae kau


tevolo, ‘ae fekau ke nau hu ki he buaka, ‘ae ‘oho ‘ae
fu‘u faga manu ki tahi, mo nau mole ai—ka ko hono
fakamo‘oni e ‘ae tagata, ‘aia kuo mole ‘ene aga kehe,
bea ‘oku ne feiga ha me‘a ke ne vala'aki. Koia, na‘a
nau ‘age hono kofu, ‘o nau tu‘u ‘o ofoofo ‘i he‘ene
ta‘utu ‘i he va‘e ‘o Jisu, ‘o haga fakafeta'i hake kiate
ia kuo ne hiki ‘ae fu‘u mala mei he‘ene mo'ui. Bea
na‘e ‘ikai ko kinautolu be, ka na‘e faifai bea toko
lahi ‘ae kakai na‘e ha‘u mei he kolo ke mamata kia
Jisu moe tagata : bea ko loto ke nau fakafeta'i ‘i he
a‘u mai ki honau fonua ha toko taha ‘oku ne mafai
ke fakateka atu ‘ae bule‘aga ‘o Setane, mo fakahaoll
kinautolu mei he g. kovi behe. Ka na‘e ‘ikai ‘aubito.
Koe me‘a be na‘a nau jio hi ai koe mole ‘enau koloa.
Koia na‘a nau hole ke ne hiki ki ha feitu'u kehe.
Ne‘ine‘i ui ‘a Jisu koe 1 Tagata ‘oe g. Mamahi ’! Bea
kohai ‘e fakamatala ki he aga ‘o hono loto ‘i he'ene
heka-vaka ‘o foki ki Kaleli, ‘oku ‘ikai mahu‘iga‘ia ‘ae
kakai ‘ia te ia, bea kuo kabuji ia mei he fonua na‘a
ue ‘alu ko hono fakamo'ui!
Ka ‘oku mo'oni ‘ae hiva, Kuo vahevahe ‘e he
‘Eiki
“Ha ‘aho ke mamahi, bea toki fiofa.”
He, ‘i he ofi ‘ae vaka ‘o Jisu ki Kabaneume, na‘a ne
vakai ‘oku hage ha fu‘u Yao ‘ae tutu‘u ‘ae kakai ‘i
‘uta, ‘o nau hagai malimali mai, ‘o fiji kitu'a ‘enau
fiefia ‘i he'ene foki leva. ‘Oku mo'oni na‘a nau fo‘i
‘i he to ‘ae taufa, ‘o nau toe bale ki ‘uta : ka na‘e
‘ikai te nau tutuku, ka nau nonofo aibe ‘o fakajio ki
he kauvai, mo faka'amu ke ne vave mai. Bea ‘oku
te behe na‘e hage ‘ae me‘a koia koe feau ki he fina-
galo lavea ‘o Kalaisi, bea tokaage ha fu‘u malaga
malie na‘a ne fai kiate kinautolu.


Bea na‘e ‘ikai koe ‘aho be koia, ka na‘e behe
ma‘ube ‘enau tokaga age, ‘o nau ha‘u mei he feitu‘u
kotoabe ki Kabaneume. Koe g. ‘aho lahi ia ki he
kolo koia, na‘e matu'aki hiki ia ki lagi ‘i he gaue
na‘e fai ai. Kae ‘oua na‘a tau behe, na‘e faka-
balataha ki he lelei; he na‘e ha‘u moe g. fili ‘o Jisu,
‘aia na‘e ‘ikai te nau ha‘u ke mou‘i, be ke fakafeta'i
‘i he fakamo'ui ‘oku fai; ka ke fakaaga be, mo kumi
ha tu'uga ki hano fakamo'ua. Hage koe molokau,
‘aia ‘oku ne kai tatau moe manu kehe, ka ‘oku liliu
‘iate ia koe me‘a kona, behe, koe kau Falosi moe kau
faiako ‘i he Lao na‘e ha‘u, ne ogo na‘a nau fanogo
tatau mo mamata tatau moe kakai, ka koe me‘a be
na‘e tubu ‘i honau loto koe meheka moe fehi'a moe ‘ita.
Koe ‘aho ‘e taha, na‘e matu‘aki fonu ‘ae fale ‘i
loto mo tu‘a: koe'uhi, tuku kehe ‘ao malie o'ene
faiako, ka koe taimi koia na‘e obe ‘ia Jisu ‘ae ivi
fakamo'ui. He koe tagata foki ‘ae ‘Eiki, bea na‘e
‘alu ‘ene mo‘ui ‘i he ‘aluga ‘0 tautolu. Bea koe
‘ulusaaara ‘e taha ‘oe kakai mafai ‘0 mamani ‘oku
O O
faka‘aho honau g. ivi. ‘Oku fakaha ‘e he kau mau,
tokua, koe ‘aho ni‘ihi ‘oku ‘ikai te nau mei lava ha
me‘a, ka koe ‘aho ni‘ihi ‘oku buna noa be ‘ae g. himi
mei honau loto : bea ka ko ha kakai ‘oku faiva lahi,
‘oku toka honau ivi ki ha faiva ‘e taha ‘i ha ‘aho ‘e
taha, ‘o mafai lahi ‘ae me‘a koia, kae taiki ‘ae g.
faiva kehe : ka nau malohi ‘i ha me‘a taha ‘a bogibogi,
‘o vaivai ‘ae ‘uluaki me‘a. Bea ‘oku hage na‘e
meimei behe mo Jisu, bea ‘oku fakaha, tokua, koe
‘aho ‘oku tau lea ki ai na‘e toka hono malohi ki he
faito‘o. Bea koia ai, ‘abe, na‘e toko lahi behe fan
‘ae ha‘u, koe ha kiate kinautolu ko honau taimi e
ke lava ‘ae g. mahaki faigata'a.


Bea ‘iloage na‘e ha‘u ha fonoga mei ‘uta ‘oku nau
lubei mai ha jiana na‘e mahaki lahi, koe mamatea.
Ka kuo nau tomui, bea ne ogo ‘enau hole kae ‘ikai
ha taha ‘e fie faka‘atsage. Kuo nau foki, nai, ka ne
tae'oua ‘ae mahino kiate kinautolu, kabau ‘e lava
‘enau mahaki kia Jisu, kuo bau be ke mo‘ui; koia
na‘a nau fakato'oto'a ai, ‘o nau ‘alu hake ki he
tu‘afale ‘o tubagi ‘ae ‘ato, ‘o tukutuku hifo ‘enau
mahaki ki he ‘ao tonu ‘o Jisu. Na‘e malie‘ia ‘a Jisu
‘i he'enau tui, he na‘e loua, koe tui ki he'ene mafai,
bea koe tui ki he'ene ‘ofa, foki, moe ‘ikai te ne tubu-
tamaki ‘i he'enau fiematamu'a. Koia na‘a ne faka-
mo'ui ‘ae jiana : ka, ‘i he aga ‘o hono fai, na‘a ne
fakamahino ki hono g. fili na‘e nofo mai, ‘oku ‘ikai
koe tagata be ia. ‘Oku mo‘oni kuo ne fakaake ‘ae
mate, bea kuo ne fai ‘ene bule ki he matagi moe
tahi; ka kuo fai ‘ae g. me‘a behe ‘e he kau balofita ;
ka koliai ha balofita kuo ne fai ‘ae fakamolemole
agahalal Na‘e totonu be ‘ae lau ‘ae kau Falesi, koe
me‘a ia ‘ae ‘Otua toko taha : ko hono kovi na‘e ‘ikai
te nau fakaiku ‘enau tesi, ‘o nau behe, ta, koe ‘Otua
‘a Jisu. Bea ‘ajili, he na‘e fai leva ha fu‘u faka-
mo‘oni, he'ene behe ki he tagata mamatea, “ Tu‘u ‘o
to‘o ho mohega ‘o mole ki ho ‘abi.” Na‘e ‘ikai ‘i ha
tagata ke fakamolemole agahala, na‘e ‘ikai foki ‘i ha
tagata ke fakamo'ui ha mahaki behe. Ke fu‘u e‘a ‘i
he ‘aho koia ‘ae ‘Otua ‘o Jisu, bea koe ta'etui ‘ae kau
Falesi koia koe ta‘e te nau fie tui.
Kuo mamahi, nai, ‘a Jisu ‘i he fefeka honau loto,
bea ne hiki mei he fale ‘o ‘alu ki matatahi: ka ‘e
‘ikai ‘aubito fie mahu'i atu ‘ae kakai, ‘o nau toubili
aibe ‘i mui; koia, na‘a ne tu‘u ‘o toe fai ‘ene ako
kiate kinautolu ‘i matatahi. Ka kuo mahino kia


Jisu ‘e ‘ikai te ne lava ke fua toko taha ‘ae gaue, bea
kuo hokqjia ‘ae taimi ke tukuage ‘ae Kau Abosetolo.
Koia, ‘i he tutuku ‘ae kakai, na‘a ne ‘alu ki he fale-
tute ke ui mai ‘a Matin. Koe Abosetolo koia, ne ogo
kuo ne nofo ki he gaue ‘ae ‘Eiki, kae hage kuo na
alea mo Jisu ke ne ma‘u ‘ene gaue fakabule'aga, kae-
‘oua, nai, ke boto hono fetogi. Bea ‘oku hage kuo ne
nofo ‘i he folau na‘e fai ke fakama'obo'obo ‘ene g.
tohi, bea, ‘i he'enc fanogo ki he fekau koeni ‘a Jisu,
na‘a ne tukuage ‘aubito ‘ene gaue, ‘o ne fakaafe ‘a
Jisu moe kau ako, ‘o ne fai ‘ae fu‘u katoaga faka-
mavae.
Koe fa‘ahiga na‘e kau ki ai ‘a Matiu, koe ha‘a
hobilikane, koe fa'ahiga fehi‘anekina. Tala'ehai na‘e
fiemalie ‘ae kakai Jiu ke tukuhau ki muli, ka te nan
kataki, ‘oka ne fai ‘e he muli be : ka koe belie ke kau
ai honau kakai ‘onautolu ‘i he ‘eke ‘oe tukuhau, koe
me‘a koia na‘a nau ‘ita lahi ai, bea ‘ajili, he na‘e fa‘a
fakalahi ‘ae tukuhau ‘e he fa'ahiga koia, ‘o ta'ofi ‘ae
hulu ma'anautolu. Koia na‘e nofo mavahe ‘ae kau
bobilikane, bea bau ai ke nau kaume'a moe fa'ahiga
maveuveu : bea koia, ‘i he katoaga koeni ‘a Matiu,
na‘e toko lahi ‘ae kakai belie, bea na‘e ‘ilo foki ‘e
Matiu, ‘e ‘ikai kovi‘ia ai ‘ae finagalo ‘oe ‘Eiki, he kuo
ne ha‘u ke kumi ‘ae sibi kuo he. Ka tala'ehai na‘e
behe ‘ae jio ki ai ‘ae kakai kehe, bea na‘e lauga ai ‘ae
kakai na‘e tutu‘u ‘itu‘a. ‘E ‘ikai, nai, tokaga ‘a Jisu
ki ai, ka ne tae‘oua ‘enau haga ‘o valoki ‘ene kau ako,
‘aia koe me‘a na‘e ‘ikai ji‘i te ne kataki.
Ka ko ‘ene tali ki ai ne ogo ko ha ki‘i momo'ime'a,
ka hono ‘ikai koe toki me‘a malie ! Koeha ha toe
tali ‘e fai ki ai ? ‘ Koe tonu ‘oe tagata faito'o ke ‘i he
kakai ‘oku mahaki.’


Ka na‘e ai mo ha fa'ahiga ‘e taha na‘e lauga, koe
kau ako ‘a Jione. Ko hono ‘uhiga o'enau fai
‘anautolu, na‘e ‘ikai koe nonofo ‘a Jisu moe kau
ta'elotu, ka koe fu‘u kai ‘oku fai; he ‘oku gali ko ha
katoaga lahi ia, ko ha katoaga faka-Loma ‘o mahili
moe me‘a na‘e fa‘a fai ‘e he Jiu. Ka ko Jione
Babitaiso koe tagata mo'ui faka‘ehi‘ehi, bea kuo ne
na‘ina‘i ‘ae me'a koia ki hono kakai, ‘o tu‘utu‘uni ha
g. ‘aho ‘aukai. Bea, ta, ko honau ‘aho ‘aukai ‘eni ‘oe
fa‘ahiga koia, bea ‘i he'enau tu‘u fiekaia ‘itu‘a, ‘o
mamata ki he hebo ‘e Jione mo Anitelu mo kinautolu
na‘a nau kau ‘i mu‘a ‘ae g. ma‘aga-gako mei he fu‘u
tisi ‘i he loto tebile, na‘e ‘ikai te nau makataki, bea
nau ‘unu'unu atu ‘o lauga ki he tagata‘eiki. Ka‘e
tali faka‘atu‘i ‘e Jisu; he, ne ogo na‘e ‘ikai haohaoa
‘ae tu‘utu‘uni, ka na‘e malo be ‘enau tauhi ki ai ;
koia na‘a ne fakamanatu be kiats kinautolu kuo ui ia
‘e honau tagata‘eiki koe ‘eikita'ane, bea kabau koia
bea ‘aukai fefe, ‘aia koe me‘a fakamamahi, he koe
aga ‘oe ta‘ane koe fakafiefia ia. Bea ne toki fai atu
ha g. lau ke mahino, koe lotu fo‘ou ‘oku ne fokotu‘u
‘e ‘ikai tau moia ‘ae vaka motu‘a, kae fa‘u be ha vaka
fo‘ou.
Pe‘uga moia moe ha‘u ha toko taha ‘i he hou‘eiki
lalahi ‘oe kolo, ko Jiailosi, ‘o ne kole ki he ‘Eiki ke
me'aage ki hono ‘ofefine, he ‘oku mahaki lahi; hei‘ilo
be te nau ma‘u age be ‘ikai. Bea tu‘u leva ‘a Jisu ‘o
‘alu, bea hage ha mahaki ha tauga beka ‘ae fe'ohofi
mai ‘ae kakai ke o moia. Na‘e ‘alu ‘ae toko lahi ko
‘enau fie mamata, nai, ki ha me‘a ‘e fai; ka na‘e ‘ikai
ke behe kotoa ; bea na‘e ai ha toko taha na‘a ne
lao'aki atu ‘i he kakai, ko ‘ene behe, ko hono ava 6
he kuo fuoloa ‘ene tatali ki ai. Koe fefine ia, bea ko


hono mahaki koe me‘a ia ‘oku ma‘i ‘e he kau fefine,
bea koia kuo ne nofo ta‘emo‘ui aibe koe faigata'a ‘ene
fakamatala ki ai. Ka na [ a ne tui ‘aubito kia Jisu,
‘o ne behe ‘oku ne mafimafi ‘o a‘u kihono taba‘i kofu;
bea ka ne faifai boa ne lava ke ofi atu ke ala ki he
bao koia na‘e taube ki lalo, te ne mo'ui. Koia na‘a
ne ‘oho atu moe kakai, ‘o ne tuiaki atu ke a‘u kia
Jisu. Koe g. hala ‘i Kabaneume ‘oku faji‘i ‘aubito
bea ka ‘iloage ‘e fakafetaulaki mai ha ni'ihi na‘e ban
ke bae atu ‘ae fonoga ‘o feta‘ota‘omi. Koia na‘e lava
ai ‘e ji‘i fefine ‘ene me‘a, ‘o ne ala ki he kofu ‘o Jisu
ta‘o‘ilo ki ai ‘e ha taha.
Koe mo‘a na‘e hoko, ‘oku ‘uhiga ai ‘ae g. me‘a lain
‘i he mo‘ui ‘a Jisu. Na‘e fakamo'ui ‘ae fefine ‘i
he'ene ala koia ; bea koe fakamo'ui koia na‘e fai ‘e
Jisu, ‘e hono ‘Otua, ka na‘e ‘ikai ‘ilo tokua ki ai ‘e
hono tagata. Na‘a ne ogo‘i ha fou atu ha ivi ‘i hono
jino, ‘o mole ki tu‘a, bea na‘e buli bate ia hono tubu-
‘aga. Na‘a mo kitautolu ‘oku ‘i ai ‘ae g. me‘a ‘oku
fai ‘iate kitautolu, ‘aia ‘oku tau ogo‘i kae ‘ikai ‘ilo.
‘Oku ‘oho hake mei he g. botu taumama'o o'etau
mo'ui, bea ‘oku ‘ikai te tau ‘ilo be koeha ‘i he
kamata‘aga : ‘oua ke fuoloa, ‘oua ke raaheni ai, ‘oua
ke ‘eke mo fakakaukau, bea toki mahino. Behe, —
tabu mo ‘Ene ‘Afio—na‘e lahi ‘ae g. me'a na‘e gaue
‘i he o‘tua ‘o Jisu, kae ‘ikai ‘ilo ‘e hono tagata : ogo‘i
be kae ‘ikai ‘uhiga—‘aea na‘a ne ta‘e‘ilo ai ‘ae g. me‘a
ni‘ihi ‘o a‘u ki he'ene bekia.
Koia na‘e tu'u leva ‘a Jisu ‘o fehu‘i be kohai ne
ala ki ai; bea ‘i he ofo ‘ae kakai, he kuo nau
femilimilihi kotoabe ‘i he ‘efi'efl ‘oe hala, na‘a ne
fakaha ‘oku taha kehe ‘ae ala koeni, he kuo ‘alu atu
‘iate ia ha fu‘u ivi, bea kuo bau kuo mo‘ni aiha taha


Bea, ‘i he ha ki he feSne kuo ‘ilo‘i ‘ene me‘a, na‘a ne
ha‘u tetetete be ‘o fakamatala. Na‘a ne manavahe
‘aubito, he na‘e tabu ki he fefine ke ala ki ha toko
taha behe, huanoa ha ‘eiki ‘o hage ko Jisu ; bea ka
ne ko ha Labai kehe, tokaage ha fu‘u tautea ‘e fai
kiate ia. Ka ka malimali mai ‘a Jisu ‘o ne behe,
“ ‘Oua te ke manavahe, ga'ata, kuo fakamo'ui koe ‘e
ho‘o tui.”
Fe‘uga moia moe cage ha ni'ihi kia Jiailosi, ‘o
fauafanaage kuo bekia hono ‘ofefine. Kae tabouage
leva ‘e Jisu, “ ‘Oua te ke lotoji‘1; kehe be ke ma'u ho‘o
tui.” Bea, ‘i he'enau fai atu, na‘e ogo mai ‘ae tagi mei
he ‘abi ‘oe matabule; he kuo mahino ‘ene vaivai ‘ae
ta'ahine, bea kuo nau uga ha kau tagi. Ko ha
fa‘ahiga ia, hage koe ha‘atufuga ‘i Toga; bea na‘a
nau ma‘u ‘enau ba'aga ‘i he ‘alu ki he g. butu ke fai
‘ae tagi. Na‘e ‘iloga ha hutu lahi ko ‘enau toko lahi
ki ai, moe ‘i ai ‘ae g. fa‘ahiga, ‘ae ifi me‘aJea, moe
tagi fetuki &C. ‘o hage koeni, bea ‘oku fakatatau ia
‘e he kakai kuo fanogo ki ai, ‘oku hage, tokua, koe
kalou ‘a ha faga kuli ‘i he bo‘uli ‘i hono fakavavana ‘o
hoto loto. Ke‘ine‘i ta‘ofi ‘e Jisu, he koe me‘a ia na‘e
tiiu moe hiteni; ‘o ne fekau ke nau ‘alu, ka ne hu mo
Jiailosi mo hono uaifi, bea moe toko tolu tu‘ukimu‘a
‘i he Kau Abosetolo ki he loki ‘oku ‘i ai ‘ae ta'ahine.
Kuo mahino ‘ene bekia, kae fakahuhulu be ji‘i
finemui, bea fakatatau ki ai ‘e Jisu hono le‘o ‘i he‘ene
‘alu atu ‘o lea ‘i he lea faka-Alemea, “ Ji’i ta‘ahine,
ke ke tu‘u.” Ka‘e ogo atu ‘ae folofola koia kitu‘a
mama, bea hage ha taba ‘a ha ‘uhila ‘ae fold mai ‘a
ji‘ono laumalie ; ‘o ne ofo hake ‘o mo‘ui.
Koe ‘aho ‘iloga ‘eni ‘i he mo‘ui ‘a Jisu—koe faiako
hegihegi, moe fakamo'ui ‘oe mamatea na‘e tuku hifo


‘i he ‘ato; koe toe faiako ‘i he matatahi, koe ui ‘o
Matiu moe katoaga ; koe fakamo‘ui ‘oe feline mahaki,
kae‘uma‘a ‘ae fakaake mei he bekia ‘ae ‘ofefine ‘o
Jiailosi—bea ko loto ke ne malolo ji‘i: ka koeni ‘oku
tuliimui ha ogo kui, ‘o tagi mai ke faito'o. Ka na‘e
maheni ‘a Kabaneume moe me‘a behe, bea koeha, nai,
‘ae me‘a na‘e ‘oho ai ‘ae kakai ‘o hage ko ha me‘a
fo‘ou 1 He koe Jiu fo na‘e ‘ikai gaiie hono loto ‘i he
lea ‘ae ogo kui, “ Hako ‘o Tevita, ‘alo'ofa mai ” 1
Koe toki lea ia ke ga'uta ai ‘enau g. ‘amanaki. Na‘a
ko hono ‘uhiga ia ‘oe fakata‘eta‘etokaga ‘e Jisu : he
kuo ne toki na‘ina‘i kia Jiailosi ke ‘oua na‘a tala ‘ae
mana koe, ‘o hage ‘oku ne fie ta'ofi ‘ae gaiie ‘ae kakai.
Koia ai, ‘abe, na‘a ne mo‘u ‘alu atu aibe ki ‘abi: ka
kuo fiemo'ui be ‘ae ogo jiana, bea na fakata‘eraalu‘ia
mai ‘o hu ki fale. Bea tokagaage leva ‘e Jisu, ne
ogo ‘ene ogojia, bea, ‘i he ha kiate ia kuo na ma‘u ‘ae
tau koia koe tui, na‘a ne ala ki hono mata ‘o na
mo‘ui.
Kuo te'eki ke meimei mahu'i atu kinaua moe hu
mai mo ha ni'ihi, ‘oku nau ‘omi ha tagata na‘e noa,
‘o ‘ikai‘ia koia, ka kuo ‘avea foki. Kuo bau kuo
ogojia ‘a Jisu ‘i he gaiie ‘oe ‘aho fakamanavahe ni, ka
ne ogo ia, ka ka haga leva ia ‘o kabuji ‘ae fa'ahikehe
kae‘uma‘a na‘a ne toe taha atu ‘o fakamo'ui ‘ene noa,
‘o ne lea. ‘Oku ha mai koe me’a fo‘ou ia, he, ne ogo
kuo lava ‘e he kau Labai ke fakabuna ‘ae tevolo mei
ha tagata, ka na‘a ne foki be ki hono aga mu‘a ; ‘o
kabau ko ha kui, na‘e kui aibe, ‘o behe. Koia koe
kaiga na‘e taki mai ‘ae jiana, ‘oku hage na‘a nau
‘amanaki be ki he faito'o ‘ene ‘avea; bea, ‘i he ‘iloage
na‘a ne kamata lea, na‘a nau fu‘u ‘oho, ‘o nau ogo‘i
kuo hoko ha kuoga £o‘ou ki he fonua.


Koe toki ‘aho ‘eni kuo ha lagilagi ai ‘a Jisu. Talu
‘ae ‘anebogibogi moe buna meiate ia ‘ae iyi fakamo‘ui,
‘o liage koe vai mei ha fauniteni. ‘Oku hage ‘oku
tau ‘i he fakatubu ‘o mamani he'etau fanogo ki
he'ene folofola mai, “Ke mo‘ui, Ke ‘a, Ke lea.” Ka
koe tumutumu ‘eni ‘ene lagilagiha, bea hoko leva
hono fakama‘l lain ; he na‘e tuku ‘e he kau Falesi
‘ene fu‘u mafai ki he Tevolo, ‘o nau behe ‘oku na kau
moe Toko Taha Kovi. ‘Oku ‘ikai ha fakamatala ki
he aga ‘o Jisu ‘i he'ene fanogo ki ai; ka kuo bau na‘a
ne ogo‘i lahi. Ka na‘e ‘ikai ha‘ane tali ‘i he ‘aho
koia; ka ne ‘alu be ki he tuku'uta, ‘o fai atu ‘ene
gaue ki he g. kolo.
Koe kolo ‘e taha na‘a ne a‘u leva ki ai, ko hono
kolo o‘ona, ‘a Kasaleti; boa ne ogo na‘a nau kabnji
ia mei ai ‘i mu‘a, ka ne toe ‘alu ki ai he na‘e kei nofo
ai hono tuofafine: kae‘uma‘a hei'ilo kuo liliu honau
loto ‘i he g. talanoa kuo nau ma‘u, bea ‘oku nau tui
‘eni kiate ia. Kae ‘ikai ‘aubito. Koe me‘a be na‘a
nau jio ki ai koe toko taha na‘e tubu ‘i honau kolo,
bea ‘oku ‘i ai be ha ni'ihi ‘i hono famili; bea mole
ke mama'o ha'anau tui koe taha kehe ia, ‘o mahili
bate kinautolu. Bea ko ‘enau ta'etui koia na‘e ogo
kia Jisu, ‘o hage kuo ha‘ijia ai; bea ‘oku fakaha ‘e
he Kosibeli na‘e ‘ikai to ne lava ke fai ai ha loko
gaue fakaofo. Koo lea koia koe me‘a fakamanavahe,
boa ‘oku ‘uhiga ai ‘ae g. me‘a lain. Ta, ne ogo ‘oku
mafimafi ‘ae ‘Otua, ka ‘oku ‘i ai ‘ae g. me‘a ‘oku ‘ikai
te ne lava—tabu moia. Bea ne‘ine‘i behe koe ta'etui
koe me‘a ‘oku melemo ai ‘ae kakai ki Heli, he koe
me‘a ia ‘oku ne lava ke fakanounou ki he nima ‘o
Jihova.
Ka na‘e ‘ikai ke behe hono tali ‘e he g. fonua kehe,


ka na‘u aukau mai kitua ke fanogo kiate ia. Na‘e
gaue hono fatu ‘i he ‘ofa ki ai, ‘o ne hoha'a ‘i he ‘ikai
te ne lava ke gaue kiate kinautolu katoa : bea ne
tu‘utu‘uni ke tuku atu ‘ae Kau Abosetolo ke ‘alu,
tautau toko, ua ki he g. fcitu'u, ‘o faito‘o mahaki mo
raalaga.
Amujiaage ‘eau na‘aku ‘i ai ke mamata ki he
fofoga ‘oe Kau Abosetolo ‘i he'enau fanogo ki he
folofola ‘a Jisu, he'ene tuku kiate kinautolu ‘ae g.
mafai koia kuo nau mamata ki ai ‘i he'ene ‘Afio —‘ae
kabuji ‘oe fa‘ahikehe ! ‘ae fakama'a ‘oe kilia ! ! ‘ae
fokotu'u ‘oe bekia !! ! ‘E hage, nai, ha miji kiate
kinautolu. Ka kohai ‘e ofo ‘i he kamata hiki honau
loto, mo nau fie foki ki Kabaneume ke kumi ha
teuteu na‘e tau mo ha gaue belie. Ka ka ta‘ofi ‘e
Jisu ; he koe kakai ‘ena ‘oku tagutu mai, bea koe
behe ke nau ‘alu ‘o kumi teuteu 2 Kabau ‘oku ‘i ai
ha'anau ba'aga be kofu, lelei; ka ‘ikai, ke nau ‘alu
aibe, ‘o falala ki he ‘Eiki ke ne ue‘i ‘ae kakai ke ‘omi
ha‘anau me‘a. Kane ogo ‘enau gali majiva behe, ka
na‘a ne tuku atu kinautolu, ‘o hage koe kau talafekau
‘a ha tu‘i. Ke nau ‘alu, tokua, ki he ‘abi ‘oe matabule
‘oku tau ke tali kinautolu, ‘o nofo ai; bea, ka ‘ikai
tali ‘e ha taha, koe me‘a kehe ‘ae tautea ‘e fai. Na'a
ne eginaki ke nau fai fakabotoboto, he koe mama
tau; bea ke ‘oua te nau ofo, ‘o kabau ‘e gaohikovia
kinautolu : kae jinoeme'a ke ‘oua te nau manavahe :
he ‘oku nau ‘i he malu ‘oe Tamai ‘oku ‘i Hevani.
Na‘e lahi mo ‘ene lau, mo jikaki kiate kinautolu,
‘io, na‘e hage ‘oku ne mamae ke tuku ke nau ‘alu; he
ko ji‘i fo‘ou, bea na‘a nau faihala, be lotoji'i. Koe
me‘a ia ‘oku boko ma‘u be kiate kitautolu; ‘oku
faifai beaa‘u mai ‘ae taimi ke tuku atu ji'eta foha, be


koe ta‘ahine, be ko ha ako : bea kohai ‘oku ! ikai ke
tala'a hono loto, ‘o ne ‘ai atu ha eginaki mo ha
eginaki na‘a galo ha me‘a 2 ‘Oku ha behe ‘ae malaga
koeni ‘a Jisu, ji‘ene na‘ina‘i mo eginaki mo fakamatala
ke nau ma‘u ba‘anau ‘uta ‘i he taimi kotoabe, moe
me‘a kotoabe. Bea ae toki tukuage ke nau fai gaue
‘i Kaleli, ka ne fou ‘eia ‘i ha hala ‘e tab a.
(‘Oku kei toe be.)


KOE YAHE V.
KOE KAMATA EAKAEILI MAI.
Hili ‘ae o ‘ae Kau Abosetolo ‘oku buli ‘a Jisu, bea
‘oku ‘ikai te tau ‘ilo be na‘a ne fai gaue ‘i fe : ka ‘oku
hage na‘a ne fou ‘i he g. botu ofi ki Selusalema, he
koe kolo ia ‘oku ne toe ha ai kiate kitautolu.
Na‘e ai ha katoaga na‘e fai ‘i he mahina ko
Febueli, koe fakamanatu ki he talotalo ‘a Hamani
koe Balemia ‘o Besia ki ha ‘aho ke tamate‘i ai ‘ae
kakai Jiu, ‘aia na‘e liliu ‘o iku ki he hakeakih ‘o
honau fa'ahiga. Ka‘e ‘ikai koe katoaga fakajiaji,
bea na‘e fakamama ‘aubito hono me‘a ni‘ihi; ka koe
Jiu ‘a Jisu, bea, ‘iloga ha me‘a na‘e kau ki hono
fa'ahiga, na‘e mamafa kiate ia. Kae‘uma‘a na‘e
matu'aki feholoi moia ‘ae Basova, ‘aia na‘e totonu ke
ne ‘alu ki ai.
Koe aga ‘oe fai gaue ‘a Jisu na‘a ne fa‘a ‘alu ki he
g. botu ‘oku fakataha'aga kakai, ‘o talanoa mo
kinautolu ‘o faka’uhiga folofola. Koe taha ‘oe g.
botu behe koe leba ‘o Sailoame, ‘aia koe fu‘u vai na‘e
tu‘u ‘i lalo ‘i he gata'aga ‘oe tele‘a na‘e vahevahe‘aki
'a Saione mo Selusalema Motu'a. Koe vai na‘e toka
ki ai na‘e tafe hifo mei ha fu‘u ‘ana ‘i he loto mo‘uga
na‘e tu‘u ai ‘ae Temibale ; bea na‘e ‘ikai tafe ma'ube,


ka ‘i he‘ene toki mahua. Koia, ‘i he ‘iloage na‘e
behe na‘e ma'ubu'ubu fakafokifa, bea gaueue ‘ae vai
‘oe leba; bea mahalo ‘e he kakai koe mana, ‘o ‘ikai te
nau ‘ilo ki hono ‘uhiga, he na‘e buli ‘ae halagavai,
bea kuo toki ‘ilo ki ai kimui ni. Bea ogoogoa atu
koe vai fakamo'ui ia ; bea lolofi mai ‘ae kakai mahaki
ke balufcu, ‘oka fai ‘ene gaue koia. Kuo bau ke
mo‘ui ai ba ui'ihi, he ‘oku ‘i ai ha fa‘ahiga mamate
‘oku tubu mei he loto, bea ka tui ‘e ha taha te ne
mo‘ui, te ne mo'ui. Bea koia kuo laga ai ‘ae lau,
‘oka gaue ‘ao vai, koe ue‘i ‘e ha agelo bea ‘iloga ‘ae
fua hobo ki ai bea mo'ui.
Koia kuo toe ui ai ‘ae vai ko Beteseta, be hoe fale
‘oku fai ai ha mesi; bea na‘e fetakoto'i aibe ha fu‘u
kakai, hei'ilo te nau ta‘imalie ha mo'ui. Bea kuo
bau ke lata ki ai ‘a Jisu, he koefe ‘ae botu totonu ke
‘i ai ‘ae faito'o, ka koe lotolotoga be ‘oe kakai mahaki.
‘Oku tau ‘ilo te ne fie fakamo'ui kinautolu kotoa ;
bea tala’ehai ‘e faigata‘a, ka na‘e ‘ikai koe finagalo
o‘ene Tamai ke ne gaue noabe ‘aki ‘ae mafai mana,
na‘a maveuveu ‘ae g. tu‘utu‘uni o‘etau mo‘ui ; koia,
na'a ne fili be ha taha, ‘aia ‘e ‘uhiga mo ‘aoga ‘ae
fakamo'ui ki ai. Koe aga ‘oe kau mahaki, ‘oka nofo
fakataha, ke talanoa‘ia ma‘ube honau alagamahaki.
Bea na‘e ai ha tagata na‘e ma‘uganofo ki he leba,
koe mamatea, bea ne lau ma'ube ki he 38 ta‘u ‘ene
‘amanaki mo‘ui kae ‘ikai. Bea ogo leva ki he
finagalo ‘o Jisu ‘ae fika koia, he koe toko taha ia na‘e
balotoloto ‘i hono ‘atamai ‘ae hisitolia ‘oe kakai, bea
koe ta‘u ia ‘oe nofo ‘ae kakai Tsileli ‘i mu‘a ‘i ve‘e-
Kenani, ‘o ‘ikai te nau lava ke hu ; hage tofu be ‘ae
jiana koia ‘i he ve‘e-leba. Ko hono ‘uhiga, nai, ia
na‘e behe ‘e Jisu te ne fakamo'ui ‘ae tagata ni, hei'ilo


‘o e‘a ki he kakai Jiu ni'ihi ko honau Jiosiua ia kuo
ha‘u ke fakahu ki he Kenani mo'oni. Bea ‘i he'ene
tokaga'i ‘ae tagata na‘a ne vavaga'i leva ‘ae aga o'ene
mahaki; na‘e ‘ikai ko hono jino be na‘e mamatea, ka
koe loto foki ; ko hono ‘uhiga o'ene fuoloa behe koe
ji‘i ‘ene fie mo'ui. Koia ia na‘a ne fai ai ‘ae fehu‘i
fakaofo koia, “ ‘Oku ke loto ke mo‘ui 1 ” Bea ha ‘i
he'ene tali ‘ae toumoua ‘o hono loto, bea ka ne tae‘oua
‘ae ‘ofa ‘ae ‘Eiki, mo ‘ene fekau ke tu‘u ‘o ha'ele,
behe ne mo‘u nofo aibe ‘o mate ‘i he ve‘e-leba.
Na‘e ne ogo‘i leva kuo ne mo'ui, ka, ‘i he'ene ofo
hake ko vakai ‘a Jisu, kuo ne lakaage ‘o hu kitua‘a,
‘o ‘ikai te ne fie ha ‘i he taimi koia, na‘a ta‘ofi ‘ene
gaue ‘i he tokaga fau ‘ae kakai kiate ia. Ka na‘e
manatu ‘e he jiana kuo tala ‘e he tagata na‘e fakamo'ui
ia ke ne to‘o hono mohega ‘o ‘alu; koia na‘a ne takai
hono fala, ‘o fua ‘o ‘alu kitua'a. Kohai ‘e fakamatala
ki he'ene fiefia ‘i he'ene tebitebi atu ‘i he hala ki
hono ‘abi ? Ka na‘e nounou be, he ‘iloage ‘oku
fakafetaulaki mai ha tu'uga matabule ko ‘enau ha‘u,
nai, mei he Temibale; bea, ‘i he'enau jio kiate ia, na‘a
nau ‘oho, ‘o nau kalaga mai ke tuku ‘ene fua mohega
he koe Sabate. Bea manavahe ‘ae jiana, he koe
lotojifi, ‘o ne fakaha koe fekau ‘ae tagata na‘a ne
fakamo'ui ia. Bea fie ‘ilo leva ‘e he hou'eiki be
kohai ‘ae fiematamu'a kuo ne le'ei ‘ae lao; bea hei‘ilo
be koeha ‘enau fakamana na‘e fai ki he jiana he'ene
maumau Sabate. Koia na‘a ne faka'amu ke ‘ilo be
kohai kuo ne fakamo'ui ia koe'uhi ke ne uga ai : bea,
‘i he ‘iloage na‘a ne maamta kiate ia ‘i he Temibale,
na‘a ne fehu‘i be kohai, bea ne ‘alu ‘0 tala ki he
hou'eiki.
‘Oku tau fehi'a ki he gaue ‘ae tagata koia, bea ‘oku


hage ‘oku ha mei ai na‘o ‘ikai ke mo'ui aibe ‘ae
laumalie ‘oe kakai na‘e fakamo‘ui honau jino. Ko
hono kovi he na‘e liliu ai ‘ae nofo ‘a Jisu. Kuo
fuoloa ‘ae ‘ita kiate ia ha ni‘ihi ‘oe hou‘eiki, ka kuo
te‘eki ke kakaha fau, be iku ki ha tu‘utu‘uni kiate
ia. Ka koe me‘a koeni na‘e toki bau ai honau loto
ke ta‘ofi‘ene gaue ; ke koe tauhi ‘oe Sabate koe taha
ia ‘oe g. me‘a na‘a nau matu‘aki mamahi'i, bea koe
ala ki ai na‘e hage koe ala ki hoto tama'imata. Koe
aga aibe ‘oe g. lotu ke faifai bea mahu‘iga‘ia ‘ae
kakai ‘i hono g. migimigi‘i me‘a, kae ma‘ama‘a ‘i hono
uho moe tefito. ‘Oku ha ia ‘i he lotu Mahometi mo
‘enau mamafa ki he a‘ahi ki Meka, moe lotu Bobi
he‘enau mamafa ki he tabukaimanu (fee. Bea na‘e
behe moe lotu faka-Jiu. Koe tauhi ‘oe Sabate koe
me‘a mei he kamata‘aga, bea ko hono tefito koe ‘ofa
ki he tagata, ke ne ma‘u ha ‘aho ke fiemalie hono
jino, bea ‘ata hono loto ke gaue ki hono laumalie moe
‘Otua. Bea, ‘i he fokotu'u ‘oe lotu faka-Jiu, na‘e ‘i ai
‘ae g. migimigi‘i tu‘utu‘uni, koe g. fakafiloga be, ke
mahino ai ‘ae aga ‘oe tauhi Sabate. Na‘e tabu ‘ae
fua kavega koe'uhi be ke fiemalie ‘ae tagata,
kae‘uma‘a ‘ae kakai-gaue moe kau bobula ; ka kuo
nau falo atu ia ke tabu ‘ete to‘o ha faga ki‘i me‘a
hage koe bine, bea tabu ‘ete ‘ai ha su ‘oku ‘i ai ha
fa‘o. Koia koe Sabate, ‘aia na‘e tu‘utu‘uni ‘e he
‘Eiki koe me‘a fakafiemalie ki he tagata, kuo hoko ia
koe toki me‘a fakamamahi, koe kavega na‘e mafajia
ai ‘ae kakai kotoa: bea ‘oku hage na‘e mamahi ‘a
Jisu ‘i he maumau behe ‘ae tu‘utu‘uni lelei a‘ene
Tamai, bea na‘e bau hono loto ke toho mai ki hono
aga totonu.
‘Oku ‘i ai mo ha me‘a ‘oku tau tokaga‘i ‘ia Jisu ‘i


he taimi koia, ‘ae ‘ikai te ne kei fufu hono tubu'aga.
‘I Kaleli kuo ne ha koe Misaia, ka koe toko taha kuo
tubu ‘i honau lotolotoga ; ka ‘i he‘ene ‘i Selusalema
na‘a ne tukua ke e‘a hono tu‘uga, ‘o ne fuataki ‘ene
tubu mei he ‘Otua. Bea tala'ehai koe me‘a ia ‘e
fiemalie ai ‘ae hou'eiki Jiu ; he na‘a nau tui ko honau
lakaga ‘i mamani ke mamahi‘i ‘ene taha be ‘ae ‘Otua,
bea ‘e ‘ikai te nau momo‘i kataki ‘ae behe ‘e ha taha
‘oku ‘i ai ha me‘a ‘oku kakuga ke ofi ki he'ene ‘Afio.
Koia, ‘i he'etau vakai ‘ae ‘ulugaaga koia ‘e ua ‘oe
kakai Jiu, moe tu'utu'uni ‘e ua ‘a Jisu, ‘oku tau ‘ilo
koe febaki ‘e fai.
Na‘e ‘ikai tuai, he, ‘i he'enau ‘ilo leva mei he
tagata ko Jisu be kuo ne fakamo'ui ia, na‘a nau
kamata ke lau‘i mo ta‘ofi ‘ene gaue. Ko loto ke nau
jio ki he fu‘u ‘ofa kuo ne fai ki he tagata, kae‘uma‘a
‘ae mana fakaofo, ka nau fakagalomi ‘ae ki‘i lakahala
—‘o kabau koe lakahala; he koe to‘o ha ki‘i fala koe
maumau Sabate 1 Ka na‘e mo'oni be ‘ae lea ‘a Jisu
‘i ha taimi ‘e taha, ‘oku nau heu‘i ‘ae namu kae folo-
fua ‘ae kameli. Ka na‘e ‘ikai ko jia‘a ‘enau me‘a.
Na‘a nau ‘amanaki, nai, ‘e tu'uga ‘ene fakakikihi ki
he ji‘i ‘oe me‘a kuo fai ‘e he tagata, be ha ; ka na‘e
‘ikai ‘aubito, bea na‘e to honau manava ‘i he'enau
fanogo ki he'ene ‘afugi ‘oku ne ma‘oluga ‘i he lao,
bea ‘oku gofua kiate ia ke gaue ‘i he sabate ‘o hage
ko ‘ene Tamai koe ‘Otua.
Koe me‘a ‘oku fakakikihi ki ai be na‘e ‘ilo lahi ‘ae
kakai Jiu ki he Toko Tolu Tabu, be ‘ikai. Ka koia
aibe, he na‘e mahino mei he behe ‘e Jisu “ ‘Eku
Tamai” ‘oku ‘ikai ko ‘ene lau ki he ‘Otua koe Tamai
‘a mamani katoa, ka ko ‘ene jio ki ha nofo kehe, ‘o


hage ko ha tamai fakamiima mo hono foha ; bea ha ai
leva ko ‘ene fakatatau ia ki he ‘Otua. Bea kakaha
ai ‘enau ‘ita, bea ‘ikai kei gata ‘enau feiga ke ta'ofi
‘ene gaiie, ka nau matu‘aki tuli hono tamate'i.
Na‘e fanogo ‘e Jisu ki he‘enau lau‘i 'ene lea
fle'otua, kae mole ke mama‘o ha'ane momoi bebeu ;
kae kehe na‘a ne ‘ai ke fu‘u matala, he'ene to‘o kiate
ia ‘ae gaiie na‘e fa‘a tuku ki he ‘Otua toko taha.
Koe fokotu‘u ‘oe bekia koe me‘a ia te ne fai, bea ‘e
vave ‘ene fai ki ha ni'ihi. ‘Oku ne fai ‘ae mo‘ui ‘iate
ia be, ‘o hage ko ‘ene ‘Afio, kae‘uma‘a koe Fakamau
Lahi kuo tuku kiate ia toko taha : bea ne kamata
leva ‘ene gaue koia ‘i he‘ene fakamau ‘enau ta'etui.
Tala‘ehai kuo ji‘i ‘ae fakamo'oni kiate ia. Ka‘e
fakamo'oni ‘e Jione Babitaiso. Koe me‘a ji‘i, nai, ia
he koe tagata, ka koe tagata na‘a nau lau koe
balofita, ‘o nau tui ki he'ene g. lea kehekeke, bea
koeha ‘oku ‘ikai ai te nau tui ki he'ene fakamo'oni
koe Misaia ia ? Kae‘uma‘a ‘ene g. gaiie fakaofo ‘o
hage koia kuo ne toki fai ki he tagata mahaki; hono
‘ikai koe fu‘u fakamo'oni ia ? Bea ka ne nau tokaga
lelei ki he'ene g. gaiie, mo ‘ene aga, te nau ‘ilo ‘iate
ia ‘ae imiji ‘oe Tamai. Bea ne ogo ‘oku ‘ikai ke utua
hono aga mei he g. me‘a koia, koe'uhi, ‘abe, ko ‘enau
ta'etokaga, ka ko loto ke nau ‘ilo kiate ia mei he
Folofola; he koe me‘a ia ‘oku nau mamafa ki ai, bea ‘oku
nau hakule ma'ube ke ‘ilo ki hono ‘uhiga : bea koe Tohi
koia ‘oku tuhu mai kiate ia hono g. boji kotoabe. Bea
koeha hono ‘uhiga o‘enau ta'etui behe ? ‘Oku nau lau
ko ‘enau fakahikihiki'i ‘ae ‘Otua, ka koe launoa, ka
ko ‘enau fie fakahikihiki‘i kinautolu. Bea ko ‘enau
fuataki ‘a Mosese koa! ko Mosese be ia te ne
talatalaki'i ‘ukinautolu ; he ‘oku mahino, ‘oku ‘ikaite


nau tui ki he‘ene tohi a‘ana, koe ‘ikai te nau tui kia
Jisu.
‘E, keu ‘i ai mai mu‘a ke mamata ki honau fofoga
‘i he'enau fanogo ki he folofola koeni ‘a Jisu !
‘Oku te behe na‘a nau taki taha ‘ilo ‘oku ‘i ai ha kovi
‘oku ne fai; ka ko Yaihi e ha'anau mahalo ‘e
talata’aaki'i kinautolu ‘i ha'anau ta'etui kia Mosese.
‘lkai ko Mosese mo ‘ene g. tohi koe Alifa mo Omeka
o'enau mo‘ui 1 koe mata'ikoloa ‘oe fonau moe kakai,
‘oe bule'aga moe lotu ? ‘lkai kuo mole ‘ae mo‘ui ‘a
honau toko lahi ‘i he mamahi'i ‘oe g. tu‘utu‘uni ‘a
Mosese ? bea na‘a mo kinautolu ‘e ‘ikai faigata‘a
‘enau fai behe. Bea koe tala mai ‘e he Jisu ni mei
Kasaleti, tokua, ‘oku ‘ikai te nau tui kihe g. tohi koia
‘a Mosese, ‘akinautolu ‘ae hou'eiki ‘oe kakai Jiu !
Fakabo ! Kohai, tii, ‘eni ! Ne‘ine‘i tafu'ua honau
loto, he koe ta ka ko ha ta ! —‘aea ‘oku fakamatala ki
ai ‘e he Tohi Hebelu, “ He koe folofola ‘ae ‘Otua koe
koto mo‘ui, moe koto malohi, bea majilaage ‘i he
heleta fakatoumata fuabe ; ‘o ne ‘aji atu ‘o maioio'i
‘ae loto moe laumalie, ‘io, hono gain hokoga moe uho ;
bea ‘oku ne vavaga'i ‘ae g. holi moe fakakaukau ‘oe
loto.”
Ko hono kovi ‘oku ‘ikai ko ha mai ‘ae me‘a na‘e
lioko; be na‘a nau ‘ita bea moulu atu ‘a Jisu, be na‘a
nau ma kinautolu ‘o hola : ka ‘oku mahino na‘e ‘ikai
ke nofo ‘a Jisu ki he Basova, ka ne ‘alu ki he tuku-
‘uta.
Lolotoga ia, na‘e hoko ha me‘a na‘e vavana ai ‘an
loto ‘oe kakai kotoa. Kuo tau fakamatala ki he li ‘o
Jione Babitaiso ki he bilisone, beakuofuoloa moe holi
‘a Helotiasi ke tamateh : ka ne ogo kuo ka'aga ‘ae
lelei ‘a Helota, ka na‘a ne teteki ke fai ha kovi behe.


Ka ka ‘ikai tuku ‘e Heletiasi ‘ene foiga, bea nac faifai
bea lava : bea na‘e fakabogi ‘a ji‘i Jione ‘i he bilisone,
bea ului hono laumalie ki he “ hosite gigila ‘oe kau
Maata.” Na‘e haga leva ‘ae loto ‘oe Kau Ako kia Jisu.
Koe taha ‘iatc kinautolu ‘i mu‘a, bea kuo ne hoko koe
Balofita lahi; ‘io, na‘e fa‘a na‘ina‘i ‘e he tagata'eiki
kuo bekia ke nau hiki ki hono lahi, kae ‘ikai te nau
fie li'aki ia lolotoga ‘ene mo'ui. Ka koeni kuo bekia,
bea ‘oku ‘ata lionau hala. Koia na‘a nau ‘alu ki ai,
‘o tala ‘ae me‘a kuo hoko, mo fakaogoki ha tu‘utu‘uni
‘o fai: bea ‘oku hage na‘a nau fakataha moe Kau Ako
‘a Jisu, ke ‘oku ‘ikai tetau kei fanogo kiate kinautolu.
Na‘e ‘ilo ‘e Jisu ‘e ogo lahi ‘ae me‘a ni ki he Kau
Abosetolo, bea te nau foki mai kiate ia ke ma‘u ha
tu‘utu‘uni; koia na‘a ne ‘alu leva ki Kabaneume ki
honau fakataha'aga, bea tuaiekemo ‘enau katoa mai.
Ko hono kovi, na‘e ‘ikai ji‘i te ne ‘atii ke ma‘u ‘enau
fakamatala, mo fakatonutonu ‘enau gaue; he kuo
mahu‘iga‘ia ‘ae kakai ‘i he‘ene foki mai, ‘o nau uofo
kiate ia mei he bogibogi ki he bo‘uli. Na‘e ‘ikai koe
kau Kabaneume be, ka koe kakai mei he g. feitu‘u
kehekehe ; ‘aia ‘oku nau ‘i ai ko ‘enau fonoga hake ki
he Basova. Koia na‘e fekau ‘e Jisu ke heka vaka ‘ae
Kau Abosetolo, bea ke nau o moia ki ha botu na‘e
mama‘o moe g. hala fakabule'aga, koe‘uhi ke ‘oua te
nau febaki moe kakai ‘oku ‘alu ki Selusaloma. Ka
koe Tahi ‘o Kaleli koe tahi ji‘i, bea na‘e ha noabe ‘ae
vaka ki he g. fonoga ‘oku nofo ‘i Kolesini mo Bete-
saita moe g. feitu'u koia ; bea o‘i ai leva honau toko
lahi ke ‘alu ki he botu ‘oku taumu'a ki ai hono vaka,
ke nau toe fanogo ki he Labai lahi, ‘aia kuo nau fa‘a
malie'ia ‘i he‘ene lea. Na‘e ai ha halakavakava ‘i he
taimi koia, ‘ae na‘e fakahoko ai ‘ae ogo feitu‘u ‘o


Betesaita ; he koe kolo ia na‘e tu‘u ‘i kauvai mo
kauvai. Bea laka ai ‘ae kakai ‘o nau vave, kae tuai
‘ae folau ‘a Jisu he ‘oku ‘au mai ‘ae hotu koia; koia
‘i he a‘u ‘a Jisu ki ‘uta, ta, ‘oku tu‘u ai ha fu‘u kakai
toko lahi, Na‘e ha leva ‘e ‘ikai lava ‘enau talanoa,
bea ne taki hake kinautolu ki he botu na‘e mohukuha,
‘o ne nofo hifo ‘i ha fo‘i ma‘oluga ‘o malaga kiate
kinautolu : ha malaga, nai, hage koia na‘a ne fai mei
he Mo‘uga.
Bea kabau koia bea ne‘ine‘i fie nofo ‘ae kakai, ‘o
galo ‘enau mama‘o mei honau g. abitaga, moe tu‘unuku
mai ‘ae bo‘uli. Ka na‘e hoha‘a ‘ae Kan Abosetolo ‘i
he‘enau mamata ki he ‘alu hifo ‘ae la‘a moe ‘ikai ha
taha ‘e gaiie, ‘o nau o‘i ‘a Jisu ke ne tukuage ‘ae
kakai ke nau kumui me‘akai, na‘a ai ha tu‘utamaki.
Kae malimali mai ‘a Jisu, ‘o ne behe, “ Koe‘uma‘a
‘enau ‘alu 1 ‘age ‘ekimoutolu ha'anau me'akai.” Bea
nau ‘oiaue fakabo ‘i he‘enau ma‘u ‘ae fekau koia,
he'enau vakai ki he mafola ‘ae fu‘u kakai; kae tala
‘e he ‘Eiki ke ‘omi ‘ae me‘a ‘oku nau ma‘u, ka nau
‘alu atu ‘o fakamilu ‘ae nofo ‘ae kakai. Bea fai.
‘Oku hage na‘e tagutu ‘a Jisu ‘i ha fo‘i ma'oluga,
bea mofele atu mei ai ‘ae g. ‘otu kakai ki he botu
kotoabe. Na‘e 50, nai, ‘ae g. ‘otu, ‘o taki toko
100 ; bea ko Bita, ‘i he‘ene fakamatala ki ai ki mui,
na‘a ne lau na‘e ha kiate ia ‘o hage ko ha goue
onioni ‘ae tu‘u ‘ae g. ‘otu. Na‘e nofo bubububu ‘ae
kau feline moe tamaiki mei he mama‘o. Bea
toki tu‘u ‘a Jisu ‘o fai ‘ene fakafeta'i, moe tabuakki
‘ae ki‘i me'akai na‘e tuku ‘i hono ‘ao. Hono ‘uke,
koe fo‘i ma baale ‘e 5, moe mata‘i ika ‘e ua ! Ka
na‘e fe‘uga be, bea, ‘i he‘ene kamata tufa, na‘e tubu
‘i hono nima hage ha buna hake ha vai mei he kele-


kele. Ko ‘ene bakiua ‘ac ma koeni kuo toe katoa leva
‘ae koga na‘e toe ; ko ‘ene motuhi ha koga ika, bea
tubu mai hono koga na‘e mole, ‘o behe be. Bea ke
faka'uta mu‘a ki he o‘o ‘ae kakai ‘i he gaobe mai ‘ae
Kau Abosetolo kuo fonu mahake ‘enau g. fu‘u kato
fakahuga ‘i he g. koga ma, he tala'ehai na‘e ha kiate
kinautolu be koe fou mei fe. ‘Oku te behe, na‘a nau
‘amanaki ‘e ‘oji vave, bea hei'ilo be te nau totofu, ka,
‘i he ha‘u mo ha‘u ‘ae Kau Abosetolo moe g. koto ma,
na‘a nau tuku ‘enau fakama‘uma‘u, ‘o nau nofo ke
fai ha fu‘u kai. ‘Oku mo'oni ne galo ‘enau fiekai ‘i
he'enau mo‘umali‘ia ‘i he malaga ‘a Jisu, ka, ‘i he logo
‘ae le‘o malie koia, na‘e toe ake ‘a Katula ‘o tagi ki
hono fatogia o‘ona. Bea hono ‘ikai lelei ‘ae ma koia
kiate kinautolu ! bea, ‘i he ‘iloage na‘e neke mai ‘e
Bita (be kohai?) ha fu‘u koto ika ‘o laku, bea kikila
honau mata he'enau to‘o ‘ae g. ma‘aga-gako koia ‘o
fa'ololo, he ko ji‘i kai hamu kinautolu, bea tiltataha
‘enau ‘ilo ki he ika. Bea koe behe koa na‘e ‘ikai ke
ogo kia Jisu ‘enau fiefia; he koia na‘a ne gaohi ‘ae
me‘akai ke ifo, ‘ikai ‘e hoho'ia ai hono loto ‘i he fua
o‘ene tu‘utu‘uni ? Tala atu, koe fu‘u faihala ‘ae faka-
‘ehi‘ehi ‘aekau Monike mei he g. me‘a ‘oku melie, ‘o
lau ‘oku hoifua ai ‘ae ‘Otua. ‘0 hoifua ‘i fe ‘i he'etau
fakata‘ehoa ‘ae g. me‘a na‘a ne gaohi ke hoa ! Bea
koia, ‘i he toe tagi ‘ae kakai ke ‘age ha‘anau ‘ika, bea
ta‘ofi ‘e he Kau Abosetolo ke ma‘ua, ka ka toe fakafonu
‘enau kato ‘e Jisu, ‘o fekau ke nau ‘ai ke matu'aki
tobono honau ‘umisi. JSTe‘ine‘i fakatumutumu ‘ae
kakai ‘o nau tukubau koe Misaia ia ! Ka koe me‘a na‘e
ogo lahi ki he Kau Abosetolo ‘enau tanaki ‘ae g. koga
me‘a na‘e toe —na‘e fu‘u fonu ‘enau kato kotoa, ‘o lahi
noabe ‘ae me‘a na‘e toe ‘i he me‘a na‘e kamata'aki.


Bea vakai leva ‘e Jisu ‘oku gaue ‘ae kakai ke fai
ha me‘a, he na‘a nau behe koe Misaia ia, bea ‘oku
totonu ke ne tu‘i, ‘o ‘oua te nau kei fakaogo ki he fa‘a
ahiga kovi ‘oku bule ni. ISTa'e ‘ilo ‘e Jisu ‘oku totonu
‘enau lau, ka koe bule'aga ‘oku ne fokotu‘u na‘e ‘ikai
ke fakamama, bea, kabau te nau fai honau loto, ‘e
ta‘ofi lahi ki he'ene gaue. Ko hono faigata'a he na‘e
kau ai moe Kau Abosetolo ; he koe me‘a koia na‘e
kavea ki ai honau loto ke ma‘u hanati tu‘uga ma‘oluga
‘i he bule‘aga ‘ae Misaia. Koia na‘a ne fekau ke
hekavaka kinautolu, bea, ‘i he'enau meimei talagata'a,
na‘a ne fai fakamalohi ki ai, bea nau toki ‘alu. Bea
foki hake ‘a Jisu ki he kakai, ‘o o‘i ke nau fonoga : ka
na‘e taiki mo ‘enau ‘alu ‘anautolu, bea koe ni‘ihi na‘e
foki mai ‘o mohe ‘i matatahi, ke lamalama ha folau ‘a
Jisu ka nau o moia.
Ka kuo ‘alu ‘a Jisu ki he fuga fonua ke teuteu'aki
‘ae lotu lilo ki he gaue ‘oe ‘abogibogi. He kuo ha
kiato ia ‘oku fakamama fau 'ae nofo ‘ae kakai kiate
ia, bea ko hono lelei mu‘a ko sivi kei tuai ‘ae g. ‘ahi-
‘ahi ‘e to. Kuo fuoloa ‘ene lotu, kuo lahi ‘ae g. houa
kuo mole ‘i he'ena feohi mo ‘ene Tamai, kae ‘iloage
na‘a ne manatu ki he'ene Kau Ako, hage ‘oku ne ogo‘i
‘oku nau tu'utamaki. Bea, ‘i he'ene vakai atu, ta, ‘oku
te'eki ji‘i ke nau ‘au ki ‘uta, bea, ne ogo ‘oku nau ogojia
fai, ka ‘oku nau baea be. Kuo no mea‘i ‘e tokai ‘ae
matagi, bea koia na‘a ne tala ke nau taumu'a ki Bete-
saita, hei'ilo te nau lalave ki Kabaneume.
Koe misiteli ‘ae me‘a na‘e hoko. ‘Oku ‘ikai te
tau faigata‘a‘ia ‘i he'ene ha'ele ‘i he fukahi tahi,
he na‘e ‘age'age ia ‘i he mana kuo ne toki fai :
ka koe me‘a ‘oku fo‘ou, ko ‘ene fai ha mana ma-
‘ana. Koia kuo mahalo ‘ae ni‘ihi ‘oku kei mo‘ua


lahi hono loto ‘i he me‘a ‘oku na lotua ki he'ene
Tamai, bea ‘oku ‘ikai to ne tokaga‘i ‘ae me‘a ‘oku
fai ; bea ko ‘ene ha'elea ‘ae fukahi moana ta‘e te
ne galo, koe fataki nima ia ‘e he kau agelo tauhi,
‘o hage koe balofisai, be koe fai ‘e hono ‘otua ta‘e
kau ai hono tagata. Kabau koia, bea ‘uhiga ai ‘ene
mei laka atu ‘iate kinautolu, ‘o ne toki ‘a hake ‘i
he'enau keke na‘e fai.
Hei‘ilo ki ai, ka ‘oku ha na‘e manavahe ‘aubito ‘ae
Kau Abosetolo ‘i he'enau vakai ki he'ene lakaage, ‘o
nau mahalo koe fa'ahikehe. ‘Anenai na‘a nau
fakaamu ke ne ha‘u, ka, ‘i he ‘iloage kuo ne ha, na‘a
nau fai ke hola, na‘a ‘iloage te ne ma‘u ‘ae vaka.
Ko kitautolu aibe ia. Kae mole leva ‘enau manavahe
‘i he ogo mai ‘ae lea malie koia, “ Fiemalie be ; ‘oua
‘e manavahe ; koau be.” Bea fu‘u buho hake ‘ae tui
‘a Bita ‘o ne behe ke fai moia, foki, ‘o hage ko ‘ene
‘Eiki. ‘Oku ‘i ai ‘ae ni'ihi ‘oku nau aga‘i ‘ae fai koia
‘a Bita, ‘o nau fakama‘ito‘a ‘i he'ene meimei tu-
‘utamaki: ka ‘oku te behe, na‘e hage ha hu‘a vai
momoko ki he finagalo ‘o Jisu a'ene falala mai; he
ne ogo na‘e ‘ikai fe'uga ‘ene tui moe fu‘u me‘a kuo ne
‘ahi‘ahi fai, ka na‘e lelei lahi ‘ene fakakoga a‘ana ‘i
he hala ‘aubito kinautolu,
Kuo fu‘u mahino eni ko honau ‘Eiki, bea nau fiefia
‘i he'ene heka mai, bea kuo te'eki ke mau lelei ‘enau
nofo, ‘iloage kuo tau ‘ae vaka ki ‘uta, bea nau toe fu‘u
ofo ;he koe ‘anenai na‘a nau ‘i he vaha‘amalie ‘oe tahi,
bea, ‘i he‘enau ‘ohovale, na‘a nau tuku ‘ae a'alo, bea
meife ‘enau fu‘u gaholo koia hage halaafi 1 Ka tala-
‘eha ‘e ha kiate kinautolu ‘ae fakabiu na‘e fai ‘e he
kau agelo.
Na‘a tau fakaha ‘anenai na‘e ai ha ni‘ihi na‘e ‘ikai


ke 6 ‘i he tutuku ‘ae kakai, ka nan uofo ‘i he matiitahi
‘o talitali ‘ae hau ‘a Jisu, hei'ilo te ne ‘omi ha'anau
belokifasi. Ka, ‘i he hobo ‘ae la‘a moe ‘ikai ha‘u ia,
na‘a nau mahalo kuo ne hala ‘uta, ‘o nan heka kinau-
tolo ki he faga ki‘i vaka na‘e tau ai ‘o nau folau ki
Kabaneume, hoi‘ilo te nau ma‘u ia ‘i ai. Ka na‘e fai,
he nae gatetetu‘u ‘ae kolo ‘i he fata ‘oe mahaki kiate
ia ; bea, ta, ‘oku nofo ‘a Jisu ‘i he sinakoke lahi, ‘o
kabui ia ‘e he hou'eiki Jiu. Bea nau ‘alu atu leva
kiate ia, ‘o fehu‘i be na‘a ne lava fakaku mai.
Kane koe tagata faka‘age‘age age ‘a Jisu, behe kuo
ne veveho kiate kinautolu, koe‘uhi ke ogo ki he hou-
‘oiki ‘ae toko lahi ‘oe kakai ‘oku kau kiate ia, ka na‘e
‘ikai ke manako ‘a Jisu ki he fokotu‘utu‘u ‘a fefie hu,’
‘o ne tala ko ‘enau kumi mai, ‘oku ‘ikai ko ‘enau ‘ofa
kiate ia, ka ko ‘enau jio me'akai. Bea ne gaohia
kinautolu ‘i he'enau fakabikobiko ‘o faka‘atukai; ‘o
ne tala ke nau ‘alu ‘o gaue, ‘o ‘ikai ki he me'akai be
‘a mamani ka ki he me‘a fakalaumalie foki.
.Na‘a nau ma ‘i honau tala behe‘i, bea na‘e ha leva
‘oku ‘ikai momo‘i liliu honau loto; he, ‘i he tala ‘o
Jisu ke nau tui bikitai kiate ia, na‘a nau ‘eke bo
koeha ‘ana kuo fai ke nau tui ai kiate ia. Fakabo !
kuo te‘eki ‘oji ‘ae ‘aho ‘e taha talu ‘enau mei fakanofo
ia ke tu‘i, ko ‘enau to‘oa ‘i he‘ene gaue fakaofo ; bea
koeni ‘oku nau eke ki ha faka'iloga ka nau tui ai
kiate ia, bea nau tuku ki mu‘a noabe ‘a Mosese mo
‘one gaue bate ia !
Koe me‘a fakaofo ‘ae fakama‘uma‘u ‘a Jisu, mo ‘ene
lava ke tali fakaalaala ki he fa'ahiga koia; ka ne ko
kitaua kuo ta fu‘u natua : ka ka lea lelei be ‘e Jisu, ‘o
ne fakamahino, na‘e ‘ikai ko Mosese na‘e ‘ohifo ‘ae
mana, ka ko ‘ene Tamai, bea na‘e ikai ke loko jia'a


‘ae ma koia, he na‘a nau kai be kae mate ; ka, ‘i
onoboni, kuo ne ‘ohifo ‘ae ma ‘oe mo'ui, ‘aia, ka kai ai
ha taha, ‘oku ne mo'ui be ‘o ‘ikai mate. Bea laga'i
ai leva ‘enau holi ki he ma koia, ‘o nau kole ke no
‘omi kiate kinautolu. Bea toki folofola ‘e Jisu, “ Ko-
au be koe ma ‘oe mo‘ui,” bea ne ‘ai mai ha tuiga
tala‘ofa mahu‘iga lahi. “ Koia ‘oku fotu mai kiate
an ‘e ‘ikai ‘aubito teu kabuji ” &c. Koe botu fe ‘o
mamani kuo ‘ikai mo‘ui ai ha toko lahi he'enau
taubiki ‘i he lea koia 1
Ka na‘e ‘ikai koe tala'ofa be na‘a ne a‘au ‘i he
taimi koia, ka na‘a ne fakaha, foki, ‘ae misiteli koia
o‘ene lotu, koe kai hono kakano mo inu hono ta‘ata‘a.
Ne'ine'i teki ‘ae kakai ‘i he lau koia, he na‘a mo
kitautolu ‘oku tau ogo'i kehe : ka na'emahino koe lau
fakamisiteli, bea nau ‘ilo leva koe nofo kiate ia ‘e
‘ikai hage ko ‘enau ‘amanaki; he tala'ehai ‘oku ‘i ai
ha lau ki ha me‘akai fakamama, be ha koloa, bo
tu‘uga. Koia ‘i he‘ene fai atu, ‘o fakababau ‘oku
toeji'i bea ne hiki mei mamani, na‘e tafuli honau loto
‘o nau gaue ke ‘alu ; bea bihia mo ‘ene Kau Ako kuo
fuoloa, bea na‘e hage ka tuku toko taha be ‘a Jisu.
Koia na‘e behe ‘e Jisu ki he Kau Abosetolo “ Ta, te
mou ‘alu mo kimoutolul” Ka na‘e mahino leva mei
he tali ‘a Bita, ko ‘enau gaue, ‘aia be ‘oku tau fai
kotoabe ‘oka tau ka mo‘ua ‘i ha fu‘u malele behe.
Hage ha vaka ‘oku fetakai mo Manavaga, ne ogo ‘ene
fakatautu'u kae gaue holo be. Malie, Bita, ho‘o lea !
“ ‘ Eiki te mau ‘alu kia hai 1 ‘oku ‘iate koe ‘ae g. lea
‘oe Mo‘ui Ta'egata.” Koe tali ma‘a mamani na'efai,
bea mahino ai ‘oku ‘ikai ke ka‘aga ‘aubito ‘etau lelei,
ka ‘oku tau kei lava ke ‘ilo ki he lelei, bea ke ‘ofa
ki ai.


Koe ‘aho kovi ‘eni ‘i he mo‘ui ‘a Jisu ; he koe
tagata, bea kohai ‘e fiemalie ‘i hono li'aki ia ‘e ha fu‘u
toko lahi behe ? bea ne ogo na'a ne fiemalie r i he lea
‘a Bita, ka na'a moia ‘e ‘ikai lelu ai ‘ene mamahi
ko ‘ene vakai ki he nofo mai ‘a Jiutasi: bea koe Kau
Abosetolo na‘e ofi. kiate ia na‘a uau ‘oho ‘i he buna
mei hono fofoga ‘ae lea, “ Na'a mo kimoutolu ko homou
toko taha koe tevolo.”
Na‘a tau fakaha na‘e foki ‘a Jisu ki Kaleli,
koe‘uhi ke ‘oua na'a ai ha febaki moe hou‘eiki, ‘o
ta‘ofi ai ‘ene gaue : bea ‘oku mo‘oni, lolotoga ‘ae
Basova na'a ne ‘ata'ata, ka, ‘i he ‘oji leva ‘ae Katoaga
koia, na'a nau buleaki'i ke fai ha me‘a kiate ia, bea
nau tuku atu ha toko lahi ke ‘alu ki Kaleli hono
vakai‘i. ‘Oku ha ‘ae mamafa ‘oe me‘a kiate kinau-
tolu, he na‘e tuku ai ‘e he ogo fa‘ahi lahi ‘enau
fe‘ite‘itani, bea na‘e kautaha ‘ae Falesi moe Satusi ke
lamaji ‘a Jisu. Na'a nau fai ma'ube, nai, kae lahi be
‘i he ‘aho Sabate, he na‘e mahino koe me‘a ia ‘oku
galigali hia ai ‘ae Labai ni, ko ‘ene maumau'i ‘ae g.
tu‘utu‘uni ‘oe ‘Aho Tabu.
Na‘e ‘ikai tuai. Koe taimi majiva ia kia Jisu moe
Kau Ako, bea koia, ‘i he tuku ‘oe malaga ‘i he falelotu,
na‘a nau ‘alu ki he goue‘aga ‘i tua‘a kolo, ‘o kamata
toli ‘ae uite. Koe me‘a ia na‘e gofua, hage koe toli-
niu ‘i Toga; ka na‘e lau ‘e he Falesi na‘e tuliimuikoe
utu ‘oe ta‘u ‘oku fai, mo hono ‘au‘au. Koia na‘a nau
lea ai kia Jisu, hei‘ilo te ne boubou kinautolu ka nau
talatalaaki‘i; he na‘e ‘ikai koe Kau Ako na‘a nau ‘ita
ai, ka ko Jisu be. Bea haga leva ia ‘o malu‘i ae Kau
Abosetolo, ‘o hage ko ‘enau ‘amanaki, ka koe me‘a
na‘e ‘ikai te nau ‘amanaki ki ai, na‘a ne fakaha ‘oku
nau fai tatau be mo honau bele ko Tevita, ‘aia na'a


ne maumau ‘ae tabu koe'uhi koe tu'utamaki.
Kae‘uma‘il na'ane toe fakaji‘iji‘i kiate kinautolu, ‘oku
nema'olnga ia ‘i he Lao, ‘io, ‘i he Lao ‘oe Sabate, foki.
Koeni kno ha‘aki leva kinautolu, ka na‘e ‘ikai te
nau boto ai, ka nau muimui atu aibe ‘o tokamalumu
kiate ia ‘i he botu kotoabe. ‘Oku lau, tokua, na‘a nau
o‘i ha tagata nimamate ke ‘alu ki he falelotu ‘i he
Sabate ‘e taha, hei‘ilo ‘e jio ki ai ‘e Jisu ‘o faito‘o.
Ka‘a ne mea‘i ‘enau tu‘utu‘uni, kae ‘ikai te ne inomo'i
tuka, ka ne fekau ki he tagata ke tu‘u mai ki loto.
Bea, ‘i he fakakaka mai ‘e ha taha, ‘obelie, “Okugofua,
‘abe, ke faito'o ‘i he Sabate? ” na‘e kikila hono fofoga
‘o ne behe, “ Kane to ha'amou sibi ki ha luo ‘i he ‘aho
Sabate, te mou fuji hake be ‘ikai ? Bea ne laiki ‘enau
g. fakakaukau kotoabe he'ene behe ki he tagata,
“ Mafao mai ho nima na ! ” Bea, ‘i he'ene fai, ‘o
mo'ui, na‘e fakabo‘uli honau loto ‘i he ‘ita, he'enau
vakai ‘oku ‘ikai mafohi ha'anau me‘a kiate ia; he
na‘a moe Falesi ‘e ‘ikai te ne fa‘a behe koe mafao hoto
nima koe maumau Sabate ia. Koia na‘a nau fa'a
fakataha, ‘o buleakhi hano tamate'i; bea ‘ajili, ko
‘enau vakai ki he fakautuutu hono tokaga‘i. He koe
taimi koia na‘e nofo kiate ia ‘ae fonua katoa; bea
na‘a nau ‘utaki kaunifo ‘i he'enau mamata ki he ha‘u
‘ae kakai mei he g. feitu‘u ‘o Kaleli, mo Tu‘a Jioatani,
mo Jiutea, ‘io mo Finisia, mo Aitumia mama‘o ‘oku
nau nofo takai ki he ki‘i komaki ‘i Kabaneume, ‘o
fanogo ki he malaga ‘a Jisu mei he vaka. Na‘e hage
tofu be koe me‘a ‘i Ijibite ‘i mu‘a, koe fakautuutu
‘enau fakamamahi'i ia kae ‘ajili ai ‘ene tubu.
Kane koe tagata ‘a Jisu, kuo ne fai atu ‘ene
fakakikihi mo kinautolu he na‘a ne malohi, ka ko
hono nafa koe kataki, bea na‘a ne hiki mei ai ‘o hola


ki ha botu kehe. Ka na‘e ‘ikai te ne lava ke ta'ofi
‘enau febaki, he na‘e tuliimui hono g. fill kiato ia, bea
na‘e vave ‘enau toe ta mai. Koe me‘a na‘e tu'uga ki
ai ‘enau fai, na‘e hage koe me‘a kuo tau fakamatala
ki ai—koe maumau'i oe g, migimigi'i tu‘utu‘uni kuo
fokotu‘u ‘e he'enau kau Labai. Ka‘e ai ‘ae g. me‘a na‘e
fekau ‘e Mosese ke nau faka‘ehi‘ehi mei ai, ‘o tokaga
ke ‘oua te nau ala ki ai, be lave ki ai hanau kofu—
hage koe ‘aga‘aga moe g. ‘uli kehekehe. Ka kuo
fakalahi noabe ‘e he matu‘a. Ka‘a nau lau ‘ae
Senitaile koe tagata kuo mate, bea koia na‘a nau
fekau ke faka‘ehi‘ehi mei ai ‘o hage ha ‘aga'aga ; ‘o
behe. Bea hoko ia koe fu‘u kavega ki he kakai Jiu,
‘o nau manavahe aibe, na‘a kuo nau lave ki ha me‘a
behe ; bea koe me‘ana‘anau fai ma'ube koefanofano,
moe babitaiso ‘oe naunau oe fale ‘aki ‘ae vai fakama'a,
na‘a kuo lave ki ai ha taha ‘oe g. me‘a na‘e tabu.
Bea tala‘ehai ‘e tokaga ‘e Jisu ki ha me‘a behe, kae
kehe te ne fie tamate'i; bea fa‘ifa‘itaki kiate ia ‘e
he‘ene Kau Ako, ‘o nau tuku, foki, ‘o nofo ke kai te'eki
ke babitaiso. Bea buke leva ki ai ‘ae fili, ‘o nau ‘eke
kiate ia, be koeha ‘oku maumau'i behe ai ‘e he'ene
kakai ‘ae lao ‘oe Jiaji. Ka‘e ‘ikai ke momo'i
fakamatala ‘e Jisu, ka ne ‘ai be honau fu‘u hoka.
Kuo nau ‘eke kiate ia be koeha kuo ne maumau'i ai
‘ae g. tu‘utu‘uni ji‘i, ka ka ‘eke ‘eia ‘enau maumau'i
‘ae g. tu‘utu‘uni lahi; kuo nau mamahi‘i ‘ae me‘ana‘e
fokotu‘u ‘e he matu‘a, kae fai ‘eia ki he me‘a kuo
fokotu'u ‘e he ‘Otua. Bea, ‘i he'enau logo be, na‘a ne
ui mai ‘ae kakai, ‘o ne hiki ‘ae fu‘u kavega kuo nau
gaobe ai fuoloa, ‘o ne tarnate‘i‘aki ha fo‘i folofola ‘ae
g. lao fakafiu kuo kona ai ‘enau mo‘ui, he‘ene behe
‘oku tatau aibe ‘i he lotu ‘ae kai moe inu moe ala


me‘a behe ; koo loto be ia ‘ae me‘a ke te tauhi ke ma‘a,
be, ka ‘uli ia ‘i ha g. fakakaukau kovi, moe aga ta‘e-
tau, ‘oku ‘ikai ‘aoga ha babitaiso ka ‘oku te mousa'a
aibe.
‘Oku ‘ikai ke loko ogo kiate kitautolu ‘ao mamafa
o‘ene lea koia, ka na‘e hage kuo liliu ‘a mamani kiate
kinautoln. Gofua koa ‘ae g. me'akai koia kuo tabu
talu mei mu‘a ! Tae‘aoga koa ‘ae g. to'oga lotu, ‘aia
kuo mo'ui'aki ‘e he'enau g. matu‘a mo ‘enau g. kui,
kae'uma'a ‘ae Falesi moe kau taula'eiki moe ha‘a
sagato ‘o honau jiaji ! ‘A, koe Tevolo be te ne lava
ke lea behe; bea nau kamata muhu‘i ‘i he'enau
muimui kiate ia “ Kuo bau kuo ‘avea.” “ Kuo ‘iate
ia ha tevolo lahi, ‘a Belesibube.”
Bea nau taukave ‘ae lau koia ne ogo ‘ao g. gaiie
lelei na‘a ne fai. Lolotoga na‘a ne nofo ‘i ha fale,
na‘e ‘omi kiate ia ha tagata na‘e kui mo noa, bea
ulujino ai ha tevolo ; bea na‘e fai leva ‘e Jisu hono
faiva, ‘o ne kabuji ‘ae fa‘ahikehe; bea, ‘i he'ene mahu'i
atu, na‘e ‘a ‘ae kui, ‘o ne lea foki. Bea ofo lahi ‘ae
kakai; he, ne ogo kuo nau maheni moe kabuji tevolo,
ka na‘e ‘ikai ke fa‘a behe-ke mo'ui ‘aubito ‘ae tagata;
ka na‘a ne fa‘a, foki, ki hono aga mu‘a : kabau koe kui,
na‘e kui aibe, ‘o behe. Bea hei'ilo be koeha ‘ae me‘a
na‘e mei hoko ‘i he‘enau ofo, ka ne ta‘oua ‘ae tamate'i
‘e he kau Palesi ‘ae kamata tui ‘ae kakai, he‘enau
behe, “ ‘Oku ne lava koe kau ai ‘a Belesibube.”
‘Oiau keu ma‘u mai ‘ae aga koia ‘a Jisu na‘e
ha ‘i he taimi koia, a‘ene fakama‘uma‘u ! ‘Oku
mahino ‘i he'etau lau ‘ae fakamatala na‘e gaue lahi
hono finagalo ‘i hono tala behe‘i. Kae fefe ?kaai ha
me‘a na‘e lahi ‘iate ia ka koefehi'a ki he agahala, bea
koe lau koa ‘oku na kau mo Setane !! ! Kane ogo


‘ene mamahi ka na‘e ‘ikai te no natua noabo, ka na‘a
ne ‘ai ke mahino ki honau ‘atamai ‘ao matamata vale
‘enau lea belie—koe fakama‘uma‘u ka ko ha fakama'u-
ma'uo he ‘oku hage ko ha fakamo‘oni ki ha tesi ‘ene
lau. Bea, ‘i he ha kiate ia ‘ae fu‘u vanu ta'ehanota-
kele kuo nau kamata to ki ai, na‘a ne liliu hono le‘o,
‘o ne na‘ina‘i mamafa na‘a nau fai ‘ae agahala ‘oku
‘ikai hano fakamolemole. ‘Oku te behe na‘e mo‘u
tafu'ua ‘ae fakataha kotoa ‘i he‘enau fanogo ki ai, he
hage na‘e ha kia Jisu ‘ae “ bo‘uli ‘o tua‘a,” bea koe
‘ata ‘oe fonua koia na‘e ‘i hono fofoga. Bea na‘e mei
hoko, nai, ha fu‘u fakatomala, ka ne ta'oua ‘ae iohoage
ha tinemotu'a, “ Monu'iaa ka koe manava na‘a ke
tokoto ai, moe ogo huhu na‘a ke huhu ai.” ! Ko ji‘i
mo'oni be ‘ae finemotu‘a, ka ko loto ke ne tatali ki ha
faigamalie, ‘o ‘oua ‘e veuveuki ‘ae malaga ‘a Jisu.
‘Oku matamata koe o‘i ‘e Setane, ‘aia na‘a ne gaue-
‘aki ‘ae loto mafana ‘ae finemotu‘a ke ta‘ofi ai ‘ae
lelei na‘e mei hoko. Na‘e ‘ikai ke faka‘ikai‘i ‘e Jisu
‘ae monu‘ia ‘o Mele, ka na‘a ne tukukimu‘a ‘ae
monu'ia ‘oe kakai ‘oku nau tauhi ‘ae folofola ‘ae
‘Otua.
Koeni kuo motu kovi ‘ene lea ‘i he hakonoa ‘ae
finemotu'a, bea kamata tutuku ‘ae kakai: kae toe
‘ahi‘ahi mai ‘ae fili, ‘o nau velo mai ‘ae fehu‘i na‘a
nau fa‘a ‘ai, koe ‘eke ki ha faka'iloga ke nau ‘ilo
mo'oni be kohai. Bea, ‘i he vakai ‘e he kakai ‘oku ofa
‘e Jisu ke toe malaga, na‘a nau foki mai ke fanogo.
Na‘e majila ‘aubito ‘ene g. lea, ka, heihlo be na‘e ‘aji
be ‘ikai. Na‘a ne fakaha, koe toki faka'iloga ‘enau
fiema'u ha faka'iloga, bea mahino ai ‘enau hiki mej
he lelei. Kane nau tauhi ma‘u honau aga totonu,
kuo nau ‘ilo ia, ‘e hage koe ‘ilo ‘o he kakai Niuive


‘a Jiona, moe ogo‘i ‘e he Kuini ‘oe Hagatoga ‘ae boto
‘a Solomone. Boa ne toki lea ‘o hago ko ‘ene fa‘a
fai ki mui ni, ‘o fakaji‘iji‘i ki he'ene ma'oluga hake ‘i
he hou'eiki katoa o'enau lotu ; bea ne faka‘oji ‘ene lea
‘i he kau tevolo, ‘aia ne ta'ofi ‘e he finemotu'a ; ‘o ne
fakaha, ne ogo kuo kabuji, ka ‘oku ‘ikai ke motu ai
leva : ka, ‘o kabau ‘e ‘ikai tokaga ‘ae kakai, te ne foki
mai ‘o kovi hake noabe : ‘o ne fakahoko ‘ae me‘a koia
kiate kinautolu.
Na'e toe ta‘ofi ‘ene malaga koe fakaha ‘e he kakai
na‘e nofo ofi, kuo ha‘u ‘ene fa‘e mo hono g. tokoua ko
‘enau fiema'u ia. Ko hono ‘uhiga, nai, kuo nau
fanogo ki he lau ‘o hono ‘avea, bea ko ‘enau ha‘u ko
hono ‘ave ia, nai, ki ha botu keho, ‘o mama'o moe kakai
kuo nau laga‘i ‘ene g. lea koia ‘oku matamata kehe.
Kae ‘ikai ‘aubito tokaga ‘e Jisu kiate kinautolu ; ka
na‘a ne fai ‘o hage ko ‘ene eginaki ki he'ene Kau Ako,
‘o tukukimu'a ‘ae gaue ‘ae ‘Otua ‘i he kaiga-ofi taha ;
kae‘uma‘a na‘a ne fakaha, koe kaiga moia ‘oku ‘ikai
ke fou ‘i he kakano, ka ‘i he laumalie.
Na'e lea mai ‘eni ha motu‘a Falesi ke ne afe mai
ki hono fale ke ma‘u ha tokoni. Na'e ‘ikai ko ha
toko taha ‘iate kinautolu na‘e ha‘u ke lamaji ia, he
koe motu'a Kaleli ; ka na‘e ‘ikai, nai, koe ‘ofa a‘ene
fakaafe ia, ka ko ‘ene fie ta‘ofi ‘ene lea : bea na'e ha
leva ‘oku ne tatau mo kinautolu ‘i he aga, he na‘a ne
kamata figofigo ‘i he ‘ikai afuhi ‘e Jisu hono kofu moe
nofo‘a ‘i he te‘eki te ne kai. Kane ai ha lelei ‘i hono
fakaafe, na'e tamate'i ‘i he‘ene gaue koia; bea na'e
haga ‘e he ‘Eiki ‘o gaohi ia moe kau Falesi kotoabe
na‘a nau kau. Kuo loa ‘ene vavaga'i ‘ae kaka na'e
‘i honau loto, ‘aia na‘a nau fa‘a kofu‘aki ‘ae lau ‘ofa
ki he lotu, moe ma‘oni‘oni loi; bea na‘a ne a‘au eni ‘i


lie g. lea na‘e vela hago ha mama, ‘o ne fakatatau
kinautolu ki he g. fouualoto ‘oku ‘ikai ha, ‘aia ‘oku
‘ikai momo‘l ‘ilo‘i ‘e he kakai ‘ae fakaliolia ‘oku ‘i ai.
‘Oku hage na‘e mo'ulogoa ‘ae kau Falesi ko ‘enau
ofo ‘i he fai ha me‘a hehe kiate kinautolu. Koe me‘a
na‘a nau maheni ai koe nofo ‘ae kakai ‘o tali aga-
vaivai ‘enau g. lea ; bea koe natua behe‘i kinautolu
koe me‘a fo‘ou. Bea na‘e ‘ahi‘ahi ta‘ofi ‘e ha toko
taha ma‘utu‘uga, ‘o ne na‘ina‘i kia Jisu ‘oku lave ‘ene
g. lea ki he hou'eiki ina'oluga hage koia. ‘Oiau, ‘ae
mohe mohe ‘e kuli bea fafagu ! Ko loto ke ne tuku
aibe ‘a Jisu ke fai atu be, ‘o faka'amu ke ne buli; ka
ko'eni kuo ne toho mai kiate ia ‘ae houhau, bea na‘o
hage koe fatuliji moe mana ‘ene to ki hono tumu'aki.
Fe‘uga moia, kuo foki mai ‘ae loto ‘oe kau Falesi, bea
na‘e gei ‘enau'ita ki he ‘Eiki. Kuo nau fai, nai, ha
me‘a kiate ia ka ne tae'oua ‘enau fanogo ki he u‘ulu
‘ae kakai ‘itu‘a, ‘aia kuo nau tanaki mai koe fu‘u
hosite lahi ‘aubito. Kane ogo na‘e ‘ikai te nau lava
ha me‘a, ka na‘e hage koe kalou ‘a ha faga kuli
he'enau lele takatakai ki ha manu ‘oku nau manavahe
ki ai, na‘o belie ‘enau ha‘o ‘a Jisu, ‘o ‘ai ‘enau g. lau
mo fehu‘i kiate ia : kae ‘ikai momo'i mafohi ha'anau
me‘a kiate ia : ka ne bale‘i kotoa ‘enau g. ta, ‘o ne
tu‘u ‘o ‘alu atu ki he kakai.
Koe ‘uluakime'a na‘a nejio ki ai, ko ‘ene Kau Ako,
‘aia na‘e ‘ikai kau ‘i he fakaafe ka ‘oku nau tutu'u ‘o
tatali kiate ia. Koia na‘a ne fuofua fai ‘one lea kiate
kinautolu, ‘o ne na‘ina‘i ke ‘oua te nau fa‘ifa‘itaki ki
he kau Falesi, ‘o lelei ‘itu‘a be ; ne ogo te nau fufu
‘enau kovi, ka ‘e faifai bea e‘a. Na‘a ne tokoni, foki,
ke ‘oua te nau manavahe ki ho ‘ita ‘a hou‘eiki, ho
‘oku ‘i ai ‘ae gata'aga o‘ouau mafai; ‘o ne tuhu, nai, ki


he faga ki‘i miji ‘oku nofo ‘i he tu‘afale, ‘o ne fakaha
na‘a mo kinautolu ka ‘oku tokaga'i ‘e he ‘Otua,
huanoa ‘ae kakai; bea ne fakatauage mo kinautolu,
ne ogo ‘e fakahobo kinautolu, mo fakamana‘i, ka ke
‘oua ‘aubito te nau fakafijiga ia; he kabau koia, te
ne fakafijiga kinautolu ‘i he ‘ao ‘oe ‘Otua, moe ‘ao ‘oe
kau agelo.
Bea toe motuhi ‘ene lea, hage koia kuo fa‘a fai ‘i
he ‘aho koe, koe ogo‘i ‘e ha motu‘a ko ha ‘eiki lahi ‘a
Jisu, ‘o ne kole ke ne fakamilu a‘ena me‘a mo hono
tokua, ‘aia ‘oku na fakakikihi ‘i ha tofi‘a. Na‘e ‘ikai
ke ‘ita ‘ae ‘Eiki, ka na‘a ne gaohi ‘ae tagata ‘i he‘ene
manumanu; ‘o ne fai ‘ene talanoa ki he Tagata
Koloa'ia na‘e mahu ‘aubito, ‘o ne behe ke ne yete hono
g. feleoko ‘o laga ke lalahi, ‘o ne ‘amanaki kai me‘a
lelei ai ‘o fuoloa, ka koe bo koia na‘e tala ke ne tuku
mai hono laumalie. Hili ia, na‘a ne fai atu ‘ene
tokoni ki he‘ene Kau Ako, ‘o ne toe lau ‘ae koga ni‘ihi
‘oe Malaga ‘i he Mo‘uga, ‘aia ‘oku kau ki he tuku ‘ete
lotomo'ua ka te falala ki he ‘Eiki. Hono ‘ikai malie
‘ene lea ! koe Jisu koiX ‘eni na‘e lea ‘auenai ‘o hage
koe ‘Otua ‘i Sainai, ‘o fakalilifu ‘ae loto kotoa ? he
‘oku ne hage ‘eni ha fefine, ‘ene amoamohi ji'ene kau
ako—“ Na‘i faga sibi toko ji‘i, ‘oua ‘e manavahe.”
Ko hono ‘uhiga, nai, he kuo kamata ha kiate ia ‘ae
faka'oji o‘ene mo'ui: ko ‘ene g. lea he ‘aho ni koe
sibiga o'ene g. malaga faka'oji ‘i he‘ene ‘i mamani.
Kuo ha kiate ia ‘ae mavae ‘oku tu'unuku mai, ‘o ne
lea kiate kinautolu ‘i he agate nau fai‘aki ‘i he‘ene
mama‘o, ‘o ne fakatata ‘aki ‘ae Tagata‘eiki mo hono
‘Ahi. Na‘e ogo'i ‘e he Kau-ako hono ‘uhiga, bea na‘e
fehu‘i ‘e Bita be ‘oku gata hono famili ‘i he Kau Ako,
be ‘oku fai atu ki he kakai kotoa. Bea tali ‘e Jisu


‘oku ‘i he tagata taki taha be ‘oku ne kau ai be ‘ikai :
ka, ‘o kabau ‘oku nau ogo'i ‘oku nau ofi, ke nau fai
be ‘o tau moia
Bea, ‘i he'ene lau behe ki he'ene ‘alu, hage na‘e fu‘u
ha ai ‘ae ‘amui kiate ia. Kuo mahino eni ‘ae aga ‘a
hono g. fili. Kuo tatala ‘ae buloa ; bea, ‘i he‘enau
fakakikihi ‘anenai, na‘e fijikitu'a ‘ae fakabo ‘i honau
mata, bea ne vakai, koe ‘atuga aibe o‘ene gaue, ‘e
laga‘i ai ‘ae ‘ita ‘ae toko lahi, bea tubu ai ‘ae
maveuveu moe mavahevahe. ‘Oku mahalo na‘e mo‘u-
tu‘ua ai ia ‘o fuofuoloa, ‘o jio fakamama'u : bea, ‘i
he'ene toe lea, na‘e ha ai ‘ae fu‘u gaue ‘a hono flnagalo,
‘aia koe fakamo'oni lahi o‘ene tagata. Na‘e mahino
‘e iku ‘ene me‘a ki he lelei lahi; ka na‘e teki hono
loto ‘i he fu‘u kovi na‘e bau ke tomu‘a hoko. ‘Oku
mo'oni na‘e ai ‘ene mamahi a‘ana, bea na‘a ne ogo‘i
ia, ka koe me‘a na‘e ha lahi koe mamahi ‘ae kakai,
kae‘uma‘a ‘ene Kauako. Kuo ne ha‘u ke laku ha afi
ki mamani, bea ke velo ha heleta ; bea ne faka‘atu‘i
‘ae mamahi ‘ae kakai.
Ka na‘e ‘ikai ko hono gata ia ‘oe me‘a na‘a ne jio
ki ai. Kuo ‘oji ‘etau fakaha koe ‘aho ni koe ‘ata ‘o
hono g. ‘aho fakamui ‘i Selusalema; bea, hage koe
taimi koia, na‘e behe ‘ene jio he ‘aho ni ki he
tu'unuku mai ‘ae tau tea ‘oe kakai Jiu, moe faka'auha
‘o Selusalema. Koia na‘a ne ‘ai atu hono le‘o ke a‘u
ki he kakai katoa, ‘o ne na‘ina‘i kiate kinautolu ‘oku
banaki honau fakamau, 'io, ‘oku nau lolotoga o moe
talatalaaki ki he fakamiiu‘aga; bea, kabau ‘e ‘ikai te
nau lava ke fakalelei, ko honau mala kuo bau.
Na‘e toki ‘oji ‘ae ‘aho tau ni, ‘aia na‘e kite mo'oni
ai ‘ae gata‘aga. Kuo nau febaki ‘i Selusalema moe g.
botu kehekehe, kae te'eki, nai, ke hage koeni; bea na‘e


hage koe ho‘ata ‘ene mahino kia Jisu, koe fai atu ‘ene
gaue koe iku be ki hono fakabogi. ‘Oku tau ‘ilo na‘e
‘ikai te ne tuka ai, ka na'a ne mahu‘i ji‘i meiate
kinautolu, ‘o ne ‘alu ki ha botu ‘e ‘ikai te nau fie
muimui ai ki ai—koe fonua ‘o Taia mo Saitoni; hei'ilo
te ne ma‘u, ‘i he lotolotoga ‘oe hiteni, ha noga ji‘i, ‘aia
na‘e ‘ikai te ne lava ‘i he‘ene nofo mo hono kakai
o‘ona.
Ka ai ha fonua na‘c tau ke ‘alu ki ai ‘a Jisu ka ko
Finisia, he na‘e nofo hage ha fa‘e ki mamani katoa.
Ka kuo ka‘aga ‘eni hono lelei, bea kuo mole hono
tokaga'i. Na‘e ‘ikai te nau fo‘ou kiate ia, he kuo loa
‘ae bavakeage ki ai hono ogoogo, bea ‘i he g. kakai
na‘e fa‘a fanogo malaga ‘i Kabaneume, moe g. feitu'u
‘o Kaleli, na‘e ‘i ai ha ni‘ihi mei Finisia : koia “ na‘e
‘ikai te ne lava ke bulk”
Na‘e lahi, nai, ‘ae g. me‘a na‘o hoko ai, bea ne ogo
koe me‘a be taha ‘oku ‘ilo bau ki ai, ka koe malie ‘i
he malieage fau. Tokua, na‘e ulujino ha tevolo ‘i ha
ta'ahine, bea na‘e tagi toubili ‘ene fa‘e kia Jisu ke ne
fakamo‘ui. Ka na‘e ‘ikai tali ‘e Jisu; kae fofe !he
ko ‘ene ha‘u ki Finisia koe‘uhi ke ne ‘ata ji‘i mei he
me‘a koia; kae‘uma‘a koe Senitaile ‘ae fefine ni, bea
kuo te'eki ke hoko ‘ae kuoga ‘oe fa'ahiga koia. Kae
fakakukafi be ‘ae fefine, ‘o ne fakafiu ki ai, bea, ne
ogo ‘enau hu ki fale, kae fakata‘emalu‘ia be ‘eia, ‘o
hu ki he ‘Eiki. Bea gaue hono finagalo ‘i he‘ene
kitaki, ‘o ne ‘ai mai hono ‘ahi‘ahi‘i, “ ‘Oku ‘ikai gofua
ke to‘o ‘ae ma ‘ae fanau ‘o li ki he faga kuli.”
‘Oku ogo fefeka ‘ae lea koia kiate kitautolu, bea, ka
ne ko ha ni‘ihi, kuo ne ‘ita ‘o foki; ka na‘e mamafa
ki he fefine ‘ae me‘a kuo ne ha‘u ai, bea ne loto lelei
ke ne kuli be ha, kehe be ke mo‘ui ‘ene ta'ahine.


Kae‘uma‘a na‘e ogo ki hono loto, hage ‘oku ‘ofa mai
‘ae ‘Eiki, he koe fa'ahiga kuli na‘a ne lau ki ai koe
kuli bele; bea tuaiekemo ‘ene buke ki he me‘a koia,
‘o ne behe, “Ka na‘e fai, ‘Eiki.” ‘Koe ‘inaji be ‘oe
kuli ‘oku ou lagi ki ai. Hono ‘uke ! ‘ae fo‘i ta'ahine
ni be ke mo‘ui! ’ Bea ‘io leva ‘e he ‘Eiki, ‘o faka'ofo-
‘ofa‘ia hono finagalo ‘i he koto lelei na‘e ha ‘i ji‘i
hiteni ni. Ne‘ine‘i lea'aki ‘ae ‘ofa ‘ae feline ki he‘ene
tama, moe behe, ‘ koe ‘ofa koe fa‘e ‘a boto ! ’
Ka na‘e ‘ikai ha‘u ‘a Jisu ki Finisia ke gaue ; koia
na‘a ne tu‘u ‘o fai atu ki loto fonua, ‘o mole mama'o.
Na‘a ne fou ‘i Saitoni moe g. feitu'u ogoogo ‘o ono-
‘aho, ‘o ne toki afe mai ‘i he talalo ‘o Lebanoni, hage
‘oku ne fie fakatotolo atu ‘ae gata'aga ‘oe Fonua
Tabu. Na‘a ne ‘i he matavai, nai, ‘o Jioatani, bea
taka, nai, ‘a Besani moe g. fonua koia, ‘o fakaofiofi
mai ki he Tahi Kaleli mei hahake.
Na‘e laui afe ‘ae kakai na‘e 6 moia, bea ne toe fai,
foki, ‘ene me‘a fakaofo koe fafaga ‘oe kakai toko lahi
‘aki ha me‘akai ji‘i. ‘Oku hage na‘e tatau tofu be
bea moe fai ‘e taha, ka na‘e ai moe g. me‘a fakaofo
na‘e ha ai: he, ne ogo na‘e toko ji‘i ‘ae kakai eni, koe
toko 4000 be, bea lahilahiage ‘ae me'akai, koe ma ‘e
fitu, ka na‘e ji‘i ‘ae toe—koe kato ‘e fitu, bea iki foki.
Na‘o toki behe ‘e Jisu ke nau foki mai ki Kaleli;
‘o nau hekavaka. ‘Oku hage na‘a nau taumu'a ki
ha feitu‘u na‘e ui ko Makatani, be Makitala, ‘aia, ‘oku
mahalo, na‘e nofo ai ‘ae fine‘eiki ko Mele, koe toko
taha kuo mo‘ui ‘i he gaue ‘a Jisu. Hei‘ilo ki ai, ka
na‘e ‘ikai ke lava; he kuo fanogo ‘e he fili ki he foki
mai ‘a Jisu, bea ‘oku nau toka malumu kiate ia ‘i he
kolo ko Taibilio. Ko loto ke nau tuku ke ne malolo
ji‘i; he ko futu ‘ene ‘alu holo ‘o taka ‘ae g. fonua


mama'o he gaue ma‘ae kakai ! Ka na‘e ‘ikai ‘aubito;
ka, ‘i he ha mai ‘ac vaka, na‘a nau ‘alu atu ‘i mata-
tahi he fakafetaulaki kiate ia, ‘o toe fai ‘ae tau.
Ka na‘e ‘ikai loto ‘a Jisu ki ai, he kuo ne fiu : koia
na ‘a ne tala ke nau toe hekavaka; bea nau faka-
teletele atu ‘i he matafonua ‘o Kaleli ‘o a‘u ki
Beteseta. Bea, lolotoga ‘enau o, na‘e talanoa kiate
kinautolu ‘e Jisu ‘i he kovi ‘oe aga koia kuo ma‘u ‘e
hono fili, ‘o fai fakatata aibe, ‘o hage ko ‘ene fa‘a fai,
‘o ui ia koe levani. Ka kuo mo‘ua kehe ‘ae loto ‘oe
kau-ako, koe'uhi ‘oku nau folau ta‘e ha tokonaki; ko
‘enau ‘amanaki nofo atu ki he fine'eiki. Koia na‘e
taki ‘ae lea ‘a Jisu ki he me‘a na‘e kavea ki ai honau
loto, ‘o nau mahalo, ko ‘ene lau ki ha tokonaki.
Koia, kuo faka‘au ke faigata'a ‘ae mo‘ui ‘ae ‘Eiki,
bea hage na‘e kamata ogo ki hono loto. Sa‘e ai ‘ene
ogo mana na‘e fai ‘i he taimi koia na‘e matamata
kehe. Na‘e hoko ha taha ‘i he kauvai, ofi ki he taimi
na‘a ne fafaga ai ‘ae toko 4000. Ka‘e ‘ikai loko
faigata‘a fau ‘ae me‘a, ‘o hage koe ni‘ihi, he koe tuli
mo le‘ovale be : kae matamata faigata'a‘ia ai ‘a Jisu ;
he na‘a ne taki kehe ‘ae tagata, bea mabuhoi mo haga
ki he lagi, bea toki lava. Behe moe mana na‘a ne
fai ‘i he'enau tu‘uta ki Betesaita. Koe tagata na‘e
kui, bea kuo laid ‘ae kakai behe kuo ne faka‘a : ka
na‘a ne taki ‘ae toko taha koeni kitua‘ii, hage ‘oku ne
manavahe na‘a ‘ikai lava; bea, ne ogo na‘a ne fai, ka
na‘e ‘ikai ke haohaoa ‘ene jio, kae'oua ke toe fai bea
ne toki ‘a lelei; ka, na‘a moia, na‘e ‘oua Ji‘i bea toki
haohaoa ‘aubito.
Koe g. me‘a fo‘ou ia ‘i he mo'ui ‘a Jisu, ka ‘oku
mahu'iga ‘aubito, he ‘oku mahino ai koe tagata
mo'oni, bea na‘e ogo ki hono loto ‘ae g. faigata'a na‘e


tau ki he'ene mo‘ui, bea toji ai ‘ene inalohi ! o hage ko
‘eta fa‘a ogo'i kitaua. Ka koe taimi ji‘i be, bea, ‘i
he'ene o‘i, na‘e ma‘u be ‘ae malohi ‘o hono loto, bea
fakautuutu ‘ene fu‘u mafai, kae‘oua ke tumntumu
‘i he fokotu'u ‘o Lasalosi mo ‘ene toetu‘u a‘ana.
('Oku kei toe be.)


KOE VAHE YI.
KOE KITE O‘ENE BEKIA.
Koe Ha Fakalagi ‘i he Mohiga.
Koe taimi kovi ‘eni ‘i ho mo'ui ‘a Jisu; boa na‘e
‘ikai hano malolo'aga, koe me'a ‘i hono fakafe'atugia ‘e
hono g. fili, koe hou'eiki Jiu. Koia, ne ogo ‘ene holi
ke foki ki hono ‘abi ‘i Kabaneume, ka na‘a ne teteki
ki ho fakakikihi ‘e boko ai, bea ne fonoga atu ki he
tokelau, ki he talalo ‘o fu‘u Hcamoni, £ aia na‘a ne ‘ilo,
‘e ‘ikai te nau loko fie ‘alu ki ai.
Bea koeni kuo mahino kiate ia ‘e ‘ikai te ne mo'ui
fuoloa; bea, hage ko kitautolu, koe me'a na‘e mamafa
ki hono loto, be kuo no lava ‘ene gaue be ‘ikai. Koe
me'a ia na‘a ne lotua lahi ki he‘ene Tamai: bea koe
‘aho ‘e taha na‘o mo'utamakia ia ‘e ho Kan Ako ‘oku
ne fai behe ; bea na‘e ‘ikai te ne mata'ofi, ka ne fehu‘i
kiate kinautolu, bo koeha ‘ao lau ‘ae kakai kiate ia.
Koe misiteli ia ‘one fehu'i behe; he ‘ikai ko Tokai-
ma'anaga ia ? Koe me‘a koia ‘oku ‘ikai te tau a‘ujia—
‘ae nonofo ‘a hono ‘Otua mo hono Tagata. ‘Oku
matamata ko hono fakatiita ‘ae Sikaina ‘i mu‘a, ‘aia
na‘e fa‘a gata ‘i he Botu Tobutabu, bea ‘ikai ‘ilo ‘e
ha taha ki ai; ka, ‘i he taimi ni'ihi, na‘e ho'ata mai


kitu'a, ‘o hulu'ia ‘ae g. feitu'u kotoa. Bea na‘a koe
taimi ‘eni ‘oe nofo ‘ae sikaina ‘i laumalie be, bea
‘uhiga leva ‘ene fehu'i ki he kau-ako ‘i he me‘a na‘e
tau ke ne ‘ilo ki ai ‘late ia.
Koe me‘a fakaofo ‘enau tali. Kuo fu‘u mahino
kiate kinautolu koe Misaia ia, bea totonu ke ‘ilo ‘e he
kakai, he hono taha ‘ae mana kuo no fai ? ka, ta, na‘e
‘ikai, bea na‘e ban ke fakaha ‘e he Kau Abosetolo kuo
lahi ‘ae tae‘aoga o'ene gaue, bea koe me‘a be kuo a‘u
ki ai ‘ae kakai, ko Jione Babitaiso ia, be ko Ilaijia
be Selemaia be ha taha ‘oe kau Balofita. Koe fu‘u
akonaki ia kiate kitautolu, ke ‘oua na‘a tau faka-
jikaka'iha me‘a koe'uhi ko ‘ene ta'efua leva : he, na‘a
moe gaiio ‘ae ‘Alo ‘oe ‘Otua, na‘e matamata tae'aoga ‘i
he kamata'aga. Hono ‘ikai mo‘oni ‘ae to‘o ‘e he ‘Eiki
kiate ia ‘ae aga ‘oe tagatal he koe nanuga aibe ‘oe
‘ikai te tau ‘otua, kuo bau ‘e ‘ikai lava ‘etau me‘a
ni‘ihi.
Ka na‘o kei toe ‘ene gaue lahi, a‘ene gaue
ki ho Kau Ako. Koe kulanoa moial Kane
belie, jio‘oto‘ofa ki mamani! Ta, kuo ka'aga mo‘oni
‘ae tagata ! Kae, monu, kuo o‘o ki honau loto
‘onautolu a‘ene g. akonaki, moe gaiie, kae‘uma‘a ‘ae
aga, bea kuo tutu ai ‘ae mama, koe mama ‘OO tui.
He, ‘i he‘ene fehu‘i be kuo fefe ‘ae lau ‘anautolu, na‘e
tali leva ‘e Bita “ Koe Misaia koe, koe ‘Alo ‘oe ‘Otua
Mo‘ui.”
Te tau fakatatau, nai, ki he ha ‘ae me‘a nil Kia
Kolomibusi, nai, ‘i he'ene mamata ki he fonua fo‘ou
‘oku falo nai Bo kia Neutoni ‘i he'ene vakai ‘oku
tonu ‘ene fika, bea kuo bau ‘ae kalavite 1 Koe ogo
‘ata ia, nai, ka koe mo'oni ‘eni, he kuo mahino ai kuo
lava ‘ene gaue ; bea hage na‘a ne lea mo Simione,


“ ‘Eiki, ko ho‘o tukuage ‘eni ho‘o tamaio'eiki ke ‘alu ‘i
he fiemalie.”
Bea nifi koil ‘one ‘ofa kia Bita, ‘aia kuo no faka-
fiemalie ki hono loto 1 Bea lahi ‘ene fiefia koe
mahino ai ‘oku na fetaiaki moe ‘Otua, ‘aia koe gaiie
na‘a ne ha‘u ki mamani ke fai, koe toe ‘omi ki he
Tamai ‘ae fa‘ahiga ne takahe‘i. Kuo ne hage ko
Maui ‘i he talatubu'a, kuo ne fakaogojia ‘i he ta‘u
‘eni ‘e ua ‘i he fuji hake ha tu'uga ke tu‘u ai hono
Jiaji, bea fakafeta'i kuo e‘a hake, he kuo mabuna
hake ‘ae tui ‘a Bita ‘o tu‘u koe fonua : bea folofola
‘ae ‘Eiki, “ Mo'oni ho higoa, Bita ; koe fo‘i malea koe,
koe tebu ‘oe Maka Ta'egata; teu laga ai hoku jiaji,
bea, na‘a moe mate, ‘e ‘ikai te ne lava ia.” Koe ‘aho
koia, ‘i he'ene fiefia, na‘a ne jio ki he fo‘i maka be
taha kuo hobo hake, ko Bita; ka, ‘oka ne tokaga'i,
kuo lahi; ‘io, na‘e ha kiate ia, ‘i ho ‘aho ‘e taha, kuo
a‘u kotoa ‘ae Kau ‘Abosetolo, ‘o ne fakaha ‘e tu'uga
ki ai kotoa ‘ae Jiaji. Ka koe taimi ni ko Bita be
na‘e ha, bea koia na‘e tala ‘e he ‘Eiki ‘e a‘ana aibe
ke kamata; bea koia ia ne fua gaiie'aki ‘ae ki, ‘o
fakaava ‘ae mataba mo tabuni. Na‘e manatu ki he
lea koia ‘e he Jiaji kimui, he'enau mamata ki he
takimu'a, mo fakanofo abosetolo mo fakahu Senitaile.
Ko hono kovi na‘e ‘ikai te nau tokaga ki he tatau
‘ae lea ‘ae ‘Eiki ki he kau ‘Abosetolo kehe ‘i he a‘u
‘enau tui ; koia na‘a nau tuku koe motu'a maka ia ‘i
lalo ; ka ko hono totonu, koe tebu be kuo hobo ki ‘oluga.
‘Oku ai ha me‘a ‘oku hoko kiate kitautolu ‘i he'etau
mo'ui. Tokaage ha ‘aho ‘e fu‘u ha ha me‘a kiate
kitautolu—‘ae mate, be koe kovi ‘oe agahala, be koe
tu'utamaki ‘ae kakai, be koe muna ‘o mamani—bea
koe ha koia ‘oku ‘ikai ke toe mole, ka ‘oku ne nofo


mo kitautolu, bea £ oku ‘ikai ke toe tatau ‘etau mo‘ui
moe taimi mu‘a. Na‘e behe mo Jisu ‘i he g. ‘aho koia.
Kuo kite kiate ia ‘ene bekia, bea kite, foki, moe Mo‘ui
Amui, ‘o ‘ikai lava ‘e he mate ke tamateh; bea hili ia,
na‘e fo‘ofo‘ou ‘ene to'oga ; na‘a ne ‘ofa aibe mo agalelei,
ka ne hage koe toko taha ‘oku ne mo‘ujioa ha me‘a
mama'o.
Na‘a ne fakaha leva ki he Kau Ako ‘ae me‘a ‘oku
kite kiate ia ; ka na‘e hage ha muna ‘ene lau ki hono
fakamamahi‘i mo hono kalusefaih. A a‘a nau ofo ai
katoa: bea na‘e behe ‘e Bita ‘oku totonu ke ne ta‘ofi,
koe'uhi koe lakaga kuo ne toki ma‘u; he, ‘i he kuoga
mu‘a, koe ‘age ‘e he tu‘i ha ki ki ha taha, koe fakanofo
ia ko ‘ene matabule: koia na‘e behe ‘e Bita koe
matabule ia ‘ae ‘Eiki, bea ‘oku a‘ana ke lea malohi.
Koia na‘a ne ‘ave ji‘i mei he kakai, ‘o ne tokoni ke
‘oua te ne lea behe. Ka ka tafuli ‘a Jisu ‘o haga ki
he Kau Ako, ‘o ne behe kia Bita. “ Tu‘u ki mui,
Setane ! ko hoku tukia'aga koe : he ‘oku ‘ikai koe g.
me‘a faka-‘Otua ‘oku jio ki ai ho loto, ka koe g. me‘a
fakaetagata.” Koe kovi aibe ia ‘oe mo‘ui ‘a Jisu;
na‘a moe kakai ofi taha kiate ia, ka na‘e ‘ikai te nau
lavea ‘ae aga o‘ene nofo ; ka, hage ko ‘ene folofola ‘i
he taimi ‘e taha, ‘oku ne toko taha aibe. Seuke,
kohai mo Bita kuo ne ma‘u fiemalie mei ai?
ka na‘a moia, na‘e bau ke ne lamalama ki ai hage ha
fili. Hoto fakabo, ‘ae g. mamahi ‘a Jisu ! kohai ‘e
fakamatala ki ai 1
Na‘e faigata'a ‘aubito ‘ae g. lea na‘e fai ‘e Jisu ‘i
he taimi koia, he‘ene fakamatala ki he‘ene Kau Ako
‘ae aga ‘oe hala ‘oku ne fou ai. Tokua, koe hala be
ia ki he kakai fua-kolosi, ‘aia koe behe, kuo ‘oji aibe
‘ete teu ki he mate ; kae‘uma‘a ke ‘oua ‘aubito te te


kuku ki he'ete mo'ui; he, kabau koia, ‘e mole; ka ko
hoto hao'aga ke te li'aki fua, bea kuo bau ‘e toe
mabuna hake. Ne‘ino‘i behe ‘eia, koe hala ia ki he
kau mateaki.
Hili ‘ae uike ‘e taha, na‘e ‘aye ‘e Jisu ‘ae toko tolu
ofi kiate ia, ‘a Bita mo Semisi mo Jione, ‘o ne behe
ke nau ‘alu hake ki Heamoni. Koe mo'uga ma'oluga
‘aubito ia, ‘o tatau, nai, moe Kao ‘e ua, bea koia na‘e
fa‘a nofo ‘ae sinou ‘i houo tumutumu, ‘o kikila ki he
mama‘o. Ko hono ‘uhiga ia, foki, na‘e tafe ma'ube
‘ae g. vai mei ‘oluga, bea kuo foa ai ‘ae g. tele'a ‘i
hono g. tafa'aki, ‘aia na‘e tu‘u ai ‘ae g. vao tata, moe
g. ‘ana, koe nofo‘aga ‘oe faga manu fekai. Ka‘e fou
‘i he g. tele'a koia ‘ae hala ki he fuga fonua; ka, koe
me‘a ‘i hono mama'o, na‘e tokoji‘i ‘ae kakai na‘e ha‘u
ki ai; kae‘uma‘a koe botu tabu talu mei mu‘a, bea,
‘i hono tebu ‘e taha, na‘e tu‘u ‘ae fale tevolo lahi, koe
nofo'aga totonu, tokua, ‘oe fa‘ahikehe lahi ‘o ono'aho—
ko Beali.
Tala‘ehai koe me‘a fo‘ou ‘ae ‘alu ‘a Jisu ki he
mo‘uga ; ka ‘oku te behe na‘a nau ofo ‘i he'ene vivili
ke a‘u ki ‘oluga. Kabau ko ‘ene fie lotu, ko hono
botu lelei ki ai ‘ae g. vao tata, be ko ha ‘ana; kae fai
atu be ‘a Jisu ki he botu ‘oku matu'aki mavahe mei
mamani. ‘Oku te behe na‘e hela ‘ae Kau Ako ‘i
he'enau a‘u ki fuga fonua, ‘o nau faka'amu ke fai
ai ‘e Jisu ‘ene lotu; ka koe botu ia ‘oku fa‘a
ha‘ele ai ‘ae fa'ahikehe, bea na‘e tuiaki atu ‘e
Jisu ki he botu ‘e ha ki lagi, ‘o galigali lave ai ‘ae
kau agelo ‘i he'enau buna Info, ‘o ‘oua ‘aubito ai ha
faka'iloga ‘o mamani, be ko lolofonua.
Bea faifai bea lava. Koe tumutumu na‘a nau a‘u
ki ai koe muifonua ‘o mamani ki lagi; koe sinou na‘a


nau nofo ai; na‘e hage koe faliki ‘o Hevani ni ‘one
hinaekiaki; koe matagi na‘e hauhaufano ai na‘e ma‘a
mei lie ‘uli ‘o mamani,'bea hage koe agi mei Balataisi.
Kuo tobono ‘eni ‘ae loto ‘oe ‘Eiki, ‘o ne kamata fai
‘ene lotu ; kae tokoto ‘ae Kau ‘Abosetolo ‘o mohe, he
kuo nau ogojia, kae‘uma‘a kuo mole ‘ae ‘aho ‘i he‘enau
fonoga, bea kuo bo‘uli. ‘E, ka ai ha me‘a ‘e faka-
tomala ai ‘a Bita ‘amui, ka koe ‘ikai te ne ‘a atu, ‘o
‘ilo ki he lolofa hifo ‘ae saliote na‘e omi ai ‘ae hou‘eiki
‘oo lagi. Kae‘uma‘a ke ne mamata ki he uloulo atu
‘ae mama Sikaina mei he finagalo ‘o Jisu, ‘o ‘aji mai
‘i hono fotuga mo hono to'ukubu, mo hono kofu,
kae‘oua ke hage koe uloafi hono kotoa. Isa ! isa !he
hoko ha me‘a behe ‘i mamani kae ‘ikai ha tagata te
ne mamata ai ! Kae, malo, na‘e ma‘u hano ‘eu.
‘lloage na‘e ‘a ‘ae Kau Ako, ‘o nau fu‘u ofo ‘i he'enau
vakai ki he toko tolu gigila ‘oku talanoa. Koe bo‘uli,
ka na‘e ha noabe honau fofoga, he na‘e ulo ‘o hage ha
tobukie ; bea nau vakai, koe taha ‘a Jisu; ka kohai
kinaua 1 Koe ogo agelo, ‘abe ? Kae vavana honau
loto ‘i he'enau fanogo ki he ui kinaua ‘e he ‘Eiki, koe
taha ko Mosese, koe taha ko Ilaijia; bea fakamo'oni
ki ai ‘e he lau ‘ae ‘Eiki ki he ‘alu hake ‘a Mosese moe
kakai mei Ijibite, moe ‘ohake ‘o Ilaijia ‘i he saliote
afi. Bea buna ‘ae fiefia ‘i he loto ‘o Bita moe ogo
me‘a. Ta, ko Mosese eni, ‘aia kuo nau lau ki ai ko
honau kololia‘aga; bea mo Ilaijia, foki, kuo nau fa‘a
talanoa ki ai moe Tagata‘eiki. ‘Oi, hono ‘ikai faka-
‘ofo'ofa hono fofoga ! hono ‘ikai molumalu ! Bea
‘ikai mafakama‘uma‘u ‘a Bita, ka na‘e buna atu ‘ene
lea, “ ‘Eiki, ‘oku sai ‘etau ‘i heni, kau gaohi, mu‘a, ha
fakahekeheke ‘e tolu, na‘a mokojia ‘ae hou'eiki ni.”
Ji‘i Bita fa‘a ‘oho ! Koe behe ke nau nofo aibe ‘


‘oluga na, ka kuo mafola ‘a mamani ‘i lalo koe koto
kovi ke gaohi? Ka na‘e mo‘oni aibe ‘a Bita, koe
koga mo‘ui fakalagi ‘oku ne mamata ai, bea tonuhia
‘ene fie kuku ki ai.
Ka koeni kuo ‘oji ! ae talanoa, bea to honau manava
‘i he'enau vakai ‘oku gaolo mai ‘ae Saliote ‘o Lagi.
Bea koeha na‘e behe ai ‘enau tetetete ‘i he'ene ofi
mai 1 ‘aeii ‘oku ogo'i ‘e he kakai kotoa, ‘io, moe kau
agelo, ‘oka ofi mai ‘ae ‘Otua. ‘Io, koe behe ke
mofuike ‘ae mo'uga ‘i he hifo ki ai ‘ae ‘Otua, ‘o ‘oua
‘e mofuike koa ‘ae loto ‘oe tagata ! Koia, ‘i he
mahiki ‘ae Saliote, bea ogo mei ai ‘ae lea. “Ko hoku
‘Alo Bele ‘ena, mou fakaogo kiate ia,” na‘a nau
mabe'e ki lalo ‘o hage ha mate. ‘lloage na‘a nau
fanogo ki he le‘o ‘o honau ‘Eiki ‘oku ne behe mai,
“ Tu‘u, ‘o ‘oua ‘e manavahe ” ; bea nau haga hake, ta,
ko Jisu be ‘oku ha mai: bea ko ‘ene ha koia na‘e
‘ikai ke toe galo ‘iate kinautolu. He kuo bo‘uli, bea
‘ajili ai, ‘i he toki hiki ‘ae fu‘u ‘ao mama, na‘e bobogi
ai honau mata ; ka, ‘i he bo‘uli koia, ‘oku tu‘u ‘a Jisu,
‘o ulo hage ha fu‘u mama: bea, hili ‘ae g. ta‘u lahi,
na‘e kei lea ki ai ‘a Bita mo Jione ‘i he'ena tohi, ‘o
lau ki he mama ulo ‘i he bo'uli.
Ka koeha ‘ae mama koia ? ‘Oku tau tui koe ulo
mai ‘ae Sikaina mei hono finagalo ; ka koeha hono
‘uhiga kia Jisu? ‘Aea na‘e ha ‘i he kuoga mu‘a ‘i
he fua ‘atu ‘ae feilaulau, ‘o hilifaki ki he olita;
na‘e buho mai, tokua, ‘ae mama ‘o tutu. Koeni
kuo kite kia Jisu ‘ae tu‘utu‘uni ‘ae Tamai ke
ne bekia, bea, ‘i he‘ene ‘i he mo'uga ni, ‘oku ne tali
“ Koau,” hage ko Aisake, ‘o ne tuku hono jino ki he
feilaulau ; bea koe buho mai e ‘ae afi mei lagi ke tutu
‘ae feilaulau.


Ka tala'ehai na‘c mabino ia ki he Kau Abosetolo —
‘o mahino koii, ka kuo te‘cki te nau tui te ne bekia !
Koia na‘e tu‘utu‘uni ‘e Jisu ke ‘oua te nau lea ki ai
kae'oua ke ne toetu'u mei he mate. Bea ‘ajili
bubutu'u ai honau loto ; he, kabau na‘e ‘ikai ‘uhiga
‘ene bekia, kae huanoa ha toetu'u. Ka koe me‘a ‘e
taha na‘e mahino, kuo nau mamata Ida Ilaijia; bea
na‘a ko ‘ene ha‘u ia kuo lau ki ai ‘ae Matu‘a, ‘o
‘amanaki ki ai ‘ae kakai Isileli kotoa, ‘o nau fakaava
ki ai ‘ae mataba ‘i he Basova 1 Ka na‘e tali ‘e Jisu
‘oku ‘ikai, he kuo loa ‘ene ha‘u ‘ana, bea kuo nau
tamate‘i, bea koe fakamo'oni ia ki he lea ‘oku ne fa‘a
fai—te ne mate tamatea moia.
Kuo ho'ata, nai, ‘i he‘enau a‘u ki lalo, ki he botu
na‘e nofo ai ‘ae Kau Ako ; bea, ‘i he'enau oti ki ai, na‘c
ha mai ha fu‘u kakai ‘oku matamata kehe ‘enau
to‘oga, ‘o hage kuo ‘i ai ha maveuveu kuo hoko. Ko
hono ‘uhiga, he kuo talu ‘ae kamata lau ‘a Jisu ki he
g. me‘a ‘oku ene ke fai ‘i Selusalema, moe tuku bau
‘e he Kau Ako ‘i honau loto, ‘oku toeji'i bea ne ha koe
Misaia, ‘o fokotu‘u hono Bule'aga. Bea nau mo‘ua
ai ki he fakakaukau ki ha tu'uga te nau ma‘u, bea
nau li'aki ai ‘enau fa‘a lotu ; ‘o fakamama fau ‘enau
tokaga. ‘lloage na‘e ‘omi kiate kinautolu ha mahaki
na‘e keheage ke nau faito'o ki ai—koe tamaji‘i na‘e
‘ulujino ai ha tevolo kovi, ‘o ‘ikai koe toki me‘a, kae
talu ‘ene valevale. Koe me‘a faigata‘a, ka na‘e ‘ikai
ha tala‘a be teki ‘ehe Kau Abosetolo, he kuo toko lahi
‘ae kakai belie kuo nau fakamo'ui, bea na‘e ‘ikai te
nau ‘ilo kuo maha honau ivi ‘i he motumotu ‘enau
lotu. Bea na‘a nau behe ke ‘omi, ‘o nau fekau ki he
tevolo ke feirao mahu‘i atu. Kae ‘ikai ‘aubito, bea,
hage ko Kolaiate, na‘a nau ofo hake ‘o ‘ilo kuo mole


‘enau malohi. Boa ‘lkai‘ia koia, ka na‘e lolofi mai
leva honau g. lili, ‘ae kau Sikalaibe, ‘o nau fakai'i
mai, ‘e ‘ikai te nau lava, Koe houa faigata'a, bea
hei‘ilo be na ! e fefe ka ne fca‘oua ‘ae ha mai ‘a Jisu moe
taba ki he'enau tau.
Na‘e mamahi ‘aubito hono finagalo ‘i he gaohi
behe‘i hono kakai. ‘lkai kuo laui afe ‘ae mahaki
behe kuo lava bea ko ‘enau manuki leva ‘i he ‘ikai
lava ha fo‘i me‘a ‘e taha ! Koe‘uma‘a ‘ene gaue ki
ha fa‘ahiga behe. ‘Oku hage na‘e ‘oho foki ‘ae kakai
‘i he'enau mamata kia Jisu, koe'uhi, ‘abe, na‘e kei ulo
hono fofoga ‘o hage ko Mosose ‘i mu‘a—kae kehe na‘a
nau tuku ‘ae kau Sikalaibe, ‘o nau felelei kiate ia.
Fokau ‘eia ke ‘omi ‘ae tamaji‘i, bea, ‘i hono ‘omi, koe
me‘a kehe hono gaohi ‘e he tevolo. Hage na‘e loto ‘e
he ‘Eiki ke ‘ilo ‘e he kakai, kao‘uma‘a ‘ae fili, ‘oku
‘ikai koe me‘a faigofua ia, ‘aia kuo ta‘elava ‘e he‘ene
Kau Ako : koia na‘e ‘ikai tene fakamo'ui leva, ka ne
‘eke ki he‘ene tamai ‘ae aga ‘oo mahaki. Koe toki
me‘a kuo ogo ki he loto ‘oe to‘utagata kotoabe ‘ae g,
tali ‘ae motu'a, ‘ene ‘ofa mamahi ki he‘ene tamaji'i
mo ‘ene feiga ke ne lava ‘ae tui te ne mo‘ui ai. Koe
Kalisitiani fe kuo ‘ikai te ne fai‘aki ‘ae lea ne lea‘aki
‘e he motu'a koia ? “ ‘Oku ou tui bo, tokoni ‘eku
ta'etui.” Koe lea koia na‘a ne ikuna ‘ae ‘Eiki, ‘o ne
fekau ki he fa'ahikehe ke ne feimo buna atu. Ka
na‘e behe ‘ae kovi ‘o hono gaohi na‘e hage kuo bekia :
ka, ‘i he ala fakamo'ui ‘ae ‘Eiki, na‘a ne tu‘u ‘o ‘alu.
Hono ji'ikoa, ‘ae fakafeta'i ‘ae Kau Ako ‘i he'ene ‘aofia
kinautolu mei he ma, ka na‘a nau ofo ‘i he ‘ikai lava
‘ekinautolu, ‘o nau fehu‘i ki he Tagata'eiki; bea toki
mahino kiate kinautolu ‘ae hala ke nau malohi faka-
laumalie ai —ke lain ‘enau lotu.


Na‘a nau told 6 ki Kabaneume : kae fai aibe ‘enau
fakakikihi ki honau tu'uga ‘i he Bule‘aga—hage na‘e
kabujigofua ‘ae tevolo ‘anenai ‘i he tevolo, ko Kakaba.
Koia, ‘i he ‘enau a‘u ki ‘abi, na‘e valoki kinautolu ‘o
Jisu, bea hage ko ‘ene fa‘a fai na‘e tu‘uga ‘ene valoki
ki ha ine'a ofi mai. Na‘e nofo mai ha ki‘i tamaji'i,
koe foha, nai, ‘o ha Abosetolo kuo ha‘u ki he‘ene
tamai, bea buke ‘e Jisu ‘o habai, ‘o ne behe kiate
kinautolu, koe tali ha tamaji'i behe ‘i hono huafa ‘e
lau ia ‘e he lagi koe tali ‘o Jisu, ‘io, koe tali ia ‘oe
‘Otua ; bea, kabau‘oku ma‘u ‘e ha tamajri ha tu'uga
behe, bea koe‘uma‘a ‘enau kakaba, be hono ai ha me‘a
ag el ko hono totonu ke nau hage koe tamajhi koia,
‘o ‘oua ‘e tokaga tu‘uga.
Ka kuo fonu honau loto ‘i he jio ki he ma‘u ‘oe
bule ‘e honau fa‘ahi, bea na‘a mo Jione na‘e ‘ikai o‘o
ki ai: ‘o ne lea mai, be koeha te nau fai ki he kakai
‘oku ‘ikai kau ki honau fa'ahi, ka ‘oku nau gaue'aki
‘ae huafa ‘o Jisu. Behe mo Bita na‘a ne fehu‘i be tu‘o
fiha ‘ene fakamolemole ha taha —ko ‘ene ‘amanaki ki
he taimi te ne matabule, he kuo ne ma‘u ‘ae ki.
Hage na‘e mamafa ki he ‘Eiki ‘enau behe, ‘o ne lea
majila kiate kinautolu ke tu'uji ‘ae aga koia, he,
kabau te nau fai‘aki, kuo bau te nau fakatukia ‘ae
vaivai, he ‘oku o aibe moe kakaba ‘ae fakajikaka :
kae‘uma‘a ‘e tubu ai ‘ae fe‘ite‘itani,bea, ka hoko ‘obehe
‘enau feagai, te nau ta'eaoga —kuo mole mei he masima
hono kona. Bea ne faka‘oji‘aki ‘ae Fakatatii ‘oe
Tamaio‘eilei agahovi, ‘aia na‘e hoa mo honau loto, he
koe lau ki ha tu‘i, mo ha sivi fakabule‘aga: ‘o
