mahino mei ai, ‘e ikai hanau momo‘i tu‘uga ‘i he
Bule'aga, ‘o kabau ‘oku nau tae'ofa ki he kakai ‘oku
nau kaugagaue.


Ne‘ine‘i mamafa ‘a Jisu Id he me'a koia, he ‘oku te
behe, ne mcimei ji‘i ‘ae kovi kuo hoko ki he jiaji mei
mamani ‘i he kovi kuo tubu ‘i he kakaha ‘ae ni‘ihi ‘i
he Kau Gaue. Kuo hau ke ai ha ni‘ihi ke hule, bea
koe fu‘u ava ia kia Setane ke fakatubu maveuveu.
Koe me'a fakaofo kiate kita ‘ae ‘ikai fai ha rneheka
kia Bita ‘i he ‘ulu‘aki Jiaji. Na‘a kuo mahino ‘ene
tau ke matahule. Ka koe tau koa !he na‘a mo ‘enau
nofo koeni ‘i Kabaneume na‘a ne toe ‘oho ‘o hala.
Na‘e ai ha tukuhau na‘e fai ki he Jiaji talu mei mu‘a,
koe hafi sikeli, fe‘uga, nai, moe silini ‘e taha moe
sikibeni. Ko hono ‘uhiga koe huhu‘i ‘oe laumalie,
bea koia na‘e fai tatau ai ‘ae koloaha moe majiva,
hage koe behe ‘oku mahuhga tatau honau laumalie.
Ka‘e hage ia ko ‘etau togltihite, bea na‘e gauo'aki ‘i
he tauhi ‘oe falelotu, moe fakatau manu ‘i he feilaulau.
moe alame'a behe. Na‘e ‘ikai fa‘a ‘eke ia ki ha
Labai, bea koe me'a fo‘ou ‘eni ‘enau ‘eke kia Jisu,
kae‘uma‘a na‘e ‘ikai ko hono taimi totonu ; koia ‘oku
matamata koe laga‘i be ‘e hono g. fili, - ae ha‘u ‘ae kau
tanaki tukuhau kia Bita ‘o fehu‘i be ‘oku fai ‘e he
Tagata‘eiki ‘ae tukuhau. ‘Oho leva ‘a Bita, ‘o tali
‘io, telia, nai, ‘ae ogoogo ‘o Jisu. Ka na‘e tau ke ne
manatu ‘oku ‘ikai ha hia ‘a Jisu ke ne huhu'i ai hono
laumalie, kae‘uma‘a koe Lami ‘ae ‘Otua ia ; bea ke
ne toe totogi koa ki ha feilaulau 1 Ka na‘e ‘ikai ke
tu‘uga ‘e Jisu ‘ene fakamatala ki he ogo me'a koia, ka
ki he fakamo‘oni kuo toki fai ‘e Bita. He koe
tukuhau koia koe tu'utu'uni ‘a Jihova, ‘aia kuo
fakaha ‘e Bita ko hono ‘Alo ‘a Jisu ; bea koe behe
koa ke tukukau ‘e he Kale‘alo?—na‘e ‘ikai ‘ilo ki ha
me'a behe ‘i mu‘a. Kane ogo ‘ae taukave ‘e Jisu
‘oku ne ‘ata'ata mei he tukuhau koia, kae ‘ikai le


ne fakama'i ‘one matabulc ; bea na‘a ne fekau ko ne
‘alu ‘o taumata'u, bea to ne ‘ilo ki he ika ‘e raa'u ha
lau‘i sikeli katoa ke fai'aki ‘ena tukuhau. Kane
ogo ‘ene faka‘atu‘i behe ‘ae ma ‘a Bita, ka na‘e ‘ikai
galo hono tu'uga, ke ne behe ke ke ‘ave “ ma'ataua,”
ka koe “ rna'aku mo koe ” —ma'aku, keu boubou ‘ae
tu‘utu‘uni ‘a ‘eku Tamai, mo koe, ke huhu‘i‘aki ho
laumalie.
{‘Oku kei toe be.)


KOE YAHE VII.
KOE KITE O‘ENE BEKIA (AIBE).
Koe 'Uluaki Kubu.
Na‘k ‘ikai ke fuoloa ‘ae nofo ‘a Jisu ‘i Kabaneume ‘i
he taimi koia, he kuo banaki ha taha ‘i he'enau g.
Katoaga lahi,bea na‘e gaueue ‘aefonua kotoake ‘alu ki
Selusalema. Koe Katoaga koia koe fakaxnanatu ki he
fonoga a ‘enau g. kui ‘i he toafa, ‘aia na‘e ‘ikai ha nau
nofo'aga ma‘u, ka nau hikihiki holo be ‘euau g. teniti,
bea na‘a nau gaohi fakahekeheke ‘aki ‘ae g. lou‘akau.
Bea koe'uhi ke fakatata ji‘i ki ai, koia ‘i he fai ‘oe
Katoaga, na‘a nau fai ta‘aga ‘i he g. rao ofi ki Selu-
salema, ‘o nau gaohi'aki ‘ae g. fale lou'akau ‘i he g.
hala ‘oe kolo, moe g. ‘abi tua‘a. Koe taimi lelei ki
ha me‘a behe, he koe faka'oji ‘o Sebitema moe ka-
mata'aga ‘o Okatoba; kuo ‘oji ‘ae mafana lahi bea
te‘eki hoko ‘ae momoko, kae‘uma‘a kuo utu ‘ae ta‘u,
‘ae uite, ‘ae ba'ale, ‘ae kalebi, ‘ae olive; koe me‘a
katoa kuo ‘i feleoko, bea ‘oku kei tuai ‘ae gaue ki he
tota‘u. Koe toki taimi ki ha katoaga, he ‘oku malolo
‘ae kelekele moe manu, bea ‘ata ‘ae tagata ke fai ‘ene
fakafeta'i ki he ‘Otua ‘i he ‘ofa kuo to.
Hei'ilobe ‘oku ‘i ai ha fonua ‘imamani ‘oku hage ko


Kenani ‘i he me‘a koia—‘ae fa‘a tanaki ki he kolo mu‘a
‘o meimei koe kakai kotoa he fai ‘oe Katoaga lalahi.
‘Oku mo‘oni ‘oku ‘i ai ha g. taimi malolo ‘i Bilitania
moe g. fonua, ‘aia ‘oku tabu ai ‘ete kouna ha taha ke
gaue, hage koe Faite Lelei, moe ‘Aloi, moe ‘aho ‘oku
hoko &c., ka ‘oku taha kehe ia, he ‘oku taki taha fai
katoaga ‘i hono fonua. Ka ‘i Kenani, ‘i he ofi mai
hono taimi, na‘e kamata fonoga mai ‘ae kakai kotoa
nae ‘ata ke ‘alu. Koe kakai ‘oe feitu'u tokelau
na‘e fuofua gaue, bea uouotu'u leva ‘ae g. hala
‘i he g. fonoga na‘e ‘alu ai. Ka‘e ‘ikai ha kolo
tu‘umo‘uga, be ha viliji ‘i ke toafa, ka ‘e ‘alu atu
hanau uofulu, nimagofulu, teau, ‘ae tagata, feline,
tamaiki, ‘o nau fou atu ‘i he g. afega ki he g. hala
fakabule‘aga. Bea ko enau a‘u atu leva ki ha kolo,
bea fakahoko mai ‘ae fonoga ‘oe kolo koia, ‘o behe be,
kae'oua ke meimei ‘ikai hao ‘ae fonua koe kakai. Koe
toki tu‘utu‘uni ke fa'utaha ai ha kakai, koe fa‘a fe-
‘iloaki ‘ae kaiga moe temomo kuo movetevete ki he g.
feitu'u; bea na‘e fehi'a ki ai aibe ‘ae houeiki muli kuo
nau buke ‘ae fonua, he koe me‘a ia na‘e ta‘ofi ai ‘ae
vaivai ‘ae kakai Jiu, he, ‘i he'enau fehloaki mo talanoa,
na‘e fa‘a ake ai ‘ae manatu ki honau tu'uga mu‘a ‘o
nau hoha‘a ‘i he nofo bule‘ia.
Ko hono ‘uhiga ia ‘oe ha‘u ‘ae g. tehina ‘o Jisu, ‘o
lea kiate ia ke ne ‘alu ki he Katoaga ‘o fai ha me‘a.
Kuo fuoloa ‘eni ‘ae fai gaue ‘a honau ta'okete, bea ‘oku
ne lau koe Misaia ia, tokua, bea koe taha kehe; ka
koeha ha me‘a kuo hoko ai? ko honau kabuji be mei
Nasaleti, mo ‘enau nofo hoha'a aibe na‘a buke ia ‘e he
hou'eiki ‘o fai ha me‘a ki ai. Ka koe ‘atuga aibe ‘o
‘ene taka ‘i he fonua tua‘a ko Kaleli, ‘o tanaki ha kau
ma'ulalo ‘o hage koe Kau Abosetolo ni. Ko hono to-


tonu ke ne ‘alu ki Selusalema ‘o fai ‘ene g. mana ‘i he
Katoaga, aia ‘o katoaki ai ‘aehou'eiki ‘oe fonua, bea
mafana ‘ae loto ‘oe kakai, bea hei'ilo ‘e toki fai ai ha
‘oho, bea toki lava ‘ene gaue fakaato.
Koe fakakaukau boto ‘i he lau fakamaraa, bea
tail mo kinautolu, he ko ‘enau muimui kia Jisu
koe fai fakajino be, kuo te'eki ke nau tui bikitai
kiate ia. Ka na‘e mea‘i ‘e Jisu kuo fakaa'au ke
kakaha ‘ae ‘ita ‘a hono g. fili, bea, kabau te ne
ma‘u ‘ae kamata'aga ‘oe Katoaga, ‘e ‘ikai a‘u ‘enau
kataki ki he ‘aho faka'oji, bea ‘oku ‘i ai ‘ene gaue ke
fai ‘i he ‘aho koia : koia na‘a ne tala ki hono g. tehina
ke nau o moe g. fonoga, he ‘e ‘ikai vave ‘ene ‘alu
a‘ana.
Na‘e ha leva ‘ae mo'oni ‘oe fakakaukau ‘a Jisu, he,
ne ogo kuo vaena ‘ae Katoga ‘i he‘ene a‘u atu, ‘o toe
‘aho tolu be, ka na‘e kamata maveuveu leva. Ka‘e
kamata aibe ‘i hono fakajikakai‘i ‘e he kau gaue
faka-Jiu, koe'uhi koe ‘ikai te ne ako ‘i ha Labai; ‘o
nau lau, foki,ki he‘ene maumau Sabate, he'ene fakamo-
‘ui ‘ae mamatea. Na‘e bau ke tali ‘e Jisu ki he me‘a
koia telia ‘ene Kau Ako ; bea ko ‘ene tali koia na‘e
hage koe ligi ha 1010 ki ha afl: he na‘a ne taukave
ko ‘ene akonaki ‘oku ‘ikai koe me‘a ke tu'uga ‘i ha
Labai be ‘ia Mosese, ka koe me‘a ‘e tu‘u ‘iate ia.
Kae‘uma‘a ko loto ke nau fai ki he Lao ‘a Mosese,
‘aia ‘oku nau lau ki ai ; he ‘oku tu‘u ‘i he'ene tohi
‘oku tabu ke fakabo, ka koeni ‘oku nau feiga ke tam-
ate‘i ia. Na‘e ‘ikai ha‘anau tali ki he g. me‘a koia ;
koia na‘a nau fai hage koe toko lahi ‘o kamata ke
talalakulaku ki ai, ‘o nau behe, ‘oku ulujino ai ha
tevolo.
Na‘e ‘ikai tali ‘e Jisu ‘enau laukovi koia, ‘o ne fai


atu be ‘ene fakamatala; bea ne ogo na‘e fakautuutu
‘ae ‘ita ‘ae ka na‘e iku be ki he tui ha toko lahi
‘i he'enau vakai ki he mo‘oni race gali ‘o ‘ene g. lea
moe ta'etau ‘oe to'oga ‘ae fa'ahi ‘e taha. Bea, ‘i he
‘ilo ki ai ‘ae kau Falesi, na‘a nau fekau atu ha kau
ofisa ke buke ia, he na‘e ‘ikai te nau kataki ko ma-
mata ki he tafokiage ‘ae kakai ke nofo kiate ia. Kae
lolotoga ‘ae lamalama -‘e he kau tagata koia ki ha
faigamalie ke nau buke ‘a Jisu, na‘e mo‘ua honau Into
‘onautolu ‘i he g. folofola malie, bea ha kiate kinautolu
‘ene makehe atu noabe moe g. koto lau ‘ae kau Labai
na‘a nau nofo ki ai; bea na‘a navi muitulia kiate ia,
‘o fanogo, hage koe kakai, ki he g. lea na‘e to mei hono
fofoga, bea galo ‘aubito ‘ae tu‘utu‘uni na‘e ha‘u mo
kinautolu ke fai.
Fe‘uga moia kuo ‘oji ‘ae ‘aho ‘e fitu ‘oe Katoaga, bea
hoko hono ‘aho valu, ‘aia koe faka'oji. Koe ‘aho koia
na‘e kehe hono aga. FTa'e lahi ‘ae g. to‘oga lotu na‘e
fai ‘i he ‘aho ‘e fitu—tuku kehe ‘ae g. feilaulau—ka
na‘e ai moe ‘utuvai na‘e fai mei Sailoame, moe tutu
mama, moe alame'a belie. Koe ‘utuvai koia koe
me‘a na‘e molumalu ‘aubito hono fai. Ka‘e tui kofu
‘ae kakai kotoa ‘o fakataha ki he Tcmibale, ‘o taki
taha to‘o ‘ene ki‘i ‘ulu‘ulu‘akau. Faifai bea to‘o ‘o
ha taula'eiki ‘e taha ha jioki koula, ‘o ‘alu hifo mei he
Temibale ki he tele'a ke ‘utu ha vai mei Sailoame.
Na‘e o moia ha fu‘u fonoga fakamanavahe, bea tutu'u
hono toe ‘i he g. loto'a ke tali ‘enau foki mai, bea,
‘i he ‘iloage na‘e fotu mai ‘ae taula'eiki moe jioki koula
na‘e fonu ‘i he vai tabu, na‘e ha‘aki mai ‘ae ifi talubite
bea mavava ‘ae fakataha kotoa. Na‘e laka ‘ae taula-
'eiki ‘o liligi ‘ae vai ki ha kumete siliva ‘i he ve‘e
olita, bea liligi ‘e ha taha ha uaine ki he kumete


siliva ‘e taha, ‘o nau fai ‘enau hiva lahi, koe
Haleli (Same cxiii.—cxviii.) mo nau takalo ‘enau
g. ‘ulu'ulu'akau ‘i he'enau fiefia. Ka, ‘i hono valu
‘oe ‘aho na‘e ‘ikai ha me‘a behe : bea ko hono fakaofo,
he talu mei mu‘a moe lau ko hono ‘aho lahi ia. Na‘a
nau tuikofu; na‘a nau to‘o ‘enau ‘ulu‘ulu‘akau ; na‘a
nau fakataha ki he Temibale; na‘a nau tutu'u ‘o hage
ko ha'anau ‘amanaki ki ha me‘a, bea kuo fai behe mo
‘enau matu'a ‘o laui toutagata, kae ‘ikai ha me‘a ke
faka‘iloga‘aki hono lahi koia. Ka, ‘i he katoaga koeni,
na‘e toki mahino ai hono ‘uhiga. He lolotoga ‘enau
tutu'u behe, ‘iloage na‘e ogo mai ha fu‘u le‘o malie
‘oku ne behe mai, “ Ka ai ha taha ‘oku fieinua, ke ne
ha‘u kiate au ‘o inu ; ‘iloga ia ‘oku ne tui bikitai kiate
au, bea hage koe lau ‘ae Tohitabu, ‘e tafe atu mei
hono manava ‘ae g. yaitafe ‘oe vaimo'ui.”
Ko Jisu ia na‘e lea : bea ne‘ine‘i ‘oho ‘ae kakai, he
kuo bau ke ‘uhiga ki he toko lahi ‘ene me‘a, ‘o ‘ikai,
nai, hono kotoa he na‘e loloto hono me‘a ni‘ihi. Koe
Jioki Koula ia, koe mo'oni ‘oe maka mana na‘e inu
mei ai ‘e he'enau g. kui ‘i he to‘afa, bea ko kinautolu
to nau inu mei ai ‘e ‘ikai te nau gata ‘i ha ki‘i hu-
‘avai, ka ‘e behe ‘enau fu‘u fonu, te nau hage ko ha
matavai ‘ekinautolu, ‘o fakainu ha toko lahi. Kane
ogo na‘e ‘ilo hanhihi ki ai, ‘o nau tui bau koe Misaia
ia, ka na‘e ‘ajili ‘ae faivale ‘ae ni‘ihi, ‘o nau behe ke
buke leva ‘o fai ha me‘a ki ai; koe faka‘iloga aibe kuo
‘oji ‘ae kataki ‘ae ‘Eiki, bea ‘oku ne tuku ‘ae kui bea
moe ‘uli ke fai aibe honau faka‘uli‘i. Ka na‘e ‘ikai
ke kau ai ‘ae kau ‘ofisa ‘a hou‘eiki, he na‘a nau ‘alu
‘o tala ki he kau Falesi, ‘e ‘ikai te nau buke ‘a Jisu,
he kuo te'eki ha tagata ‘e lea hage koia. Bea hoko
ai ha fu‘u ke ‘i he fakataha, he na‘a mo Nikotimasi


na‘e ‘ikai te ne fa‘a kataki ‘enau g. lau kia Jisu, ‘o
ne tu‘u ke taukabo'i.
Kao ‘ikai ‘aubito toka'i ‘e Jisu ‘enau gaiie, ne ogo
na‘a ne mea‘i ‘ae me‘a ‘oku nau fai. Koe to‘a mo'oni
ia, ‘o ne ‘alu fano be ‘o fai hono lakaga, ne ogo na‘a
ne ‘ilo ‘oku tokamalumu kiate ia hono g. fili ‘i he
botu kotoabe. Koe bo koia na‘a ne fakataha atu ki
he Temibale moe kakai, ‘o hage ko ‘enau fa‘a fai, ne
ogo na‘a ne ‘ilo koe faigamalio ia kiate kinautolu ke
buke ia. Koe g. bo kuo hili na‘e ai ha me‘a na‘e fai,
he na‘e tutu ha fu‘u mama, ‘o ‘ai ki ha tu'uga
ma'oluga ke fakatata'aki ‘ae bouafi na‘e tataki'aki
‘enau g. kui ‘i he to'afa. Bea, ‘i he ulo atu hono
mama ki he kolo, na‘e mavava ‘ae kakai ‘i he fiefia,
‘o nau talanoa ki he ‘ofa ‘ae ‘Otua na‘o fai, mo ‘Ene
huluhulu ‘ae bo‘uli ‘oe toafa, ‘o taki tonu ‘enau
matu‘a ‘i he g. bo koia ‘o a‘u mai ki he fonua koia
‘oku nau ‘i ai. Ka, ‘i he bo koia, ‘a hono valu, na‘e
‘ikai ha mama ‘e tutu, bea, ne ogo na‘e fakataha mai
‘ae kakai, ka ‘oku te behe na‘a nau ofo ‘i hono
tu‘utu‘uni koia, moe ui ‘oe ‘aho koia koe ‘Aho Lahi.
Kae lolotoga ‘enau tutu‘u ‘i he bo'uli, moe toe ogo
mai ‘ae le‘o malie koia, “ Koau be koe mama ‘o mamani:
koia ‘oku ne muimui kiate au, ‘e ‘ikai ‘aubito te ne
fonoga ‘i he bo'uli, ka te ne ma‘u ‘ae Mama ‘oe
Mo‘ui.” Ta, ko hono ‘uhiga ia na‘e ‘ikai ke tutu ‘ae g.
mama fakatata koe'uhi ke ha ‘ae Mama Mo'onia:
kuo to‘o meiate kinautolu ‘ae mama na‘e gaohi ‘e he
tagata koe'uhi ke nau ‘ilo ki he mama kuo ‘ohifo
mei lagi. Bea hono ‘ikai fiefia ‘akinautolu na‘e lotu
mo‘oni ko ‘enau ‘ilo kuo'i ai ha nau bou-mama ke
taki hala kiate kinautolu ‘i he toafa ‘oe mo‘ui ni ?
‘Oku ‘i ai ha ‘akau, tokua, ‘oku tu‘u ta'cfua ‘o teau


ta‘u, bea ne toki fua ‘o mate leva. Na‘e tatau moia
‘ae Katoaga ‘oe Pale-lou‘akau. Kofutu hono tauhi ‘e
he kakai Jiu, ‘o fai aibe ‘ao ‘utuvai moe tutu mama,
kae'uraa'a ‘ae lau ko hono ‘aho lahi ‘ae valu. Ta,
koe tuhu bo kia Jisu. Ta, koe faka'amanaki ‘oe kakai
ki he Vai mo'ui moe Mama Mo'oni. Bea, ‘i he ‘alu
koeni ‘a Jisu ki ai, na‘e toki fakaai ‘ae ge‘cji ‘oe ‘aho
valu ; koe ‘aho koia na‘e fakae'a ‘ae matavai ‘oe
Yaiola, bea tutu ‘ae Mama ‘o Mamani : bea, ‘i he'ene
fua behe, bea mate ‘ae Katoaga : na‘e fai be, ka koe
ge'eji me‘a, bea kuo mole mo Jisu hono ‘uhiga.
Bea kamata ai leva ha fakakikihi ‘a Jisu moe hou-
‘eiki Jiu. JSTa'e mahino kiate kinautolu koe toko
taha ia ‘oku ne ‘afugi ‘oku ne ma‘oluga ‘i he'enau lao,
bea nau ‘ita ai : bea, ne ogo na‘a nau lea ‘o hage ‘oku
nau fie'ilo ki hono tu'uga, ka koe launoa be ; be te
ne ha kohai kuo ban te nau teke'i ia. Na‘e ha ia
kia Jisu, bea na‘e ai ha taimi na‘a ne mei tuku be
kinautolu; ka ne toe kataki be koe'uhi na‘e ‘i ai
‘ene g. lea na‘a ne fie fai, ‘aia na‘a ne behe ‘e aoga ki
he kakai. Bea na‘e behe, he ‘oku fakaha na‘e toko
lahi na‘e tui ‘o kau moia. Bea fakautuutu ai ‘ae
mamahi ‘ae fili, ‘o nau fakai'i mai, hei‘ilo te ne ‘ohovale
o fai ha mo‘a ke nau buko ki ai. Kae ‘ikai ‘aubito
gate ‘a Jisu, ka ne lea be ‘o tau mo hono tubu'aga,
‘o tuku ke e‘a ji‘i hono lagilagi. Bea ogo'i leva ‘e he
hou‘eiki, ta, ‘oku ‘ikai ke gata ‘i he Lao ‘ene fakaji-
kaka, ka na‘a mo Mosese moe kau Beteliake ‘oku
‘ikai to ne toka'i kinautolu. Bea ‘i he‘enau vale ‘i
he ‘ita, ‘o nau beheage be kuo na fefe mo Ebalahame ;
bea tali ‘e Jisu, “ Na‘e hakailagitau ‘a Ebalahame ‘i
he'ene ‘amanaki mamata ki hoku ‘aho ; bea na‘a no
mamata ki ai ‘o fiefia.” Bea, ‘i he'enau tekaki ‘ae lau


koia, bea toki ‘ai ‘e Jisu hono aga totonu ‘o ne to‘o
kiate ia ‘ae Huafa Tobutabu ‘o bonau ‘Otua, ko Koau.
Na‘e ogo kiate kinautolu ‘ae le‘o koia ‘o hage ko ha
le‘o mei Sainai ; ka kuo nau kui ‘i he ‘ita, bea na'e
‘ikai te nau ‘ilo‘i. Koe me'a be na‘e ha kiate kinau-
tolu koe tagata ia kuo ala ki he tu‘uga ‘oe ‘Otua, bea
nau to‘o ‘ae g. maka na‘e fai'aki ‘ae laga ‘oe
Temibale, bea, ka ne tae'oua ‘ae moulu mai ‘a Jisu,
kuo nau fai leva hono tamateh.
Ne ogo ‘oku ‘ikai ha fakamatala ki ai, ka ‘oku tau
‘ilo koe me'a kehe ‘ae g. fakataha ‘a hou'eiki ‘i he
uike koia —‘enau ‘ita, ‘enau lau, ‘enau feiga ha me'a
ke lava ‘aki honau fili ! he koe me'a ia na‘e kona ai
honau loto, koe ‘ikai felave ha‘anau me'a ki ai : ‘io,
ne ogo ‘ene toki meimei tu'utamaki, ka ‘oku ne ‘alu
holo be, ‘o fai ‘ene gaue ‘o hage ‘oku ‘ikai ha me'a.
Bea, ‘i hehoko ‘ae Sabate, na'e ogo mai kiate kinautolu
kuo ne toe fai ha fu‘u mana faka‘ulia, koe faka‘a ha
tagata na'e fanau'i kui. Na‘e ‘ajili ‘enau ‘ita ai koe-
‘uhi ko hono fai ‘i he ‘aho Sabate, ‘o hage ‘oku nofo
‘a Jisu ke laiki ‘enau g. tu'utu'uni.
Koia na'e ‘omi ‘ae tagata ‘o ‘eke, ‘o nau feiga ke
faka‘ikai‘i ‘ae mana. Kae ‘ikai ‘aubito, he na'e houga
ki he tagata ‘ae ‘ofa kuo fai kiate ia, bea ‘ikai te ne
hiki mei he'ene fakamatala. Koe toko taha ia na‘e
fanau'i kui, kuo te‘eki ke ne ‘a ‘i ha taimi; bea na'e
‘ikai te ne ‘amanaki ki ai be kole, kae ‘iloage na‘e
ha‘u ha tagata ‘oku ui ko Jisu, ‘o bani'aki hono mata
ha me‘i belebela, ‘o ne fekau ke ‘alu ki Sailoame ‘o
fufulu, bea, ‘i he‘ene fai koia, na‘a ne ‘a.
Koe me'a kehe ‘ae feiga ‘ae hou‘eiki ke tamate'i
‘ae me'a, kae ‘ikai; na‘e belie ‘enau fakamalohi na‘e
kalo ‘ae matu'a ‘ae tagata, kae ‘ikai ‘aubito gaue


‘ae jiana, bea ‘ikai foki te ne tuku ke nau faka-
bubutu‘u ia, ka, ‘oka matamata fihi ‘enau fehu‘i, na‘a
ne tuku be, ka ne taukave be, “ Koe kui au, ka ‘oku
ou ‘a ni.” Moe me‘a ‘etaba na‘a ne fai, ‘ae taukabo'i
‘oe tagata na‘a ne fakamo'ui ia; bea ‘ikai kataki ‘e
he hou‘eiki ‘ene fai koia, ‘o nau Info ia mei he lotu.
Ka tala'ehai na‘e tobono ai honau loto, he ko Jisu
na‘a nau ‘ita ki ai, bea lolotoga na‘e ‘ata'ata ia, na‘e
‘ikai ha‘anau fiemalie. ‘Oku hage na‘a nau lama
ma‘ube ki ai; bea koe ‘aho ‘e taha na‘a nau vakai ki
he‘ena fetaulaki moe tagata, moe hu ‘ae tagata kiate
ia, bea, ‘i he‘enau ‘alu atu ke fanogo, na‘e ogo mai ‘ae
folofola ‘a Jisu ‘o behe, kuo ne ha‘u ke ‘iloga ha kui
bea ‘a, bea ‘iloga ha ‘a, tokua, bea nau kui. Bea buke
ki ai ‘ae hou'eiki ‘o nau lea manukiage, “ Ta, ‘abe,
‘oku kui mo kimautolu, foki, o ! ” bea tafokiage leva
‘a Jisu, ‘o ne fai ‘ene Fakatata ki he Loto‘d-sibi, ke
fakamo‘oni ki he‘enau kui.
Koe me‘a koia kuo nau maheni ai kotoabe, moe
tuku ai ‘ae faga sibi ‘i he bo'uli, kae toki ha‘u ‘ae
tauhi ofi ki he ‘aho, ‘o ui a‘ene faga sibi, ‘o ne taki
kinautolu ki ha botu ‘itua‘a ke nau ma‘u me‘a lelei.
Koe Jiaji faka-Jiu ‘ae loto’a koia, ‘o hageko ‘enau fa‘a
lau ; bea, ka ne nau ‘a, kuo nau ‘ilo ia ko honau tauhi,
bea kuo nau agimui ki ai ‘o fai ki he‘ene taki. Bea,
hage aibe koe fa‘a fai ‘a Jisu, na‘e ‘ikai ke gata ‘ene
lea ‘i he me‘a na‘e tubu ai, kae ‘alu atu ki he g. me‘a
ta'egata. Koia na‘e hulu ‘ene talanoa ‘o kau ki he g.
me‘a na‘e teu hoko ; ne ogo koe faga ulofi kinautolu,
kae ‘ikai te ne kalo, ka te ne tuku ‘ene mo‘ui koe‘uhi
koe faga sibi. ‘Oiau, kohai ‘oku ‘ikai ke faka'amu
ke fanogo mai ki he‘ene ‘ai ‘ae lea koia, “ Koau koe
Tauhi Lelei,” mo ‘ene ‘alu ke kumi ‘ene faga sibi ‘i he


botu kehekehe, bea moe ‘ikai te nau toe hu ki ha
loto‘a, ka nau kaikai atu aibe ‘i he me‘a fo‘ou, ‘o nau
rna‘u ha mo‘ui ‘oku lahi ‘aubito. Xe ! ine‘i liliu ‘ae
loto ‘oe ni‘ihi ‘i hono g. fili ‘i he'enau fauogo ki he g.
lea behe. Ko hono fakaofo koe ‘ikai te nau tafoki ai
kotoabe, ‘0 ha‘u mei he fakabo'uli ki he mama.
('Oku kei toe be.)


KOE YAHE VIII.
KOE KITE O'ENE BEKIA (AIBE).
Koe Mavae mo Kaleli, moe Fonoga Lahi.
Hili ‘ae Katoaga Fale-lou‘akau, na‘e foki ‘a Jisu ki
Kaleli; ka na‘e ‘ikai ke ne nofo ai, ka koe‘uhi ke ne
mavae moe feitu'u koia, he kuo ‘oji ‘ene gaue, bea
ko ‘ene bekia e ‘oku tu'unuku mai. Bea, lolotoga
‘ene ‘i ai, na‘a ne ma‘u ‘ae fakatiita o'ene bekia, he
na‘e ogoogoage kuo feligiaki ‘i he Temibale ‘ae toto
‘oe feilaulau bea moe toto ‘o ha kau jiana faka-
maveuveu; ‘o hage tofu be ‘ene ‘amanaki tautau ‘i
he kolosi ‘i he vaha‘a ‘oe ogo kaiha'a. ‘Oku ha mei
he me‘a koia ‘ae aga ‘oe kuoga na‘a nau ‘i ai. Kuo
mafana ‘ae loto ‘ae kakai ‘i he'enau ‘amanaki ki he
Misaia, bea na‘e ‘ikai malomi kinautolu ‘i he‘enau
‘alu ki he g. botu tabu ‘o honau fonua; bea, ‘i he
manavahe ‘ae Kovana na‘a hoko ha maveuveu, na‘a
ne kouna atu, tokua, ‘ene kakai ke hu moe g. hele
fufu ki he g. katoaga fakalotu, ‘o te‘ia ‘ae kakai na‘e
‘iloga. Ka‘e vavana ‘ae loto ‘oe kakai ‘i he'enau
mamata ki he tafe atu ‘ae toto fakataha moe toto ‘oe
feilaulau, bea nau behe, tokaage ha fu‘u agahala kuo
fai ‘e he kakai na, ‘aia kuo nau iku ai ki ha me‘a


faka'ulia behe. Koe gaiie ‘e taha'na'e ‘i mamani
ai ‘a Jisu ke fakatonutonu ‘ae g. fakakaukau ‘ae
kakai : bea, ne ogo na‘a ne mo‘ua, ka na‘a ne sivi ‘ae
lau koia ; ‘o ne tala, ke ‘oua te nau fua'aki ‘ae lelei
‘oe tagata ‘ae g. me‘a ‘oku boko kiate ia ; he koe
ni‘ihi ‘oku to vave ki ai ‘ae nunu'a o‘enau kovi, ka
koe ni‘ihi ‘oku fakatotoka ; bea ne ogo ‘enau vavana
‘i he bekia behe ‘ae kau Kaleli, ka ‘e vavana behe
mo mamani ‘i ha‘anau bekia behe ‘anautolu, o kabau
‘e ‘ikai te nau liiiu. Bea ne ‘ai atu foki ‘ae Fakatata
‘oe Filei Ta‘efua ke mahino ‘e vave hono ta.
Koe ‘alu koeni ‘a Jisu na‘e ‘ikai hage ko ‘ene.fa‘a
fai. ‘Oku tau ‘ilo ko ‘ene aga ke faka‘ehi‘ehi mei
he ogoogo moe e‘a, ka koe taimi ni na‘e ‘ikai te ne
kei fufu hono tu‘uga. Na‘a ne tuku atu ha toko
fitugofulu ke fakamelomelo kiate ia, bea ne fonoga
mo ha fu‘u toko lahi ‘o tau mo ha Balofita ‘o Kaleli, moe
Hako ‘o Tevita. Ka na‘e ‘ikai lelei ‘ene mavae mo
Kaleli. Mo'oni ‘oku bikitai kiate ia ha ni‘ihi, ka
kuo li‘aki ia ‘e he fonua kotoa. Bea, ‘i he'ene vakai
holo ‘ae g. fonua kuo ne gaiie lahi ki ai, na‘a ne
‘oiaue ‘i he kui honau loto moe fefeka honau aga.
Ko Nasaleti e na‘a ne tubu ai; ko Kabaneume na‘e
tu‘u ai hono nofo'aga—kuo na fakatou fakataleh ‘ae
monu'ia na‘a ne tala humaki ki ai. Koeha ha nie‘a
‘oku toe ki he g. feitu‘u behe, ka koe mala‘ia ‘o
taegata 1 Bea ko ‘ene “ ‘Oiaue Kolesini! ‘Oiaue
Betesaita ! ” ‘oku kei ogo mai ki he muiva'e ‘o taimi,
koe tuhu ki ha mala kuo bau. Na‘e ‘ahi‘ahi
mo hono tu‘i ke fakavave ‘ene ‘alu, kae ‘ikai toka‘i
‘e Jisu ‘one fakamana, ka ne fekau ke nau foki ‘o
tala ki he “ Fokisi ” koia, te ne toki ‘alu ‘oka boko
‘ae taimi kuo ne tu‘utu‘uni ki ai.


Koia ‘oku tau behe na‘e mavae kovi ‘a Jisu mo
Kaleli. Ka na‘e ‘ikai ko ‘ene aga ke mamahi fuoloa,
bea na‘e toeji'i bea ne fakafiefia ‘i he'ene vakai ha
ni'ihi kuo tui mo‘oni kiate ia. Bea ne fai atu. Ka
na‘e toe ta‘ofi leva ‘i he agakovi ‘ae kau Samelia, ‘aia
na‘e ‘ikai te nau fie tali ia ekinautolu, be tuku ‘ene
Kau Ako ke feimea‘aki ‘i honau kolo. Koe bau‘u lahi
ia, bea na‘e loto ‘a Semisi mo Jione ke tubutubu-
lefanua ke to mai ha ‘afi mei he lagi ki ai, ‘o hage
koe fai ‘a Ilaijia ki he kau Samelia ‘i mu‘a. Kae
ta‘ofi ‘e Jisu, ‘o ne tali agavaivai ‘enau teke‘i ia, ‘o
ne fou ‘i he hala-lalo. Ta, kuo faka‘au ke bito ‘ene
ibu ‘i he mamahi. Ko Samelia ‘eni kuo kabuji ia ;
koe botu fe, nai, te ne ma‘u ai ji‘a fiemalie ? Ka na‘e
‘ikai te ne tu'enia ‘enau kovi, bea, ‘i he ha‘u ha kau
kilia, na‘a ne fakamo'ui honau kotoa, koe toko hogo-
fulu, bea ne faka‘ali‘ali ki mamani ‘ae lelei ‘ae toko
taha na‘e foki ke fakafeta‘i, ne ogo koe Samelia ia.
Bea koe toki me‘a ‘oku ha lahi ai ‘ae agalelei ‘a Jisu
‘etau manatu na‘e fe‘uga moe taimi koia a‘ene fai
‘ae Pakatata ‘oe Samaletani Lelei, ‘aia koe kauga‘abi
‘ofa mo'oni na‘a ne faito'o ‘ae lavea mo fakaai ‘ae
majiva ‘oe tagata kuo mo‘ua ‘i he kaiha‘akau, bea
kuo li'ekina ‘e hono kakai o‘ona. Bea ko loto ke filiage
‘e he ‘Eiki ha fonua age ke tuku ki ai ‘ae tagata lelei
koia ; kae fakakuikui ‘a Jisu ki he kovi kuo toki fai
kiate ia, ‘o ne behe koe Samelia ia. Hono ‘ikai koe
toki taubotu eni ‘i he kataki ?
‘Oku hage na‘e foki leva ‘ae Kau Fitugofulu ‘i he
mahino ‘e ‘ikai fai atu ‘a Jisu ‘i he halakuo ne tu‘utu-
‘uni. Kuo nau ‘alu ki he botu kotoabe (he na‘e ‘ikai
tabu ‘enau o ki he Senitaile ‘o hage koe Kau Abose-
tolo) ; ka ne ogo ha botu te nau i ai, ka kuo 0 mo


kinautolu ‘ae ivi ‘o Jisu, ‘o tulaki mo kabuji ‘ae kovi
kotoabemei he jino ‘oe kakai. Kae‘uma‘a, ‘i he ‘omi
‘e he ni'ihi honau kaiga kuo ‘avea, na‘a nau loto lahi
ke ‘ahi'ahi ke kabuji, ne ogo na‘e ‘ikai hanau fekau
behe meia Jisu. Bea tali ‘eia ‘enau tui, bea na‘e
mahu‘i ‘ae kau tevolo ‘i he‘enau lea. Koe ‘aoga
‘oe me‘a koia kiate kinautolu koe o‘o ki honau loto
‘ae nima loloa ‘a Jisu.
Koe aga ‘oe ‘Otua, ka tu'unuku mai ha kovi ki
hono kakai ‘oku ne taka ofi kiate kinautolu ‘o fa‘a
hifo tokoni. Koia koe ‘aho ‘e taha, ‘i he fai ‘e Jisu
‘enau lotu, na‘e to hafu'u tabuaki fakamanavahe, bea
malama ‘ene fofoga he‘ene kelesi'ia. Bea jio ki ai
‘ae Kau Ako, ‘o nau faka‘amu ke nau lava ha lotu ‘oku
vave behe hono tali. He koe aga ‘oe kuoga mu‘a,
na‘a nau mahalo ‘oku ai ‘ae g. lea ‘oku ogo ki he
Ta'ehamai, bea talagofua ki ai ‘ae g. fa‘ahikehe, ‘o
hage koe “ tubutubulefanua ”‘i Toga. Ka, ‘i he nofo
‘e he ‘Eiki ke fai ki he‘enau kole, ta, ko ‘ene motu‘a
lotu be na‘a ne a‘au mai, ‘aia “ Ko ‘Emau Tamai <kc.,”
bea ne toki malaga kiate kinautolu ke nau ‘ilo koe
aga ‘oe hu ‘oku ‘ikai ke tu‘u ‘i he lea, ka ‘i he aga ‘oe
lotomoe fakamatoato hono fai.
Ne ogo ‘ae ‘ita ‘ae hou'eiki Jiu kiate ia mo ‘enau
hifo ia mei he falelotu, ka na‘e ‘ikai mamafa ‘enau
bule ki he falelotu kotoabe. Bea koia, ‘i he‘ene fonoga
‘oku fai, na‘a ne fa‘a ‘alu ki he falelotu ‘0 fai ‘enau
ako. Bea tala'ehai na‘a ne fa‘a tuku ke ikuna ia ‘e he
kovi ‘oe hou'eiki; ka na‘a ne fai aibe ‘ene g. gaue
‘ofa ‘i he ‘aho Sabate. Koe Sabate ‘e taha na‘a ne
fakamo'ui ‘ae feline na‘e bikoua fuoloa ; bea koe Sabate
‘e taha na‘a ne fakamo'ui ‘ae tagata na‘e mahaki fatu.
Koe me‘a ki he tagata koia ‘oku matamata na‘e gaue


‘aki ia ke tauheloli ‘ae ‘Eiki. Kuo ‘oji ‘ene malaga ‘i
he falelotu bea kuo ne ha'ele ki he fakaafe, bea, ta, na‘e
fokotu'u ‘ae tagata mahamahaki fe'uga moia, ko ‘enau
‘ilo ‘e gaiie ‘ae fatu ‘o Jisu ke fakamo‘ui ia. Ka na‘e
fai; bea to moia honau akonaki na‘e ‘ikai te nau lava
ke tali.
‘Oku ha koe fakaafe koia ‘ae ‘eiki Ealesi na‘e ‘ikai
fai koe ‘ofa, kakoe'uhi, nai, ko hono tu'uga, he koe ‘alu
ta'etokoni ha Labai hage ko Jisu koe me‘a fakama ki he
kolo. Bea, ‘i he bau leva ke ne fakaafe, hage na‘a ne fa’
ha fu‘u me‘a lahi ke ne ogoogoa ai. Koiana'e teu ha
fu‘u tina ‘i lie efiafi,‘aia na‘egofuahe na‘e ‘oji ‘ae tabu ‘i
he to ‘aela‘a. Koe katoaga fakalotu ia ; bea, ka ne fai
‘i hono aga tonu, ‘o tanaki ‘aa kakai kehekehe ke ma-
laga ki ai ‘a Jisu, ‘e nifi ‘ae fiefia ‘ae ‘Eiki. Ka na‘a ne
vakai, ‘oku tala be ‘ae kai ki he kaiga mo ha‘a ma‘oluga,
ka koe fa'ahiga na‘a ne ha‘u tonu ki ai, ‘ae agahala moe
lauvale, na‘e ikai ha taha ‘i ai. Koia na‘a ne lea ai
ki ai ‘o tala ke ‘oua te ne filifilimanako ‘i he lotu, be
gaiie ki ho'ota. Na‘e fohi‘a, foki, hono finagalo ki
he aga ‘oe kakai na'e ha‘u ki he Katoaga, ‘enau
‘afugi mo kakaba mo fieme'a. Koe aga ‘oe nofo ‘i he
taimi koia na‘e taki sofa ‘e tolu ‘ae tebile, bea taki
toko tolu ki he sofa; bea koe sofa loto na‘e lau koe
nofo mu‘a, kae‘uma‘a ‘ae nofo loto ‘i ai; bea koe
taufa'ao ‘oe g. nofo koia ‘e he kakai koe me‘a
fakalielia. Na‘e fehi‘a ‘ae ‘Eiki ki ai, ‘o ne valoki
kinautolu ‘i he‘enau fai ta'etau behe. Ko hono
fakaofo he na‘a ne tu‘uga ‘ene eginaki koia ki hono
‘aoga ‘oe fai behe, ‘o ‘ikai ki hono totonu, ‘o hage
koe fai ki he tamaiki, be ki ha kakai ‘oku ‘ikai
ogo ki ai ‘ae totonu. Ka nae fai; ke koe kau Palesi
koia koe fa‘ahiga teba, ko honau mata ‘e taha na'e jio


Id he lagi, bea koe taha ki mamani. Na‘a nau biki
ki he lotu ko ‘enau ma‘u koloa ai, bea na ! a nau le'ei mo
biko'i ‘ae g. tu‘utu‘uni ‘oe lotu koe'uhi ke lava ai
‘enau ma'ume'a. Ko hono ‘uhiga ia na‘e fa‘a lau
‘aoga ai ‘e he ‘Eiki ‘o ‘ikai lau totonu, hei'ilo 'e
ue‘i ai ha ni'ihi ke kumi ki he Bule'aga ‘oe Lagi.
‘Oku ha ‘ae kovi o'enau aga ‘i he'ene ‘ai atu ‘ao
Fakatata ‘oe Matabule TauhiJcoloa Kdlcd. Koe
Fakatata koia ‘oku ofo ai ‘ae toko lahi, ‘o nau meimei
lau na‘e ta‘etau mo Jisu ke ‘ai ; he ko hono ki'i lelei
‘oku taha, koe ‘ilo ‘e he matabule ‘oku tu'unuku
mai ‘ae kovi, ‘o ne gaue kei ‘i kaba ke hao. ‘Aua;
na‘e tae'aoga ‘ae lau totonu ki he Falesi; ka ko loto
ke nau ‘ilo ki he houhau ‘oku tu'unuku mai ‘o nau
hola.
Kuo loa ‘ene mahino ki he ‘Eiki, ‘e ‘ikai ha‘ane
‘aoga ki he Falesi. Ne ogoko ‘ene ha‘u mei Lagi moe
fugani lotu kuo mamata ki ai a mamani, kae ‘ikai te
nau manako ai. ‘Oku hage koe ta ‘o ha hiva malie ki ha
manu ‘oku ‘ikai hano teliga. Bea ne‘ine‘i tafoki ia ki ha
fa‘ahiga ‘e taha, ‘aia na‘a nau tuliimui kiateia, ‘o tali
‘ene g. lea, ‘Oku mo‘oni koe fa‘ahiga ta‘etoka‘i, bea lahi
‘enau kovi, ka na‘e ai hanau ‘uluga‘aga lelei, bea na‘e
fa‘a tala ‘e Jisu ki he kau Falesi, ‘e mn'omu'a ‘aekau
agahala ni iate kinautola. Ijolotoga ‘ae tina kuo tau
lea ki ai, kuo ne lea Fakatata ki ai, ‘o fakatatau ‘ae
Bule'aga ‘o Lagi ki ha fu‘u katoaga lahi mo malie,
‘aia ‘e ‘ikai ma‘u ‘e ha hou'eiki ko ‘enau ma'ama'a ki
ai, ka ‘e to koe ‘inaji ‘oe kakai majiva mo henoa.
Bea ‘ajili ‘ae nofo kiate ia ‘ae kau agahala, kae-
‘uma'a ‘ae fa'ahiga kotoabe na‘e ta‘etoka‘i ‘o hage koe
Bobilikane. Bea ‘amujia kinautolu ‘enau kai ma'aga
gako, he koe taimi ia na‘a ne ‘abac g. Fakatata malie


taha, koe Sibi na‘e He, koe Ba‘aga na‘e Mole, moe
Folia Maimauholoa. Bea, ‘i he faifai bea e‘a kiate
kinautolu hono ‘uhiga ‘oe ‘u Fakatata koia, ‘ae behe
‘oku mo‘ua ‘ae Tolu Tabu ‘i he kumi kinautolu ; bea
*oku talitali mai ‘ae bulubulu fugani lelei moe manu
tali-‘eiki ma'anautolu, bea nifi koa ‘enau fiefia ? ‘Oiau
hono ‘ikai tu'utai ‘ae gaue ‘a Jisu : ‘ene faka‘atu‘i ji‘i
ta'aliekina mo fafaga'aki ‘ae g. me‘a molu behe ; kae
‘atu me‘a fefeka ki he kau Falesi, ‘o hage koe Fakatata
kia Taivasi holi tae'aoga, moe Falesi ‘afugi na‘e lotu
ta'etali, kae fakakoloa ‘ae Bobilikane. Ke‘ine‘i behe
‘enau lau, kuo te‘eki ha taha ‘e lea hage koe tagata ni.
Bea ke tau manatu, na‘e fai kotoabe ‘oku kite ‘ae
Kolosi. Kane ko koe moau, behe kuo ta ‘oho ; he
koe aga ia ‘oe kakai kuo nau ogo'i kuo bau ‘enau mo-
'ui. Kae fai atu be ‘e Jisu ‘o hage ‘oku ‘ikai ha me‘a,
‘o tuha aibe ‘ene lea moe fa'ahiga ‘oku fai ki ai. ‘Io
ne ogo na‘e hage ha hu‘a-vai momoko ‘ae toka ‘ae
loto ‘oe toko lahi kiate ia, ka na‘a ne ‘ilo ‘e ‘ikai te
nau fe‘uga moe fu‘u faigata'a ‘oku ene ke hoko ; bea
‘e lelei mu‘a ‘enau mahu‘i kei mama'o. Koia na‘a ne
tala ki hono lahi ke nau sivi kinautolu, be te nau
lava ke kataki ‘ae g. ko ri ‘oku bau ke hoko ; bea ka
‘ikai ke nau nofo. Ka na‘e ta‘e‘aoga; bea na‘e
fakatokolahi aibe ‘ae kakai na‘a nau fonoga. Bea
na‘a moe kau Falesi na‘a nau kamata mahalo na‘a ‘oku
teu ke fai ha me‘a, ‘o nau ‘eke kiate ia be hoko
fakaku ‘ae Bule'aga ‘oe Lagi. Bea toki ‘ai mai ‘e Jisu
‘ae fo‘i akonaki koia, ‘aia koe alifa moe omeka ‘oe
hisitolia, koe behe ‘oku ‘ikai ha fakaku be ha ‘ife ; ka
ka ‘iloga habotu be ha taimi kuo fakaka'aga ai ‘e ha
kakai a‘enau lelei, ‘e hoko ai ‘ae fie gaue ‘a Lagi ko
tamate'i ‘ae kovi mo fokotu'u fo‘ou ‘ae lelei.


‘Oku ‘ikai te te toe ‘ilo ha taimi ‘oku ha haohaoa
‘ai ‘a Jisu hage koe fonoga ni. ‘Oku tau ‘ilo na‘a ne
haohaoa aibe ; ka, na‘a moia, na‘a ne tubu ‘i he kelesi:
bea, ‘i he fonoga koia, ‘oku hage ‘oku tau jio ki ha
fakakakato ‘o hono ivi ‘oku keheage. Ne ogo hono
ta‘omia ‘i he g. kavega, kae ‘ikai kulukia ; ne ogo na‘e
ue‘i malohi mei he botu kotoabe, kae ‘ikai gaue ; ka
na‘a ne ha‘ele tebitebiatn ‘i he g. viliji ‘o ‘ikai ‘oho
be fai tuai, ‘o ne tufa tatau be ‘ae g. tabuaki fakalagi
ki he kakai fulibe.
Bea hono ‘ikai malie ‘ae me‘a ‘oku faka‘oji‘aki ‘ae
talanoa ki he fonoga koia ! Tokua, kuo ne a‘u ki Olive,
bea kuo ne ‘alu ke malold ji‘i ‘i he fale koia ‘i Betani,
‘aia ko hono hufaga ‘i mamani. Na‘a nau ‘ofa koto-
abe kiate ia, ‘a Ma‘ata mo Mele mo Lasalosi, ka koe
‘ofa ‘a Mele na‘e lolotoage; bea koe aga aibe ‘oe
‘ofa behe ‘oku ne vavaga ki he me‘a ‘oku ‘i he
loto ‘oe ‘ofa'aga. Bea ha leva Ida Mele ‘oku lahi ‘ae
me‘a ‘oku fie talanoa ki ai ‘a Jisu ; koia na‘a ne faite
atu ‘i hono va‘e ‘o ne fakanoga hono loto mo fakale-
lulelu hono g. mamahi ‘i he'ene fakaai ‘ene fie talanoa.
Lolotoga ia, ‘oku haka fano ‘ae ta'okete, ko Ma‘ata, ‘i
he ta‘o keke moe gaohi faikakai, ‘o ne lau he iaki ki he
nofo mo ‘ene tae'ofa ki he ‘Eiki, ‘o ‘ikai fie ala he
gaohi o'ene me‘a tokoni. Eaifai bea ne lea tonu mai
ki ai, ‘o ne meimei gaohi ‘ae ‘Eiki ‘i he‘ene tae'ofa.
Toki haga hake ai ‘a Jisu ‘o tali : ka ko ha tali be ko
ha tali! tala'ehai ‘oku ne fie tautea ‘a Ma'ata, he ko
ji'ene ‘ofa aibe, ka koe ‘ofa ‘a Mele ‘oku fugani; bea
kuo bau ke ne taukabod —‘E, koe botu koia koe koga
‘o Iteni, bea, ka ne lava ke behe ‘ae g. famili ‘o mamani,
kuo kamata ‘a Lagi ‘i heni.


KOE YAHE IX.
KOE KITE O'EHE BEKIA (AIBE.)
Koe Ogo Betani.
Kuo hoko eni ‘ae mahina faka'oji ‘oe ta‘u ko hono
29 T. J. Bea ‘alu ‘a Jisu ki Selusalema ke kau ‘i he
Katoaga na‘e fai ia. Na‘e ui koe Katoaga ‘oe Hufi
Fo‘ou, he koe fakamanatu ki he toe fai lotu ki he
Temibale hili hono tabuni fuoloa ‘e Aniteoko
Ebifana. Koe fa‘ahita‘u momoko, bea koia na‘e ha‘ele
‘a Jisu ‘i he falehala ‘o Solomone, ko ‘ene mafana,
nai, he na‘e haga ki hahake. Kuo bau na‘e mo‘ua
hono loto ‘i he me‘a na‘e tefito ki ai ‘ae Katoaga, mo
ne fakamanatu hake ‘ae tu'utai ‘ae fu‘u helo ne ne
matetiki ‘ae kakai, ‘o fakatau‘ataina mei he nofo
hoboate ki he Tui Silia—‘a Jiutasi Mitknhaeo.
Hei‘ilo be na‘e ai mo ha taha ‘i he kau to‘a ‘o
ono'aho ‘e fiemalie behe ‘ae fmagalo ‘o Jisu ‘i he
manatu ki ai ‘o hage ko Jiutasi, he koe toko
taha koia na‘a ne fakaai kotoa ‘ae g. tu‘utu‘uni ‘ae
‘Eiki ki he Tu‘i, ‘i he ma'a o‘ene mo‘ui, mo ‘ene
falala aibe ki he ‘Eiki, mo tauhi ke haohaca ‘ene g.
fekau. Ka kuo bau na‘e iiofio mamahi, foki, ‘ae
manatu ‘a Jisu ki ai, he, ne ogo na‘a ne tatau mo
Jiutasi ‘i he fie lagomekina ‘ae fonua mo fakama‘a ‘ae
loto, ka ko Jiutasi na‘a ne lava, bea toka taha ‘ae


fonua kiate ia ; ka koe me'a kiate ia, kuo Icahuji ia
‘i he g. feitu'u, bea ‘oku toeji'i ke fulitu'a kiate ia ‘e
he fonua kotoa. Bea koia, na‘e toe mole ‘ae mafana
mei hono loto, ‘o ne ha‘cle fakamamahu'i be.
Na‘e belie, nai, moe hou‘eiki Jiu. Kuo bau na‘a
nan mafana ‘i he kamata'aga ‘oe Katoaga ‘i he
manatu he : enau mamata ki he g. ba na‘e tautau ‘i he
mata-Temibale, koe fakamanatu ki he g. tail na‘e fai,
kae'uma'a ‘ae g. kalauni koula na‘e tau ai, koe
faka‘iloga ‘oe lagilagi kuo ma‘u ‘e he kau to‘a na‘a
nau tau ma‘a honau fonua ; bea, ‘i he'enau lau ki he
g. gaue fakaofo ‘ae kau mafi koia, na‘e fakautuutu
‘enau fiefia ‘o nau haga atu ki he g. me'a lalahi'age
ka fai ‘e he Misaia. Bea, ‘i he'enau ‘alu behe mo
lau, ‘iloage, na‘a nau vakai kia Jisu bea nau toe
momoko, he kuo tala mai, koe Misaia e; bea ‘oku
mo‘oni kuo lahi ‘ene me'a fakaofo kuo fai, kae
tala'ehai ‘oku ne momo'i hage ko Makabaeo, ‘o gali
ke taki ha tau ke fai mo Loma. ‘lloage, na‘a nau
behe ke ‘eke malohi kiate ia be koeha ‘ana ‘oku
‘amanaki. Koia na‘a nau kabui ia, ‘o nau tala ke ne
lea fakabatonu mai be koe Misaia ia, koe'uhi ke nau
teuteu ki he gaue te ne fai.
Koe me'a koia ‘oku ha ai ae lotoma'u ‘a Jisu, mo
‘ene ‘ilo maraa'o. Kane ko ha ni'ihi, kuo nau tali
leva ‘ae o‘i kuo fai, bea kuo nofo ke fai ‘ae gaue
faka-Misaia. Bea koe toki taimi tu'umalie ki ai, he
kuo mafana ‘ae loto ‘oe kakai ‘i he lau ‘ae g. tau
fakaofo a'enau g. kui. Bea, ka ne tu‘u mai ‘a Jisu
‘o o‘i ‘ae tau mo Loma, ne ‘ikai ha taha ‘e nofo, bea
kuo bau ne matafi atu ‘a Loma ki tahi. Kane ogo
ia, koeha hono ‘aoga, he koe koto kovi ‘ae kakai,
tatau ‘ae houeiki moe me‘avale 1 ISTa'e gutuhuaage


‘ae nofo, koe lolomi ‘e he muli ; bea, ka ki‘i avaage,
na‘e fekainaki ‘ae g. fa'ahiga, bea obeobe i he fonua
‘ae fakamalohi moe fakalielia. Koia, na‘e tala ‘e
Jisu, koe‘uma‘a ‘enau fehi'a ki hono tu‘uga, he kuo
loa ‘ene mahino, ka koe kovi koe ‘ikai te nau fai ki
he‘ene agi. ‘Oku mo'oni ‘oku fai kehe ‘ene agi mo
hono loto, ka koe me‘a kuo bau ke nau ma‘u mo‘ui
ai, ‘o ‘ikai koe mo'ui ni be, ka koe Mo'ui Ta‘egata
fold, he ‘oku ne mafai ki he Ta'ehamai ‘o hage ko
‘ene Tamai.
Bea laga'i ai leva ‘enau ‘ita, ‘i he lea fie'otua koia,
‘o nau holi ke tamate'i ia. Bea, ko hono kovi, na‘e
tu‘u ofi mai hono lava'aga, he ko hono tautea totonu
koe tolomaka'i, bea na‘e tu‘utu‘uholo ae g. fokotu‘uga
maka, ‘aia na‘e fai'aki ‘ae gaohi ‘oe Temibale, Koia
na‘a nau ‘oho leva ki ai ‘o ene ke tologi. Kae ‘ikai
momo'i gaiie ‘a Jisu, ka ne lea fakahobohobokubu
mai ‘o fehu'i, “ Koefe ha‘aku gaue lelei ‘oku mou fai
ke tologi ai au? Bea na‘a nau ma ai, ‘o taki taha
tuku hifo ‘ene maka ; he na‘a nau manatu ki he toko
lahi kuo ne fakamo'ui, ka nau mamahi, foki, he koeha
kuo ne ui ia koe ‘Otua. Bea tali leva ‘e Jisu,
“ Seuke ! na‘a mo Tevita na‘a ne ui behe ha ni'ihi ‘i
he hou'eiki; bea oku kovi fefe ha‘aku ui au koe Poha
‘oe ‘Otua, ‘oji ‘oku ou fai ‘ae g. gaue ‘oku tau moia 1 ”
Bea toe tubu ‘enau ‘ita, ‘o nau fai ke buke ia, ka ka
moulu atu be ia ‘o ‘ikai ma‘u ha‘anau ala ; hei'ilo be
koe teke'i ‘e hono ‘otua, be ko ‘enau malu‘ia. Ka
na'e tatau aibe, he na‘e hage koe kabuji mei he
fonua. Bea na'e hiki ‘a Jisu ki he botu be taha
na'e kei toe kiate ia, ‘a Tu‘a Jioatani, ‘o ne nofo ‘i
he feitu'u na‘a ne kamata ai ‘ene gaue, ‘a Betani-‘i-
Kauvai


Kane koe tagata be ‘a Jisu, te tau ‘ilo ki he aga
‘o hono loto ‘i he'ene ‘alu koia ki Betani. Kuo bau
te ne manatu ki he'ene fuofua nofo ai. “Koe botu
e na'aku kamata ai ‘eku gaue. Koe botu koe,
na‘aku ma‘u ai ‘eku ‘uluaki akoga. Koe botu koeni,
na‘e fakaha'i au ki mamani koe Lami ‘ae Otua ; bea,
‘i he'eku alu atu ke malaga, na‘aku ‘amanaki ‘e ‘ilo
leva ‘e he kakai ko honau Misaia au. Ka kuou foli
eni ‘ae fonua ‘o tu‘o lahi, ‘o malaga mo fai mana; bea
kohai kuo tui kiate au ? Kuo fulitu'a ‘a Samelia mo
Kaleli, mo Selusalema foki, bea koe falukuga kakai
ni be kuo biki kiate au—‘ae Kau Abosetolo ; bea, na‘a
mo kinautolu, ko honau toko taha ‘oku tali faigamalie
ke lavald'i au, bea ‘oku gali feia au ‘o hage ko ha
lami.”
Kane koe tagata be, ‘e fou behe, nai, ‘ae faka-
kaukau ‘a Jisu, ka ‘oku ‘ikai te tau ‘ilo ki he tokoni
‘a hono ‘otua ‘o fakalelulelu ki he'ene mamabi, ka
‘oku fakaofo kiate kitautolu ‘ene foki behe ‘i he ‘oji
‘ene gaue ki he botu na‘a ne kamata ke fai,
kae‘uma‘a ‘ene ‘alu ki he botu na‘e tuhu‘i ai ia koe
Lami ‘i he'ene ogo'i kuo ‘ofi hono feia. Koe uluga-
‘aga fakatagata ia, bea kuo toko lahi ‘ae kau ogoogo
kuo fai behe. Bea, ne ogo na‘a ne mamahi ‘i he'ene
manatu ki he taimi kuo hili, mo mafajia ‘i he manatu
ki he kaha'u—‘ene bekia ‘oku tu'unuku mai, ka na‘e
‘ikai ke lofajia hono loto. Bea na‘e malohi ‘ene g.
malaga moe g. mana na‘a ne fai, bea ofo ‘ae kakai,
‘o nau tuku ki mu‘a noabe ia ia Jiono, ‘ae balofita
na‘a nau fa‘a viki.
Ka tala'ehai na‘e tuku ‘e hono g. fili ke ne ata
fuoloa, bea, koe ‘aho ‘e taha, na‘e laga ha'anau
malumu kiate ia. Koe me‘a gali boto ‘ae ta na‘a


nau ten ke fai kiate ia. Na‘e tu‘utu‘uni ‘e Mosese,
‘oku gofua ki he tagata ke veto mei hono uaifi ‘o
kabau ‘oku ne ‘ilo ha kovi iate ia. Hei‘ilo be koeha
hono tonu ‘oe me'a na‘e jio ki ai ‘a Mosese ‘i he tu-
‘utu'uni koia, ka ‘oku matamata koe lau ki he g.
me‘a ‘oku ta‘ofi ai ‘ac nonofo ‘a ha ogo me‘a. Ka, ‘i
hono kofukofu behe ‘o lea fakaji‘iji‘i be, koia kuo
taki ‘e he kau Labaia ‘e fakagofua ki he me‘a kotoabe.
Ke ogo be koeha ha me‘a ji‘i kuo kovi'ia ai ‘ae
tagata ki hono unoho, ka na‘e gofua be ke ne nofo
hifo ‘o fai ha vete, ‘o kabuji mei hono fale ; bea na‘e
vete ha ni'ihi, tokua, koe ‘ikai te nau gaohi lelei ‘ae
kai, moe ni‘ihi koe'uhi kuo tokaga ‘e honau huse-
baniti ki ha fefine kehe. Ka na‘e ‘ikai behe ‘ae kau
Labai kotoa. Koe taimi koia na‘e ua ‘ae Koliji
lalahi, ‘ae Koliji ‘a Hileli moe Koliji ‘a Samai. Bea
ko kinautolu na‘e ako ia Hileli na‘a nau vete ‘i he
me'a kotoabe, ‘o hage koia kuo tau lau; ka ko
kinautolu na‘a ako ia Samai na‘a nau behe, ‘oku ‘ikai
totonu ke vete, ka ‘i he faikovi be. Koia na‘e faka-
kaukau ‘e he g. fili ‘o Jisu ke fehu‘i kiate ia be
koeha ‘ae totonu ‘oe me‘a ; he ne ogo be koeha ‘ene
tali, kuo ban te ne febaki ai moe fa'ahi ‘e taha, kae-
‘uma‘a, kabau to ne lau moe kau Samai, ‘oku tabu
‘ae vete noa, ‘oku galigali ‘ita ai ‘ae Tu‘i ‘oe fonua,
ko Helota, bea hei‘ilo te ne tamate‘i ia ‘o hage ko
‘ene fai Ida Jione.
Hono ‘ikai mo‘oni ‘ae lau ki he gaue'aki ‘e he ‘Eiki
‘ae ‘ita ‘ae tagata ! He na'e behe ‘ae tali ‘a Jisu,
koia na‘e liliu ai ‘enau kaka koe fugani ‘oe me'a ‘aoga
ki mamani katoa. Na'e fakaha ‘e Jisu ‘ae aga
totonu ‘oe mali, koe nonofo ‘ae tokoua, ‘aia ‘oku
totonu ke na matu'aki taha, ‘o hage ‘oku ‘ikai te na


kei toko ua; bea ‘e ‘ikai ha me‘a ‘e vote kinaua ka
koe faikovi be. Kae‘uma‘a ua‘a ne fakaha, ‘oku
‘ikai ha leleiage ‘i he nofo taka be, ka koe me‘a ‘oku
hoho'ia ai ‘ae finagalo ‘oe ‘Eiki ko ‘enau nofo faka-
famili, ‘o meimei ko hono katoa. Kohai ‘e fa‘a
fakamatala ki he fiefia ‘ae kau fefine ‘i he‘enau
fanogo ki he g. lea koia, he na‘e kovi ‘aubito honau
tu'uga ‘i he taimi koia! Na‘e lau kinautolu koe
me‘a ‘uli, bea koe nonofo ha tagata mo kinautolu koe
me‘a kataki be. Ka koeni ‘oku lau ‘e he Balifita
lahi ni koe hoa totonu kinautolu ‘oe tagata, moe
kakano taha, bea ko honau lakaga ‘i mamani koe
me‘a ma‘oni‘oniage fau, koe me‘a fakalagi. Ha‘e
hage kuo hiki ‘ae kavega kuo mafajia ai ‘enau mo‘ui,
bea, ‘i he ma‘ama‘a honau loto, na‘a nau lele ki ‘abi
‘o ‘orai ‘enau faga valevale ke ‘ala ki ‘a Jisu, ‘o nau
fakata‘emalu‘ia mai koe'uhi koe g. lea kuo nau toki
fanogo ki ai. Ka kuo te'eki ke o‘o ‘ae g. lea koia ‘i
he loto ‘oe kau Abosetolo, ‘o nau tu‘u hake ke teke'i,
he'enau lau na‘e ta'etau ‘ae ha‘u belie ha kau fefine
ki ha Labai ma‘oni‘oni hage ko Jisu —tuku kehe ‘ae
faga tamaiki na. Ka na‘e ha leva ‘ae mo‘oni ‘oe lea
‘a Jisu na‘e toki fai, ‘o ne fakalagilagi'i ‘ae nofo faka-
famili ‘i he‘ene ‘ai atu ‘ae folofola faka‘ofo‘ofa koia,
“ Tuku be ‘ae kau tamaiki ke nau ha‘u kiate au, ‘o
‘ouae ta‘ofi kinautolu, he ‘oku ma‘ae fa‘ahiga koia ‘ae
Bule'aga ‘oe ‘Otua.” Bea na‘a ne fakakakato ‘ene
gaue ‘i he‘ene habai ‘ae kau tamaiki, mo ‘ai hono
nima kiate kinautolu, mo fu‘u tabu‘ekina. Koe toki
‘aho ‘aoga ia ki mamani; bea, ‘i he'etau vakai ki he

Koe taimi koia, foki, na‘e hoko ai ‘ena talanoa moe
matabule talavou na‘e fie uku mama'o ‘i he lotu.
‘Oku lahi ‘ae g. akonaki ‘oku ha ai, ka koe me‘a ‘oku
tau tokagab koe e‘a ‘ae aga ‘o Jisu, ‘a ‘ene hu'ufa-
taha moe finagalo ‘oe Eiki. He ko ‘ene fanogo leva

kotoabe!
‘Oiaue, ‘ae loloto ‘oe Lotu kuo ne ha‘u ke fokotu'u !
Kuo ne fakaha ki he matabule talavou, ‘oku ‘i ai ha
mea lolotoage ‘i he lao, ‘aia koe ‘ofa lioa. Bea
fanogo ki ai ‘a Bita, bea ne behe leva kuo nau a'ujia
ia ‘e he Kau Abosetolo. Kae tala ‘e Jisu ke ‘oua te
nau falala ki ai, he na‘a moia ‘oku ai ha mu'omua mo
ha muimui; ‘o ne fai ha Fahatdtd ki he Uga Gaue lei
he Oomvaine, ke fakamahino koe fugani ‘oe me‘a lelei
‘ae ‘ofa lioa, ‘o kabau ko hono tefito koe ‘ofa; ka ‘o

hone mahubga. ‘Oiseukeseuke, hoto ofa ki he Kau
Abosetolo, ji'onau gaohi kuo fai! Lolotoga na‘a nau

Bule‘aga ‘oe Lagi, bea, ‘i he‘enau hu ki ai, ko ‘enau

‘ikai koe akonaki taubotu ia oe lotu faka-Kalaisi—‘ae

Na‘a nau taki taha hono ‘aoga. Ko Ma'ata na‘e

majiva koia. Ko Mele na‘e fakaai ‘ene g. holi

Semisi mo Jione na‘a nau taki fakakakano ‘ene g.
me‘a lahi. Koe Mele ni be na‘a na huafe'ilogaki moe
‘Eiki ‘i he g. me‘a mama‘o. Koia be na‘a ne ogona

ha sesele. ‘A, malo mo koe Mele ‘o Betani, ha‘o

a'utaki ho loto ke tali ‘ene g. folofola faigata'a !
Ka ‘oku te behe ko Lasalosi na‘e tokoni lahi ai hono
loto. He ‘oku ua ‘ae fa'ahiga ‘ofa ; koe ofa ‘oku tau
fai ki he toko lahi, tagata be fefine, bea moe ‘ofa ‘oku
tau fai ki he toko ji‘i. Fefe ke tau ui ia koe ofa
mafana P Bea koe ‘ofa ia na‘e ogo‘i ‘e Jisu kia
Lasalosi, bea kuo bau ko hona kaume'a koe me‘a

o ‘i he fouga ‘oe kakai, ‘o tauhoa mo ha fefine jte
ma‘u ha feohi; kae ai hanau kaume'a, koe tagata


‘oku ne matu'aki mate'aki kinautolu ; bea koe talanoa

Mamani, koe elito o‘enau mo‘ui.
Koia ‘oku tau belie, ka ai ha taha na‘e gali malu
mei he kovi ka ko Lasalosi, he koe to'utakaga ‘oe
‘Eiki. Ka na‘e ‘ikai; kae hage na‘e tubu ‘ae
tu'utumaki ‘a Jiobe mei hono fakabelebele'i ‘e Lagi,
behe na‘c ban ko majila ‘ae fai ‘a Setane kia Lasalosi
ko ‘ene lafilafi ki he ‘Eiki, ‘o hage koe lea ‘a Jisu,
“ Koia ‘oku taka ofi kiate au, ‘oku ofi ki ha afi.”
Koia, ‘iloage na‘e ogo mai mei ho Betani ‘e taha,
“ Eiki, koe jiana ‘oku ke ‘ofa ai ‘oku mahaki.”
‘Oku tau be mo Sekisibea, moe fa'ahiga ‘oku boto
‘i he tafa ‘oe loto ‘oe kakai, ke fakamatala ‘ae gaue
‘oe finagalo ‘o Jisu ‘i he a‘u mai ‘ae fekau kiate ia.
‘Oku mo'oni na‘a ne mea‘i hono ‘ikuaga • ka ‘ikai
‘oku tau tagi kitautolu ‘i he g. tu'utamaki ‘oku hoko,
ne ogo ‘oku tau ‘ilo ‘e ai hano ‘ikuaga lolei 1 Bea koe
me‘a noa koil ‘ae ii mamahi ‘e ogo‘i ‘e he tu'uga me‘a
Betani ‘i he me‘a ‘oku ‘ene ke to. Kane ko ha taha
faka‘atu‘atu ‘a Jisu, te ne ogo‘i lahi ‘ae to‘e hono g.
kaume'a, kae huanoa ‘i he'ene haohaoa. Bea ko
hono fakabo, he kuo mahino ‘e ‘ikai te ne lava ke ‘alu
ki ai ke fakalelulelu ‘enau mamahi. Kuo fai, nai, ha
alca ‘i he Lagi ‘o hage koia ia Jiobe, bea kuo tukuage
‘a ji‘i Lasalosi ke fa‘iteliha ai ‘ae fili ‘o hulu atu ‘ene
mafai ‘i he Beteliake, he na‘e gofua ke ne tamate‘i
‘aubito, ‘o maumau hono jino ‘o a‘u ki he'ene eho.
Koia ne ogo ‘ene ‘ofa ai, ka ‘oku tabu ‘ene ala ke
tokoni, bea na‘a moe ‘alu ki ai, ‘e ‘ikai fai, he ‘ikai
lava ha taha ke mate ‘oku ne ‘i ai—na‘a moe ogo
kaiha'a ‘i he kolosi na‘e ‘oua ke ne bekia ia bea na
toki faka'au hifo. Koia, na‘e hage ko ha heleta


fakatoumata ‘ae lea ‘oe fekau, he na‘e ha ai ‘ae
fakama‘uma‘u ‘ae ogo fafine ‘o ‘ikai te naufie tala ‘ae
me‘a ki he ‘Eiki kae'oua ke tau'aki ji'ona tuoga'ane,
na‘a ha‘u ‘a Jisu ki he botu ‘oku ‘i ai hono g. fili ;
hage na‘a ua lotomo'ua ke bekia hona tokoua ‘i he
hoko ha tu'utaraaki kia Jisu. Kae‘uma‘a be,
tala'ehai na‘a na belie ke ne ha‘u. Seuke 1 na‘a na
‘ilo ‘e tuaiekemo ‘ene ‘i ai. Bea ke ‘oua na‘a
hoke‘ia koa ‘ae finagalo ‘o Jisu ‘i he bau ke ne
faka‘amanakinoa‘i ‘ae falala koia. ‘Oku lau ‘e he
Balofita.ki he g. afo ‘oe tagata; bea ‘ikai koe told
afo malohi eni ‘ae li'aki falala ‘e ha fefine kia kita
‘Oiau ‘ae mahelehele ‘ae loto ‘o Jisu ‘i he lea ni! bea
ko ‘ene fakama‘uma‘u ‘o nofo be ‘i kauvai ‘o aho ua,
tala atu, koe taha ia ‘i he'ene g. gaue faigata'a.
Fakafokifa na‘a ne behe ki ho kau Abosetolo ke
nau toe o ki Jiutea ; bea nau fu‘u ‘oho ai, he kuo ne
toki meimei tu‘utamaki ‘i he botu koia; ‘o hage na‘a
nau fie ta'ofi. Bea toki tala ‘e Jisu hono ‘uhiga
tokua, kuo bekia honau kaume‘a ko Lasalosi. Ka
na‘a moia na‘e ‘ikai te nau fie ‘alu, ko ‘ene mahino
kiate kinautolu kuo bau ke fai ha me‘a ‘e he hou'eiki
kia Jisu. Kae lolotoga ‘enau nonofo behe, kuo tu‘u
mai ‘a Tomasi —‘a Tomasi vaivai, ‘a Tomasi ta'etui—‘o
ne behe, “ Tau o foki ke tail mate moia.” Hage koe
fakamo'oni ia ki he lea na‘e toki fai ‘e he ‘Eiki kia
Bita, ke ne tokaga na‘a mu‘omu‘a ‘ae muimui. Na‘e
‘ikai tuai honau fonoga, he tala'ehai na‘e vamama'o
‘ae ogo Betani, bea fe‘uga, nai, moe efiafi ‘oe ‘aho
koia kuo nau ‘i ai. Ha‘e ‘ikai ke hu ‘a Jisu ki kolo,
he kuo toko lahi ‘ae hou'eiki Jiu kuo ia Mele mo
Ma‘ata, kae ha‘u kitua‘a ‘ae ogo fafine kiate ia. Ko
Ma‘ata na‘e fua ha‘u ; bea koe malie ka ko ha malie


‘ene lea nae fai! “ ‘Eiki, ka ne ke ‘i heni, behe ne
‘ikai ke bekia hoku tuoga'ane. Bea na‘a moia, ka
‘oku ou ‘ilo ne ogo be koeha ho‘o kole ‘e fai ki he
Otua, ‘e ‘atu be ‘e he ‘Otua.” ‘Oku fa‘a lau‘i ‘a
Ma‘ata ‘e ha ni'ihi; ka hono ‘ikai koe toki lea hao-
haoa ia—‘ene ta'elauga mo ‘ene tui malohi?
Kae‘uma‘a na‘e laga'i ai ‘ao fugani folofola ‘a Jisu
“ Koau koe Toetu‘u moe Mo'ui.” ‘E fakamatala
‘ehai ‘ae mamafa ‘oe fo‘i lea koia ? Ko hono tuha be
koe g. folofola na‘e gaohi'aki ‘a mamani ‘i he
kamata'aga.
Toki ha‘u ‘a Mele ‘o ne higa ki lalo ‘o tagi, “ Eiki
ka ne ke ‘i heni, behe no ‘ikai bekia ji'oku tuoga‘ane.”
Bea gaue kehe ‘ae finagalo ‘o Jisu, ‘o ‘ikai hage ko ‘ene
fai mo Ma‘ata. Koe feline lotoma‘u ia, bea tali
‘a Jisu ‘o hage koia. Ka, ‘i he fu‘u fakafoa ‘a
Mele moe bihia ai ‘ae kakai ‘o nau tagi foki, na‘e vai
moe loto ‘o Jisu, bea tutulu hono fofoga. Bea hei'ilo
be koefe na‘a mahu'iga—a'ene lea kia Ma'ata bea ko
‘ena fetagihi mo Mele. He, koe m‘ea ‘i he‘ene behe,
‘oku tau ala katakki ai ‘ae g. tu‘utu‘uni ‘ae ‘Otua
kiate kitautolu, he ‘oku mahino, ne ogo kuo bau ke
ne fakamamahi kitautolu, ka ‘oku ne kau ‘i he
mamahi koia. ‘Oku ai mo ha lea ‘e taha ‘oku ai ‘e ho
evagelio ki he gaue hono fmagolo, he ‘oku no behe
‘eia, tu‘o ua, na‘e ‘ita ‘a Jisu. ‘Oku ‘ikai mahino bea
koe ‘ita ki he ha; be koe ‘ita ki he telito‘i kovi, ‘aia
‘oku va‘ava‘a mei ai 'ae g. mamahi ni, be koe ‘ita ki
he Fili ‘i he'ene gaue kuo fai kia Lasalosi, be koe ‘ita
ki he tagi fakakiika mai ‘ae hou'eiki Jiu. Ka ‘oku
mahino na‘e ga'uta ‘ae finagalo ‘o Jisu ‘o a‘u ki hono
tefito.
Bea nau saiki he fonualoto. Kuo ‘aho fa eui ‘ae


telio ‘oe me‘afaka‘eiki bea na‘e meimei fie ta'ofi ‘e
Ma'ata ‘ae hiki ‘oe makakafu ko ‘ene ‘ilo kuo kovi.
Kae ‘ikai tokaga ‘ae kakai ia, koe to‘oa honau loto ‘i
he aga ‘oe le‘o ‘o Jisu, ‘aia na‘e ‘ikai kei hage ko ha
mama, ka koe toko taka kehe. Bea ‘ajili, ‘i he'ene
tagaki hake hono fofoga ‘o lea hake ki he Lagi. Ka
ne ‘ogo ia, ka na‘e hage ha mofuike ‘ae gaue ‘ae
fakataha ‘i he ogo mai ‘ene kalaga, “ Lasalosi, tutu
mai kitu‘a.” Bea mo'utafuua kotoa ‘i he hake ‘ae
bekia ki ‘oluga kuo mahino ‘oku ne mo‘ui, bea ‘ikai
ha taha ‘e ala ke vete hono g. no‘o, —kuo behe fau ‘enau
ilifia.
Ke‘ine‘i tui-bikitai ‘ae toko lahi kiate ia. Koe me‘a
‘oku tau ofo ai ‘ae ta‘etui ha toho taha. Ka na‘e
mo'oni ‘ae lea ‘a Jisu kia Taivasi, ‘oku ai ae ni‘ihi
‘e ‘ikai tui, ne ogo ‘e toe tu‘u ha taha me‘i he mate.
Bea ‘oku ai ha toe me‘a ‘oku ha ai ‘ae ka'aga ‘oe
hou'eiki Jiu ka ko ‘enau fai leva ha fakataha ‘o
hikinima ke tamate‘i ‘a Jisu. ‘Oku lau ‘e he Labai ‘e
taha na‘e ifi talubite leva ‘i he Temibale ‘o fakaha ia.
Heifilo ki ai, ka na‘e ‘ikai buli. Bea na‘e bau ke
toe li‘aki ‘e Jisu hono utaga'alu ‘o toi ‘i he ve‘e
toafa ; ‘o ikai ko ha‘ane kalo, ka koe‘uhi kuo te‘eki
hoko hono taimi. Ka‘e behe ‘ae faka'oji ‘o hono Ono
‘oe Kuoga ‘i he Mo‘ui ‘a Jisu.
{‘Oku kei toe he.)


KOE YAHE X.
KOE BASIOJSTE.
Koe g. ‘Aho Teuteu.
‘Oku ‘ikai ‘ilo fakababau be na‘e tu‘u ‘i fe ‘ae ld‘i
kolo ko Ifalemi, ‘aia na‘e nofo lilo ai ‘a Jisu ‘i be g.
‘aho koia ‘i he vaha‘a ‘o hono tuku ke mate mo
hono buke ‘e he kakai Jiu. Behe moe gaue na‘a
ne fai. Ka kuo bau na‘a ne uafui ‘ae ako‘i ‘oe
Kau Abosetolo, ‘o teuteu kinautolu ki he gaue na‘e
tu'unuku mai. Faifai bea kamata hoko mai ‘ae g.
fonoga mei he botu kehekehe, ko ‘enau ‘alu hake ki
Selusalema ki he Basova, bea ne ‘ilo kuo hoko mai
hono taimi ke feia. Koia, na‘a ne fekau ki he
Kau Abosetolo ke teuteu ke nau o ki Selusalema, boa,
‘i he taiki ‘enau ‘alu, na‘a ne lakaage ‘o tebitebi ‘i
mu‘a. Bea fu‘u ofo honau loto, ko ‘enau behe,
“ ‘lkai ‘oku mea‘i ‘o Tagata'eiki kuo tuku ia ‘e he
hou'eiki ke bekia 1 ”
Bea, ‘i be'enau faigata‘a‘ia behe, na‘e ha ki ha
ni‘ihi, na‘a ‘oku ne teu fai ha me‘a, he na‘a nau tui
koe Misaia ia. Koia na‘e fakakaukau ‘ae ogo foha
‘o Sebeti ke fakatoka mu‘a ‘ena tala tu‘uga, ‘o na
fakafai ‘ena kole ‘i he‘ena fa‘e. ‘Oiau ‘ae g. mamahi
‘a Jisu !he koe taimi ia ke manako tu'uga? ‘lkai


koe hou‘eiki kotoa kuo nau li‘aki ia, bea kuo nau
ten hano tamate‘i 1 Ka na‘e ‘ikai ha‘u ‘a Jisu ke
fakamo'ui ‘ae kakai ma‘oni‘oni, ka koe agahala be,
bea koia, na‘e ‘ikai te ne lolomi ‘aibe ‘enau mo'ua ‘i
he higa ‘a Mamani. Bea na‘e ‘ikai te ne tautea ‘a
Semisi mo Jione, ka na‘a ne fehu‘i, be te na lava ‘ae
gaue ‘oe tu‘uga ‘oku na kumi ki ai, bea ne a‘au ‘ae
akonaki faigata'a o'etau lotu, ‘o behe, koe hala ki he
malohi ‘oku fou ‘i he fakavaivai, bea koe hala ki he
bule ‘oku fou ‘i he taliagi, bea koe hala ki he mo‘ui
‘oku fou ‘i he mate.
Bea fai atu ‘enau fonoga, bea nau a‘u ki Jieliko,
‘aia koe kolo ‘a hou'eiki na‘e masani ‘aubito. Lolo-
toga ‘ene ‘alu ai, na‘a ne faka'a ‘ae mata ‘oe ogo
kui, ‘aia koe taha ko Batimiosi, koe tagata kuo
ogoogoa hono higoa ‘i Mamani ko ‘ene ‘alovili mo
ta'elomia.
jSTa'e ha ai moe ta'elomia ‘a Jisu, he, ne ogo na‘e
fa‘a lauga kiate ia ‘i he‘ene ‘ofa ki he kau agahala
moe bobilikane, ka na‘e ‘ikai te ne tuku ‘ene fai,
kae kehe, na‘a ne ‘aunofo ki he fale ‘oe taha ‘i he
fa'ahiga fehi'anekina koia, ko Sakiasi, ‘aia kuo ne
kaka hake ‘i ne ‘akau, koe'uhi ke ne mamata lelei
kia Jisu. Bea kamata mafana ‘ae loto ‘oe kakai ‘i
he g.me'a koia bea nau tui bau kuo ofi ‘ene fokotu'u
‘ae Bule'aga. Bea vakai ki ai ‘e Jisu, bea ne
tu‘utu‘uni leva ke ta'ofi, ‘o ne fai ‘ae Fahaiata ‘oe g.
Mina. Koe gane faigata‘a ke faka‘amanakinoa aibe
‘ae feiga ‘ae kakai ‘oku tui mai. Ka na‘e fai ‘e Jisu,
‘o ne fakamahino ‘oku kei tuai ‘aubito ‘ae Bule'aga
‘oku nau jioki ai. Bea, ‘i he'enau mo‘utu‘ua ai, na‘a
ne laka atu ‘i honau ao, ‘o taki ‘i he fonoga ‘e
iku ki he‘ene bekia.


Koe hala kovi ia, ‘aia ‘oku ‘alu hake ‘i he mo'uga mei
Jieliko ki Selusalema, bea, ‘i he mahina koia, na‘e
toi hole ai ‘ae kau kaiha'a ke ‘ohofia ‘ae kakai na‘e
‘alu ki he Basova. Ka na‘e toko lahi fau ‘ae fonoga
‘o Jisu, bea na‘a nau a‘u lelei ki Betani ‘i he ‘efiafi
Falaite, ko h. 31 ‘o Maaji. ‘I he to ‘ae la‘a na‘e
Sabate leva, ‘ae Sabate faka'oji ‘oe mo'ui ‘a Jisu.
‘Oku ‘ikai ha mai ‘ae me'a na‘a ne fai, koe lotu be,
nai, moe talanoa mo‘ene Kau Ako ko hono ‘aho kumi
malohi eni ki he g. faigata'a na‘e tu'unuku mai.
‘Oku hage, foki, na‘a ne toe lea ki he‘ene bekia ‘oku
ofi kehe kuo ‘i ai ha toko ua kuo kamata mahino ki
ai, ta, ‘e mate ‘enau Balofita. Koe toko ua koia, ko
Jiutasi mo Mele. Ka ‘oiau ‘ae faikehekehe ‘oe gaue
‘ae ilo koia ‘i hona loto ! Na‘e tubu ai ia Jiutasi ‘ae
fakakaukau ke lavaki‘i ia, he‘ene behe, “Ka kuo
bau ‘ene bekia, kehe ke ‘aoga ia kiate au.” Ka ko
ji‘i Mele, na‘e feiga ji‘ono loto‘i feline be koeha
ha‘ane me'a ‘e lava ke fai ki he Tagata‘eiki. Koe
me'a be na‘a ne manavahe ki ai, na‘a te‘ia ia ‘i he
Temibale, be ha botu ‘e ikai te ne lava ke fai ki ai ke
ma‘u ‘ae me‘afaka‘eiki. Koia na‘a ne tu‘utu‘uni ke
lamalama ha faigamalie ke takai hono jino ‘i he
te'eki ke ne ‘alu ki ai, koo'uhi ke ne bekia
namukakala'ia.
Ka‘e ‘ikai tuai. ‘I he'ene gofua leva ‘i he bo
koia, na‘e fai ha fu‘u saba kia Jisu, he kuo ha‘u ‘ae
kaiga toko lahi mei Selusalema ke fe'iloaki moia bea
ke mamata kia Lasalosi. Bea, ‘i he tu‘u ‘a Mele ‘o
mamata kia Jisu, mo ‘ene manatu, hei‘ilo be te ne
toe jio ki ai be ‘ikai, na‘e ‘ikai te ne fa‘a faka-
ma‘uma‘u, ‘o ne ‘alu ‘o ‘omi ha hina 1010, koe fa‘ahiga
mahu‘iga ‘aubito, bea mahu‘iga moe hina na‘e utu ai,


‘o ne ‘alu ‘o foa‘i, ‘o ne liligi ki he fofoga ‘o hono
‘Eiki. ‘0 ‘ikai‘ia koia, ka koe me‘a na‘e toe ‘i he
hina na‘a ne banhaki hono va‘e ‘o ne holoholo‘aki
hono lau. Hage na‘e ‘oho kotoa ‘ae kakai na‘a nau
keinaga. Bea ne‘ine‘i, he kuo te'eki ke nau mamata
ki ha bani behe; na‘a moe tu‘i Loma na‘e ‘ikai fai
behe kae‘uma‘a na‘e ha mei hono gagatu koe 1010,
fugani lelei. Bea kuo iku ‘enau ofo ki ha fakamalo,
nai, ka netae'oua ae kamata gugulu ‘a Jiutasi, be
koeha kuo maumau ba'aga behe ai ‘e he fefine. Ka
ne fo‘aki ‘ae 1010 ki he'enau kautaha, behe kuo nau
fakatau ia ‘o ma‘u ha ba‘aga, ‘o tufa ki ha majiva, ‘o
behe mo behe. Bea nau bihia ai kotoabe ‘i he aga
koia, ‘o nau kamata fakaaga ki ai. Ka ka ‘ikai
kataki ‘e Jisu ‘ae gaohi ‘o ji‘i fefine kuo ‘ofa kiate ia,
‘o ne taukabofi ‘a Mele, ‘o ne behe, foki, koe takai ia
hono jino ki he bekia.
Fe‘uga moia kuo hoko ‘ae loto ‘o Jiutasi, ‘o hage
ko ha tahi hou. ‘Oku tau behe na‘e ‘i ai ‘ene ‘ofa
kia Jisu, ka kuo ta‘omia ‘i he ‘ofa ki he ba‘aga, moe
mamahi, nai, ‘i he valoki moe manavahe na‘a faka-
maumatea ‘a Jisu, bea hoko ‘ene ‘alu fano ai a‘ana ‘i
he g. ta‘u koeni, koe koto faka‘amanakinoa. Koe g.
feiga koia na‘e ga‘uta ai hono loto, ‘o fakabo'uli ‘ae
totonu moe lelei. Koe me‘a be taha na‘e ha mahino,
ne ogo be koeha ‘e hoko, kehe ke ‘aoga kiate ia—ke ne
ma‘u ai ha me‘a ‘eia. Koia ne ‘alu ai ki he kau
Taula‘eiki, ‘o vakai be koeha te ne lava.
Koe Sabate Baame.
Koe higoa eni kuo ‘ai ‘e Mamani ki he ‘aho koia
na‘e hoko moe katoaga ‘i Betani. Bogibogi hake


na‘e tu‘u ai leva ‘a Jisu bea fai atu ‘ene fonoga ki
Selusalema. Bea kuo ne tu'utu'uni ke ne ha‘ele
faka‘ei‘eiki ki ai, ‘o tau mo hano tu‘i, ke mahino ki
Mamani, ne ogo ‘ene fakalogo be, ka ‘oku ‘ikai te
ne tukuage hono tu‘uga. Na‘a ne faka‘atu‘i, foki,
‘ae faka'amu a‘ene Kau Ako ke jio kiate ia koe
Misaia, ‘aia kuo nau li‘aki ai lionau g. fonua mo
honau kaiga. Ka na‘a ne tokaga ke ‘oua na‘a faka-
tubu ai ha mahalo ‘ae kau Loma. Koia na‘e ‘ikai te
ne heka ki ha fu‘u hosi be te ne tuku ke to‘o mahafu
hono kakai, ka na‘a ne fekau ha toko ua ke ‘omi ha
ogo asi mei he viliji ko Betefeji ‘o ne heka ki he manu
ji‘i, ‘aia kuo te‘eki ke gaue'aki ‘e ha taha.
Kuo lahi ‘aubito ‘ae ‘amanaki kiate ia ‘i he ‘aho
koia, he talu ‘ae fokotu‘u ‘o Lasalosi moe fie mamata
kiate ia ‘e he kakai; ka nau manavahe na‘e ‘ikai fie
ha‘u ia telia ‘ae hou‘eiki. Ka, ‘i he bo ‘anebo, kuo
foki ‘ae ni‘ihi mei Betani ‘o fakaha kuo ne ‘i ai, bea
te ne hu ki Selusalema ‘abogibogi. Koia na‘e ha‘u
mei Selusalema ha toko lahi ke fakafetaulaki.
Lolotoga ia, moe fai atu ‘a Jisu mo hono lahi, ‘aia
koe kakai kuo tanaki mai mei he botu kehekehe.
Koe kau ‘ofa mo‘oni kiate ia, bea, ‘i he'enau mamata
ki he‘ene heka ki he asi ke ha'ele atu, ‘o hage koe g.
tu‘i ‘oe kuoga mu‘a, na‘e mafana honau loto, ‘o nau
to‘o honau bulubulu ‘o faliki‘aki ‘ae hala ; bea, ‘i he
ji‘i ia, na‘a nau tu‘uji ‘ae g. loirakau ‘o fai'aki, he koe
aga ‘oe ha‘ele faka‘ei‘eiki ‘aubito ke ‘oua na‘a te lave
ki he kelekele. Bakafokifa, na‘a nau a‘u ki he tumu-
tumu ‘o Olive, ‘aia na‘e ha ki ai ‘ae kolo. Koe me‘a
fakamanavahe ke jio ki ai! Koe taimi koia na‘e tu‘u
ai ‘ae g. fale faka‘ei‘eiki ‘aubito, ma‘oluga, teugaha,
lahi ‘ae buha moe taua; bea falo atu ki he mama‘o


‘ae g. tu'afale ‘o a‘u ki he fu‘u ‘a ‘e tolu na‘e ‘alu
takai. Ka ko hono masani lahi koe Temibale na‘e
hobo hake ‘i he kau tele'a, ‘o gali ko ha fale fakalagi
hono fu‘u lahi mo hono ‘ato koula ‘o fetabatabaki
hage ha la‘a hobo. Koe me'a ia ko mafana ai ‘ae
loto ‘o hono tu‘i, ka, ‘i he vakai hake ‘e he Kau Ako
kia Jisu, ta, ‘oku tutulu hono fofoga. Bea nan
mo'ulogoa ‘o ofoofo honau loto ‘i he‘enau fanogo ki
He'ene mabuhoi mo tagilaulau, “ Taumaiil ne ke
lavea ‘ae g. me'a ‘oku tutu ai ho‘o lelei.” Bea
ne‘ine‘ia, he na‘o ha ki Hono finagalo ‘ae lofa hifo ‘ae
faga ikale ki ai, hono ‘akolo‘i ‘e he kau Loma, ‘ae
holoki ‘o hono g. fale lelei na, ‘ae fakalielia'i hono g.
botu tabu, ‘ae fokotu'u ‘ae ‘aga'aga ‘oe kakai.
Fe‘uga moia kuo a‘u mai ha fu‘u fonoga mei
Selusalema, koe kakai kuo ha‘u ke fetaba kiate ia,
kuo nau to‘o ‘ae g. va‘a baame, ‘o hage ko ‘enau fai ‘i
lie g. ‘aho fakafiefia. Bea na‘a nau tatakalo kia
Jisu, ‘o nau hua ‘enau taua'alo ‘o tuku ai kia Jisu ‘ae
g. huafa ‘oe Misaia. Bea nau hifo atu leva kotoa ke
‘alu ki he kolo. Mu'omu'a ‘akinautolu na‘e toki ha‘u
‘oku nau tatakalo be mo hiva ; hoko ai ‘a Jisu kuo ne
heka ki he asi, bea muimui mai ‘ae Kau Ako moe
fonoga mei ‘uta, ‘o nau hiva fetaliaki moe ‘uluaki fono-
ga, ‘onafui ‘ae lau “ Hosana ki he Tu‘i Isileli.” Ka'e
fakamanatu, foki, ‘e he ni‘ihi ki he hiva ‘ae kau agelo
‘i hono ‘alo‘i, he tala melino ki Mamani moe kololia
ki Lagi Taubotu. Koe me'a lagilagi ‘aubito ‘enau
‘alu, bea, ‘i he'enau hake mei Kitioloni, na‘e ga'uta
‘ae kolo kotoa ‘o felelei mai lie mamata. Bea ke
faka'uta mu‘a ki he ‘ita ‘a hou‘eiki-‘enau vakai ki he
hakeakhi ‘oe tagata ni kuo nau toki li‘aki. Ha‘e
‘ikai mafakama‘uma‘u ha ni‘ihi, ‘o nau leaage kia Jisu


ke ne ta'ofi ‘ene Kau Ako. Kae tali be ‘eia, “ kabau
te nau fakalogo ‘ekinautolu, ‘e kalakalaga ‘ae g.
maka.” Bea nau ‘ilo leva kuo kovi ‘ae mo‘a.
' Oku hage na‘e tutuku ‘ae fonoga ‘i he‘enau ofi
ki he Temibale, kae ‘ikai tuku ‘ae mavava : he koe
hu leva ‘a Jisu ki ai bea ha‘aki mai ‘e he kau tamaiki
na‘e hiva ai, ‘o behe, “ Hosana ki he Hako ‘o Tevita.”
Koe me‘a koia na‘e ‘ikai lava ke kataki ‘e he hou'eiki,
ka, ‘i he‘enau fai ke ta'ofi, na‘e tataha kinautolu ‘e he
‘Eiki ‘aki ha fo‘i folofola Same, ‘aia na‘e kikite ai ‘e
Tevita ki he fai behe ‘ae tamaiki ki he Misaia. Kuo
bau na‘e ha ki honau loto ‘i he momeniti koia koe
Misaia ia, ka na‘e kuku be ‘enau ta'etui, bea kukuta
tu‘u honau loto ‘i he ‘ita, ‘i he'enau vakai ‘oku ‘ikai
mafohi ha'anau me‘a kiate la. Nae gaue moe finagalo
‘o Jisu, o ‘ikai koe‘uhi be ko ‘enau ta'etui ka ko ‘ene
vakai kuo fakalielia'i ‘ae Temibale ‘i he‘enau manu-
manu. Ke ogo ‘ene kabuji ‘ae kau fakatau ‘i he
kamata ‘ene gaue, ka kuo nau toe fakafonu be ‘ae
fale, bea, lolotoga ‘e ‘atu ‘oe feilaulau, moe tutu ‘oe
inisenisi, moe fai ‘oe hiva moe lotu, ‘oku ogooga'a
mai a'enau tau‘aki kaka. Ka kuo ‘efiafi fau, bea
na‘a ne tu‘u ‘o foki ki Betani ‘o toka ai. Koe
Sabate Baame ia.
Ko Monite.
Bogibogi hake, na‘e ne fonoga atu kei hegihegi ke
fai ‘ae gaue ‘i he Temibale. Tokua, na‘a ne halofia,
koe'uhi, nai, kuo te‘eki ‘oji ‘ae ‘atu ‘oe feilaulau ‘i he
Temibale, ‘aia na‘e tatali ki ai ‘e he kakai Jiu ke fai
‘enau belekifasi. Koia, ‘i he'ene vakai ki ha fu‘u


fiki ‘i he ve‘ehala, na‘a ne alu ki ai ke toli ha‘ane
kai, he kuo fa‘u lau ‘ae ‘akau, bea koe aga ‘oe fiki oku
muomua ‘ae fua ‘i he lau. Ka‘i he'ene a‘u ki ai, kuo
‘ikai ha me‘a. Bea tu'utu'uni leva ‘e Jisu ke tu‘uga
ki ai ha akonaki ki he‘ene Kau Ako ki he kovi ‘oe
mo‘ui ta'efua. Koia na‘a ne folofola ke ‘oua na‘a toe
kai ‘e ha taha ‘ae fiki koia ; ‘o ne laka atu. Na‘e
‘ikai ke tokaga ‘ae Kau Ako ki ha me‘a ‘i he ‘aho
koia, ka, ‘i he'enau jitu‘a leva, bea kamata mae.
Koia fe'uga moe bo'uli kuo mate aubito —-koe faka-
‘iloga, ‘o a‘u ki he gata'aga ‘o Taimi,
Ne ogo ‘ete lau
‘0 hage ko ha uite,
Mo jino fai tatau,
Ka to te tu'umalie ?
Koe fua bo ‘0 fai ki ai
‘Ae utu ‘oe ta‘u ‘o Lagi.
Bea hu ai ‘a Jisu ki he Temibale ke fai ‘ene fu‘u
ako fakmui ki he kakai. Ka na‘e ‘ikai te ne lava ke
fai, kuo behe fau hono fakalielia ‘i he gaue fakamama
‘oku fai ai. Koia na‘a ne haga ‘o kabuji ‘ae kau
fakatau ‘o hage ko ‘ene fai mu‘a. Keu mamata mai
ki he‘enau fekalei kitu‘a mei he ao ‘o Jisu, mo ‘ene
tu‘u kuo kikila hono fofoga ‘i he ‘ita, bea hage ha
mana ‘ene lea ! He tala'ehai na‘e ‘i ai ‘ene me‘a-ta
‘i he'ene fai koia, ka ko honau g. konisenisi na‘a nau
fo‘i ai. He koe‘uma‘a ke fakatale'i ia ‘e he hou'eiki,
he ko ‘ene nofo e na‘e hage ko ha tu‘i, bea na‘a ne
bule ‘i he Temibale ‘o tau moe ‘Alo ‘oe ‘Otua na‘e
o‘ona ia, ‘o ne kabuji mo fakafoki ‘ae kakai ko ‘ene
fa‘iteliha be. Bea, ‘i he'ene ma‘u leva ‘ae fale, na‘a ne
toki nofo hifo ‘o fai ‘ene ako ki he kakai, bea, ne ogo
‘oku ‘ikai te tau ‘ilo be koeha na‘e kau ki ai ‘ene


malaga, ka kuo bau na‘e mamafa, he kuo tuku ! ae
fakaalala, he kuo hokojia ‘ae taimi ke ta. Kae‘uma‘a
kuo mo'ua hono loto ki he me'a ‘oku tuhmuku mai
kiate ia, bea bau ke boboi ‘ene lea koe mamalu mai
‘a Itaniti.
Bea na‘a koe taimi koia na‘e ‘aluage ‘ae kau Kalisi
‘o fehloaki moia. Ka‘a nau fuofua bo‘aki kia Filibo,
bea ‘oku ha ‘ae aga ‘oe Kau Abosetolo moe ta‘eo‘o
‘ene g. fakamatala, ho na‘e tala‘a ‘a Filibe, be fie
fe‘iloaki mo kinautolu ‘e he Eiki be ‘ikai. Oiseuke !
koe me‘a koia na‘e ha‘u ki ai ‘ae Eiki —ke ne toho
mai ‘a Mamani katoa ; bea ko enau ‘omi, ‘ae tu'uga
me'a koia, koe bekebekatama ki lie ha‘u ‘ae g, kakai,
he ko Kalisi koe fonua tu‘umu‘a. Tokua, na‘e gaiie
kehe ‘ae finagalo ‘o Jisu ‘i he fotu mai koia ‘ae
Senetaile kiate ia. Na‘e tu‘u mei he botu ‘e taha
‘ene bekia, ‘o hage ha movete ‘o ha fo‘i tega kuo to,
kae tu‘u mei he botu ‘e taha ‘ae toki kau mai ‘ae toko
lahi, ‘o hage koe fua ha tega kuo behe. Bea, ne ogo
na‘e teki hono jino ‘i he ‘amanaki lusa, kae fiefia
hono loto ‘i he ha mai ‘ae ‘aoga lahi ‘o ‘ene bekia ka
fai. Bea hage ko Baula, na‘e fetohoaki ia ‘e he me'a
koia ‘e ua, ‘o ne folofola hake, “ ‘B, kuo takatu'u eni
‘eku mo‘ui, bea koeha ai ‘eku lea ‘e fai 1 Ala, Tamai,
fakaha‘ofi au mei he houa koeni. ‘A, ka ko hono
‘uhiga e na'aku hoko mei ai ki he houa ni.”
Koe me‘a malie hono fakaha mai hono toumo'ua
behe hono loto, he kohai ‘iate kitautolu ‘oku ‘ikai ke
mo‘ua ‘i he me'a koia ha taimi ? Bea fakafeta'i ‘oku
ha ai ‘oku ‘ikai koe agahala, he na‘e behe ‘a Jisu. Ka
na‘e ‘ikai ke fuoloa ‘ae fetohoaki. Koe kemo be kuo ne
‘ikuna ‘ene teki ki he mate, ‘o ne kalaga, “ Ala Tamai,
fakalagilagi'i Ho‘ou Huafa.” Bea hage koe molo-


molornuiva'e ‘ao mana ki he ‘uhila, belie ‘ae tali leva
mei he Lagi ‘ae lea ‘a Jisu, ‘o behe, “ Kuou fakalagi-
lagi'i ia bea teu toe fakalagilagki foki.”
Na‘e fu‘u ‘oho ‘ae kakai ‘i he me‘a koia. Lau ‘e
he ni'ihi koe mana ; lau ‘e he ni‘ihi koe agelo na‘e
lea. Kae tala tonu ‘e Jisu koe lea, kae‘uma‘ii na‘a
ne fakaha kuo bau eni ‘a Setane. Koe me‘a
fakatubu fifili ‘ene lea koia, bea ‘oku ha mei ai koe
fefa‘uhi ‘a ha toko taha mo hono loto, kae'oua ke ne
lava ke li‘aki ‘ene mo‘ui ma‘ae ‘Eiki—koe fu‘u hoka
ia kia Setane mo hono Bule'aga.
Koia na‘e hakailagitau ai ‘a Jisu, he, ne ogo na‘e
ha kiate ia te ne tautau ‘i he ‘akau kovi, ka na‘e
‘ikai te ne toka‘i ia ko ‘ene ogo‘i te ne toho ‘a
Mamani. ‘Oku ha mei he tohi ‘a Jione, na'e tui ‘ae
toko lain kiate ia ‘i he ‘aho koia, ka na‘a nau
manavahe ke fakaha na‘a “fakahifo kinautolu mei he
falelotu,” he koe tautea lahi ‘aubito. Koia na‘e
na‘ina‘i ‘e Jisu ke nau fai leva lolotoga ‘oku ne ‘i ai,
he ‘oku nau ma‘u ai ha mama, kae faigata'a ‘enau
otu ‘oka ‘alu ia.
Bea na‘a koe taimi ia na‘e ‘omi kiate ia ‘ae feline
na‘e ma‘u ‘i he‘ene tono tagata, mo nau fai ‘ae fehu‘i
kitkil kiate ia, be koeha ‘ene boa ki he tautea ‘e fai.
Koe me‘a koia na'e ha ai ‘ae ‘ulugaaga ‘e taha ‘o Jisu.
Ke ogo koe tagata, ka na‘e hage ko ha feline ‘i he
me‘a ni‘ihi. ‘Oku lau‘ilo kotoabe ‘oku ai ha g. me‘a
‘oku tabu ke lea ki ai ‘i he ao ‘oe feline, he ne ogo ‘ene
‘ata'ata ‘eia, ka ‘oku hage ko hono fakama'i ‘ae lau ki
he aliime‘a behe —kehe ko hono aga ia ‘o Babalagi.
Bea koe lau ‘ae kau Falesi ki he aga o‘enau buko, koe
me‘a ia ke ma ha feline ‘i he'ene fanogo ki ai. Bea
‘oku matamata ko hono ‘uhiga ia ‘oe bunou ‘a Jisu ‘0


tohi ‘i he kelekele ko ‘ene fakaogonoa‘i. Ka, ‘i
he‘enau haganaki hono fehu'i, na‘a ne malaga hake ‘o
ne beheage, “Koia ‘iate kimoutolu ‘oku ‘ata'ata mei
he agahala, ke a‘ana ‘ae fuofua tolo ki he fefine.”

boto o'ene tali koia ! Ka'e ‘ikai te ne fakama‘ama‘a

fili—koe hoka ka ko ha hoka! Ne‘ine‘i ui ‘ae

Falesi, be fou ‘i he fouga ‘onautolu.

Koe Ohomohe.
‘Oku vahavaha'i ‘aki ‘ae g. ‘aho teuteu moe g. ‘aho
fai'aki ‘ae ‘aho Bulelulu, ‘aia ‘oku ‘ikai te tau
momo'i ma‘u talanoa ki ai: ka koe tokoni ki he'otau
faka'eke koe me‘a ‘oku tau ‘ilo ki ai ‘i he aga ‘oe
mo'ui ‘a Jisu. ‘Oku mahino mei he g. fakamatala
kuo fai, ka ai ha‘ane ‘amanaki mo‘ua ‘i ha gaue
maniafa, na‘a ne teuteu ki ai ‘aki ba lotu fuoloa.
Bea ‘e lauga gaue mamafa ki he me‘a na‘e ene ‘a Jisu
ke fai? ‘ikai koia na‘a ne ha‘u ai ki mamani? Bea
‘oku tau behe na‘e mole ‘ae ‘aho Bulelulu ‘i he lotu
ki he'ene Tamai, ke ‘omi ha ivi ke ne mafai‘aki ‘ene
gaue. Moe malolo foki telia hono jino ;he na‘e ‘ikai
ke ta‘etoka‘i ‘e Jisu hono jino hage koe ni'ihi, ka
na‘a ne ‘ilo, ka ‘ikai tauhi ki ai, ne ogo ‘oku ‘i ai ha
loto ke fai ‘ae gaue, ka ‘e ‘ikai lava. ‘Oku tau behe
na‘e ‘i ai ha‘ane talanoa, foki, moe Kau Ako; kae hage
na‘e ‘ikai finagalo ‘ae Laumalie ke fakaha ki mamani;
bea tau tuku aibe ke behe. Koe bo koia na‘e fai ai
‘e Jisu ‘ene toka fakamui, bea, ‘i he‘ene ‘a, na‘e ‘ikai
te ne toe mohe ‘i mamani.


Koe Tu'abulelulu.

levani.”

Koe me‘a fakamamahi ia ki he finagalo ‘o Jisu.
