‘oji! Ne‘ine‘l ui ia ‘e Jione ko ‘ene ‘of a taubotu !
Bea toe ‘ai ‘eia hono kofu ‘o nofo hifo, ‘o ne faka-
‘uhiga ‘ae me‘a kuo ne toki fai ke gata leva ‘enau
kakaba ki he g. tu‘uga ma'oluga, mo ‘enau ta‘e fie
fai ‘ae g. gaue ma‘ulalo; he, ne ogo ko honau ‘eiki ia
mo honau Labai, ka ‘oku ‘ikai te ne behe koe me‘a
ta'etau ke ne fai ‘ae gaue fakatamaio'eiki, ‘o kabau
te ne ‘aoga ai ki hanau toko taha. Bea, ‘i he'ene
‘ofa, na‘a ne faka‘atu‘i honau faka'amanakinoa ‘i
he lau ke nau tamaio'eiki, ‘oji na‘a nau ‘amanaki
ma'oluga ‘i he Bule'aga ‘oe Misaia; koia na‘a ne
behe, “ ‘E ai homou bule'aga, bea te mou nofo taloni,
he ko kimoutolu ia kuo mou nofo ma‘u mo au ‘i hoku
g. ‘ahi'ahi.” Bea, ‘i he'ene lau ki he'ene ‘ofa kiate
kinautolu, mo ogo‘i koe me‘a ji‘i ia kuo ne fai, ka
‘oku ne lava noabe ke mate ma'anautolu, bea hage
na‘e fu‘u fotu hake ‘ae ta'ohouga ‘a ha toko taha, ‘o


no meimei tagi ‘i he‘ene behe, “ Koau e ‘oku ou tala
atu, koe toko taha ‘iate kimoutolu te ne lavaki'i au,
‘io, koe toko taha ‘oku ne kai moau.” Bea nau loto
mamahi ‘aubito, bea nau haga ‘o lelea taha kiate ia,
‘o behe, “ ‘Oku ‘ikai, nai, ko au, ‘Eiki, ‘e 1 ” Na‘e
‘ikai, nai, fai kotoa, he ‘eke koa ‘e Jione, be ko Bita?
ko Tomasi be moe ni‘ihi na‘e fakamanatu ‘e honau
loto ‘a‘enau fa‘a vaivai: ko Jiutasi, foki, na‘e logobe.
Na‘e ‘ikai ha‘ane tali ‘a Jisu, ka ne fai atu be, “ Koe
toko taha kuo ne velo hono nima fakataha moau ki
he tisi; ‘o ne tuhu ki he kumete kuo nau ala kotoabe
ki ai: bea ne toe me‘a mai, “ Oiaue ‘ae tagata, ‘aia te
ne lavakki ‘ae Panautama ‘a Tagata ! ne gutuhuaage
‘ae tagata koia ‘oka ne ‘ikai fanau'i.” ‘E ‘ikai lauga
lea mamafa ki he lea koia, he koe fai ‘e ‘Ofa Mo'onia :
bea ‘oku hage na‘e fu‘u ‘oho ai ‘ae loto ‘o Jiutasi, ‘o
ne fanafanaage ki he ‘Eiki, “ ‘Oku ‘ikai, nai, koau,
Labai 1 ” bea toki tali ‘e Jisu, “ ‘E toe lau ? ” —ka na‘a
ne le‘o ji‘i be, nai, hei‘ilo ‘e ‘aoga ‘ene na‘ina‘i kuo
toki fai, bea ‘oku matamata ko Matiu be na‘a ne
fanogo ki ai, ‘aia na‘e ofi.
Bea na‘a koe taimi ia na‘a ne fokotu'u ai ‘ae
Sakalameniti ; ka ‘oku mahalo ‘e he ni‘ihi na‘e ‘oua
be ia ke ‘alu ‘a Jiutasi. Ka‘e tu‘o fa ‘ae fakatau
‘oe kava ‘i he fai ‘oe Basova; koe taha ‘i he nofo
hifo, koe taha ‘i he'enau tutuku, bea moe ua lolotoga
‘ae kai. Kuo fai, nai, ‘ae ‘uluaki mo hono ua—
kehe ‘oku lau ‘e Luke ki ha kava na‘e tufa, ‘aia
na'e folofola ai ‘ae ‘Eiki, ‘e ‘ikai te ne toe inu
ha kava kae'oua ke hoko ‘ae Bule'aga ‘oe Lagi—.
bea ‘oku galigali ko hono tolu ‘eni na'e teu hono
fakatau, ‘aia na‘e ui koe “ ibu ‘oe fakafeta'i.” Tlo-
nge, na‘e to‘o ‘e he ‘Eiki ha fo‘i ma, ‘o ne tabuaki‘l


mo bakibaki, ‘o ne told tufa kiate kinautolu, ‘o ne
behe, “ Ko hoku jino ‘eni, ‘aia ‘oku ou foaki koe'uhi
ko kimoutolu; mou fai ‘eni moku fakamanatu.”
Kuo bau na‘a nau fu‘u ‘oho ‘i he fai behe, he koe
me‘a ia na‘a nau maheni ai, koe to'oga ‘e taha ‘oe
hutu, koe me‘a na‘e fai ‘e he motu'a na‘e a‘ana ‘ae
me‘a faka‘eiki ‘i he'enau foki mei fa‘itoka. Ko hono
g. ‘uhiga kehe na‘e buli, nai, kiate kinautolu ‘i he
taimi koia. Kae ‘oua na‘a tau ofo ai, he hono e‘a
kiate kitautolu hono kotoa, ne ogo kuo gaue ki ai ‘ae
kau faifekau ‘o lahi senituli ? Kae‘uma‘a na‘e tanunu
mai ‘ene me‘a ; ‘oku nau kei bubutu'u ‘i he tufa ‘oe
ma fakamanatu, moe toe fakatau ‘ae kava, ‘o ui koe
“ toto fuakava,” tokua. Koe ‘atamai fe ‘e lava ke
falute leva ha g. fu’u me‘a behe ? Na‘e ‘ilo ‘e Jisu ‘e
‘ikai te nau lava, ‘aia na‘a ne lea ai kimui, ‘o ne
behe te ne fekau atu hono Laumalie ke fakamanatu
‘ae g. me‘a, mo faka'uhiga foki. Koia na‘e ‘ikai te
ne mamahi ai; koe me‘a be na‘a ne mamahi ai, he
koeni kuo ne lau ke liligi hono toto ma'anautolu, ka
‘oku ai ha toko taha ‘oku ‘ikai ke hougalki ai ‘ene ‘ofa.
Koia na‘a ne lea hake, “ Kane ogo ia, vakia koo
nima ‘o hoku lavaki ‘oku ala mo au ki he tebile ni.”
Bea ‘ikai fiemalie ‘a Bita ke tuku buli ‘ae me‘a,
‘Oku tau maheni mo ‘ene aga'oho, ka ko honau
matabule foki, bea ka ai ha lavaki ‘oku teu, ‘oku
totonu ke ne ‘ilo ki ai ka ne ta'ofi. Koia na‘a ne
ki‘i teba hake kia Jione ‘i hono tu‘a ke ne ma‘u mei
he ‘Eiki be kohai. Bea falala atu ‘a Jione ‘o ne faki
ki he fatafata ‘o Jisu, ‘o ne fanafana hake, “ Eiki,
kohai ia?” Bea tali ‘e Jisu, “Koia ia ‘aia teu unu
‘eku koga ma, ‘o ‘age ma‘ana.” Koe me‘a ia kuo fai
‘i Esia talu mei mu‘a koe fakahloga o‘ete ‘ofa ki ha


taha; bea, ‘i lie fai ‘e Jisu kia Jiutasi, ‘oku ‘ikai te
tau ‘ilo be koefe te tau ofo lahi ai—ao ‘ofa ‘a Jisu be
koe ta‘ehouga ‘a Jiutasi. Kuo ne ‘ilo ‘oku mea‘i ‘e
he ‘Eiki ‘ae kaka ‘oku ne teu fai, ka ne ogo ia, ka
‘oku ne fai kiate ia ‘ae to‘oga ‘oe ‘ofa‘aga. Kane
momo‘i toe ha lelei ‘ia Jiutasi, kuo vai hono loto ‘i
he me‘a koia koe gaue faka'oji ia ‘a Lagi ki ai;
koe ui ta tu‘o taha ki he sibi na‘e he kae tuku hono
kumi : bea, ‘i he ‘ikai tali, na‘e toki behe ‘e Lagi,
“ Tukuaibea " : bea ‘i hono motuhi behe mei he lelei,
na‘e matu'aki hu ‘a Setane ki ai, ‘o fa'iteliha kiate
ia. Kuo bau ‘eni ‘ae me‘a, bea hage ko kitautolu
kotoa na‘e faka'amu ‘e Jisu ke faka'oji leva, ‘o ne
folofola ki hono lavaki, “Fai vave age ‘ae me‘a
‘oku ke fai ; ” bea tu‘u leva ia ‘o ‘alu ki tu‘a. Ka‘e
mahalo a‘e toko lahi ko ‘ene ‘alu ke tokonaki; koe
toko tolu be, nai, na‘e ‘ilo hono ‘uhiga : bea ko honau
toko taha ko Jione, na‘e vavana hono loto, ‘o ne jio
kia Jiutasi ‘o hage koe tevolo ‘ata, ‘o ne tokagah ko
‘ene hu leva kitu‘a bea kehe ‘ae bo‘uli—kae fefe, he
ko Heli ‘oku ‘i hono loto !
‘Oku hage na‘e ‘alu mo Jiutasi ‘ae me‘a na‘e
mafajia ai ‘ae ‘Eiki, bea mabuna hake hono loto ‘o
fiemalie. Koe kakai ko‘ena ko ‘ene kau mateaki
kotoabe ia, bea na‘e ‘ikai ha toe fakabinebine ki
he‘ene lau ‘ofa, he ‘oku nau ‘ofa kotoabe kiate ia.
Faka'amu ‘eia ke nau nonofo ma‘ube, ka ‘e ‘ikai lava
ia; koia na‘a ne tala kuo bau ‘ae mavae, he koe hala
‘oku ne ‘amanald fou ai ‘e ‘ikai fa‘a‘ ‘uhi ai ha taha
kebe: ka, ‘i he‘ene mama‘o, ke jinoeme'a ke nau
uouagataha mo fe‘ofa‘aki, ‘o ‘oua ‘e fakafeveikaji'aki
hage koia kuo nau toki fai.
Te tau ‘amanaki kuo mahiuo eni ki he Kau


Abosetolo ‘ao mo‘a ‘oku ne ene ke fai, ka na‘e kei
fakakakano fau honau loto, ‘o nau mahalo ko ‘ene fie
fai tokotaha be ha gaue faigata'a, ko ‘ene faka‘atu‘i
kinautolu. Koia na‘e ‘eke leva ‘e Bita be koeha oku
‘ikai te ne fie ‘ave ai ia, he ne ogo koe me‘a te ne
mate ai, kae ‘ikai te ne kalo. Bea fakaha ‘e Jisu
kuo tala ‘e Setane ke tukuage kinautolu ko ne sivi,
hage ko ‘ene fai kia Jiobe, bea ‘oku ‘ikai ha ta'ofi,
bea koe me‘a be kuo ne lava ‘i he hufia, ke ‘oua na‘a
mate ‘aubito ‘ae tui ‘a Bita : koia, tauage moia ‘oka
toe ake ‘ene tui, ke ne boubou ‘ae Kau Abosetolo.
Ka ko Yaihi e ha lava ‘e Bita ke tui te ne kakuga
ke li‘aki ‘ae ‘Eiki, ‘o ne toe lau ki he ‘oji teu hono
loto ke ‘alu mo Jisu ki he bilisone moe mate. ‘Oua
na‘a tau lau‘i ‘a Bita. Seuke ! na‘a ne lea mei he
mo‘oni ‘o hono loto ; bea ko hotau fu‘u toko lahi, ka
ne fakaha kiate kitautolu ‘i he'etau tagata hake ‘ae
g. me‘a te tau fai ‘i he te‘eki te tau bekia, ‘e ‘ikai te
tau momo‘i tui ki ai. Na‘e fakamo‘oni katoabe
‘ae Kau Abosetolo ki he lau ‘a Bita, (he na‘a mo
kinautolu na'a nau ogo‘i behe) ‘e ‘ikai te nau
li‘aki ‘a Jisu, kae huanoa honau matabule, he ko
Maka foki. Koia na‘e hage ha fanaga ‘ae lea ‘a
Jisu na‘e fai, “ Bita, ‘oku ou tala,” ‘E ‘ikai u‘ua
‘ae moa ‘anai, kae'oua ke ke faka‘ikai ‘o tu‘o tolu
malo ‘oku ke ‘ilo au.” Na‘a ne mea‘i ‘enauta ‘etui,
‘o ne feiga ke fakahu ki honau loto ‘ae aga ‘oe me‘a
kuo nau hoko ki ai. Koia na‘a ne fakamanatu ‘ae
aga o'enau mavae mu‘a, ‘aia na‘a nau ‘alu fano ai ‘i
Kenani ‘o malaga, mo ‘enau fu‘u tu'umalie na‘e fai ;
ne ogo na'a nau mahafu'aki ‘ae tokotoko be. Bea
ne na‘ina‘i ‘e ‘ikai behe ‘enau mavae koeni, bea na‘e
mei tauage ‘enau ma‘u heleta ‘i he tokotoko. Ko


‘ene lea fakatata, nai, ke o‘o. Bea nau ogo‘i ‘oku
tu‘unuku mai ha tu‘utamaki; ka nau behe ko ‘ene
lea mo'oni ki he heleta, ‘o nau tali hake, ‘oku ‘i ai ha
me‘a behe ‘e ua, kae fefe ha'anau toe kumi 2 kae
ta'ofi ‘eia he kuo lahi.
Na‘e mahino eni mei honau fofoga kuo o‘o ‘ene lea
kiate kinautolu, bea ‘oku nau ogo‘i mo‘oni kuo oil
mai ha fu‘u me‘a fakamamahi. Koia na‘e haga ai ‘e
Jisu, ‘o ne fai ‘ae lea fakafiemalio ‘oku tu‘u ‘i h. 14
‘oe vahe ‘i he Kosibeli ‘a Jione, ‘aia kuo fakalelulelu-
‘aki ‘ae g. mamahi ‘ae kakai ‘i ne g. to‘utagata lahi;
“ ‘Oua na‘a tuku ke bubutu'u homou loto ; tui bikitai
ki he ‘Otua, tui bikitai foki kiate au.” ‘Oku mo‘oni
‘ene ‘alu, ka koe ‘alu ke teuteu ha nofo'aga mo‘onau-
tolu. Bea, hage ha finemotua ‘aia ‘oku ne ui ki
he‘ene tamajih mei he mama‘o, “ ‘Oku ou ha‘u be;”
behe na‘e lea ‘a Jisu ki hono tiikaga ni, ne ogo ‘ene
‘alu ka ‘oku ne ha‘u be, boa koe botu ‘oku ne ‘i ai te
nau ‘i ai foki, he ‘oku ‘ilo ‘ae hala ki ai. Na'a nau
‘ilo be—kehe kuo ne tala tu‘o lahi—ka kuo bubutu‘u
‘ae loto, bea na‘e fai ‘e Tomasi ‘enau lea he‘ene behe,
“ ‘Eiki, ‘oku ‘ikai te mau ‘ilo be ko ho‘o me‘a ki fe,
bea mau ‘ilo fefe ‘ae hala ki ai?” Ji‘i Tomasi loto
tala‘a, na‘a ne lau, ‘abe, koe hala mama‘o mo ‘ilogata'a,
‘oji koena ia ‘oku nau femata‘aki. Kae folofola leva
‘e Jisu, “ Koau be koe Hala, bea moe Mo'oni moe
Mo‘ui.” Koe taha ia ‘oe g. fu‘u lea ‘oe Eolofola, koe
katuba tofu be ki he Ta'ehamai.
Kuo kamata eni ke takataka kehe ‘enau talanoa,
‘o namu misiteli, mo namu Hevani mo namu Itaniti;
bea mo‘uofo ‘ae loto ‘oe Kau Abosetolo, ‘o faka‘amu
ke habo ‘ae g. lea mamafa koia. Ka, ‘i he‘ene lau koe
hala ia ki he Tamai, na‘e lea hake leva ‘a Filibe, he


koe fo‘i me‘a na‘e mahino ki hono ‘atamai, ka uau ka
lava ke jio ki he Tamai kuo ! oji ‘ae kovi, boa talu ‘ae
gaohi ‘o mamani moe feiga ‘ae laumalie ‘oe tagata ke
ha'ele mai ‘ae ‘Otua ‘o fakatonutonu ‘ae hala. ‘Oiaue
‘ae g. mamahi ‘o Jisu ! Kofutu ‘ene ‘iate kinautolu,
bea kuo te‘eki ke mahino koe ‘imiji totonu ia ‘oe
‘Otua ; ‘o ‘ikai'ia koia, ko koe Tamai ‘oku ‘iate ia,
‘o jio‘aki hono mata —tabu moia—mo lea'aki hono
fofoga. Ka na‘e ‘ikai te ne tautea kinautolu, ka na‘a
ne fai atu ‘ae g. tala'ofa na‘e keheage. Te nau fai
‘ae g. gaue ‘oku hulu ‘i ha‘ana ; bea ne ogo be koeha
ha me‘a te nau kole ‘i hono higoa, ka te ne fai;
kae‘uma‘a te ne tuku atu ha Taukabo ‘e taba, bea ‘e
‘ikai te nau toe mavae moia, bea koe me‘a koia ‘e
‘ikai ma‘u ‘e mamani—ko ‘enau koloa be ‘anautolu.
Bea faigata‘a‘ia ai a Jiutasi ‘ae Jiutasi koia ‘oku
higoa tolu, ko Jiutasi, mo Lebiusi, mo Tatiusi; ‘ae
Jiutasi na‘e ‘ikai ko Isikaliote—‘o ne fehu‘i, “ ‘Eiki,
koeha kuo behe ai ho‘o teu fakaha‘i koe kiate
kimautolu, kae ‘ikai ki mamani?” Fakafeta‘i kia
Jiutasi ‘ene fehu'i, ‘aia ‘oku tau ma‘u ai ‘ae koloa ‘o
hono tali. “ Kabau ‘oku ‘ofa ha taha kiate au, te ne
tauhi ‘eku g. lea : bea ‘e ‘ofa kiate ia ‘eku Tamai,
bea te ma omi kiate ia, ‘o ma nofo'aga taha moia ; ”
bea ne toe fakababau ‘ae ha‘u ‘ae Laumalie Ma‘oni‘oni
ke taukabo'i kinautolu, bea ke fakamanatu ‘ene g.
tala, bea ke toe fai atu honau ako ‘i he me‘a kotoabe.
Bea koeha ha lea te tau fakamatala'aki ki he'enc
talatuku, “ Ko ‘eku ‘alu ‘eni kau tuku ha fiemalie
kiate kimoutolu ; ko ha fiemalie a‘aku ‘oku ou foakl
kiate kimoutolu ; ‘oku ‘ikai hage koe foaki ‘a mamani
a'eku foaki kiate kimoutolu. ‘Oua na‘a tuku ke
bubutu'u homou loto, ‘uma'a ha‘ane manavahe.”


Koe fa'ahiga lea ia ‘e ‘ikai ala fa‘u ‘e ha tagata; ka
‘oku hage ha hikuhikule‘o mei Lagi, ‘ae botu ‘oku
‘ikai ha mamahi, bea ‘oku noga ai ‘ae kakai ogojia.
Bea ne motuhi ai ‘enau talanoa ; he na‘a ne ogo‘i
kuo mei ta hono houa—‘ae houa o‘ene femilimilihi
moe ‘eiki ‘o mamani, ‘aia te ne laiki hono muiva'e.
Hage na‘a ne ogo'i ‘ae ha‘u ‘ae tevolo ko hono kumi,
‘o ne fekau ke nau tu‘u atu ke fakafetaulaki kiate ia.
(‘Oku kei toe be.)


KOE VAHE XII.
KOE BASIONE
Koe Mavae.
Koe aga ‘oe fai ‘oe Basova ‘e he kakai Jiu, na‘e
hiva'aki ‘ae g. same ni‘ihi ‘i he te‘eki te nau tutuku.
Koia, ‘i he tutu‘u ‘a Jisu moe Kau Abosetolo ke ‘alu,
na‘a nau hua leva ‘ae g. same koia ‘aia, ko h. cxvi.,
cxvii., cxvm.
Hei'ilo ki he Kau Abosetolo be na‘e fefe ‘ennu ‘ogo‘l
‘ae g. same koia; ka kuo bau ke mamafa kiate kinau-
tolu ‘ae kubu ni‘ihl, he ‘oku mahino na‘a nau ‘ilo ‘oku
tu'unuku mai ha kovi kiate kinautolu kotoa, kae
lahi ki honau takimu'a. Ka koe me‘a kia Jisu, koe
kubu fe na‘e ‘ikai o‘o ? ‘Ae lau ki he kabui ia ‘e he
g. kafa a Mate, mo ‘ene ‘ilo ki he tnamahi lahi; ‘a
‘ene tautaba ki he ‘Eiki: ‘ae tokoni na‘e fai, mo
‘ene fakafiemalie'aki hono laumalie; ‘ae lau ki he
fakahaofi o‘ene mo‘ui, mo ‘ene toe ha‘ele ‘i mamani—
koia tofu be ‘oku ne ‘amanaki ki ai. Kae‘uma‘a ‘ae
same ‘e taha—‘ene lau ki he kau ‘ae ‘Eiki, koia ‘e
‘ikai te te manavahe ki he tagata; ‘ae behe ke ‘oua
na‘a te falala ki he hou‘eikl; ‘ae behe ‘e ‘ikai teu
mate ka teu mo‘ui be: ‘ae lau ki hoto kiniji ‘e he


‘Eiki kae ‘ikai tamatefi: ‘ae lau ki he maka na‘e
li'aki ‘e he kau tufuga, mo ‘ene hoko koe maka tau-
‘oluga. ‘Oku ‘ikai ha fo‘i kubu ‘e ta'eogo ki he loto
‘o Jisu, bea koe fugani he me‘a ke teuteu‘aki hono
laumalie; he ko hono uho ‘oe g. same koia koe behe
‘oku kau ‘ae ‘Eiki mo kita. Kuo bau na‘e kilala‘aki
hono loto ‘ae hiva koia. ‘Oku mo'oni ‘oku ene mai
‘ae g. mamahi, ka koe g. me‘a kuo ‘oji mea‘i ‘e he
‘Eiki, bea te ne tauhi ia ‘i ai, he koe fakamamai be
ke lava ‘ae g. tu‘utu‘uni ‘a‘ene Tamai. Koia ‘i
he'ene a‘u ki he kubu faka‘oji ‘oe same, ‘aia koe behe,
“ Ha‘i ‘ae feilaulau ki he nifo ‘oe olita,” kuo bau na‘a
ne fai'aki hono loto kotoa, ‘o ne tebitebi atu ki hono
feia, ‘o hage koe lami feilaulau ni'ihi ‘oku talanoa ki
ai, ‘aia na‘e ‘ikai fiu‘a toho ‘e he kakai, ka na‘a nau
vekeveke ‘alu be ki he taula'eiki ke feia.
Koe hala ki he mo‘uga Olivo na‘e ‘alu ofi ki he
Temibale, bea toki hifo ki he Tele'a Kitilone. Bea, ‘i
he'enau ‘alu ai, na‘a nau mamata ki ha vaine.
Tokaage hano ‘uhiga ‘o‘enau tokaga ki ai. Na‘a ‘oku
tu‘u ofi ki he matanikolo ‘i ha va‘i ‘ata, bea fu‘u
mahino ‘i he huhulu ‘ae mahina, he ‘oku ‘ikai loko
mama ‘ae g. hala ‘o Selusalema koe‘uhi ko ‘ene faji'i.
Bea na‘a kuo nau tokaga ki ai koe lain hono lau, he
kuo te‘eki ke fakalau mai ‘ae g. akau. Bea nau
tokaga ‘oku lau kotoa ‘ae g. va‘a koe taha be ‘oku
‘ikai; bea, ‘i he‘enau vakai, ta, kuo tu'uji ‘e he
tagata ‘i ho'ene ‘auhani ‘ae vaine. Ka‘e lahi moe faga
ki‘i va‘a na‘e ‘auhani, ka kuo fokotu'u ia ki ha boto
ke tutu ai, kae kei ma‘u ha‘i be ‘ae va‘a koe, ne ogo
kuo motu. Bea fokotu'u ai ‘e Jisu ‘ene malaga.
“Koau koe Vaine Mo'onia, bea ko ‘eku Tamai koe
tauhigoue ia. Tioga ha va‘a ‘iate au ‘oku ‘ikai fua,


‘oku ne motuhi ia; bea ‘iloga ha va‘a ‘oku fua, ‘oku ne
‘auhani ia, ke ‘ajili ‘ene fua. . . Koau koe Yaine,
ko kimoutolu koe g. va‘a; ‘ai ke mou nofo ma‘u ‘iate
au; he, ka mavae mo au, ‘oku ‘ikai te mou fa‘a fai
ha me'a. Ka ai ha taha ne ‘ikai nofo ma‘u ‘iate au,
ne li‘aki atu hage koe va‘a na bea ne mae • bea ‘oku
nau tanaki ‘ae g. me‘a behe, ‘o laku ki he afi, bea
‘oku vela.”
‘ Oku vavana hotau loto ‘i he‘etau fanogo ki he g.
o O
lea koia, he ko Jiutasi ena kuo li‘aki atu; bea koe
kakai Jiu ena ‘oku ene ke motuhi. Bea, ne ogo na‘e
‘ikai mahino behe ki he Kau Abosetolo, ka na‘a nau
ogo‘i be ha me'a, bea ‘e ‘ajili mafatukituki ai houau
‘atamai.
Ka kuo ne lau ki he ‘auhani kinautolu ‘o he'ene
Tamai, koia ‘oku ne fai atu ke fakaha, koe fai be ‘i he
‘ofa kiate ia, koe'uhi ke ne lagilagi'ia ‘i he‘ene ma‘u
ha kau ako lelei. Bea ne toki lau ki he'ene ‘ofa a‘ana
kiate kinautolu: na‘a mo ‘ene mo‘ui ‘oku ‘ikai te ne
mamae ki ai; bea koia ‘e ‘ikai te ne kataki ke nau
tamaio'eiki kiate ia, ka te nau kaume'a be ; bea koe
me‘a ‘i he‘enau behe, te nau fa‘iteliha ki he koloa a'ene
Tamai. Ka ke nau manatu koe tu'uga faigata'a; he
koe fehi'anekina ia, bea te nau behe foki: ka koia
aibe, he koe fehi'anekina lelei. Bea ke ‘oua te nau
manavahe ki he'ene ‘alu, he ai hano fetogi ‘e ha‘u
mo’onau taukabo. Bea ne kamata lau ki he g. kovi
‘e hoko kiate kinautolu koe'uhi koia; ka, ‘i he‘ene
me‘a ki honau mata, na‘a ne vakai ‘e ‘ikai te nau ala
kataki, ‘o ne behe ke ma‘uii ‘ae talanoa koia.
Bea toki ogo‘i xnamahi ‘e hono aga tagata. Hono
ta'iga ‘ene lau ki he g. mamahi ‘oku ene ke to kiate
ia, ka hono fohu‘i ‘e ha taha be koeha 1 ‘Oku mo'oni


na‘e ‘ilo ‘e hono aga ‘otua ‘oku nau ‘ofa kiate ia, ka
na‘e tagi ‘e hono aga tagata ke ne mamata mo fanogo
ki ai. Seuke, kohai ‘e kataki ko talanoa mo hono g.
kaume'a ki ha 'u mamahi behe ‘oku ene ke to, kae
‘ikai ha'anau momo‘i tekia age?
Ka koe ki‘i mamahi fuonounou ia, bea na‘e lomia
ia ‘e he‘ene ‘ofa kiate kinautolu. Na‘a ne tala ke
‘oua te nan loto vaivai ‘i he‘ene lau ‘alu, he kabau ‘e
‘ikai te ne ‘alu, ‘e ‘ikai ha‘u ‘ae Taukabo ‘e taha ; bea,
no ogo ‘oku nau ‘ofa kiate ia, ka ‘e lelei lahiage ‘ae
Taukabo koia. Bea na‘a ne vakai honau loto, hage
‘oku nau behe, “ Oku mau fiema'u koe : ” koia na‘a ne
fakamatala ‘e tatau aibe mo ‘ene ‘i ai, he koe gaue ‘ae
Taukabo koia ke a‘au ‘ene g. me‘a a‘ana; bea koia ‘e
hage be ‘oku nau kei feagaiga. Hoto mate ‘ofa ki he
ogo fa‘ahi fakatou‘oji ‘i he‘enau talanoa ‘i he bo koe.
Ko J isu e, ‘oku ne feiga ke a‘au ‘ae g. me'a mamafa
kiate kinautolu, he ‘oku too ji‘i hono taimi. Bea koe
Kau Abosetolo e, ‘oku nau feiga ke tali ‘ene g. lea, ka
‘oku ‘ikai te nau matali, he ‘oku mafajia honau loto
‘i he ‘amanaki ki ha me'a, kae‘uma‘ii ko ‘ene g. lau—
tabu moia—na‘e mamafa, ‘o ta'choa mo honau ‘atamai:
bea na‘e hage ko ha mahua atu ha vai lahi ki ha hina
gutujhi. Kae hage kuo nau ma‘u eni ha me'a: ta,
‘oku ne ‘amanaki ‘alu kae ha‘u hono fetogi ‘o nau
nonofo ma‘u. Ka, ‘i he'enau lau kuo mahino ia, na‘a
nau toe bubutu'u ‘i he behe mai ‘e Jisu “ Toe ji‘i bea
‘e ‘ikai te mou milta au, bea toe ji‘i atu bea te mou
toe jio kiate au.”
Hoto ‘ofa ki he Kau Ako ! ta, ne‘ine‘i femuhumuhu'i
honau ni‘ihi, he na‘e hage koe lea ‘ae kau toutai, “ Oku
‘ikai ha taumu'a ‘e lau ! ” Bea nau behe ke fehu‘i ‘e
Me‘a—‘e Anitelu nai. Kae fanafana mai ia, “ E ‘ikai


teu lava ; fehu‘i koe, i'ilibe.” “A, ‘e ‘ikai teu lava :
neu ‘ahi‘ahi ‘anenai, ka hono jia‘a ! ” Bea na‘e mo'oni;
he na‘e matu‘utu‘utamaki ‘enau g. fehu‘i kotoa ‘i he
bo kola. ‘lloage kuo lea mai ‘a Jisu ki he me‘a ‘oku
‘i honau loto, ‘o ne fakamatala ki he “ toe ‘ o ne
‘ai ke mahino kiate kinautolu ‘ene ‘alu mo ‘ene toe
ha‘u, bea ko ‘ene hau koia ‘e fu‘u fakahikihiki‘l ai
kinautolu.
Bea ofo ai ‘ae Kau Ako ‘i he‘ene ‘ilo ki he g. me‘a
‘oku ‘i honau loto, bea ake fo‘ou ai ‘enau tui kiate ia.
Kae‘uma‘a na‘a nau ma‘u ‘ae lea ‘a Jisu, hage koe
behe te ne toe foki mai koe Misaia, ‘o fokotu‘u ‘ae
Bule‘aga; bea nau tala kiate ia “ Kuo fu‘u mahino
eni, bea ‘oku mau tui kiate koe.”
‘Oku tau ‘ilo kuo kuo nau toe hala, bea na‘e mea‘i ‘e
Jisu : ka koe‘uma‘a ke fa'olaki me‘a ki honau loto, he
‘oku ‘ikai te nau lava ha me‘a ‘i he taimi ni. Koia
na‘a ne tuku ; ka ne fakatonutonu ‘enau he ‘i he‘ene
behe, “Oku mou tui koa eni? Talaatu ‘e vetekina
kimoutolu taki taha ki hono ‘abi ‘o tuku au toko
taha.” Bea ne toki kelesi‘aki ‘ene talanoa ‘ae fo‘i lea
malie koeni, “ I mamani ‘oku mou ma‘u fakamamahi:
ka mou lototo'a, kuou ikuna ‘a mamani ‘eau.”
Koe aga ‘i babalagi ; ka fai ha folau be ha fonoga
mama‘o, ka ‘oji fai ‘e he tagata‘eiki ‘ene na‘ina‘i mo
‘ene tatau ki hono famiii mo kinautolu ‘e lele‘o, ‘oku
ne tu‘ulutui ke fai ha lotu, ‘o tuku hono ‘abi ki he
‘Eiki. Bea na‘e behe mo Jisu. Kuo ‘oji ‘ene lea
tuku ki he‘ene Kau Ako, bea ne haga hake ki he lagi,
‘o ne tuku kinautolu ki he ‘Otua. Koe lotu ka ko
ha lotu ! hage na‘e toki fanogo ai ‘e he tagata ki
he fefolofola‘i ‘ae ‘Afilio. Na‘e ‘ikai te ne hiki hono
nima, ‘o hage koe fa‘a fai ‘e he kakai, ‘aia koe faka-


‘aba'aba moe kole; bea koe fa‘ahiga lea na‘a ne gaue-
‘aki, ‘aia koe alea ha ogo me‘a ‘oku tatau. Ne‘ine‘i
o‘o ‘i he loto ‘o Jione, he koe aga ‘o hono atamai ke
kebi ‘ae g. lea kotoabe ‘a Jisuna‘ekau ki he'ene tubu
fakalagi, kae‘uma‘a ‘ena feagaiga mo 1 ene Tamai. Kola
na‘a ne tali habo ‘ae g. lea, ‘o tohi ma'atautolu. Ka
ko hono toe ‘oe Kau Ako na‘e to‘oa honau loto ‘i he g.
lea na‘eogo mai, kae ‘ikai te nau teitei a‘ujia ha me'a
ka nau mo‘u ofoofoa be. Ji‘i tu‘u ‘ae Tagata'eiki ena
‘oku ne alea moe ‘Otua ‘o Lagi, ‘o lau ki he'ene ma‘u
‘ae bule kotoabe ‘o mamani, moe lea ‘ene ‘afio ‘i lagi
te‘eki ke tu‘u ‘a mamani ! ‘Oiseukeseuke ! ta ‘oku
‘ikai ‘aubito ko hono aga eni. Bea nau kamata ogo‘i
‘ene makehe. Ka na‘a ne toe ofi mai ‘i he‘ene hufia
kinautolu na‘a ne fai —ke tauhi kinautolu ke
matauhi, bea ke fakatabu‘i kinautolu ke nau hoko
koe koto fakatabu‘l. Bea toe hage ha fanaga ‘ene
lau te nau malaga ki mamani, bea mo ‘enau taha moe
Tamai hage koia. Talu e tu‘u ‘a mamani ko ‘ene
toki tau e ki he teliga ‘o ha mama ha fa'ahiga lea
behe. Ka koe lea turnutumu ‘oe lotu ‘aeni : “ Ala
Tamai, koe me'a kuo ke foaki mai, ko hoku loto ki ai;
koebotu ‘oku ou ‘iai au ke nau ‘i ai ‘akinautolu, foki,
mo au, ke nau jiofia ‘ae lagilagi a‘aku, ‘aia kuo ke
foaki mai; he na‘a ke ‘ofa kiate au ‘i he te'eki ke
tanu bou ‘a mamani.” Kohai ‘e fakamatala ke
mahu igamalie ‘ae fo‘i lea koia? ‘Ae “Ko hoku loto
ki ai”—‘oku hage koe hikuhikule'o oe lea ‘i Senesi,
“ Ha'u ke tau gaohi tagata.”
Bea koeni kuo fai ‘ene lea faka'oji, bea kuo ne
tuku ki he‘ene Tamai ‘ae tauhi ‘o hono takaga. Kuo
‘oji ‘a mamani kiate ia. Koia na‘a ne uiage ‘ene Kau


Ako, ‘o nau kamata laka hifo ki Kitilone, koe ‘alu ki
he botu ‘o hono lavaki'i. Bea ne manatu ai kuo
te'eki ha'ane tu‘utu‘uni kiate kinautolu ki ha botu te
nau fakataha ki ai hili ‘ene toetu'u ; koia na‘a ne
behe ai kiate kinautolu, “ Kuo tohi, ‘ Teu ta‘i ‘ae tauhi
bea ‘e movete ‘ae faga sibi kuo ne tauhi ’; ka, ‘oka
hili ‘eku fokotu‘u, teu mu‘omu‘a kiate kimoutolu ki
Kaleli.”
Lau ‘eau ‘e mamafa kia Bita ae g. lea kuo ne toki
fanogo ki ai, bea te ne ogo‘i hono ‘otua ‘o Jisu, ‘o
‘ouae fakatau‘i lea age. Kae kei jio fakamama ia,
‘o ne lau koe Misaia be; bea ne behe, nai, ‘oku tau
moia ke lagomekina ‘ae Kau Ako, he ko honau mata-
bule ia : koia na‘a ne tali ki he lea ‘a Jisu, ‘o ne behe
kiai, “ Ne ogo ‘e tukia kotoabe bate koe, ka koau ‘e
‘ikai teu tukia ‘o ta'egata.”
Bea toe tala ‘e Jisu, ‘o hage ko ‘one lea ‘i fale ‘i he
‘ohomohe, te ne fakafijiga ia ‘anai; be ne fakababau,
foki, hon > taimi ‘o behe, Ka u‘ua ‘ae moa hono tu‘o
ua, kuo tu‘o tolu ‘ene fakafijiga.
Bea nafui ‘e Bita ‘ene lau ‘e ‘ikai ‘aubito lava; te
ne mate mu‘a ; bea kau ai kotoa moe Kau Ako, ‘e
‘ikai ‘aubito te nau kakuga ke fai ha me‘a behe.
‘Oiaue ‘ae fekohub ‘enau lau, ka ko Ketisemani ena
‘oku kite mai, moe ha ki he finagalo ‘oe ‘Eiki ‘ae hola
kalekaleaki te nau fai ‘anai ‘i he hala koe ‘oku ha na.
Maumau ‘ae mavae ‘i he lea ‘afugi koia ; ka ka
faka‘atu‘i kinautolu ‘e he ‘Eiki, he na‘a ne mea‘i
honau aga, ‘o ‘ikai ha‘ane valoki ‘e fai.
[‘Oku kei toe he.)


KOE VAHE XIII,
KOE BASIONE.
Ko Ketisemani.
Na‘e tafe ha ki‘i vai ‘i he vaha'a ‘o Selusalema mo
Olive ‘i he taimi koia. Na‘e ui ko Kitilone, bea, ‘i
he'enau laka ai, na‘a nau a‘u leva ki he g. goue olive.
Koe botu ia na‘a nau ma'uga nofo ki ai, bea tokaage
ha g. talanoa malie kuo nau fai ‘i he 1010 ‘akau na.
He koe ala botu behe na‘a ne manako ke ha'ele ki
ai, (‘o hage ko ‘ene manako ke ha‘ele faka-‘otua ‘i he
‘uluaki gouetabu ‘i he hauhaufano ‘oe ‘aho) he na‘e
ha ki ai ‘a Selusalema, kae ‘ikai ha hono kovi; ko
hono masani be mo hono gali ‘eiki, ‘o tau moe
kolohau ‘oe Tu‘i Lahi. ‘Oku ‘ikai te tau ‘ilo be koe
goue ‘ahai, ke koe gouetabu; bea tu‘u ai ha bubuga
‘akau olive, bea kuo gaohi ai ha tata‘oaga-1010, ‘aia
na‘e tubu ai hono higoa ko Ketisemani, “ koe
tata‘oaga-lolo.”
Bea kuo nau hu ki he goue, na‘a ne ogo'i ‘ae
kamata hoko ha me‘a ki hono loto, ‘o hage koe ‘ilo ‘e
Natula ‘ae kamata ke mate ‘ae la‘a ; bea ne behe ki
he'ene Kau Ako, “ Mou nofo heni, kau ‘alu ji‘i ki he
‘o lotu. Bea mou lotu, foki, ke ‘oua na‘a mou hu ki
ha ‘ahi‘ahi.” Bea ne ui age ‘ae toko toiu na‘a ne
bele'aki, ‘a Bita mo Semesi mo Jione, ‘o nau toe taha


atu ki he luto-goue; bea, ‘i he laka atu ‘a Jisu, na‘e
fakautuutu ‘ae mamahi ‘o hono loto. ‘Oku hage na‘e
te‘eki ko mahino kiate ia bo koeha : koe me‘a be,
na‘a ne ogo‘i ha fu‘u mamahi. ‘Oku tau behe be
kitautolu—kehe ‘oku ‘i ai ha ni‘ihi ‘oku vavaga ki ha
kovi ‘oku tu‘unuku mai. Tokaage ha ‘aho ‘oku
mafajia ‘aubito honau loto ta‘e hano‘ uhiga; ka, ‘i he
‘abogibogi, ‘oku nau fanogo ‘oku ‘i ai ha tu‘utamaki
kuo hoko. ‘Oku hage ‘oku ‘i ai ha'atau me‘a —be
koe atamai be koe laumalie—‘oku ogogofua ki he
ta‘ehamai, ‘0 hage ‘oku ‘ilo ‘e he tala ki he matagi
kei mama'o. Behe na‘e ogo‘i ha me‘a ‘e he g. ulugaaga
‘o Jisu na‘e taubofcu atu ki he ‘Otua, ka kuo te‘eki a‘u
mai ki hono ‘atamai ke mahino.
Ka behe ha me‘a, ‘oku tagi hotau aga ki hakaiga
ke fakalelulelu mai; koia na‘e behe ‘e Jisu ki he toko
tolu, “ ‘Oku mamahi fu‘u hoku laumale ‘0 hage ka
mate; mou tatali ‘i heni ‘o fe‘ao mo au.” Kane ogo
‘e fiema‘u kinautolu ‘e hono aga tagata, ka na‘a ne ‘ilo
‘oku ‘ikai te nau fe'uga ke tokoni kiate ia; ko ‘ene
Tamai be te ne lava. Koia na‘a ne toe ‘unu‘unu atu
ki he loto-goue, ‘o ne ofa'aki ‘ene lotu. Ka na‘e
‘ikai ke momo‘i ma‘u ha fiemalie, ka na‘e fakautuutu
be ‘ene mamahi.
Bea na‘e kamata ha, foki, hono ‘uhiga. Kuo ne ‘ilo
fuoloa kuo bolo‘i ia koe Lami ke ‘ave ‘ae agahala ‘a
Mamani; bea, ta, kuo hokojia ‘ae taimi ke hilifaki mai
‘ae g. hia koia. Kuo tu‘o lain ‘ene mamata ki ai ‘i he
Temibale —‘ae hilifaki ‘e he Taula'eiki hono nima ki
he manu, hono vete ‘oe hia ‘ae kakai kotoabe, moo
hoko leva ‘ae manu koe me‘a agahala‘ia, bea faka'ehi-
ehi mei ai ‘ae kakai kotoabe, na‘a nau lave ki ai ‘o
‘uli. Bea nei‘ine‘i mafatukituki hono loto, he ‘oku


fai ‘ae hilifaki kiate ia ‘oe hia ‘a mamani katoa—‘ae
g. fakabo, ‘ae g. fakalielia, ‘oe kakai ‘i mu‘a moe
kakai ‘i mui, ‘o lau kotoa kiate ia, ‘aia ‘oku ne
fakalili'a ki he kovi ‘o hage ‘oku tau fakalili‘a ki ha
me‘a raousa'a age fau. Ne‘ine‘i mamahi ‘i he‘ene
ogo‘i ‘oku gaohi ia koe me'a agahala, bea na‘a mo ‘ene
Tamai ‘oku ne faka‘ehi‘ehi meiate ia !
Ka‘e ‘ikai te ne loko mama‘o mei he toko tolu—
na‘a nau lau kimui na‘e fe‘uga moe liji‘aga-maka
bea na‘e ogo mai 'ene g. to‘e mo ‘ene fa‘a tautaba.
Na‘e lahi ‘ene lea na‘e fai, ka koe me‘a na‘e fa‘a fai,
koe kole ki he‘ene Tamai ke fakalaka ‘ae ibu, ‘o
kabau ‘e lava; kae ‘ikai fai ki hono loto. Koe lea
fakatata, ka na‘e ‘ilo ‘e he Jiu kotoa hono ‘uhiga,
koe lau ki ha mamahi ‘oku tu'unuku mai, moe kole
ke ‘oua na‘a hoko. Ka‘e mate ‘ofa ‘ae toko tolu ki
honau ‘eiki, bea nau faka‘amu ke ‘aoga kiate ia; ka
na‘e ‘ikai te nau hlo be koeha ‘ae mamahi ‘oku lau,
bea nau ogo‘i ‘e ‘ikai te nau lava ha tokoni. Bea
lolotoga ‘enau ‘unaloto, na‘a nau vakai ‘oku ‘i ai ha
taha ‘oku ne holoholo hono lo‘i fofoga, mo tokoni
kiate ia. Na‘a nau ‘ilo ‘oku ‘ikai koe Mama, ka koe
agelo be, bea nau manatu na‘e fai behe foki kiate ia
‘i ne hoko hono fu‘u ‘ahi‘ahi ‘i he toafa, bea nau
fiefia.
Bea, ‘i he fiemalie honau loto, na‘a nau tulemohe,
he kuo fuoloa ‘ae bo‘uli, bea kuo nau ogojia ‘i he
gaue ‘aho. ‘lloage na‘a nau ofo hake, ta, ko Jisu ena
kuo ne fafagu kinautolu ; bea nau ma. Bea haga
‘eia kia Bita, ‘o ne fakamanatu mai ‘ene bolebole
‘anenai ‘i he hifoga mei Selusalema, he‘ene behe, “ E
Saimone, ‘oku ke mohe koa ? ‘Oku ‘ikai te ke lava
ke ‘a ‘o houa taha? Le‘o be mo lotu, ke ‘oua na‘a


mou bu ki ha ‘ahi‘ahi. ‘Oku loto be ‘a laiimalie ke
fai, ka ‘oku vaivai ‘a kakano,”
Bea toe me‘a atu ‘a Jisu ki he botu, bea nofo hake
‘ae Kau Abosetolo ‘o mamata. Bea bage na‘e
fakautuutu ‘ene feiga. Tokaage ha taimi te ne
mabe'e ki be kelekele, ‘o to‘e be mo lotu ; bea, bili ia,
te ne haga ki be la gi, ‘o tautaba ki be‘ene Tamai, ka
ko ‘ene lea na‘e fa‘a ogo mai na‘e behe, “ Ala, Tamai,
kabau ‘e ‘ikai lava ke tolona eni, ka ‘i be‘eku inu ia,
bea ke fai ho finagalo.” Bea bage na‘e toki tataha
mai ‘ae ha‘aha‘a o‘ene mamahi, bea gafuhia bono
loto, ‘o ‘ikai te ne kei lava ke lea; bea, ‘i he‘ene
fakalogo, na‘e ogo mai ‘ae vagana ‘ae g. tuluta ki he
kelekele. Bea ‘ilbage na‘a ne haga hake, bea hulu'ia
bono fofoga ‘i be mabina, bea nau vakai ‘oku bani
ta‘ata‘a —ta, ‘oku ne tauta'a ta‘ata‘a !
‘Oku ‘ikai koe me'a ia ‘oku fa‘a boko, ka ‘oku ‘i ai
ba ni‘ihi kuo fai behe ‘oka fu‘u labi fau ‘enau feiga—
koe fakabloga ia ‘oe mamahi taubotu. Tokua, ‘oku
ai ha gata ‘i Amelika Saute, ‘aia ‘oku behe ‘ae
fakamamabi o‘ene u‘u. ‘Oku buna ‘ae toto ‘i'he kili
‘oe kakai, ‘o fijiki kitu'a ‘o bage ha bubuha ‘i
he'enau mamahi, Bea kuo hukia ‘a Jisu ‘e he Gata
koe agahala, bea ko bono o e ‘ae ta‘ata‘a ‘oku
gagana. Ke‘ine‘i ui koe “ Tagata ‘oe gahi mamahi.”
Faifai bea malonolona hifo, bea ha‘u ‘a Jisu ke
talanoa mo ‘ene Kau Ako, mo fakafiemalie ji‘i mo
kinautolu, he na‘a ne ‘ilo koe fakatofutofu be kae toe
hiko. Fakabo kuo nau toe mohe. ‘Oku tau ‘ilo koe
fu‘u hoka ia ki he finagalo ‘oe ‘Eiki : ka na‘a ne
faka‘atu‘i be ‘ae vaivai bonau kakano, ‘o ‘ikai
ha‘ane tautea ‘e fai; ka na‘a nau fu‘u ma be, ‘o ‘ikai
te nau lava ke tali ‘ene lea. Bea ogo‘i ‘e Jisu ‘oku


vave be ‘ae toe hoko mai ‘ae mamahi, ‘o ne toe ‘alu
‘o lotu. Bea hei'ilo be koe ji‘i ‘oe ‘ae Kau Ako
(he na‘a nau toe mohe), ka ‘oku ha mei he'enau
fakamatala hage na‘e ma‘ama‘a ‘ae mamahi ‘i hono
tu‘o tolu mai. Kehe be koe me‘a be ‘oku tau ‘ilo ki
ai ko ‘ene fai'aki aibe ‘a‘ene lotu, “Ke fai be Ho
finagalo.” ‘Oiaue ji‘i Jisu ! ‘E lauga mamahi ki
ho‘o mamahi ? Na‘e ‘ikai ko ho‘o fakamajiva'i mo
ho‘o gaue ogojia ‘i mamani na‘a ke ogo‘i, bea na‘a mo
ho li‘aki ‘e he kakai koe mamahi ji‘i be, he na‘e
buna ai ‘ae lo‘i fofoga be. Koeni be ‘ae mamahi, ‘ae
lau Koe koe agahala, moe mahu'i ai ho‘o Tamai
meiate koe. Koe mamahi koia ‘e ‘ikai mafakamatala.
Kuo tau ogo‘i ji‘i ‘e hotau ni'ihi, ‘i he lau kitautolu
koe kaiha'a be koe fakabo, bea tafoki ai ‘ae kakano
‘o hoto manava ‘o fehi'a mai; ka na‘a tau kataki, he
ua‘e tokoni mai ‘ae ‘Otua. Ka ko Jisu na‘e li‘aki ‘e
he'enc Tamai ‘i Lagi, bea mohe hono takaga ‘i
mamani. Mo‘oni ‘ae lea ‘ae Balofita ‘i he'ene
kikite,
“• Kuou fai toko taha be ‘i he tata'oaga.”
{‘Oku kei toe be.]


KOE YAHE XIV,
KOE BASIONE,
Koe Lavaki.
Ne ogo kuo ta tu‘o ua honu fafagu ‘e he ‘Eiki, ka ‘i
he‘ene toe ha‘u kiate kinautolu kuo nau toe mohe be.
‘Oku tau fehi'a ki ai, he ‘ikai ko kinautolu koe ha‘a
fili mei mamani katoa ke fai ‘ae fakafe‘ao moia ‘i
he'ene mamahi 2 Ka ke tau manatu ‘oku ‘ikai koe
gaue ia ‘ae tagata : koe nafa be ia ‘a fafine; bea ‘oku
te tui, ka ne ta‘e‘oua koe me‘a fakabo‘uli ‘i he 1010
‘akau, kuo ne fili ki he gaue koia ‘e Mele mo Maata,
bea kuo na ‘a noabe. Koai na‘e ‘ikai valoki kinau-
tolu ‘e Jisu, ka ne behe, “ Mohe aibea eni mo malolo.”
Kuo mahili. Kuo ‘oji ‘ae mamahi, bea koe‘uma‘a
‘enau kei ‘a. Na‘e behe ‘ene faka‘atu‘i kinautolu.
Kae lolotoga ‘ene lea, na‘a ne ogo'i ‘oku logologo
tagata kiate ia; ta, ‘oku ha‘u hono lavaki: bea ne
fafagu leva ‘ae kau tagata ka nau ‘a. Bea nau 6ke
vakai hono toe ‘oe Kau Abosetolo na‘a mo'utamakia
kinautolu ‘oku nau kei mohe. Bea, ‘i he‘enau oh ki
he mataba ‘oe goue, na‘e fotu mai ha fu‘u fonoga.
Koe kau tau Loma eni ‘oku to‘o heleta, ‘aia na‘e
fetabaki ‘i he mahina; bea mu‘omu‘a mai ‘ae kau


bolisi na‘e tauhi ‘ae Temibale ‘oku nau faka'akau,
bea ‘alu ‘i tafa‘aki mo tafa‘aki ‘ae kau tamaio‘eiki ‘ae
kau Taula'eiki; bea to‘o mama ha ni‘ihi, he, ne ogo
‘oku huhulu ‘ae mabina, ka na‘e fakabo'uli ‘ae goue
koe lolo‘akaua —bea fakabo! ko Jiutasi ‘oku taki-
hala !
Tokua, kuo fa‘ufa‘ufono ‘ae jiana koia moe kau
bolisi ke nau jio be kiate ia, bea ‘iloga ia te ne ‘uma
ki ai, ko Jisu ia. Bea tetaimu'a leva ia, ‘o hu ki he
goue ke ajiaji be ‘oku ‘i ai ‘a Jisu; bea, ka ‘ikai leva
te ne jio ki ai, bea nau movete atu ‘o kabui ae botu,
kae kumi ‘e ha ni‘ihi. Koe tu‘utu‘uni boto, nai, kae
hage koia ‘oku fa‘a hoko ‘i he fai agahala ‘ae kakai,
na‘e matu‘utu‘utamaki ‘ene tu‘utu‘uni koe to‘oa, nai,
hono loto be ha. He ko ‘ene mamata leva kia Jisu
‘o ‘ikai te ne tatali ke ofi mai ‘ae kau bolisi, ka ne
‘ohofua leva ke ‘uma ki ai, ‘o ne behe, “ Labai,
ji‘oto‘ofa/’ Bea, ‘i he'ene fai kia Jisu, hage na‘e
fakateteke ‘eia ‘ene behe, “ Jiutasi, koe ‘uma koa ‘oku
ke lavaki‘i‘aki ‘ae Fanautama ‘a Tagata 1 ” Lau
‘ekita kuo ne tuku ‘i he lea koia, ka ka buke atu be
‘eia ‘ae ‘ulu ‘o Jisu, ‘o ne ‘uma lolomi kiate ia. Koe
fakamatala ia ‘a Matiu mo Bita, ‘aia na‘a na tutu'u
‘o ofogi ‘ae me'a ‘oku fai. Na‘e ‘ikai ko ha ‘uma
fe'iloaki, ka koe ‘uma ki hoto ‘ofa'aga—be koe tamai
ki hono foha—‘aia na‘a ne fai. ‘Oiau ‘ae kataki ‘ae
‘Eiki ! Be koeha na‘e ‘ikai te ne to ‘o mate ai leva !
Kuobau na‘e gaue ‘ae loto ‘o Jisu ‘o a‘u ki he uho ‘o
hono finagalo ; ka ne fakama‘uma‘u be, ‘o ne behe
“ Jiana, koe me‘a kuo ke ha‘u ai —” Hei'ilo be na‘a
ne ‘amanaki faka‘oji fefe ‘ene lea koia. Kuo mahalo
‘e he ni‘ihi ko ‘ene fakaha ‘ae vavana ‘a hono loto ‘i
hekaka taubotu ni; ka koe lea ‘oku kamata'aki,


“ Jiana,” ‘oku jio ki he’ena kaugagaue, ‘o hage ‘oku
ne fie fakamanatu ki he‘ena kaume'a fuoloa, hei‘ilo te
ne fakatomala. Ka koia aibe ha me‘a na‘e ‘i hono
finagalo, he na‘e ‘ikai te ne lava ke faka‘oji, he ‘oku
gatata mai ‘ae fonoga, bea ‘oho ki tua'a ‘a Jiutasi ke
fakafetaulaki ki ai, ‘o tala ko Jisu eni. Bea manavahe
‘ae ‘Eiki na‘a nau hu mai ki loto, ‘o ma‘u ai mo ‘ene
Kau Ako. Koia na‘a ne tebitebi atu ki he mataba, ‘o
hu‘ki tu‘a ke fakabinebine; bea muimui ki ai ‘a bita
mo Jione (mo Semesi, nai), ‘o tutu'u ‘i he mataba.
‘Oku hage na‘e momou ‘ae fu‘u fonoga ‘i he‘enau
mamata kiate ia. ‘Oku tau ‘ilo kuo fagailube ki
hihifo ‘ae mahina, bea, ‘i he‘ene hu mai ki tua'a, ‘e
fa‘aki tonu hono mama kiate ia, bea te ne fu'u e‘a
kiate kinautolu. ‘Oku tau ‘ilo ko Jisu koe mo‘onia‘i
tagata, bea, ka tu‘u mai ha taha behe, ‘oku a‘aba ki
ho'otautolu loto. Kae‘uma‘a ko hotau aga ‘oku ‘i ai
ha tagata ‘oe kovi; bea, ka boko hono ‘aho, ‘oku hao
ai. Bea na‘e hao ‘a Jisu ‘i he bo koia. Ko hono
jino ia, bea, ‘iloage, na‘a ne haga hake, ‘o hulu‘ia hono
fofoga ‘i he mahina. ‘Oi! kuo bani ta‘ata‘a —koe
bolo kuo tau ! Talaatu, ne vai honau loto he to atu
hono geia.
Fokifa kuo ne folofola mai, “ Kohai ‘oku mou
kumi ki ail” ‘Oku ha meia Jione na‘a ne fai behe
ke mahino ‘oku ‘ikai tu‘u ‘ae Kau Abosetolo ‘i he tohi
fekau. Bea na‘a mo'oni, ko Jisu be kuo tuku atu ki
ai ‘ae kaate ‘e Bailato, ka na‘a nau ‘amanaki, nai, ke
buke honau kotoa. Ka, ‘i he ‘eke behe ‘e Jisu, na‘e
tali ‘e he ‘eikitau, “Ko Jisu mei Nasaleti.” Folofola
mai ‘eia, “ KOAU ! ” ‘Oiseukeseuke ! ‘ae ba atu ‘ae
lea koia ! Na‘e hage ha taba mai ‘a ha ‘uhila, ‘o ne
tulekina ha fu‘u ‘akau, he na‘e holomui mai ‘ae fu'u


fonoga kotoa ‘o fo'ohake. ‘Oku ‘ikai te tau ofo ai,
he ‘ikai koe huafa tobutabu ia ‘oe ‘Otua? bea oku
tui ‘e mamani katoa ‘oku ‘i ai ha niana ‘oe ‘Otua ‘oku
omo hono huafa. Vakaiage ! Ko ‘enau ha‘u, tokua,
ke buke ia; bea ko ‘ene ki‘i faka‘ataage hono ‘otua
ke ‘aji mai, koe kemo kuo nau mabe‘e fua ki lalo.
Bea tala‘ehai koe fai ma'ana, ka koe ‘aofaki be ‘o
ji‘ono g. kaume'a. ‘Oku fakaofo ‘ae fakamatala ‘a
Jione. ‘Oku hage na‘a ne tu‘u ‘o jiofi ‘a Jiutasi, ‘o ne
faka‘amu, nai, ke fai ha me‘a ki ai, ‘o hage ko ‘ene fie
tubutubulefanua ke to mai ha afi ‘o fakamomofi ‘ae kau
Samelia. Bea, ‘iloage, ‘i he ba atu ‘ae folofola ‘ae ‘Eiki,
na‘a ne yakai ‘oku ‘oho ‘a Jiutasi, ‘o hage kuo fana'i,
‘o ne buna ki mui ‘o to fo'ohake, bea ‘alu atu mei ai
‘ae me‘a (be koeha) ki honau kotoa, ‘o nau fo'okake.
Bea, ‘i he'enau tu‘u hake, na‘a ne toe fehu‘i kiate
kinautolu, be kohai ‘oku nau kumi ki ai. Bea toe
tali mai, “Ko Jisu me Nasaloti.” Bea toe ‘ai atu ‘e
Jisu ‘ae lea, “ KOATJ,” kae ‘ikai ‘ata‘ata be, ‘o hage
koe ‘anenai, ka ne hu‘ihu‘i ‘aki ‘ae g. lea kehe,
kae‘uma‘a na‘a ne behe, ‘ Kabau ko au ‘oku mou kumi
ki ai, bea tukuage ‘ae tu'uga me‘a ni ke ‘alu.’ ‘Oiau
‘ae ‘ofa ‘a Jisu, mo ‘ene boto, foki, he‘ene ‘ai ke mahino
mai ‘oku ‘ikai ke kau ‘ae Kau Ako ‘i he tohi-fekau.
Bea hono ‘ikai gali foki ! Ta‘etau ke lavaki‘i‘aki ha
‘uma, hage koe kaka‘i ‘o Samisoni ‘e he fefine ko
Tilila. ‘Oku mo‘uni na‘e fai ‘ae ‘uma moe Lavaki, ka
na‘e ‘ikai jia‘a ‘enau tauhele, bea ko ‘enau ‘ilo ia ko
‘ene fakaha be ‘eia. Koe faigata'a ‘oe gaue ‘a Jisu
ko ‘ene falute ‘ae g. lakaga. Mo'oni kuo na alea
moe Tamai ke ne lami, ka ko hono lakaga ke ne
laione, foki. Bea koia na‘e ‘ikai ta ne tuku ke nau
‘oholulu mai, ‘o buke noabe ia, ka ne tomu'a ha‘aki


kotoa, ‘o ne told fehulunakinima, ‘o ne behe, KOAU
eni; mou ‘ave. Hono ‘ikai gali !
Ka ‘oku te'eki ke mahino ‘ae me‘a koia ki hono g.
fili, be ki hono kaiga. Na‘e ‘unu'unu mai leva e, ‘i
he'enau ‘ilo kuo hiki hono geia, ke nan ala kia Jisu ;
bea ‘oho leva ‘a Bita ke teke'i, ‘o ne unuhi ‘ene heleta
ho'ene behe, “ ‘Eiki, ka man ta.” Ka, ‘i he ala leva
ha taha ki hono ‘Eiki, na‘e ‘ikai te ne matatali, ‘o ne
tataha leva. Hoto ‘ofa ki he matabule ‘oka ne laine
mo Jisu ‘a Bita, he tala'ehai koe taha ia ke fakanene
‘ene ta : ka kuo tau ‘ilo kuo ne ‘i hono takafalu bea
te ne ta fakalaka mai ‘ia Jisu, ‘aea na‘e mo'ua ai
hono teliga. Na‘e ‘ikai ‘ilo ‘e Bita koe toko taha
tabu kuo ne te‘ia —ka ne ‘ilo ‘e tatau aibe —ka na‘e
vakai ‘e Jione ko Malikusi koe tamaio‘eiki ‘ae Taula-
‘eiki-lahi, he ‘oku ne fa‘a ma'uga ki he fale o'ene
‘eiki. Kane ogo ia, ka na‘a ne tagane'ia ‘i he fai ‘a
Bita, bea ‘i he'ene talanoa ki ai kimui na‘a ne behe,
“‘A Maka foki! ” Seuke ! kuo ne fai moia ha me‘a ka
ne ‘i ai ha‘ane heleta Bea kohai ‘e behe na‘e kovi
‘ae gaue ‘a Bita 1 ‘Oku mo‘oni na‘e me‘a mai leva ‘e
he ‘ Eiki ke ne fakafoki ‘ae heleta ki hono ‘aiga, kae
tuka be ke ne inu ‘ae ibu kuo teu ‘e he‘ene Tamai.
Bea ‘oku ma'oni na‘e tau, nai, ke ‘ilo ‘e Bita na‘e
faigofua kiate ia ke ma‘u ha g. kogakau agelo ke
malu'i ia ; ka na‘e ‘ikai ‘a Bita ia. Kabau na‘e fie
kataki ‘e he ‘ Eiki ko ha‘ae ‘Eiki ia; ka ko Bita koe
matabule ‘oe tiikaga, bea ko hono lakaga ke ‘aofi ‘ae
‘Eiki. ‘Oku te fakafeta‘i kita koe ‘i ai ‘a Bita, bea
ne fai hono nafa, he koe ma'aga ia ‘o mamani ‘oka
ne to ‘etau Eanautama, kae ‘ikai ha taha ke ‘ahi ahi
‘aofi. Tonuhia ‘ae ‘Eiki ‘ene fie mate noa; tonuhia
‘a Bita ‘ene feiga ke ta‘ofi.


Kuo ma‘u buke eni ‘a Jisu ; ka ‘i he'ene vakai ki
he fetafei ‘ae teliga ‘o Malikusi, na‘a ne hamuji age
hono nima he'ene behe, ‘ Tukuji'i age kae'oua ke lava
eni’; ‘o ne ala ki he lau‘i teliga, ‘o mo‘ui leva
‘Oiseukeseuke ‘ae lotoma‘u ‘a Jisu ! Mo ene aga ‘e
taha foki. Koe f aho koe ne ne fakatatau ai ia ki he
motu‘a moa ‘oku fie malu'i hono fagaga ‘i hono
kabakau, ka koe ‘aho ni ‘oku ne matu‘aki fai ‘ae
‘ulugaaga ‘oe motu'a mo‘a he‘ene ‘oho mai ‘o taukohi
‘ae fili, kae hao ‘ene fanau. He, fe‘uga moia, ne hola
‘ene Kau Ako koe mahino ‘e ‘ikai lava ha me‘a. Bea
na‘e ‘ikai te ne ‘ita, kae kehe, na‘a ne kamata ke
fakaleaage ki he hou‘eiki moe kakai be koehi kuo
nau ha‘u moe mahafu ke buke ia, he koe kaiha'akau 2
—‘o behe mo behe, ko ji‘ene fakatalanoa‘i kinautolu
kae ‘oua ke mama'o atu ‘ene Kau Ako. Kane
tae'oua ia ne ma‘u kinautolu, he, ‘i he ‘iloagena'a nau
jio ki ha taha ‘oku matamata kau mo Jisu, na‘a nau
buke leva ki ai. ‘Oku ‘ikai tala hono higoa, ka kuo
bau ko Lasalosi, he na‘a ne nofo ‘i he mo'uga koia,
bea kuo ne fanogo ki he maveuveu, ‘o ne lele hifo ke
vakai be koeha. Bea, ‘i ho'ene ‘ilo ko ji‘ono ‘ofa'aga
‘oku taki atu, na‘a ne muimui ki ai. Ka‘e ‘iloga koe
tubenu ‘oku ne bulubulu'aki, he ko hono feta'u (he
talu ‘ene toetu'u mo ‘ene ‘ai ma'ube ia) bea kuo
fekau ‘e he hou‘eiki ke nau ‘ahi‘ahi ke ma‘u ‘a
Lasalosi. Koia ni‘a nau ala leva ‘o buke hono
bulubulu ; ka ka li‘aki ia ‘eia, ‘o ne hola hake ki he
mo'uga. Bea, ‘i he'ene ‘alu ‘ana, na‘e ‘ikai ha taha,
ka kuo toe tukuahaujia ‘ae ‘Eiki, ‘ohageko ‘ene toko
taha ‘i he loto-goue. Bea, ‘i he fekau, ‘ae ‘eikitau
na‘a nau ha‘i ia ‘o taki ki Selusalema.
{‘Oku kei toe he.)


KOE YAHE XY.
KOE BASIONE,
Koe Fakamau.
Kok Taula‘eiki-lahi ‘i he taimi koia ko Kaiafasi.
Na‘e ‘ikai koe I'aula‘eiki totonu ia ; ko Anasi na‘e
o‘ona ‘ae lakaga koia, ka kuo hifo fuoloa ia ‘e he kau
Loma, bea kuo nau fokotu‘u mo hifo ha ni‘ihi kehe,
koe'uhi, nai, ke ma'ama'a ‘ae tu'uga. Kae hage na‘e
kei jio ‘e he kakai Jiu kia Anasi ko honau ‘eiki totonu ;
bea ‘ajili, he koe koga tahi gaiie hono loto, bea ‘oku
matamata koe tefito ia ‘oe buleaki ke tamate'i ‘a Jisu.
Oku lau ‘e he g. tohi faka-Jiu koe fa‘ahiga manu-
‘manu ‘aia mo hono famili, bea kuo nau to‘o ma'anau-
tolu ‘ae fakatau manu ki be feilaulau, ‘aia na‘a nau
ma‘u ai ‘ae ba‘aga lahi; bea ‘oku mahalo koe me‘a
ia na‘e laga‘i ai ‘enau ‘ita kia Jisu ko‘ene kabuji ‘ae
kau fakatau mei he Temibale.
Koe toko taha koia na‘e fua ‘ave ki ai ‘a Jisu ke
fai ‘ae ‘ulualci ‘oe fitu'i fakamau ‘o hotau Fakamo‘ui.
Na‘e tu‘u hono fale ofi ki he Temibale, bea ko hono
aga na‘e hage koe Koliji Eefine, ‘o fale takai kae
loto‘a ‘a loto. Na‘e ‘o Anasi ‘ae fa‘ahi ‘e taha, kae
‘o Kaiafasi ‘ae fa‘ahi ‘e taha. Koe mataba ki he


Balasi na‘e hu mei loto'a, bea na‘e tauhi ‘e ha fefine
kaunaga ‘a Kaiafasi. Kuo hili ‘ae tu‘uabo ‘i he a‘u
ki ai ‘ae kau ofisa mo Jisu, bea, fe'ugaimoia, kuo foki
mai ‘ae loto ‘oe toko ua ‘i he Kau Ako na‘e hola, ko
Jione mo Bita ; bea kuo na lele mai, ‘o ma‘u ‘ae fonoga.
Bea, ‘i he vakai ‘e Jione ‘oku nau hu ki he loto'a koe,
na‘e ne fakatebitebi, ‘o hu mo kinautolu, bea na‘e
‘ikai ta‘ofi ‘e he fefine he kuo na maheni, he na‘e fa‘a
‘alu ‘a Jione ki he fale koia. Ka na‘e faigata‘a kia
Bita ke hu behe, he koe fo‘ou, ‘o ne nofo ‘i tu‘a; kae,
‘iloage, na‘e manatu ‘e Jione ki ai, ‘o ne lea ki he
fefine ke fakahu ia he ko hono kaume'a; bea ne to‘o
‘ae mataba ‘o fakahu mai.
‘Oku mahino koe me‘a na‘e faigataa‘ia ai ‘ae
hou'cki Jiu be koeha ha talatalaaki ‘o Jisu ‘e
fai. ‘E ‘ikai ‘aoga ha'anau lau ki he'ene kabuji
‘ae kau fakatau mei he Temibale, he koe me'a ia
na‘e maliefia ai ‘ae kau Falesi. Behe ‘e ‘ikai te
nau fa‘a lau ki he‘ene nofo koe Misaia telia ‘ae
kakai, he koe loto ‘oe kakai, ke ne fai ‘ae to‘oga ‘oe
Misaia. Bea na‘e ‘ikai te nau fa‘a lau ki he'ene mau-
mau Sabate, moe g. tu'utu'uni faka-Jiu, na‘a ha ‘ae
g. fu‘u mana na‘a ne fai. Koia na‘e ‘eke ‘e Anasi
ki he'ene ma‘u ha Kau Ako, moe aga o‘ene fa‘a malaga,
hei'ilo, ‘e ‘i ai ha‘ane lea ‘e mefihugatamaki ke ne buke
ki ai, ‘o ‘ave ki he fakamau ka fai ‘e Kaiafasi. Tokua,
na‘e ui ‘e he kakai Jiu ‘a Anasi mo hono famili koe
fagaga gaia, koe'uhi ko ‘enau 010, ka na‘e ‘ikai felave
‘ene 010 kia Jisu. Na‘e vakai ‘eia ki he nofo mai ‘ae
ni'ihi ‘i he kau lavaki ‘a Anasi, ‘aia kuo nau ha‘u ki
he'ene g. malaga ke tohi ‘ene lea, ‘o ne behe, ‘ Koeha
‘oku ke fehu‘i ai kiate au ? ‘Oku ‘ilo ‘ekinautolu ni
ki he'eku fa‘a lea, he ‘oku ‘ikai koe toko taha au ke


fai fufunaki ha lea, ka ‘oku ou lea ‘i he ‘ao ‘o
mamani.”
Koe fu‘u ta ia kia Anasi ‘ene lau ki he ‘ikai te ne
fai fufunaki ha me‘a; he koe ‘eke fufu behe he tuu-
uabo koe me‘a na‘e tabu ‘i he lao; bea na‘e ogo behe
ki ha toko taha ‘i he kau ofisa, ‘o ne ‘ai ha bekalae ‘o
Jisu, ‘o ne behe, “ ‘Oku behe koa ho‘o tali ki he
Taula‘eiki-lahi ? ” Hei'ilo be kohai ‘ae tagata koia,
ka koe me‘a fakaofo ‘ene buli, he ‘oku ne meimei tu‘u
bau mo Jiutasi he'ene fahu ‘ae tabu ‘oe jino ‘o Jisu.
Hage na‘e fakame‘avale‘i ai ia, bea ‘oku ‘ikai ke ogo
kiate kitautolu hono fakama‘i kimui, ‘o tatau moe fua
ta koia. Bea ‘oku hage na‘e behe mo Jisu. Na‘a
ne logo ‘i hono taukae‘i kimui, ka na ‘ane lea‘i he
bekalae koeni; bea te fakafeta'i ai, he, ka ne ‘ikai ogo‘i
‘e hono tagata hono bau‘uji‘i behe, ta, ‘oku ‘ikai koe
tagata ia hage ko kitautolu. Kuo fakaaga ki ai ‘e he
ni‘ihi, be koeha na‘e ‘ikai te ne fulihi hono kou'ahe
‘e taha, hage koe ‘ene lea ‘i he Malaga ‘i he Mo'uga :
ka ‘oku mahino mei ai, koe ala tu‘utu‘uni behe ‘oku
‘ikai koe me‘a ke fai kui ki ai. Kane koe fakataga
‘oku fai, ‘aia kuo sibi‘i tu‘uga‘a ai ‘a Jisu, behe ne
fulihi, nai, hono kou'ahe ; ka koe fakamau eni koe ‘eke
ki he totonu, bea ne tu'uaki ‘ae totonu. Bea na‘e ai,
nai, hano ‘uhiga ‘e taha. Tokua, koe me‘a ‘e taha na‘e
fehi'anekina ai ‘ae famili ‘o Anasi koe‘uhi koe fielahi
o‘enau kau tamaio'eiki, ‘o fa‘a ta‘i noa ‘ae kakai.
Bea na‘a koe lea eni ‘a Jisu ke taukabo‘i ji‘ono fa-
‘ahiga. Bea hono ‘ikai gali ‘ene lea ! Ka‘e ‘ikai te
ne tubutubulefanua ke to mai ha kovi, hage ko Baula
‘i hono ta‘i behe—seuke, ka ne momo'i kilo ki ai
‘a Jisu kuo ne ‘auha—ka ko ‘ene lea na‘e behe,
“ Kabau ‘oku kovi ha‘aku lea, be‘i fakaha'i ‘ae


kovi; ka ‘o kabau ‘oku lelei, bea kocha ‘oku ke ta‘i
ai au 1 ”
Bea tuku ai ‘e Anasi ‘ene ‘eke, hei‘ilo be koe mahino
kiate ia ‘e ‘ikai te ne lava ba me‘a, be koe'uhi koe
fakaha kuo hatoa mai ‘ae Fakataha Tokoni, bea ‘oku
tatali mai ‘a Kaiafasi. Kae kehe, na‘e fekau ‘e Anasi
ke ‘ave ia ki ai—bea ‘oji ‘ae ‘uluahi fakamau ‘o Jisu;
bea ne ogo kuo ‘ikai raa'u ba me‘a, ka, ‘i be‘ene fekau
ke ‘ave ha‘i, na‘e bebe ‘e Anasi ‘oku balaia.
Ko hono ua ‘oe fakamau ‘oku fakamatala ki ai ‘e
Matiu mo Maake, bea kuo mahalo ‘e be ni‘ihi koe
fai ia ‘e be Sanetalimi, koe‘uhi koe bebe, “ Ka‘e faka-
taha kiate ia ‘ae bou‘eiki taula'eiki kotoabe, moe kau
matu‘a, moe kau Sikalaibe ” (Maake xiv. 53). Ka
na‘e tabu ke fakataha ‘ae Sanetalimi bo‘uli, bea ‘e
ikai kataki ‘e be kau Falesi ke maumau ba tu‘utu‘uni
bebe. Bea ‘oku mahino ‘ae me‘a na‘e fai mei he g.
tohi faka-Jiu. Tokua, na‘e fili mei he Sanetalimi ha
komiti ‘e tolu ke tokoni ki be Taula‘eiki-lahi ‘i be fai
‘oe me‘a ni‘ihi, bea ke teuteu me‘a ki he fakataha lahi.
Bea koeni ia na‘e fakataha mo Kaiafasi, ke tomu‘a
‘eke kia Jisu, kae fai ‘ae fakataha lahi ‘oka ma‘a ‘ae
‘aho; bea ‘i he bebe na‘e katoa ‘ae kau taula‘eiki-lahi,
‘oku tau bebe koe fa‘ahi be ia ‘a Anasi, bea ‘e ‘i ai
ha toko nima ‘i he fagaga gata, bea ono ‘aki ‘a Kaia-
fasi. Ko hono katoa ‘oe Komiti koe toko uofulu
tubu.
Kuo ba mei be ‘eke ‘a Anasi ‘e ikai ‘aoga ba‘anau
tauheleb ia, ka ko hono me‘a be ke nau kumi faka-
mo‘oni. Na‘e tali, tokua, ha kau tukuaki, kae ‘ikai
jia‘a, bea nau fili ba hala kehe. ‘Oku ba ‘enau 010
‘i he me‘a na‘a nau bebe ke talatalaakbi ai ia. Na‘a
nau ‘ilo, ka nau ka fai ki he moe, ‘e ‘ikai kau ai kotoa,


hage ko ‘etau fakamatala. Ka na‘e ai ha fo‘i me‘a ‘e
taha te ne katoi ‘ae fa‘ahi kotoa. Kabau te nau lava
ke fakamo'oni kuo ne talaka'i ‘ae Temibale, ‘e laga‘i ai
‘ae ‘ita ‘ae kakai kotoa—tatau ai ‘ae Falesi moe Satusi,
‘ae hou'eiki moe lauvale. Koia na‘a nau huhii, be kuo
‘ikai fanogo ‘e ha ni‘ihi ki ha‘ane lea behe. Bea tu‘u
leva ha toko ua, ‘o fakamatala ki he‘ene lea, ‘i he'ene
‘uluaki a‘ahi ki Selusalema, ki he maumau ‘oe
Temibale mo ‘ene toe laga ‘i ha ‘aho ‘e tolu, Ka‘e
mahalo ‘e he fakataha kuo nau ma‘u ha me‘a, he na‘e
fakababau ‘e he toko taha, tokua, na‘e behe ‘e Jisu te
ne vete ‘ae faletabu ni ‘o gaohi ha faletabu ‘e taha ‘i he
‘aho ‘e tolu. Ka‘e gali kovi mo'oni ia, he koe behe koa
ke ne ala ki honau faletabu ! kae tu‘u mai ha toko taha,
‘o ne taukave koe lea ‘a Jisu na‘e behe, “ Oku faigofua
kiate au ke vete ‘ae faletabu ni ‘oe ‘Otua.” Taha
kehe ia : na‘e gali koe lea ‘a ha sesele, ka tala‘ehai
koe agahala. Kae‘uma‘a ‘oku ha ai ‘ene faka‘aba‘aba
ki he fale —“ koe faletabu ‘oe ‘Otua.” Ta ‘e ‘ikai
jiva'u ha me‘a ; bea nau ‘ita, bea ‘ajili koe tu‘u logo
‘a Jisu, hage ‘oku ‘ikai te ne toka‘i ‘enau me‘a.
Bea ‘ikai mafakamau‘ma‘u ‘ae Taula‘eiki-lahi, ‘one
buna mai ki loto kia Jisu, bea ne kalaga, “ Koeha ‘oku
‘ikai te ke lea ai ? ” Kane logo aibe, bea toki fai ‘e
he Taula‘eiki-lahi ‘ae me‘a taubotu ‘o hono lakaga,
‘0 ne lea tuki ki he ‘Otua ke ne tala be koe Misaia ia,
koe ‘Alo ‘oe ‘Otua. Koe aga aibe ‘0 Jisu ke ‘ilo ‘ae
hou‘eiki ‘i he'enau fai honau lakaga totonu, bea koe
taha ia ‘i he gaue ‘ae Taula‘eiki-lahi, ha lea mamafa
behe. Koia na‘a ne tali leva, “ Koia be ‘oku ke me‘a :
ka ‘oku ou tala atu, hili eni, te mou mamata ki he
Fanautama ‘a Tagata ‘oku ne nofo ki he nima to-
‘omata‘u ‘o Malohi, bea ‘oku ne hoko mai ‘oku heka


ki he g. ‘ao ‘o lagi.” Koe lea mamafa ‘aubito ia, he
ko ‘ene belie, koe toko taha ia na‘e kikite ki ai ‘e
Taniela ‘oku ne fakatou Misaia mo ‘Alo ‘oe ‘Otua ;
bea, ka ne tae'oua ‘enau ‘ita, te nau manatu na‘e
fakaha ‘e he balofita koia, koe Misaia koia te ne mate
tamateb; bea ko ‘ene gali vaivai behe na‘e hoa moe
balofisai. Na‘e ‘ilo ki ai ‘a Kaiafasi, he kuo ne toki
lea ‘i ha fakataha ‘e taha kuo bau ke mate ha taha
koe‘uhi koe kakai (Jione xi. 50). Ka ka fakafefeka
‘eia hono loto, ‘o ne hae hifo hono kofu (‘aia koe me‘a
na‘e tabu ke ne fai, gata be ‘i ha'ane fanogo ki he lea
fie'otau), bea ne ‘ioho hage ‘oku ne vavana ai, “ Kuo
ne lea fie'otua ! koeha ho'omou boa ? ” Bea nau feka-
lagi'i kotoabe, “ Koe koto mate be ia.” Koe ‘oji ia ‘o
hono fakamau tu‘o ua faka-Jiu, bea kuo toe tuku koe
halaia.
Na'e kei tuai hono tolu, he ‘e ‘ikai fakataha ‘ae
Sanetalimi kae'oua ke ‘aho ; ka na‘e lau kotoa koe
fakamaumatea ia, ‘o nau kamata hano gaohikovi'i.
Koe me'a ia ‘oku fai kehekehe ai ‘ae kuoga mu‘a mo
eni. ‘I he taimi ni, ka mahino ‘ae tamate'i ‘o ha
taha, bea ‘oku fai fakaalaala ki ai mo tauhi lelei; ka,
‘i he kuoga mu‘a, na‘e hage ko Hina hono gaohi—
na'e mate ‘ae faka‘aba‘aba moe ‘ofa. Bea koia ‘i
he'enau buke ‘a Jisu ke taki atu, na‘a nau gaohi ‘o
hage ha manu. Na'e ‘oho mai ‘ae ni‘ihi, ‘o ‘ai hano
fu’u bekalae—tabu mo ‘Ene ‘ Afio ! —bea haga ha
ni'ihi ‘o ‘anuhi hono fofoga—‘oiseukeseuke ! koeha
na'e ‘ikai taba mai leva ‘ae ‘uhila ‘o faka'auha kinau-
tolu ! “ Oku matamata koe kakai tu‘a ia ; ka ‘oku
hage na‘e kau ai moe hou'eiki foki, bea ko kinautolu
ia na‘e taka luma ‘enau me‘a. “ Oua koa. Tokua,
koe Misaia ia : tau vakai ‘ene Misaia ; ’ bea nau to‘o


ha kofu ‘o fakabulou ia, bea nau toki ‘ai hano fu‘u
tuki, ‘o nau behe, “ E Misaia, mate mai be kohai
na‘e ta‘i koe.” Ko hono ua eni ‘oe goohikovi'i ‘o
Jisu, bea fakaofo, na‘e ‘ikai te ne lea be fai ha me'a.
Ko kitautolu ‘oku ‘ikai te tau mei kataki ke lau
hono fakamatala—‘oku tau ‘ita ; ‘oku tau faka'amu
ke hoko ha me'a kiate kinautolu ; bea koe kataki ‘e
Jisu ‘ae fakalielia‘i behe ‘o hono tagata koe misiteli
‘e ‘ikai te tau fa‘a a‘ujia—koe me'a be ‘oku tau
lave‘i, koe kataki ma‘atautolu.
Bea na‘a ‘oku lolotoga ha mamahi kehe ‘a Jisu na‘e
hulu atu, ‘o ne ogonoa ai, he ‘oku matamata koe
taimi ia ‘oku fai ‘e Bita ‘ene fakafijiga hono ‘Eiki.
Kuo ne hu mai ki loto‘a, hage ko ‘etau fakamatala,
bea ‘i he'ene ogo‘i ‘oku ne ‘i he lotolotoga ‘oe fili, na‘a
ne behe ‘e lelei mu‘a ‘ene fai malohi; he kabau te ne
fakateketeka meiate kinautolu, bea na‘a mahalokovi
ha ni'ihi. Koia na‘a ne fakata‘emalu‘ia atu, ‘o ne
‘unu'unu ki he afi kuo tafu ‘i he loto‘a, ‘o mumu ai
fakataha moe kau tamaio'eiki. Eaifai bea fetogi ‘ae
feline na‘e le‘o mataba ‘e ha feline ‘e taha, bea ha‘u
ia ke mumu foki, he ‘oku momoko ‘ae g. bo ‘i he
mahina koia. Bea, lolotoga ‘ene fai ‘ene laubisi ki
he kau tagata, ‘iloage, na‘a ne tokaga'i koe kehe ena
‘oku mumu, ‘o ne ofogi be kohai. Ka, ‘i he'ene jio faka-
mama'u ki ai, na‘a ne manatu koe toko taha ia na‘e hu
mai moe f aka tau ika ko Jione, ‘o ne behe leva, “ Ko
koe, foki, na‘a ke ‘i he motu‘a mei Nasaleti, ‘a Jisu.”
Koe mo'utamakia ia ‘o Bita, bea, ‘i he'ene ‘oho, na‘e
buna atu ‘ae lea, “ Oku ‘ikai teu ‘ilo ia, bea ‘oku
‘ikai mahino kiate au he ko ho‘o lau ki he ha.”
Oku ‘ikai teu kau au mo kinautolu ‘oku nau tuku
koe fo‘i ‘a Bita he'ene lea behe. Kane koe fo‘i, kuo


‘ikai te ne hu mai. Na‘e ‘ikai koe foi, ka koe hala
hono taumu'a. Kane hu mai koe akoga ‘a Jisu>
hage ko Jione, ne ‘ikai behe ‘ene tali; ka kuo ne
tu‘utu‘uni ke fufunaki ‘ene kau mo Jisu, ko hono o
ia na‘a ne hele ai. Koe me‘a koia ‘oku tau maheni
ai ‘i he ‘aho kotoahe—koe tu‘utu‘uni ‘a hotau loto
‘oku ne bule'i ‘etau lea, ‘o mio‘i ki he mo e.
Bea hiki ‘a Bita, ‘o ‘alu ki he mataba, ko ‘ene
behe, nai, ‘e lelei ‘ene ‘alu kitu‘a he kuo ‘iloa. Ka, ‘i
he‘ene a‘u ki ai, na‘e u‘ua ha moa, ‘o ne manatu leva
ki he‘ene tukuba na‘e fai. Bea na‘a koe taimi ia
na‘e taki mai ai ‘a Jisu mei he feitu'u ‘a Anasi ki he
feitu'u ‘a Kaiafasi, bea toki ake mui ‘ae ‘ofa ‘a Bita,
‘o ne behe te ne nofo atu be ke vakai hono iku‘aga.
Ka kuo talanoa ‘e he ‘uluaki fefine kiate ia kuo
fetogi ia ki he‘ene fakahu mai ‘a Bita, mo ‘one kau
ki he tagata ‘oku fakamau'i. Bea kuo oage ha kau
takatu'u ke talanoa moe fefine le‘o ki he fakamau
‘oku fai, tokua, koe toko taha ‘oku lau koe Misaia,
moeha fua ha me‘a kuo nau ogo‘i. Bea tuhu ‘ae
fefine le‘o kia Bita, ‘o ne behe, koe taha ia ‘oku kau
ki ai; bea boubou ki ai ha taha ‘i he kau takatu'u.
Bea koeha ha toe me‘a ‘a Bita ke fai ka koe faka'ikai
be. Koe mala ia ‘oe loi; ‘oku ‘ikai ke ala tu‘u taha,
ka kuo bau ke ne ‘omi ha loi ‘e taha mdno fokouofo.
Koia na‘e tali hake ‘e ji‘i Bita, “ Tagata, ‘oku ‘ikai; ”
‘o ne ‘ai ‘ene lea tuki ke fakamamafa ki ai; kae-
‘uma‘a na‘a ne toe ‘alu atu ki he afi, ‘o hage ‘oku
‘ikai ha'ane manavahe.
Bea mole ha fu‘u houa moe mumu be ‘a Bita, ‘o
‘ikai ha taha ‘e lea ki ai. Bea ne fiefia ‘i he‘ene hao,
ka ne behe ‘e lelei mu‘a ‘ene talanoa mo kata, na‘a
fai ha mahalo ki ai. Koia na‘a ne kamata ‘ene laubisi


bage ko kinautolu, ‘o ‘ikai te ne manatu koe Mua ia
—‘isa, koe Kaleli—‘o faji kehe. Bea fakatokaga‘i
ai ‘e he ni‘ihi, ‘o nau jio fakamama‘u kiate ia. Bea
koe toko taha na‘e ‘alu ‘i he fonoga ke buke ‘a Jisu,
(bea koe kaiga fold ‘oe tagata na‘e lavea) na‘a ne
manatu kuo ne fanogo ki ha faji behe, ‘o ne lea hake,
“ ‘lkai na‘aku jio kiate koe ‘i he gouetabu fakataha
moia 1 ” Bea toki manavahe mo‘oni ‘a Bita, na‘a
‘iloa ia koe toko taha na‘a ne ta‘i ‘ae tamaio‘eiki ‘ae
Taula‘eiki-lahi, he koe hiamatea ia; bea ne haga ai
‘o tuki mo fuakava, “ ‘Oku ‘ikai teu ‘ilo ‘ae tagata
koia ‘oku mou lau ki ai.” Fokifa na‘e u‘ua ‘ae moa,
bea, ‘i he ofo hake ai ‘a Bita, na‘a ne ‘ilo hono ‘Eiki
mei he mama‘o ‘oku haga mai. Kuo ‘ikai te ne
gaue ‘i hono ‘anuhi, mo hono sibi'i, mo hono tukid;
ka koe fakafiji ‘a hono ako na‘e toki lavea ai hono
loto, ‘o ue‘i ia mei he‘ene kataki. Kohai ‘e mafaka-
matala ‘ae mamahi ‘a Jisu ‘i hono gaohi behe‘i ‘e
he‘ene bele 1 Ko hono fakatata totonu koe mamahi
‘a Jiuliasi Sisa ko ‘ene vakai ko Boluto ‘oku kau ‘i
he laba. Ko hono me‘a be, he kuo ‘amanaki ki ai ‘a
Jisu, bea molia ai ha koga ji‘i ‘oe mamahi. Kae
kehe, ‘oku mahino koe me‘a na‘e ha ‘i he ogo fo‘i
fofoga ‘oe ‘Eiki ‘i he haga ki ai ‘a Bita, na‘e ‘ikai
koe ‘ita, ka na‘e fefiofi ai ‘ae ofo moe ‘ofa. Bea ‘aji
hifo ‘ae fo‘i kilo koia ki he loto ‘o Bita; bea, hage
koe taba ‘ae ‘uhila ‘i he bo‘uli, na‘e fakae‘a ai ‘ene
baga mo tae‘ofa, ‘o ne fakabulou leva, ‘o oho ki tu‘a
‘o tagi —koe tagi ka ko ha tagi. Monu na‘e ‘ikai koe
tagi loto fefeka—koe tagi fakatomala be moe tagi ‘ofa ;
bea ne ‘ilo ‘ae mo‘oni ‘oe lea ‘a hono ‘Eiki, “ Monu-
‘iaa ka ko kinautohi ‘oku fakamamahi; he ‘e faka-
fiemalie ‘akinautolu.”


Faifai bea karaata mama mai ‘ae ‘aho, bea na‘e
takiage ‘a Jisu ke fai hono fakamau tu‘o iolu ‘i he
‘ao ‘oe Sanetalimi. Koeni ia ‘oku fakamatala ki ai
‘e Luke; bea ne‘ine‘i, he koena be ‘ae fakamau'aga
totonu, bea koia be na‘e tokaga ki ai ‘a Luke he koe
Senitaile, kae mamafa kia Matiu mo Maake mo
Jione ‘ae ogo fakamau koe, ko ‘enau ‘ilo ‘oku fa‘a
buloa be ‘ae me‘a ‘ae fakataha labi, bea koe mo'oni
ia, ‘aia kuo tu'utu'uni ‘e he hou'eiki Satusi ‘i he‘enau
g. fakataha faka'ekinautolu. Koe ni‘ibi ‘i he Sane-
talimi na‘e kau ‘i be fakataha ‘anenai, bea te nau
fakamatala ki he'ene lea fie'otua; ka koe loto ‘oe
fakataha ke ma‘u ha me‘a ke nau taki koe agatu'u,
he na‘a nau faka‘amu ke no mate kalusefai he koe
taubotu ‘oe me‘a fakama. Kane koe taimi mu‘a, ‘e
‘ikai te nau ogojia kumi tu‘uga, ka kuo nau hikiniina
leva ‘o fai; kae talu ‘enau to ki Loma moe to‘o ‘ae
mafai koia meiate kinautolu, o ta'ofi ki he Kovana
be ‘ae fakamaumatea. Koia na‘e hu‘u ‘enau fehu'i
ki he'ene nofo mai koe Misaia, hei‘ilo ‘e ai ha‘ane lea
ke nau buke ki ai, ‘o kau ki he'ene tu‘u ki he Bule-
‘aga ‘o Loma. Kae ‘ikai felave ha‘anau 010 kiate ia
‘oku ne hakule ‘ae loto. Na‘e mahino ‘ae hele, ‘o ne
le‘ei noa he‘ene belie, “ Kabau teu tala kiate kimou-
tolu, tala‘ehai te mou tui ; boa kabau teu ‘ai atu ha
febu‘i, tala'ehai te mou tali.” Na‘a nau ‘ilo bo ko
‘ene mo‘oni: na‘e ‘ikai ko ‘enau tagi ki be totonu,
ka ke ne halaia be—bea hono taha ‘ae fakamau'aga
kuo fai bebe ki mui ni !
Ka na‘e ‘ikai koe finagalo ‘o Jisu ke fufu hono
iakaga ‘i be ‘ao ‘oe fakataha labi ‘o hono fonua;
koia na‘a ne tala fakahagatonu, koe Misaia ia. Ka
na‘a ne tuku ‘ae me‘a na‘a nau tali habo mei ai, ‘ae


gaiio ‘ae Misaia ‘i mamani, ‘o ne lau ki he lakaga ‘oe
Misaia ‘i he Lagi he'ene behe, ‘e nofo ‘ae Fanautama
‘a Tagata ki he nima to‘omata‘u ‘oe Mafimafi ‘oe
‘Otua. ‘Oiau ‘ae boto ! Kuo ne fakaha 'ene Misaia,
ka ne bale‘i ‘enau ta. Kae hage na‘e ‘ikai t.e nau
tokagafi ia ‘i he to‘oa honau loto ‘i he ‘afugi ‘ae
tagata na ‘oku o'ona ‘ae tu‘uga tobutabu koia; ‘o
nau ‘ioho leva kotoabe, “ lo ! bea koe ‘Alo ‘oe ‘Otua
koe? ” Kane koe tagata be ‘a Jisu kuo ne ma ‘i he
fehu'i koia, be kuo ne fu‘u hiki. Ka ka fofoga
ta‘eto'oto‘oa mai ‘ae ‘Eiki, ‘o ne behe, “Ka na‘e fai;
koau.” Koia na‘e iku ai ‘ae fakamau ‘o hage koe
fakamau ‘anenai. Koe me‘a be kuo nau ma’u koe lea
fie ‘otua; bea, ne ogo na‘a nau ‘ilo ‘e ’ikai mamafa ia
ki he kovana, he koe Loma, ka, ne ogo e me‘a ke
fefe, talu ‘anebo mo ‘enau fai tukuigata kae ‘ikai
ilo ha‘ane momo'i agahala. Koia na‘a nau faka-
kaukau ke ‘ave aibe ki he Kovana, ‘o lau be koe
tagata halaia; bea ke nau ‘alu kotoabe, heifilo ‘e
mamafa ki he Kovana ‘enau fai behe, bea ne tu‘utu-
‘uni hono tautea ta‘e ‘eke. Koe ‘oji eni hono tolu
‘oe fakamau ‘0 Jisu, bea ne ogo kuo ‘ikai ha me‘a ‘e
ma‘u, ka na‘e taki atu koe halaia.
‘Oku ha ‘ae mamafa o'enau fakahalaia ‘a Jisu ‘i he
me‘a na‘e hoko, lolotoga ‘enau teuteu ke ‘alu ki he
kovana. Fakafokifa na‘e ha ‘a Jiutasi ‘i he tu‘a-
mataba, kuo fulihi hono mata ‘o jio'aki ‘ae me‘a
hinehina. Bea ‘i he‘enau ofogi ia, bea ogo mai ‘ene
lea hage kuo fulutamaki, “ Kuou faihala, he kuou
lavaki‘l ‘ae ta'ehalaia.” Na‘e mahino na‘e hage ha
heli hono loto, bea kuo toki ha kiate ia ‘ae lain ‘oe
kovi kuo ne fai. Ka koe behe ke nau ‘ofa kiate ia 3
‘Anefe na‘e ‘ofeina ha lavaki? ‘Oku gaue‘aki bea


toki li'aki, hage ha moli kuo ‘oji inu. ‘lkai: na‘e
‘ikai faka‘atu‘i ia ‘e ha taha ‘oe kau taula‘eiki na.
Na‘a nau katakata'anifotea, ‘o nau behe, “ He ‘oku
mau kau ai ? ‘oku ‘iate koe be ia.” Talaatu, na‘o ‘ilo
‘e Jiutasi ‘ae kona ‘o Heli ‘i he momeniti koia. Ne
ogo ‘ene mo'ui, ka kuo ne a‘ujia ‘ae luo ta‘e-hano-
takele. Bea ha leva ‘ae to‘oga ‘oe kakai kuo nau
oso‘i kuo nau malaia, ‘aia koe fehi‘a mate ki he me‘a
O '
na‘e tubu ai ‘enau to. Tokua, kuo ‘i ai ha kau fefine
kuo nau fakahigaki ha kau tagata, bea faifai bea nau
hoko koe iehi'anekina lain ‘oe kau tagata koia. Bea
behe mo ha ‘ita ha kakai ki ha ni‘ihi kuo takihed
kinautolu. Koia, ‘i he jio ‘e Jiutasi ki he siliva na‘e
toho'aki hono loto ke fai ‘ae lavaki, na‘e ake ‘ene
fehi‘a mate ki ai, ‘o ne haga ‘o laku atu ki he loto
fale kiate kinautolu, ‘o ne ‘alu ‘o no‘ou‘a.
Kuo lahi ‘ae fifili ki he me‘a koia ‘a Jiutasi, be
na‘e tubu ‘i he ha ‘ene fai behe. Koe fakakaukau ‘e
taha, tokua, na‘e jio tu‘uga ‘a Jiutasi ‘i he bule'aga
‘oe Misaia; bea kuo ne ‘ita Ida Jisu ‘i he‘ene fai
fakaalaala, ‘o ‘ikai te ne fokotu‘u leva hono Bule'aga.
Koia kuo ne fakakaukau, tokua, ke lavakid hono
‘Eiki ki he Bule'aga, ko ‘ene behe ‘e toki o‘io‘i ‘a
Jisu, ‘o gaue‘aki hono mafimafi, ‘o tulaki hono g.
fili, ‘o to‘o ‘ae bule'aga mo'ona. Ka, ‘i he‘ene vakai
ki he kataki ‘e Jisu hono buke, mo hono had, mo hono
takiekina fano, mo fakamaumatea, bea ne toki dlo
kuo hala ‘ene fakakaukau, bea kuo bau ‘a jid Jisu
ko ‘ene gaue. Bea dhe tautea ia ‘e hono loto, kuo ne
haga ‘o fai hage ko ‘etau fakamatala. Taumaia ke
te tui ki he fakakaukau koia, kae jidjid ai ‘ae kovi
‘ae Abosetolo, bea jidjid ai ‘ao namukfi ‘o hotau
fa'ahiga kotoa—he ‘oku hage kuo bani'uli ai ‘ae


hako‘i tagata kotoa, ‘i he a‘ujia ‘e hatau toko taha
ha agahala behe. Ka koe fakakaukau koia ‘e ‘ikai
tu‘u ‘oka sivi. He koe behe ke ne lavakih ‘a Jisu
ke faka‘oho ia ke fokotu‘u hono Bule‘aga ka ne m‘au
lakaga ai—‘o ma‘ulakaga koa ‘e ha lavaki ? u ! u !
koe tesi iku launoa ia. ‘lkai: koe koula be na‘e
tubu ai ‘ene gaue bago, bea koe ‘uhiga o‘ene momou,
he koe aga ‘oe g. agahala lalahi ke fu‘u ‘ea ‘aubito
hili hono fai, hage koe ‘oho ki mui ha me‘afanafonua
‘i hono fakaba. Bea koia, ‘i he vakai ‘e Jiutasi ki he
ten taki atu ‘o Jisu ki he Kovana ke tamateh, na‘e
toki ofo hono loto, ‘o ne ‘ilo ki he kilukilua ‘oe
agahala kuo ne fai—hono ta‘ehouga, hono tae‘ofa,
hono ta'etau, hono fakalielia, hono ban ke fehi-
‘anekina, hono ta'emafakamolemolea. Ne‘ine‘i faka-
tatau ‘e Militoni ‘ae agahala ki ha fefine ‘oku faka-
‘ofo'ofa ‘i ‘oluga, ka koe gata huhu kona ‘i lalo!
Kuo ‘oji ‘ia Jiutasi ‘ae malie ‘oe me‘a, bea kuo hukia
eni hono loto ‘i he huhu kona. ‘Oku ai ha toko lahi
kuo nau faka‘ehi‘ehi mei he agahala ko ‘enau mana-
vahe ki he'ene holomui mai koia ; bea ne‘ine‘i!
Na‘a tau behe ‘anenai kuo ake ‘a Heli ‘i he loto ‘o
Jiutasi; bea ‘oku lau ‘e Militoni ki he mama ‘a Heli
‘oku ‘aoga be ke ha ai ‘ae bo'uli. Bea na‘e behe ‘a
Jiutasi. Na‘e ha ‘ae agahala kuo ne fai, honololoa
mo hono maukubu : kae ‘ikai ha ai ha fakatu‘amelie,
ha jio fakamolemole, be ha. Fou atu ‘eia, tokua, ki
he ‘abi kuo ne tokaga ke fakatau‘aki ‘ae ba‘aga, kuo
bo‘uli hono loto mo hono mata. Kuo ‘ikai, nai, te ne
jio ki he la‘a kuo hobo ki mamani. Na‘e ‘ikai te ne
kei kataki ke mo‘ui, ‘o ne kaka ‘i he ‘akau, ‘o
no‘otaki ‘ae maea ki ha va‘a ‘i ‘oluga, ‘o ne fuhi
hono kia ‘o hobo. Kae motu ai ‘ae va‘a, be koe


maea, ‘o ne bafua; bea na‘eliligi ‘ae to‘oto‘oga
kitu‘a.
Bea ‘omi hono talanoa koia ki he liou‘eiki ‘oku
nau lolotoga fakakaukau ki ha me‘a ‘e fai'aki ‘ae
ba‘aga kuo momoi, Na‘e ha ai ‘ae mo‘oui ‘oe
fakatata na‘e fai ‘e Jisu fuofuoloa atu, tokua, ‘oku
nau sivi mei honau inu ha namu, kae folo fua ha
kameli. Kuo bau honau loto ke fakabogi ‘a Jisu ;
kuo nau folo noa ia: ka koe mea na‘a nau mei lo‘oa
ai ‘ae li ‘ae baaga koia ki he seifi ‘ae jiaji, he koe
totogi toto. Ka, ‘i he‘enau fanogo ki he mate ‘a
Jiutasi ‘i he botu na‘a ne ‘amanaki fakatau, na‘a
nau behe, “ Ta ko hono lelei e ke fakaai ‘ene tu‘utu-
uni, ‘o fakatau'aki ‘ene ba‘aga ‘ae koga kelekele koe,
‘o tanu ai ‘ae tagata : bea ‘aoga ia ke fai ai ha ni‘ihi
hili mai, kuo ‘ikai ha'anau fa‘itoka. Bea fai; bea,
ta, koe fua o‘ene layaki koe fa‘itoka be—bea ‘oku
hage koe mala ia ‘oe lavaki kotoabe. Ka kuo ‘oho
a Selusalema ‘i he me‘a, ‘o nau behe kuo ‘i ai ha
mala ‘i he botu koia, ‘o ‘ikai mole ‘ae nanamu ‘oe
toto ‘o Jiutasi. Bea ‘oku tala mai ‘e Babiasa, na‘a
mo hono taimi o‘ona, koe kakai kotoa na‘e ‘alu ai
na‘a nau ku-ihu.
Koe Kovana ‘o Jiutea ‘i he taimi koia ko Bonitusi
(be Bonito) Bailato. Koe higoa ia kuo ogoogokovi
‘i mamani katoa ko ‘ene kau ‘i ho fakamau koeni, ‘o
fakahalaia ‘ae tagata na‘a ne ‘ilo ‘oku tonuhia; ka
hono taha ‘ae Bailato ki mui! Kuo fa ta‘u, nai, ‘ene
kovana, bea ko ‘ene feagai moe kakai koe takaga-a-
bibi-mo-kahi; hei'ilo be ko ‘ene vale, be ko ‘one
fielahi na‘e na‘e tubu ai ‘enau behe. Tokua, hili ji‘i
hono fakanofo, na‘a no tuku ke ‘alu mo ‘ene tau ki
Selusalema ‘enau g. fuka. Koe g. fuka koia koe


fakatata ‘oe ikale, bea na‘e ha ki he kakai Jiu koe
‘omi ia ‘oe g. aitoli ke fakafeagai kia Jihova. Koe
ine‘a kehe ‘enau ‘ita. Na‘a nan ‘alu toko lahi ki
Selsalia, ‘aia koe nofo'aga ‘oe Kovana, ‘o nau kabui
hono balasi ‘o ‘aho nima, ke kole ke ne fekau ke
fakafoki ‘ae g. fuka mei he kolo tabu. ‘I hono ono
‘oe ‘aho na‘e fekau ‘e Bailato ‘ene tau ke kabui
kinautolu, bea ne toki tala ki he kakai, kabau ‘e
‘ikai te nau ‘alu, te ne tamate‘i kinautolu. Kae
‘ikai ‘aubito ogo. Kae kehe, na‘a nau fo'ohifo, ‘o tuku
mai honau kia ke tu‘uji; bea toki vaivai ‘a Bailato,
‘o ne fekau ke fai ki honau loto, kae talu ai mo ‘ene
fehi‘a kiate kinautolu, ‘o lau koe fa'ahiga mataila.
Bea tala'ehai koia be. Tokua, na‘e hoge vai ‘a
Selusalema, bea haga ai ‘e Bailato, ‘o gaohi ha vaitaki
ke ‘omi hanau vai mei he g. leba na‘e higoa kia
Solomone. Ka na‘e maumau ‘ene gaue ‘aoga ko ‘ene
ala ki he ba‘aga tabu na‘e tauhi ‘i he Temibale, ‘aia
na‘e ui koe “ kobano.” Bea nau toe kabui hono fale
hage koia ‘i Sosalia, ‘o nau gaohi fakalielia ia koe‘uhi
ko ‘ene ala ki he‘enau me‘a tabu. Bea ‘ita ‘a Bailito,
‘o ne fekau ha ni‘ihi o‘ene tau ke ‘ai kofu faka-Jiu,
‘o fptuiaki moe kakai; bea ne toki agi atu, bea
nau taki taha to‘o ‘ene hele ‘o tui‘i ha taha na‘e
ofi. Bea na‘e toko lahi ‘ae kakai na‘e mate ‘i he
maveuveu.
Na‘e ai mo ‘ene g. me‘a behe kuo fai, bea kuo ‘alu
tu‘o taha hono talatalaaki‘i ki Loma ki he Sisa ko
Taibilio, ‘aia na‘a ne volokia ‘a Bailato ‘i he‘ene ta‘e
faka‘atu‘i ‘ae kakai; he ne ogo ‘ene ma‘ama‘a ‘ae g.
me‘a behe ki he Loma, ka ‘oku mahino ‘oku mamafa
ki ai ‘ae kakai. Koia koe aga ‘oe loto ‘o Bailato ki
he kakai Jiu, na‘a ne fakalili‘a kiate kinautolu, ka


ne manavahe, foki, na‘a toe fai hono talalaaki‘i, bea
ne hifo ai.
Ko hono nofo‘aga totonu ‘a Sesalia, ka ‘i he hoko
‘ae Basova, na‘e bau ke ne ‘alu hake ki Selusalema,
he koe taimi ia na‘e fa‘a hoko ai ‘ae g. maveuveu, koe
fakataha ‘ae g. fa‘ahi ke fai ‘enau Katoaga Tabu.
Koe fale na‘a ne nofo ai koe fu‘u balasi na‘e laga ‘e
Helota Lahi. Na‘e tu‘u ‘i Motu‘a Selusalema, ‘i he
mo'uga ki hihifo, ‘ae feitu'u na‘e ma'oluga taha, bea
na‘e gaohi mabeli hono g. loki moe falehala, bea togi
hono g. bou na‘e lanu kehekehe, bea lahi ‘ae fauniteni
moe leba, moe gouetabu koe lata‘aga ‘oe faga lube.
Kane ogo ‘ene masani, talaatu, ne faka‘amu ‘e
Bailato kuo ne ‘i ha fale ji‘i, kae kehe, ke ne mama'o
moe kolo mataila ni, he ‘oku hage na‘o vavalo ‘e hono
loto ‘e ai ha me‘a.
Na‘e ‘i ai ha fu‘u tele'a ‘i he vaha‘a ‘o Motu‘a
Selusalema moe Temibale, ka na‘e fakahoko'aki ‘ae
ogo mo‘ugo ha fu‘u halafakakavakava maka. Bea, ‘i
he jio ki ai hegihegi ‘e Bailato mei hono loki ‘i ho
Balasi, na‘a ne ‘ilo ki he fu‘u fonoga ‘oku ha‘u.
‘Oiau ! ‘oku taki ‘e he Taula‘eiki-lahi na‘e ‘iloga ko

Pefe ka ne ki‘i tautea ‘a Jisu: hei‘ilo ‘e tobono ji‘i

he bea ‘oku ‘ikai lelei ki he.
