‘ae maveuveu, ka ne feiga ke bale‘i ‘ae nunn'a ‘oe
gaue behe. Koia na‘a ne fekau ke ‘omi ha vai, ‘o ne
fanofano ‘i honau ‘ao, ‘o ne behe, “ Kuou ‘ata‘ata au
mei he toto ‘oe tagata ma‘oni‘oni ni; ‘oku ‘iate
kimoutolu ia.” Kuo hulu eni ‘ao loto ‘oe kakai, bea,
‘i he‘enau vakai kuo lava ‘enau holi, na‘a nau
fekalagai, “ Lelei be, ke eke hono toto kiate
kimautolu mo ‘emau fanau! ” Bea hono ‘ikai kuo
fai, he na‘e tafe honau toto, moe toto o‘enau fanau ‘i
he g. hala ‘o Selusalema. Bea ne ogo e fanofano ‘a
Bailato, ka hono ma‘a meiate ia ‘ae ta‘ata‘a ‘o Jisu 1
Mo'oni e lea ‘a Sekesibea, “‘e ‘oji ‘ae oseni ‘i he‘ene
fanofano ai ‘e he tagata fakabo, kae ‘ikai ma‘a ai ;
kae kehe, ‘e toto kotoa ai ‘ae moana.” ‘Oku fakaha
‘e he hisitolia, na‘e toe ji‘i bea hifo ‘a Bailato, mo
fakaheh ; bea ne tamateh ia ‘eia ‘i ha botu matna'o.
Bea ‘oku lau ‘e he kakai ‘oe fonua na‘a ne mate ai,
‘oku ne fa‘a mabuna hake ‘i he anovai na‘a ne uku
ai, bea ‘oku nau jio hage ‘oku ne kei fanofano be.


“ Bea ne toki vete kiate kinautolu ‘a Balabasa, ka
ne kau‘imaea ‘a Jisu, ‘o ne tuku ke kalusefai.” Lau
'ekita ‘e lahi be ke kalusefai, he koe taubotu ia ‘oe
raate'aga fakamamahi; kae‘uma‘a kuo mahino ‘ae fie
fakahaofi ‘o Jisu ‘e Bailato; bea ne ogo kuo ‘ikai
lava ia, kehe ke ne fakaji‘iji‘i ‘ene marnahi. Ko
hono ‘uhiga lahi, nai, o‘ene fekau ke fai ha kau'imaea,
he koe me‘a ia na‘e fa‘a fai, ‘oka bau ‘ae mate ‘o ha
toko taha. Kae‘uma‘a ‘oku tau ‘ilo hotau aga. Ka
kut hoko ki ha taha hage koia na‘e hoko kia Bailato,
bea kuo fakamalohia kita ke fai ha me‘a ‘oku te
fehi'a ki ai, ‘oku fa‘a to ‘ote ‘ita kiate kinautolu ‘oku
te ‘ofa ai. Bea koeni kuo ‘ita ‘a Bailato ‘i he loki ia
ke fai ha me‘a ‘oku ‘ikai te ne fie fai, bea to ‘ene ‘ita
kia Jisu —hage ko ha ‘ita ‘a ha finemotu'a ki he'ene
1-amaji‘i, ‘o ne ta‘i, koe'uhi koia kuo tubu ai ‘ae me‘a
‘oji ‘oku ‘ata‘atii ‘ae tamaji'i.
Kae kehe, na‘e taki age ‘a ji‘i Jisu ke kau'imaea
‘Oiau! kohai ‘e fakamatala ki ai! Hage na‘e ‘ikai
kataki ‘e he kau Evagelio ke lea ki ai. Ka‘e vete
hono kofu kotoa (hehilo be na‘e vala be ‘ikai) ; ‘na‘e
ha‘i bunou ia ki ha bou, bea koe me‘a na‘e haha'aki
koe busi-leta, ‘aia kuo fakamata'aki ha g. koga bulu
be ukamea, koe‘uhi ke ne ta'aki mai ‘ae kakano.
Bea tala'ehai na‘e fakagatagata ‘ae ta—koe ni‘ihi
na‘e matu'aki mate ai. Bea kuo hage kuo ‘ita ‘ae
kau tau Loma kia Jisu, ko ‘enau behe, ‘oku galigali
hoko ‘iate ia ha‘anau febaki moo kau Jiu, ‘aia na‘a
nau teteki ki ai ko ‘enau fa‘a kaime'akovi meiate
kinautolu. Koia na‘a nau tukuigata hono haha, ‘o
nau toki ta'ofi na‘a ne bekia. Ko ji‘i toki mo‘oni e
‘ae kikite, “Na‘a ne tuku hono takafalu ki he kau
ta.”


Ka na‘e ‘ikai tobono ai honau loto, ka nau ‘ave ia
ki he fale lain ‘oe Balasi, ! o nau tanaki ‘ae vahegatau
kotoa ke vaiga‘aki ia. Kuo nau fanogo, tokua, koe
tu‘i ia, ‘o nau belie leva “ ‘Omi hano kofu fakatuh.”
Koe lanu ‘oe kofu ‘oe Tu‘i Loma koe kulabo‘ubo‘uli,
bea na‘e fa‘a mea‘ofa‘aki ‘e lie Tu‘i Loma ki ha tu‘i
kehe ke fakaha ‘ene ‘ofa. Bea na‘a koe kofu eni na‘e
‘omi mei Loma kia Helota Lahi, be ha taha ‘i mu'a
atu, ‘aia na‘a nau ‘ai kia Jisu. Bea ‘ikai‘ia koia, ka
nau fi ha fa‘ufa‘u mei he ‘akau talatala, ‘o hage koe
kalauni na‘e ‘ai ‘e he hou‘eiki Sisa, ‘o nau takai ki
hono fofoga ; bea nau feji maisha kaho babalagi, ‘o ‘ai
ki hono nima to‘omata‘u mono sebita. Tokua, ko
hono fakanofo ia, bea nau told fai ‘ae to'oga ‘oe
hou'eiki ki ha tu‘i fo‘ou, ‘aia koe fakaholo mai, ‘o
tu‘ulutui, ‘o ‘atu ha falukuga koula. ‘A, ‘oku
faigata‘a ‘etau talanoa ki ai. Ko Jisu e ‘oku nofo
moe kofu kulokula, ‘o gali tu‘i ‘aubito, ne ogo koe
veve be ‘ae kalauni moe sebita ; bea fakaholo mai e
‘ae kau tau, ‘o taki taha salute, “ Ei, Tu‘i Jiu; ” bea
nau toki bunou, ‘o humaki atu honau nima, ‘o hage
koe ‘atu tukuhau —ta, koe fu‘u bekalae ki ji‘i fofoga
gafuhia!!! Bea nau toki tu‘u, ‘o ‘anuhia, bea nau
to‘o ‘ae kaho, ‘o hau'aki ‘ae kalauni, kae huhu ‘ae
tala‘i-kalauni ‘i hono fofoga. ‘Oi! ‘ae kataki me‘a
behe ‘e he ‘Alo ‘oe ‘Otua ! kae hoto naba'a lilo ‘e he
kataki ma‘ata !
Lolotoga ia, kuo nofo ‘a Bailato ‘o fakajio ; bea gaue
hono loto ‘o a‘u ki hono takele. Kuo ne maheni moe
fakamamahi behe‘i ‘oe kakai, ‘o ‘ikai ogo ki hono loto
tekejio; ka kuo te'eki te ne mamata ki ha toko taha
kuo behe. He koe aga ‘oe kakai kuo gaohi behe‘i ke
ha ma‘ama‘a mo fakalielia. Ka ko Jisu na‘e fakautu-


‘utu ai hono lagilagi. Bea o‘i ai hono loto ki he ‘ofa
—he ko hotau aga, hage koe tiki ‘oe uaji ‘ene
fefokiaki—‘o ne belie ke ne toe ‘ahi‘ahi, hei'ilo ‘e
tobono ‘ae loto ‘oe hou'eiki ‘i he'enau vakai ki he
mamahi ‘a honau fili. Kae‘uma‘a na‘e ai ha fa‘ahiga
fakamau mu‘a na‘e ui koe ‘ehe fa‘i; bea fakakaukan,
nai, ‘e Bailato ke taki behe, ‘o ne me‘a kitu‘a ‘o lea
kiate kinautolu, tokua, kuo ne ‘eke ta‘i, bea kuo
mahino ‘oku ne ‘ata'ata. Bea taki mei ai ‘a Jisu,
kuo ‘ai kiate ia ‘ae kalauni talatala, moe kofu
kulokula : bea tuhu ki ai ‘e Bailato, ‘0 no behe,
“ Yakai, koena ‘ae Tagata ! ”
Na‘e amanaki ‘e Bailito te nau momou he'enau jio
ki he‘ene mamahi, ‘ae tu‘u ‘ae g. tala ‘i ‘oluga, moe
taka'uli hono fofoga, mo bani ta‘ata‘a; mo nau
manatu ki hono kau'imaea na‘e toki fai. Kae ‘ikai
‘aubito; kae fekalagad mei he botu kotoabe,
“ Kalusefai ia ! kalusefae ia! ” Bea ‘ita ai ‘a Bailato,
‘o ne behe, “ Be‘i ‘ave ia ‘o kalusefai ‘ekimoutolu ; he
koau ‘oku ‘ikai teu ‘ilo ha'ane hia.” Kae ‘ikai fie fai
ia ‘e he hou'eiki Jiu, na‘a tu‘uganaki ia ‘e Bailato
hanau talatalaaid‘l ki Loma, ‘i he'enau tamated ‘ae
tagata kuo ‘oji fakaha ‘e he Kovana kuo ne ‘ata'ata.
Bea koeni, kuo ‘oji ‘enau g. talatalaaki launoa, ‘aia
koe behe koe agatu'u moe fie tu‘i &c. bea kuo hao ‘a
Jisu. Koia na‘e bau ke nau ‘omi ‘ae talatalaaki
mo‘oni kuo nau ha‘u mo kinautolu mei honau
fakamau'aga, ‘aia ko ‘ene behe, koe ‘ Alo ‘oe ‘Otua ia.
Bea ‘ai ‘e Bailato ‘ene fu'u teki, he‘ene fanogo ki
he me‘a koia; he na‘e hoa moe lau ‘a hono uaifi, mo
‘ene ogo'i a‘ana koe taha kehe ia. Bea ne toe ‘ave ia
ki he loto balasi, ‘o ne behe Ida Jisu, “ Mei fe, tu,
koe?” Kae ‘ikai momo'i tali ‘e Jisu ha me‘a. Bea


ofo ‘a Bailato, he, ne ogo kuo ne logo ‘i he ‘ao ‘oe
hou‘eiki, ka na‘e ‘ikai te ne amanaki te ne fai behe
kiate ia. Kola na‘a ne hehe ki ai, “ ‘Oku ‘ikai te ke
lea kiate au koa 1 ‘oku ‘ikai koa te ke ‘ilo ‘oku ou
aafai ke tukuage koe, bea ‘oku ou mafai ke kalusefai
koe ? ” Bea toki mato'o ‘ae fofoga ‘o Jisu, bea to mai
‘ae lea fakaofo koeni, “ ‘E ‘ikai te ke momo'i mafai
ha me‘a kiate au, ‘oka ne tae'oua hono tuku kiate
koe mei ‘Oluga. Koia ‘oku hulu atu ‘ae agabala a‘ana
na‘a ne tukuage au kiate koe.” Talaatu ua‘e hage
‘oku ‘ikai koe launoa, ka koe Tu‘i Loma mo'oni ‘oku
lea—‘a, koe taha ma'olugaage, he ko ‘ene lau ki he
tuku hono mafai mei ‘Oluga koe tali ‘ia ‘oe fehu‘i ‘a
Bailato, bea mahino ai ‘oku ‘ikai koe Mama. Bea
ogo‘i behe ‘e Bailato, kao‘uma‘a na‘a ne vakai kuo
fetogi tu‘uga—koena ia ‘ae fakamau, bea koia ‘ae
halaia. Kae‘uma‘a koe fakamau ‘au‘autotonu : he
kuo ne behe, ‘oku ke halaia koe, Bailito, kae hulu atu
be ‘a Kaiafasi mo kinautolu. Hono ‘ikai koe toki
fakamau fakaofo eni, ‘a hono tu‘o fitu, he ‘oku ‘ikai
ke gata ‘i ho takatonuhia ‘o Jisu ‘e he fakamau, ka
na‘e iku ki he fakahalaia ‘oe fakamau ‘eia na‘e
hobo.
Bea bau leva ‘ao loto ‘o Bailato ‘e ‘ikai mate ‘a
Jisu, ‘o ne ‘alu kitu‘a ke toe ‘ahi‘ahi. Kae fakaofo,
na‘e toe fakamau'i ia ‘e he kakai ‘itu‘a. Kuo nau
tuku kuo bau ‘a Jisu, bea, ‘i he mahino leva ‘oku fie
‘aofi ia ‘e Bailato, koe me‘a gei ‘enau ‘ita. Na‘a nau
tuku ‘ae faka‘aba‘aba, ka nau talatalaaki'i ‘ae
Kovana, tokua, ‘oku ne lago ki he tagata kuo agatu‘u
kia Sisa. Koe lea fakailifia ‘aubito eni, he ‘oku tau
lau'ilo kotoabe ki he nofo teteki ‘a Taibilio ‘i hono
motu, moe fakabogi aibe ‘oe hou‘eiki na‘a ne mahalo


kovi ki ai. Kane ogo ‘ene manavahe, kae toe
‘ahi‘ahi ‘e Bailato, ‘o ne fekau ke taki mai ‘a Jisu.
Koe ta faka‘oji eni hage koe febaki ‘ae ogo kaate ‘i
Uatalu ; bea na‘e ogo‘i behe ‘e Jione, ‘aia na‘a ne tu‘u
‘o mamata, bea ‘oku ne fakamatala hono g. migimigi'i
me‘a kotoa. Tokua, na‘e hu ‘a Bailato ki fale, ‘o ne
‘omi ‘a Jisu ‘eia, bea ne toki nofo ‘i hono taloni.
Na‘e tu‘u ia ‘i Kabata, ‘aia ko ha balebale na‘e
faliki maka. Koe me‘a tobutabu, bea na‘e ‘ave holo ‘e
he hou‘eiki ma‘oluga hage ko Jiuliasi Sisa, koe behe,
‘abe, koe koga ‘o Loma ‘oku nau nofo ai. ‘Oku fakaha,
foki, ‘e Jione hono ‘aho mo hono houa. Bea tala‘ehai
na‘e buli hono mamafa ki he hou'eiki, bea na‘a mo
kinautolu na‘a nau jilogo ai. Fokifa na‘e haga ‘e he
Kovana ki he kakai, ‘o ne tuhu kia Jisu ‘o ne behe,
“ Vakai, koena homou tu‘i! ”
Koe ta mo aga‘i ia ‘a Bailato. Kuo nau talatala-
aki'i ia ‘oku ne kau moe tagata ke tu‘u kia Sisi, kae
hage ‘oku ne behe, “Ko ‘eku lago ki ai koa 1 ‘lkai
kuou kau'imaea, mo va‘iga‘aki, mo fakalieliah ” Ko
‘ene bale‘i ia ‘enau ta. Bea ko hono ‘uhiga ‘e taha, ‘aia
na‘a ne ‘amanaki lava‘aki honau loto, hage na‘a ne
behe, “ Na'a mou ‘omi ‘ae tagata ki heni, koe‘uhi ko
‘ene taku koe tu‘i ia, bea na‘a tau kovi ki he bule‘aga.
Boa koeni kuou ‘eke hakili ki he me‘a, bea,,ta, ‘oku
mo'oni: ko homou tu‘i ia kuo mou ‘amanaki fuoloa
ki ai, bea ‘oku ‘ata ke mou ‘ave ‘o fakanofo, bea ‘e
‘ikai tau kovi ki Loma.”
Hono ‘ikai malie ‘ae fai ‘a Bailato, bea ‘oku
fakaofo ‘ae ta‘etali ‘ae hou‘eiki. Hono tagege ‘ae g.
senituli mo ‘enau nofo ‘o fakatetu'a ki ha hoko mai
honau tu‘i; bea koeni ‘oku tala mai ‘e he fakafafoga
‘oe Bule‘aga Eiki, kuo ‘ilo, bea ‘oku ‘ata ke nau


ma‘u. ‘Oiau ‘ao momeniti mamafa, he ‘oku tu‘u ‘i he
tali ‘ae hou'eiki Jiu ‘ae menu moe mala ‘o honau
fa‘ahiga! Ka kuo fuoloa fau ‘enau tuku ke bale
kiate kinautolu ‘ae meheka, moe manumanu, moe ‘ita,
moe fakafajifaji; kuo ‘akiha ai ‘ae lelei mei honau loto.
Kuo ban ke mate ‘a Jisu. Ka na‘o ha mai ‘e ikai
te nau lava honau loto kola ka ‘i he'enau li‘aki ‘enau
koloa kanokato —‘a ‘enau ‘amanaki ki he Misaia.
Kuo ta faka‘oji mai ‘e Bailato, bea nau ta faka'oji atu
kinautolu, ‘o nau moifua ‘ao Misaia ke fakaai ‘enau
‘ita, ‘o nau kalaga, “ ‘Oku ‘ikai hamau tu‘i ko Sisa
be.”
Bea nau toki lava. Na‘e manavahe ‘a Bailato ke
toe fai atu. Kuo nau momoi honau tu‘i, ‘o nofo kia
Sisa; bea, ka ne ne kei taukabo‘i ‘a Jisu, to ne tu-‘uta-
maki. Bea kanoni'aki ‘one manavahe ‘ene mamae
ki hono tu‘uga moe koloa, bea ikuna ai ‘ae ki‘i leiei
kuo ake ‘i hono loto. Koia na‘a ne ‘ai atu ‘ae lea
fakailifia “ ‘Alu ha taha ‘o teuteu ‘ae kolosi.” Kuo
‘oji. Kuo fai. Kuo tau ‘ae tau: kuo tu‘u ‘ae
hou‘eiki Jiu : kuo vaivai ‘a Bailato. Ka na‘e tatau
‘ae ogo fa‘ahi ‘i he me‘a ni—he na‘e talu ai ‘ae tuli
‘ae mala kiate kinautolu.
{‘Oku kei toe be.)


KOE VAHE XVI.
KOE BASIONE.
Koe Kalusefai.
‘I he lau ‘ae kakai Loma kuo kamata ‘ae kalusefai,
he koe kauhmaea koe koga ia ‘oe tautea. Koia ‘oku
ma‘ugata‘a ‘ae houa totonu ‘oe taki age ‘o Jisu ke
feia. Koe aga ‘oe Jiu na‘e ‘ikai te nau fa‘a lau ‘ae
houa kotoabe, ka koe g. houa be na‘e mamafa—hago
koe tolu moe ono moe hiva, ‘aia ko ‘etau hiva
bogibogi, moe ho‘ata, moe tolu efiafi: bea, ka ko ha
taimi ‘i he vaha'a ‘0 ha ogo houa behe, na‘e lau ‘e he
ni‘ihi ki he, ka koe ni‘ihi ki he. ‘Oku behe ‘e Maake,
“ Bea kuo hoko hono tolu ‘oe houa ‘i he'enau kalusefai
ia ”; ka ko Jione, “Ko hono houa koe ono nai.”
Koia, kabau na‘e hoko ‘i he vaha'a ‘oe 10 moe 11 ‘e
fakatou mo‘oni —koe jio ‘e ha taha ki he 3 kuo ‘oji,
koe taha ki he 6 ka hoko mai.
Koe ‘uluaki me‘a na‘e fai ‘e he kau tau ‘i he tuku
mai ‘o Jisu, na‘a nau to‘o ‘ae kofu kulokula. Kuo
‘oji ‘etau fakaha koe fakahloga ia ‘oe Tu‘i Loma, bea,
ka ne nau ‘ave ‘a Jisu ke kalusefai kuo kofo behe, ‘e
hage koe talakah honau tu‘i. He koe mate‘aga koia,
koe bekia ‘i he kolosi, koe toki me‘a na‘e fakalili‘a ki


ai ‘ae Loma. Seuke, na‘e behe moe Jiu. Na‘a uau
lau koe taubotu ‘i he mala‘ia, koe mala kuo o‘o, koe
me‘a fakamousa'a fonua. Ka na‘e ‘age‘age ia ‘i he
fehi'a ‘ae Loma ki ai. Na‘e tabu ‘aubito ‘aubito ke
tautea behe ha Loma : koe me‘a be ‘ae bobula : bea
na‘e tala ‘e honau tama boto ko Kikelo, “na‘a mo
hono higoa ‘oku ‘ikai tau ke manatu ki ai ‘e ha Loma,
'iima'a ha'ane jio ki ai be fanogoa.” Bea na‘e fehi‘a
ki ai mo Natula foki; he na‘e febaki moe aga ‘o
Natula ‘ofa, ‘aia koe fakafaigofua ‘ete bekia. He
koe mate ‘i ho kolosi, koe toki mate‘aga fakamamahi
age fau. He na‘e sivi ‘e he kau Loma, bea ‘oku tu‘u
ia ‘i he‘enau tohi lao, koe me‘a ia ki he agahala
taubotu, he ‘oku lahi hono mamahi ‘i he fakamomofi.
Ta ne‘ine‘i tuku ‘a Jisu ki ai, he koe fetogi ‘oe
Mama kuo bobuia, moe Mama kuo mala‘ia, moe Mama
kuo hilio hono agahala.
Koe aga ‘oe ‘uluaki kolosi koe fu‘u va‘akau na‘e
fakamata ‘o fokotu‘u, bea na‘e be‘ehi ki ai ‘ae kakai,
‘o fakatufanah. ‘Oku vavana hotau loto ‘i he
fakakaukau ki ai, ka ‘oku matamata na‘e tuku hono
aga koia koe ji‘i hono mamahi koe vave ‘enau bekia.
Koia na‘a nau tuku ‘ae fakatufana‘i, ka nau fuhi be,
fakanimataha be fakave‘etaha, ‘o tuku aibe; bea
na‘e kovi age ia, tokua, ‘io, na‘e behe ‘ae fakalili‘a
‘ae kakai ki ai na‘a nau faka‘ehi‘ehi mei he me‘a
ni‘ihi na‘a tautau behe kinautolu ‘olea MU ‘enau hehla.
Na‘e ai ha fonua, tokua, na‘e lahi ai ‘ete tamate‘i kita
‘ekita, bea na‘e ta‘ofi koe tala ‘e honau ‘eiki, ka mate
behe ha taha, ‘e tautau ‘i he kolosi hono ‘aga‘aga
na‘e behe ‘ene o‘o kiate kinautolu ‘ae mala ‘oe mate
kalusefai.
Ka na‘e faifai, ‘o nau fa‘u ‘ae kolosi ‘aki ha ‘akau


‘e ua, ‘o nau ‘ahi'ahi ha aga kehekehe, ko ‘euau feiga
aibe ke fakalahi mo fakatologa houo mamahi. Koe
fa'ahiga ‘e taha na‘e hage ha X, bea ‘oku ui ia koe
Kolosi ‘a Sa Anitelu, koe‘uhi, tokua, na‘e mate ia ‘i
ha kolosi ‘e taha na‘e hage koia. Koe kolosi ‘e taha
no‘a hage koe T, bea ‘oku ui koe Kolosi ‘a Sa
Anitoni, koe'uhi na‘e bule'i behe ‘ae kofu ‘oe sagato
koia. Ka koe kolosi na‘e lain hono gaue'aki koe
Kolosi faka-Loma ( + ) bea koia ia ‘oku tau maheni ai
‘i he g. fakatata ki he kalusefai ‘o Jisu : bea ‘oku
mahino koia ia na‘e feia ai hotau fakamo‘ui. Na‘e
'ikai gaohi'aki ‘ae ‘akau mahu‘iga, ka koe ‘akau
vale be : koe taha na‘e loloa, ‘o tu‘u ‘i he kelekele;
koe taha na‘e nounou ‘o ‘ai fakalava, ofi ki he ‘ulu‘i
‘akau, ‘aia na‘e tomo hake ke tu‘u ai ‘ae higoa, moe
agahala ‘oku ne mate ai. Na‘e fakama‘u ‘ae ogo
nima ki he ogo mui ‘oe ‘akau fakalava, bea ko va‘e
ki he ‘akau loto : bea na‘e tuku taube ai, kae‘oua ke
nau mate ‘i he mamahi. Koe ni‘ihi na‘e fakama‘u
ha‘i, koe ni‘ihi na‘e tuki fa‘o: bea, ‘i he‘enau vakai
‘oku vave ‘ae mate koe mamafa ‘oe jino ‘o mahae ai
‘ae nima, koia na‘a nau ‘ai ha ki‘i me‘a fe‘uga moe
tu‘ugaiku ke ta‘ofi ‘ene homo hifo.
Koe aga ia ‘oe kolosi na‘e ‘omi ‘o hilifaki kia Jisu,
bea mo ha ogo jiano na‘a na ‘i he kaiha‘akau, nai, mo
Balabasa. Kuo hao honau takimu‘a ko Jisu Ba
Labasa, ‘aia na‘e totonu ke ne lotoloto‘i ‘iate kinaua;
bea kuo fetogi ia e Jisu Ba-Jiosifa, ‘ae Aga‘ofa mo
Ma‘oni‘oni. Na‘e toki fakamo‘oni ai ki he kikite ‘a
Aisea, “ ‘e lau ‘ae Misaia fakataha moe kau faikovi.”
Na‘e mu‘omu‘a ‘iate kinautolu, taki taha, ha tagata,
‘oku ne to‘o ha laubaba kuo tohi ai ‘ae higoa moe
agahala ‘oku ne mate ai. Bea na‘e tu‘u takai ‘ae


tu'uga tau Loma kuo tuku kiato kinautolu hono fai.
Kabau na‘a nau taki fa, hage ko Jisu, ta na‘e toko
12 be ‘ae kau sotia. Ka na‘e ‘ikai tuku ‘e Bailito
hono fai ki ha ofisa jib, ka ne fekau ha fu‘u senitulio
ke ‘alu ‘o bule ai, ko ‘ene ogo‘i, nai, koe me‘a mamafa.
Na‘e behe ‘ae fonoga na‘e matuku atu mei he Balasi
‘i Selusalema, ‘i he ‘aho Faite, ko h. 5 ‘o Ebeleli ‘i h.
30 T.J.
‘Oku lahi ‘ae fakamatala ‘oku tu‘u ‘i he g. tohi
Katolika ki he ‘alu koia mei he balasi ki Kalevale,
‘aia ‘oku nau ui ko “"Via Tololosa” (ko “ Hala
Mamahi ”) ; bea kuo nau faka‘iloga‘i ‘i Selusalema
‘ae g. botu na‘a nau tutu‘u ai. - Oku te faka'amu
kita ke te tui ki ha me‘a ni'ihi—seuke, kohai ‘oku
‘ikai te ne fie ‘alu, ‘o ‘uma ki he maka ‘oe hala na‘e
lave ki ai ji'ono to'ukubu na‘e tukifa'o ma'ata? Ka
ko hono kovi koe fakamahalo hono kotoa. Na‘e holoki
‘ae kolo, ‘o li'aki; bea, ‘i hono toe nofoba, kuo buli
hono g. me‘a lahi; bea na‘e ‘ikai ha lau ki Via Tolo-
losa, kae'oua ke hili -ae afe‘i ta‘u tubu. Kae‘uma‘a
na‘e hala ‘enau lau ki he tu'uga ‘o Kalevale; boa
kuo told ‘ilo ki mui ni hono totonu. Koia kuo bau
ke tau tuku ‘ae g. fakamatala koia, ka tau gata be ‘i
he me‘a ‘oku tu‘u ‘i ho Tohitabu.
Kuo to leva ki tu‘a-balasi ‘ae fonoga, bea lolofi mai
ha fu‘u kakai ‘o muimui atu. ‘Oku matamata na‘e
ha‘u koe fie mamata, bea ai, nai, ha manuki ‘e fai, he
koe taimi koia na‘e ‘ikai ha ‘ofa ki he tu‘utamaki.
Koe me‘a ki hono g. fili, ko ha‘a taula‘eiki, te nau hala
kehe, nai, ‘o mu‘omu‘a ki he botu ‘e fai ai ‘ae tautea.

Bea, ‘i he hilifaki ki ai ‘ae fu‘u ‘akau ‘e ua, na‘e ‘ikai

‘akau ‘ekinautolu. Fokifa ‘oku nau jio ki ha togata
‘oku ha‘u mei ‘uta mo ‘ene tokonaki. Ko hono higoa

kolosi na‘a bogia ‘ae tagata.” Bea fai. ‘Oku hage


na‘e ‘ikai loto ki ai ‘a Saimone. Kane ogo ‘ene teteki,

‘ikai fie fetogi 1

Koe me‘a na‘e o‘o, koe fu‘u mala ‘oku tu‘unuku mai ki
ji‘i kau feline na, ‘aia kuo nau ogo‘i hono fakalielia‘i.
Ko honau ni‘ihi ‘e mo‘ui atu ki he ‘akolo'i ‘o Selusa-
lema, ‘o nau ‘ilo ha g. mamahi ‘e keheage. Koe me‘a

he fu‘u mamahi! ‘Ae maikiiki ‘a hono nima moe
va‘e, bea gatoto, foki, ‘ae g. hokotaga hui! Kane

hua‘i—hei'ilo be fonu ha besoni be ‘ikai. Kane lahi
ha ta‘ata‘a ‘e mahua, behe ‘e vave ‘ene bogia, moe

‘ae boko ‘ae g. to‘oga ‘OO lavea moe taube. Koe me‘a

ai ‘ae fetafeaki ‘oe toto ‘o fa‘olaki ki ha botu ni‘ihi—

kita, ‘aia na‘e bau ke me‘a mo hoko ; bea kohai ‘e lau

ha mama ‘ae g. matamonuka, koe ta moe me'akula ;

Koe Tu‘i Jiu eni.

mo'oni be ‘ae kau taula'eiki : na‘e ‘ikai te ne lava
ko fakamo‘ui ia ; ‘o ‘ikai koe‘uhi ko ha‘ane faigata'a,
ka koe'uhi koe malohi o‘ene ‘ofa. Ko ‘ene ‘ofa be
na‘e ma‘utagl ai ‘ae fa‘o, ‘o ne rao'utaubea aibe.
Ka kuo ban na‘a ne ogo‘i ‘enau lea fakamahuahu he
koe tagata: bea na‘e lea ‘e he loto ‘o hono jino ke ne
ta‘aki ‘ae fa‘o, ‘o ‘alu hifo mei he ‘akau, ke fakamo-
‘oni ko Misaia ia. Kae monu, na‘e lomia ‘e hono
finagalo‘ofa, ‘o no toe ikuna ‘i he tau koia, foki, ‘o ne
ukuma fakalogobe.
Lolotoga ia na‘e ai ha me‘a na‘e fai ‘i he lalo
Kolosi, ‘aia ‘oku fakaofo, koe'uhi na‘e kikite ki ai ‘e
Tevita koe afe‘i ta‘u ki mu‘a atu. Koe aga aibe ‘oe
kakai ‘oku mate tamate'i ‘oku ma‘u honau kofu
‘ekinautolu ‘oku fai. Tala'ehai na‘e lahi ‘ae kofu
‘o Jisu, koe sote be, naf, moe bulubulu. Koe me‘a ki
he bulubulu, na‘a nau hae fa, ke nau taki taha ha
matai; ka, ‘oka ne nau fai behe ki he sote, ‘e maumau,
he na‘e lalaga fua be. Bea na‘a nau behe ke talotalo
ki ai, ‘o nau nofo hifo ‘o fai; bea ma‘u ‘eia na‘e tonu
ki ai. Hono ‘ikai fakaofo ! Lolotoga ‘oku taukave
‘e he kau taula'eiki na ‘oku ‘ikai koe Misaia ia, kae
fai ‘e he kau hiteni ni kiate ia ‘ae me'a ne tfilai/a'i
mei mu‘a koe faka'iloga o‘ene Misaia!
Kae taunoni aibe ‘ae tuvagia ‘o Jisu. Ka‘e ‘ikai


koo hou'eiki be, ka na‘e bihia ai moc kakai na‘e ha‘u
ke mamata. Koia na‘e ogo mai mei he botu kotoabe
‘ae talaka'i ‘o hotau ‘Eiki, ‘a hono manukhi mo
fakajikaka'i. ‘Oku tau ‘ilo na‘e ‘ajili ai hono
mamahi, bca ‘e tagi hono loto'i tagata ke ta‘aki mai
‘ae fa‘o, ‘o ‘alu hifo, ke tamate'aki ‘enau lau. Ka
na‘e malohi be hono fmagalo, ‘o ne fakama‘uma‘u, ho
koe Lami ‘ae ‘Otua ia, bea ne fakalogo be hage ha
lami noa. Ka kuo tokagah ‘e he kaiha‘akau ‘e taha
‘enau lea na‘e kau ki he‘ene Misaia, ‘o ne gaohia ‘a
Jisu he'eno behe, “‘lkai koe Misaia koe? be‘i
fakahaofi koe mo kimaua.” ‘E, ‘oua na‘a tau lau‘i
ia, ho kuo ne ‘i ho kona ‘oe mamahi. Seuko, ‘oku
meimei ha kiate au kuo ai ‘ene ki‘i tui koe Misaia ‘a
Jisu, ‘aia na‘a ne ‘ita ai ‘i he‘cne ta'efai ha me‘a.
Hei'ilo ai; ka kuo bau na‘e ogo kiate kinaua ‘ae
to'oga kehe ‘ae toko taha ni ‘oku nau kaugamamahi,
‘a ‘ene hufia na‘e fai, ‘a ‘ene kataki fakalogo ; bea
na‘a kuo kamata ‘ae fakabo‘uli ‘ae la‘a. Kae kehe,
na‘e faifai bea e‘a ki he kaiha‘akau ‘e taha koe
Misaia mo'oni eni, koe Tu‘i Jiu, ‘o hage koe tohi na;
bea ne tafoki kia Jisu, ‘o ne behe, “ ‘E Jisu, manatu'i
au, ‘oka ke ka hoko mai kuo ke bule‘aga.” Kohai
‘e lau ki. he fakafiemalie ‘o Jisu ‘e he fo‘i lea koia?
Na‘e mei faigofua ke tui ki he‘ene Misaia ‘e he kau
Tisaibale na‘e mamata ki he‘ene faka‘a ‘ae kui mo
fakama'a ‘ae kilia, mo fafaga ‘ae g. toko afe : ka koe
lava ‘e ha toko taha te tui kiate ia ‘oku ne tautau ‘i
he kolosi —tala atu koe toki tui ia ; bea na‘e hage ha
vai kauaki, ‘o lelu ji‘i ai ‘ene mamahi. Bea ne tali
leva ‘ae lea ‘a ji‘i tagata, ‘o ne hagai fofoga ki he'ene

‘aho ni tb kb ‘I Balataisi mo au.” Tagane ! ‘ae


tu‘utai ‘a hotau To‘a ! ne ogo koo tau milimilijinc
‘oku fai moe Fill Fakamui, ka ‘oku hage ‘oku ne fai

laumalie kuo mei ‘ave ‘e he Tovolo!
‘Oku tau ‘ilo na‘e lau ‘o Jisu ko hono kaiga a‘ene
Kau Tisaibale ; ko kinautolu ko ‘ene fa‘e mo hono
faga tokoua. Bea koeni kuo ne tokonaki ma‘a hono
kaiga koe, bea ne manatu ai ki hono kaiga ino'oni
na‘e tu‘u hena ‘o fakafe‘ao. ‘Oiaue, hono li‘aki ‘oku
fai! Kofa'a ‘a Bita fie-‘alu-bilisone-moia, mo Semisi
fie-nofo-hono-to‘omata‘u 1 Ko Jione be, nai, na‘e kei
fai hono fatogia, ‘o ne tu‘u ofi ki hono kaume'a.
Koia be, nai, ‘i he kau tagata na‘o fakato‘oto‘a ke
ha‘u ‘o mamata ; ka na‘e toko lahi ‘ae kau fefine, he
ko ho'onautolu ia tau ke li‘aki mo‘ui ma‘a honau
‘ofa‘aga. Koe toko fa ‘oku lau ki ai ‘e he tohi ‘a
Jione, bea ko honau toko tolu ko ‘ene fa‘e ‘i he lau
faka-Toga, ko Mele mei Makitala be na‘e ‘ikai ko
hono kaiga : kae kehe, ‘oku lau ‘e he g. talatubu'a,
ko Mele, koe uaifi ‘o Kaliobasi, mo Salome koe fa‘e ‘a
Jione, koe fetokigataha mo ‘ene fa‘e ko Mele.
Ka‘e fakamo'oni eni Ida Mele ‘ae lea ‘a Sakalaia ‘i
he Temibale, ‘o behe ‘e ulu ha heleta ‘i hono loto ‘i
he‘ene tama. Bea koe fefine fe ‘e ‘ikai lavea hono
loto ‘i he‘ene jio ki he'ene tama ‘oku behe hono
fakamamahifi. Bea tala‘ehai na‘e buli ‘ia Jisu ‘ene
tu‘u, bea ne ogo e fu‘u tau ‘oku ne mo'ua ai, ka na‘a
ne manatu ki ji‘i feline kuone fakahuhu ia, motauhi
ia ‘i he‘ene valevale; bea ne fakakaukau hano tauhi
‘oka hiki ia". Na‘e ‘ikai ‘i ai ha taha ‘o hono foto-
tehina mo‘oni ke ne tuku ki ai ‘enau fa‘e ; kae‘uma‘a
kuo te‘eki ke nau tui kiate ia, bea na‘e ‘ikai te ne
fa‘a falala kiate kinautolu. Ka ko Jione ena hono

fekau te ne tuku kiate ia, te ne fai: kae‘uma‘a ‘oku
ne ofi kiate ia ‘i he Kau Tisaibale kotoabe ‘i he
‘ulugaaga koia koe ‘ofa. Bea tala'ehai koe taha atu,
he, ‘i he lau faka-Toga koe tama ‘aMele, he koetama,

bea koe‘uma‘a ‘ene mamata ki ai. Koia na‘a ne haga
kia Mele, ‘one behe, “Fepinb, kobna ho‘o tama ; ”
bea ne toki haga kia Jione, ‘o ne behe, “ Koena
ho‘o pa‘e.” ‘Oku hage, foki, na‘a ne kamo ki ai ko
‘ave leva, bea ‘ilo ‘e Jione hono ‘uhiga, ‘o ne taki ‘a
Mele ki hono ‘abi o‘ona na‘e tu‘u ‘i Selusalema, ‘o ne
toki foki mai ki he Kolosi ke mamata ki hono faka'oji.
Kuo ‘oji eni ‘a Mamani; kuo ne hu‘ihu‘i hono
kakaikotoa ‘o a‘u ki hono mo‘oni mo'oni, bea kuo ne
toko taha. Ka na‘e ‘ikai hage ko ‘ene lau mu‘a ‘oku
ne toko taha, he ne ‘iate ia ‘ae Tamai ; ka, na‘a moe
kau koia, kuo boko hono taimi ke mavae. Na‘a ne
‘ilo be ki ai; kae kehe, na‘a ne ogona ‘ae ha‘u ha
kovi ‘oku taha ‘ana, ‘o hulu atu ‘i he me‘a na‘a ne
ago‘i ‘i Ketisemani. Bea ta koia. Kuo behe ‘ene
mousa'a ‘i he agahala ‘ae kakai, na‘a mo ‘ene Tamai
‘oku ne li'aki ia. Koe misiteli ia : hage ‘oku feiga
‘e he kau agelo ke fakajio hifo ki ai, ka ‘oku ‘ikai.
Na‘e ‘ilo ‘e he lagi, bea na‘e gatoto ‘ae “ Seakale ‘o
Natula.” Kae fefe ! Hage koe ‘oho ‘a ha bule‘aga
‘i heni ‘i he bau ‘ae finagalo ‘oe tu‘i ‘e mate tamate‘i
hono ‘alo koe‘uhi ko ‘ene agahala, ne ogo koe Hoko;
behe na‘e vavana ‘ae hou‘eiki ‘oe Univesi ‘i he ha
kuo motu ‘ae feohi ‘ae ‘Afifio, bea kuo haga kehe ‘ae
Tamai mei he ‘Alo, ‘aia ‘oku tatau moe mate ‘i heni.


Na‘e ‘ai tauaga‘aleva ‘ae ‘Alofi. Na‘e gatole mai ha
fu'u me‘a, ‘o fakabulou ‘ae la‘a—na‘e ‘ikai koe la‘a-
mate, he kuo katoa ‘ae mahina—bea na‘e ofogi ‘o he
g. fonua, be koeha ha fu‘u me‘a ‘oku fai. Hage na‘e
logo ai ‘ae hou‘eiki moe kakai, ‘o ‘ikai ‘kei fai ha lau;
kae mo'ulogoa ‘ae fa'ahiga kotoa, hea vavana ‘ae
lofco fulibe, ‘o nau hoha‘a tu‘u, ‘o nau behe, “ Na‘a
koe mo'oni koe Misaia eni.”
Koe houa ‘e tolu ‘ene behe, mei he ho'ata ki he
tolu efiafi, he koe me‘a fakalagi, koe tautea faka-
‘Otua. Bea koe mamahi ‘a Jisu ‘i he g. houa koia ‘e
‘ikai lava ‘e ha taha ke fakamatala. Koe me‘a be
‘oku tau ‘ilo ki ai—
“ Ne inumia ‘ae ‘ibu mala.”
,Na‘e hilifaki kiate ia ‘ae tautea taubotu koe mavahe
mei he ‘Otua. Na'a ne kataki fakalogobe, he koe
kotoa ‘o hono ivi na‘e fai‘aki. Fakafeta'i he tuku
‘ae gaue fakamo'ui ki ha taha na‘e fita ; ka ne ‘ikai,
behe ne ‘ikai lava hono fuejia ‘o hotau tautea. ‘Oku
tau ‘ilo, ka lahi ha mamahi, ‘oku tatau ha fo‘i
momeniti mo ha fu‘u houa. Bea ke faka‘uta mu‘a ki
he gali fuoloa ‘oe g. momeniti, ‘oe houa ‘e tolu koia.
Talaatu, na‘e hage ha itaniti.
Ka na‘e faifai bea ‘oji. Kuo ukiukivale ‘a Mala :
kuo maha hono ivi, kae kei tu‘u be ‘a Jisu. Kuo
<ata eni ke foki mai ‘ae ‘Otua. Na‘e ‘ilo leva ‘a
Lagi, bea ulo mai ha fo‘i huelo mei he la‘a. Bea ‘ilo
mo Jisu. Ka, ‘i he toe haga mai ‘ae fofoga o‘ene

ne kalaga, Ilai, Ilia, lama sabakatanai ! (‘E
hoku ‘Otda, ‘b hoku ‘Otua, na‘a ke li‘aki au
kae ha !) ”


Koe toki lea eni ‘oku ha ai ‘ae mamahi ‘a Jisu, ‘a
! ene kakuga he lau behe ki he‘ene Tamai, ‘o meimei
hage ko ha hanu. Ka hono ‘ikai mahino ai koe
tagata ‘a Jisu? Ko hotau aga ia ‘oku ha ‘i he lea
koia. Talaatu ko hono tagata na‘e fai'aki ‘ae tau ‘i
he ‘akau; bea ne ogo kuo lava, ka koe koto volu
hono kotoa.
Moe me‘a ‘e taha. Ko hotau aga ka faigataa'ia
behe, ke tokonhaki hotau loto ha fakamatala ki ha
kakai kehe na‘e mo‘ua behe, ‘o tau lau ‘enau to‘oga
na‘e fai, mo ‘enau lea, ke lotaki'aki hotau g.
ulugaaga ke ukuma. Bea na‘e behe mo Jisu. Na‘e
tu‘o lahi ‘ae tukuhaujia a‘ene kui ko Tevita, ‘ene
mo‘ua ‘i he tau mo hono g. fili; bea, monu, ne ne fa‘u

fai, bea koe tohi himi ia ‘oe jiaji ‘o 0110‘aho. Bea
kuo ma‘u loto ‘e Jisu hono me‘a lahi; bea hage ko
‘etau fili,ha himi ‘oku hoa mo hoto mamahi ‘oku fai,
‘o te lau mo lau ke bine‘i‘aki hoto loto; behe kuo

na‘e hoa ‘aubito mo ‘ene me‘a—ko h. xxii. Tokaase
O
ha faigata‘a na‘e hoko kia Tevita, ‘o tubu ai ‘ene

‘i he ‘akau, ‘o vili hono nima mo hono va‘e ke fuhi-

Na‘a ke li'aki au kae ha?
Ka na‘e ogo kehe ia ki lie kakai na‘e nofo ofi mai,
he koe lea “ Ilai ” koe fakanounou ‘oe higoa ko Ilaijia ;
bea, ‘i he taimi koe, na‘a nau nofo ‘amanaki ‘e toe
ha‘u ‘ae balofita kola —seuke, ‘i he fai ‘oe Basova
‘anebo na‘a nau tuku ava ha nofo‘aga ‘e taha mo'ona,
na‘a ‘iloage, te ne ha‘u. Bea na‘e lau ‘e he kau
Balofita, ka ofi ‘ene ha‘ele mai, ‘e taka'uli ‘ae la‘a :
bea na‘a koeni ia ‘oku fai : bea koe ui eni ki ai ‘e he
tagata gali Misaia ni, ‘Oku ‘ikai mahino ‘ae me‘a
na‘e hoko ai. ‘Oku hage na‘e tu‘u ha taha ke fai ha
me‘a, kae ta‘ofi ‘e he kakai kehe ke tukua, ke nau
yakai be ha‘u ‘a Ilaijia be ‘ikai. Na‘a ko Bita kuo
ne totolo mai ‘i he bo‘uli, bea, ‘i he‘ene fanogo ki
he le‘o ‘oe Tagata'eiki, kuo ne ‘oho ke vete ia mei he
akau—be ha fua. Kae kehe ‘oku gali ko Bita na‘e
ma‘u mei ai hono fa koeni ‘oe g. lea ‘a Jisu, ‘i he
kolosi. Na‘e ‘ikai ‘i ai ‘a Jione —kuo ne ‘alu mo
Mele ki ‘abi. ‘Oku ‘ikai ha lau ‘a Luke ki ai—he
kuo ‘alu ‘a Mele, ‘aia na‘e fa‘a ma‘u mei ai ‘e Luke
‘ene fakamatala. ‘Oku tu‘u ‘ia Matiu, ka ‘oku
matamata koe ma‘u talanoa, he kuo ne ‘ai faka-
Hebelu. Ko Maake be, ‘aia koe Kosibeli ‘a Bita,
tokua, ‘oku ha faka-Alamea ai ‘o belie, “ Iloi, Iloi! ” :
bea ‘oku tau ogona leva koe fakamatala ia ‘a ha taha
na‘e ‘i ai tonu, ‘o fanogo. Talaatu, ne moulu mai ‘a
Bita‘i he to mai ‘ae bo'uli, bea, ‘i he'ene fanogo ki he
tagi mamahi ‘a ji‘ono ‘Eiki, na‘a ne ‘oho atu ke
hamuji mai, be ha, ka ne toe fo‘i ‘i he lau ‘ae kakai.


Ee'uga moia, kuo foki mai ‘a Jione, ‘o ne fanogo ki
hono nirna ‘oe lea ‘a Jisu. ‘Oku tau ‘ilo hotau aga.
Koe lolotoga ‘ae mamahi lahi ‘i he‘ete kukuta, ‘oku
hage ‘aku mate ‘ae g. oga‘aga ‘oe jino, bea ‘oku ‘ikai
te tau mei jio, be fanogo, be ogo‘i ha me‘a : ka, ‘i
he'ene maluluage leva, ‘oku toe ake hake ‘ae g. aga
‘oe jino. Bea behe mo Jisu. ‘Oku tau ‘ilo koe me‘a
‘oku vivili ‘i he kakai ‘oku kalusefai koe fieinu; bea
koe houa eni ‘e tolu moe tagi inu ‘e he jino ‘o hotau
‘Eiki, kae ta'omi ia ‘e he mamahi lahi ‘i he‘ene
mavae mo ‘ene Tamai. Ka, ‘i he malona hifo leva,
na‘a ne ogo‘i ‘ae tagi hono jino, ‘o ne lea hifo, “ Oku
ou fienda.” Na‘e ‘ikai ko ‘enau aga ke tali ‘ae
kole behe ‘ae kakai na‘e kalusefai, ka kuo ogo ki
honau loto ‘ae fakabo'uli ‘ae la‘a, moe to'oga kehe
‘ae Toko Taha koeni ; kae‘uma‘a na‘a nau loto ke ne
tologa ke vakai be ha‘u ‘a Ilaijia be ‘ikai. Koia na‘e
‘alu ‘ae sotia ‘e taha ki he‘ene ‘aga-uaine, ‘o ne to‘o
‘ae oma na‘e tabuni ‘aki, ‘o ne unu ki he uaine.
Bea ‘i he ‘ikai te ne a’u ki he fofoga ‘o Jisu, na‘a ne
hunuki ha ki‘i va'akau ki he oma, ‘o ne ‘ohake'aki
kia Jisu ke ne miji mei ai. ‘Oku ui ‘e he kau
Evagelio ‘ae me‘a na‘a ne inu koe vinika, bea ‘oku
rao‘oni hono higoa koia, he na‘e mahimahi ‘ae uaine
na‘e me‘ainu‘aki ‘e he tau Loma, ‘o tatau mate moe
vinika ‘o onoboni. Tau moia ‘ae me'ainu ‘ae tau, he
kuo ne ne hoko koe tagata-tau.
‘Oku faikehekehe ‘ae lau ‘ae kau Evagelio ki he
va'akau na‘e hunuki ki he oma. ‘Oku behe ‘e Matiu
koe Jcaho, ka ko Jione koe isdbe. Te tau tui kia
Jione he na‘e ofi, ka ‘oku mahino mei he lau behe ‘e
Matiu, kuo ne ma‘u koe va‘akau na‘e fai‘aki hono
manuki‘i, ‘aia na‘a ne mahalo ai koe kaho. Koia


‘oku tau behe koe va‘a isobe koia koe me‘a ia na‘e
fa‘u‘aki hono kalauni talatala —■ he na‘e ai ha
fa‘ahiga isobe, tokua, na‘o tala. Bea hono ‘ikai koe
bekebeklitama ia ki ho me‘a ‘e hoko ? Na‘a moeni
kuo kamata ‘aoga hono mamahhaga mo hono
manuki‘aga.
Ka ‘i he‘etau fanogo leva ki he lea “ isobe,” ‘oku
fotu mai mo ha me‘a. ‘Oku lau'ilo kotoabe koe me‘a
ia ‘na‘e gaue‘aki ‘i he fakama‘a ‘oe kilia ‘oka matafi;
bea kuo hoko ia koe lea, hage koe lau ‘a Tevita,
“Ke ke fakama'a isobe au ” (Same lx.) ; ‘o behe, ke
mahino kuo ne ma‘a mei he me‘a mousa‘aage fau
kuo ne fai, ‘i he fakabogi ‘o Ulaia moe tono‘i ‘o hono
unoho. Koia, ne ogo na‘e ‘uhiga kehe ‘ae ‘ai ‘ae
isobe kia Jisu, ka ‘oku tau behe na‘e ai mo hono
‘uhiga faka-Jiu —koe behe, kuo matafi ‘ae mousa‘a ‘oe
agahala ‘a Mamani na‘e hilifaki ki ai. Bea ‘ajili
‘etau tui ki ai, he na‘e faka‘uhiga ‘0 he Labai ni'ihi
‘a h. liii. ‘o Aisea, koe behe, ‘e hoko ‘ae Misaia koe
kilia. Kae fefe! he koe kilia koe taibe, koe taha
‘oku agahala'ia ‘aubito. Bea, ‘i he hoko ‘a Jisu koe
me‘a agahala koe'uhi ko kitautolu, ko hono taibe
totonu, koe kilia. Ka, ‘i he ‘ai ‘ae isobe ki ai, na‘e
hage koe fakaha kuo matafi ia : kuo mate ‘ae tabu,
kuo ‘ata ‘ae hu, kuo gofua ‘ae feohi.
Koia na‘e bekia ‘a Kalaisi koe ikuna. Hage koe
‘eikitau ni‘ihi, ‘aia kuo nau to ‘i he tau, ka nau tologa
be ke nau ‘ilo kuo lava; behe ‘a Jisu, na‘e mahino ki
hono finagalo ‘i he‘ene hokotaki, kuo toka ‘ae fili.
Hage kuo ‘aoga kiate ia ‘ene ki‘i inu, ‘o mama ai
hono fofoga, ‘o ne fakama‘u hifo ke faka‘oji. Kuo
bau hono loto ke bekia, ka te ne fa‘iteliha ki hano
taimi, he koe ‘Eiki ‘oe mo‘ui; bea ko ‘ene fakavaivai


kia Mate koe fai tau‘ataina be. ‘Io, ‘oku te tui ko
hono ‘uhiga ia o‘one fie tali ‘ae vinika ko ‘ene tie
bekia malohi, ‘o ‘oua na‘a gali ko ha vaivai. Ko
Mate ena ‘oku inovelo hono tao, kae ‘ikai ji‘i te ne
lava ha me‘a, kae'oua ke ne ‘ata mei hono ‘Eiki.
Bea vakai ‘e Jisu kuo hoko hono taimi lelei, Na‘e
‘ikai te ne fie fakanounou ‘ene mamahi, ‘o hage ko
ha‘ane kalo; ka, ‘oka toloi atu, ‘e ha‘u ‘ae sotia ‘o
feji‘i hono va‘e, ‘o ne bekia. Koia na‘a ne behe ke
fai leva. Ka, ‘i he te'eki ke ne ‘ai ‘ene fu‘u uku ki he
me‘a na‘a ne teteki ki ai, na‘a ne tilgaki hake ki
ji‘ono ‘ofa‘aga ‘i he lagi, ‘o ne behe, “ ‘Ala Tamai,
‘OKU OU TUKU HOKU LAUMALIE KI HO NIMA,” bea ne
toki haga ki he Fill Fakamui, ‘o ne ha‘aki atu hono
fu‘u le‘o, “ KUO ‘OJI! ” Veloi leva ‘e he Fill hono
tao fakamate, bea foa ‘ae mafu ‘o J isu (tabu mo ‘Ene
‘Afio) ; ‘o ne bunou hifo— kuo bekia.
(‘Oku kei toe be.)


KOE YAHE XVII.
KOE BASIONE.
Koe Telio,
Tald mei mu‘a moe lau ‘oku ogo kia Natula ‘ae g,
me‘a mamafa ‘oku lioko ‘i mamani; bea ‘oku ‘ikai ke
faigata'a ‘etau tui ki ai, ko ‘etau ‘ilo ‘oku fetu‘utaki
O ’
‘ae manu moe tagata moe agelo. Bea ka ‘oku kakai
‘ae Ta‘ehamai ‘i he kau agelo, bea ne‘ine‘i hoko ha g.
me‘a fakaofo ‘oka ai ha me‘a ‘e fai ‘i heni ‘oku ogo
kiate kinautolu; he ‘oku hage ‘oku nau fa‘iteliha kia
Natula. Kuo bau na‘e katoa mai ‘a Hevani, ‘o kabui
‘ae kolosi, he, talu ‘ae tu‘u ‘ae univesi koe toki me‘a
mamafa e kuo fai —koe Tub ‘o Lagi ‘oku hokataki.
Xa‘a ko ha ‘ao agelo na‘e fakabo‘uli ai ‘ae la‘a. Bea
ka ne ko ha kau Mama ‘oku nau kabui honau tub
‘oku bekia, he nifi koa ‘ae me‘a ‘e fai? ‘ae lau‘aitui
‘ae fetuki 2 ‘ae hae kofu ? Bea ke ‘oua na‘a fai ‘e he
kau agelo ha me‘a? Nebneb fakaha ‘e he Tohitabu
na‘e galulu ‘ae fonua ‘i he ‘iloage na‘e hala ‘ae ‘Eiki.
Talaatu, koe fetuki ia ‘ae kau agelo.
‘Oku ‘ikai teu tui koe mofuike ia na‘e jib. ‘Oku ou
behe na‘e ogo ki he gata‘aga ‘o Mamani; ka tala'ehai
na‘a nau bio ki hono ‘uhiga ke tohi. Ka ‘oku ai ha


lau ‘i ha tohi faka-Jiu ki ha fu‘u mofuike na‘e hoko
‘i he taimi koia, ‘o maumau'i ha koga ‘oe Temibale.
Kuo bau na‘e ogo‘i ‘e he kau mamata, ‘o fakalahi
‘enau bubutu'u: “ Na‘e mate ‘ae la‘a ‘anenai, bea
koeni ‘oku tete ‘ae fonua. Koeha, tama 1 ” Ka koe
senitulio be, nai, na‘e ‘ilo ki hono ‘uhiga. Ka‘a ne ‘i
he Balasi, nai, he fakafe'ao ‘oe Kovana, ‘i he fakamau'i
‘o Jisu, mo lau koe ‘Alo ‘oe ‘Otua ia; bea kuo ne
ogo‘i ‘ae matamatakehe ‘ae to‘oga kotoa ‘oe tagata ni
‘i hono kalusefai. Bea koia be, nai, na‘e tokaga‘l ‘ene
hekia, moe hoko leva ‘ae mofuike, ‘o ne behe, “ Ta
koe tagata ta‘ehalaia eni. Ta, na‘a ne mo‘oni be, koe
‘Alo ia ‘oe ‘Otua.”
He tala'ehai koe mofuike be. Koe feitu‘u koia na‘e
lahi ai ‘ae fonualoto na‘e foa ‘i he makatu'u, ‘o taki
taha tabuni'aki ha i’u‘u maka hage ha fuaga takai.
Bea, ‘i he hoko ‘ae mofuike koeni, na‘e teketeka mai
‘ae g. maka ‘iate ia be, ‘o tuku ava ‘ae g. fonualoto.
Ne‘ine‘i behe na‘a ne ilifia. Kohai ‘e ta'eilifia? Ka
hono ‘ikai malie ! Lau ‘e Mamani kuo mate ‘a Jisu ;
kae ‘ilo ‘e he kau agelo ko Mate be kuo mate, ‘o nau
hae leva ‘ae mataba ‘oe g. bilisone ni‘ihi kuo ne ki‘i
ai hani kakai. Koe bekebekatama ‘oe me‘a ‘e hoko
ki he fa'itoka kotoabe. Hono ‘ikai mo‘oni ‘a Baula,
“ E Mate kofa‘a ho‘o ikuna na ! ”
Bea ai mo ha me‘a na‘e fai ‘e ho kau agelo, nai.
Talu mei mu‘a moe tau ‘i he loto Temibale ha fu‘u
tatau ke tabui ‘ae Botu Tobutabu. Koe me'a
matalelei mo‘oni, he na‘e gaohi‘aki ‘ae tubenu lanu
kehekehe, ‘o ta ai hani selubimi. Ka ko hono ‘uhiga
na‘e kovi, he na‘e hage koe tu'u ‘ae selubimi ‘i he
mataba ‘o Balataisi, koe vahe‘i ‘oe tagata mei he
‘Otua. Ka, ‘i he momeniti koia na'e hala ai ‘a Jisu,


na‘e lele ‘ae kau agelo, ‘o hae hifo moe fiefia—kuo mate
‘ae tabu, kuo ‘at a ‘ae hu. Koe bokebekiitama moia,
foki, ki he holoki ‘oe ‘a-vahevahe, ‘o fakatahataha ‘ae
famili ‘oe ‘Otua.
Ka ua‘e buli ‘ae g. ‘uhiga koia ki he kakai. Koe
me‘a be na‘a nau ogo'i koe ilifia ; bea, ‘ajili ai, ko ‘enau
manatu ki he vavalo ‘a Jisu na‘e fai ‘i liono taki mai,
ki he tu'unuku ‘ae taimi te nau faka'amu ke higa mai
‘ae g. mo‘uga na ke nau uga ai. Koia, ‘i he ‘iloage
na‘e tala mai kuo bekia, na‘a nau fakaholo atu he
foki ki kolo, ‘o nau ji fatafata ‘i he ilifia, moe ‘ofa ‘i
he bekia.
Ka na‘e ‘ikai ‘alu kotoa. Ko ji‘i kau feline koia
na‘e tu‘u ofl ki he Kolosi, moe Kau Tisaibale ni‘ihi,
na‘e ‘ikai te nau ‘alu ‘i he ‘alu, ka nau nofo be ‘o alea
‘i ha me‘a ‘e fai; he koe to'oga ‘e taha ‘oe fefine, ka
bekia ha taha, bea gaile honau fatu ke teu‘i. Kate
nau ma‘u fefe ‘a ji‘i me‘afaka‘eiki na! Kuo nau
faigataa'ia mo'oni. Kuo ‘i ai ha kau kalusefai ni‘ihi
kuo ‘ohifo vave mei he kolosi, ‘o nau toe mo‘ui; koia
na‘e tabu ke yete ‘o fuoloa—‘aho ‘e ua be tolu—bea
o‘ku le‘o ‘ae kau sotia na‘a ala ha taha ki ai. Ka
kuo mahino kuo bekia j honau ‘ofa'aga, bea kabau ‘e
tuku fuoloa ‘e kovi. Kae‘uma‘a koe la‘a eka to, bea,
ka to leva, bea tabu he koe Sabate.
Monu kuo gaue moe loto ‘o honau g. fili koe hou'eiki
taula'eiki, he'enau manatu koe Sabate ‘abogibogi,
moe Katoaga Tobutabu; bea ‘e maumau ‘o kabau ‘e
tuku ai ‘ae mea fakamousa‘a, koe kau kalusefai. Koia
na‘a nau fakakaukau ke fai ‘ae fejifeji va‘e. Koe
me‘a koia na‘e tatataha hono fai, he na‘e fakavave ai
‘ae bekia, ka koe ‘uhiga ‘oe tautea kalusefai koe'uhi
ke tologa ‘ae mamahi ; bea ‘e ‘ikai lava ‘e he senitulio


ke fai ‘iate ia, bea na‘e bau ke nau ‘alu ki he Kovana
‘o kole. Ka‘e tali leva ‘e Bailato ko ‘ene ‘ofa, nai, kia
Jisu ; bea ‘i he ma‘u ‘e he senitulio ‘ae fekau na‘a ne
tuku ke nau fai ki he tagata koe moe, ka ne ta‘ofi
‘enau fai kia Jisu, he nn‘a ne ‘ilo kuo ne bekia. Bea
na‘e ofo ai ‘ae kau sotia ‘i he belie kuo bekia ‘a Jisu,
he koe me‘a fo'ou ha mate rave behe. Ka ‘oku
mo‘oni ‘oku taube hono ‘ulu moe jino ‘o hage ha
bekia j ka na‘a koe bogia be, bea ne toe ake, ‘o nau
fiu he nofo hono vakai. Koia na‘e haga ‘ae jiana ‘e
taha, ‘o veloi hono vakavaka ‘aki hono fu‘u tao—bea,
fakaofo, na‘e tafe mai ‘ae ta‘ata‘a moe vai !
‘Oku ‘ikai mahino be koe mana eni be ‘ikai. ‘Oku
lau ‘e he kau faito‘o, kuo ai ha ni'ihi kuo bekia koe
foa honau mafu ; bea, ‘i hono tafa, kuo ‘iloa ha me‘a
‘oku meimei hage koe vai ‘oku nofo fakataha moe
ta'ata'a. Ka koia aibe, ka koe me‘a ‘uhiga lahi; bea
‘oku tau fakafeta‘i ‘i he ‘i ai ‘a Jione ‘o mamata.
Bea hage na‘e ogo‘i behe ‘e Jione, he ‘oku ne ‘ai
mamafa ‘aubito ‘ene lea, “ Bea koia na‘a ne mamata
ai kuo ne fakamo'oni ki ai, bea ko ‘ene fakamo'oni
koe mo'oni ‘oe mo'oni: bea ‘oku ‘ilo ‘e he toko taha
koia ‘oku mo‘oni be ‘ene lau, koe'uhia ke mou tui
foki.”
Na‘e ha foki kia Jione ‘ae mamafa ‘oe tuku
ta'efeji’i ‘ae va‘e ‘o Jisu, ‘o fetogi'aki ‘ae hoka; ka
koe me‘a ia na‘e kikite ki ai. Koe tu‘utu‘uni ki he
fai ‘oe lami Basova, “ E ‘ikai te mou feji‘i hano hui ‘e
taha o‘ona.” Bea na‘e kikite foki ‘e Sakalaia (xi.),
“Te nau mamata kiate ia kuo nau hoka'i,” Ka na‘e
ai hano mamafa ‘oe me‘a na‘e ‘ikai ‘ilo ki ai ‘e Jione.
‘Oku ai ha fa‘ahiga ‘i onoboni ‘oku faigata‘a ‘enau tui
ne bekia ‘a Kalaisi, bea toetu'u ; bea ‘oku nau fie


taukave na‘e ‘ikai, tokua, ke mate ‘a Jisu, kae bogia
be. Kane ta'oua be ‘ae hoka ‘oku nau faigataa'ia ai.
Ta, ne toka mea‘i ‘e ho ‘Otua ‘e ai ha fa'ahiga behe,
‘o no tu‘utu‘uni ke fai ha me‘a ‘e matu‘aki mahino ai,
ne bekia mo'oni hono ‘Alo.
Na‘e ai ha toko ua ‘i he hou'eiki na‘e ‘ikai kau ‘i
he'enau gaiie bago—‘a Jiosifa mei Alematea mo
Kikotimasi. Koe ogo matabule lelei kinaua, bea na
tui kia Jisu ; ka na‘e ‘ikai to na o moe Kau Tisaibale,
koe taha ko ‘ene manavaji'i, bea koe taha ko hono
tu'uga ma'oluga. Ka na fakatou ‘ofa be ki ai. Bea,
‘i he mahino koe lote ‘oe hou'eiki ke tanu vave ‘ae
kau kalusefai na, na‘a na behe ko hono ava e ke fai
ha ‘ofa ki he ‘Eiki. Koia na‘e ‘alu ‘a Kikotimasi ke
kumi ahi fakatologa, kae ‘a Jiosifa ‘ae kole ki he
Kovana ‘ae me‘afaka‘eiki. Ke ogo kuo tu‘utu‘uni ‘e
Bailato ke fai ‘ae feji va‘e, ka na‘e ‘ikai te ne
‘amanaki ‘e vave behe ha me‘a, koia na‘a ne ta'ofi ‘a
Jiosifa kae‘oua ko ha‘u ‘ae senitulio ke ne ‘eke ; bea
ne toki tali fie tali, he ‘oku kei ogo ‘a Jisu ki hono
loto. Na‘e toki fakamo'oni ai ki he kikite, “‘E‘i he
kau koloaha ‘ae Misaia ‘i he‘ene bekia.”
Bea afe ‘a Jiosifa ki ha falekoloa, ‘o fakatau ha fu‘u
tubenu mahuhga, ‘o ne ‘alu moia ki Kalevale; bea
koia mo Jione moe kau fefine na‘a nau ‘ohifo ‘ae jino
‘o Jisu. Na‘e ‘ikai ha taimi ke tatafi lelei, ka nau
behe ke ‘ai atu be telia ‘ae Sabate, ka nau toki gaohi
lelei ‘i he ‘aho ‘e taha. Monu, na‘e lahi ‘enau me‘a
fakatologa, he na‘e ha‘u mo Nikotimasi ha fu‘u koto
mula moe alosi kuo fetuiaki, ‘aia koe me‘a ‘oku ne
ta‘ofi ‘ae kovi. ‘Oku fakaha ‘e he g. tohi faka-Jiu
koe ‘eiki koloaha fakamanavahe ‘a ISTikotimasi, bea
‘oku ha ia ‘i he lahi ‘oe ahi kuo ne ‘omi, he koe bauui


‘e teau hono mamafa. Koia na‘a nau folahi ‘ae
tubenu, bea ‘ai ki aiha fu‘u ahi, bea nau fakaha‘ele
ki ai ‘ae ‘Eiki, ‘o tanu ahi, bea nau toki ha‘i takai-
‘aki ‘ae tubenu ke ma‘u ko fatu'a be na‘e ha‘i‘aki
ha holoholo.
Kuo mei a‘u ki lalo eni ‘ae la‘a, bea ka ne mama‘o
‘ae fa‘itoka ‘e faigata'a. Kae monu, na‘e ma‘u ‘abi ‘e
Jiosifa ‘i he tafa‘aki ‘o Kalevale, ‘o tu‘u ai ‘ene goue-
tabu, ‘aia kuo ne foa ai ‘i he maka ha fonualoto
mo'ona; bea ne fekau ke fakaha'ele ‘ae me‘afaka‘eiki
ki ai, ‘o tuku ai he taimi ni, kae toki hikitaga ‘o
kabau ‘e loto hono kaiga ke ‘ave ki hono fonua o‘ona.
Bea fai; tala'ehai na‘e mama'o, ka koe me‘a lahi ‘ae
mamahi na‘e fa'olaki ki honau loto ‘i he'enau fataage.
Koe Misaia eni kuo nau falala ki ai, ‘o ‘amanaki ato
ai ; bea koeni kuo bekia, ‘o bekia kalusefai foki, ‘o
‘ikai te nau lava ke bole ai koe ma. Ka na‘e hulu,
nai, ‘ae mamahi ‘a ji‘i kau feline na‘e muimui tagi
mai, he koe aga aibe ‘o fafine ke o‘o ai ‘ae g. me‘a
behe ; bea na‘e ‘ajili koe ‘ikai lava lelei hono teu, ‘o
nau alea ke nofo ha ni'ihi ‘o le‘o, kae lelo ha ni'ihi ki
kolo, hekilo ‘e lava ke fakatau ha teu te'eki tabu.
Koia, ‘i he a‘u ki fa'itoka, na‘e o ‘a Salome mo me‘a
ki kolo, kae nofo ‘ae ogo Mele ke le‘o.
Koe aga ‘OO g. fonualoto faka-Jiu ke ai hono
hu'aga, bea mo ha g. leke takatakai; ka hei'ilo be
na‘e behe eni, he koe toki gaohi; bea matamata na‘e
taha be ‘ae leke kuo lava. Bea nau fakaha'ele ‘a ji‘i
Jisu ki ai, ‘o hilifaki ; ‘o nau toki teka‘i mai hono
maka tabuni, ‘o sogo'aki ‘ae hu'aga. Fe uga mola
na‘e to ‘ae la‘a, bea nau tutuku ; ko Mele be mo
Mele na‘e nofo ‘o vakai ‘ae fonualoto.
Hei'ilo be na‘e fuoloa be fuonounou ‘ena fakafe'ao


ki he ‘Eiki; ka, ‘i he‘ena o, na‘e fetogi kinaua ‘e ha
le‘o kehe, ‘aia koe kau tau Loma to‘o mahafu. Ko
hono ‘uhiga o‘enau omi koe manatu ‘a hou‘eiki ki ha
lau ‘a Jisu, tokua, te ne toe tu‘u ‘i hono ‘aho tolu,
Na‘e ‘ikai te nau momo‘i tui ki ai, ka na‘a ai ha
me‘a ‘e fai ‘e he KauAko, ‘o tu'uga ki ai ha lau kuo
ne toetu'u. Koia na‘a nau ‘alu ki he Kovana ‘o kole
ha kau le‘o ke malu'i ‘ae fonualoto. ‘Oku hage kuo
fiu ‘a Bailato ‘i he'enau fa‘a kole, ‘o ne ofo ‘i he‘enau
kei babaka ki he tagata kuo bekia ; bea na‘a ne
tali fakamahuahu age, “ Seuke, ma‘u be ha kau
le‘o, ‘o tukuigata hono nialu'i ‘oe fonualoto.” Bea
fai. Na‘e ha'ele atu ha fo‘i tau ke le‘o ai; bea ‘alu
moe hou‘eiki ‘o fekau ke nau ki‘i fakateka ‘ae
maka ke nau ‘ilo mo'oni ‘oku ‘i ai ‘a Jisu, bea nau
toe tabuni ‘o sila'i ‘ae maka, ke ‘ilogofua ‘oka to‘o e
ha taha.
Koe aga ia ‘oe fa'itoka ‘i he Sabate koia. Ko ji‘i
jino maumau ‘o hotau ‘Eiki ‘oku malolo ‘i hono
mohega maka, ‘o talitali ki ha me‘a ‘e fai. Kane ko
ha ‘aga'aga kehe ‘oku gaue hake ‘ae ivi koia ‘o
Katula, ‘aia ‘oku ne feiga ke fakafoki ‘ae g. me‘a ki
honau elemeniti. Ka kuo tala‘ofa ‘e he'ena Tamai,
‘e ‘ikai te ne ‘ilo ‘ae me‘a ‘oku ne teki ki ai, koe
‘au'auha; bea na‘e fakaai ‘ae tu‘utu‘uni koia ‘e
Nikotimasi, ‘i he'ene ‘omi ‘ae fu‘u me‘a koia na‘e
lava ai hono faka‘one‘one ahi, ‘o ‘ikai lava ke ofi ai
‘ae nanuga ‘oe ‘auha. Kuo bau na‘e fonu ‘ae fa'itoka
‘i he kau agelo, ‘o nau fakajio hifo ki he misiteli-
Ko hono toe, nai, ‘oe kogakau fakalagi kue nau ‘ave
ji'onau Bilinisi ki Balataisi, ‘aia moe laumalie ‘oe
kaiha'akau—he kuo bau na‘e tatali ‘a Jisu ki ai, ‘ae
koloa kuo ne fa‘ao mei he fili, lolotoga na‘a na fefa‘uhi.


Na‘e hage ia koe me‘a ma‘e ui ‘e he kau Loma koe
“ Mata ‘oe vete.”
‘E, ke tala mai ‘e ha agelo na‘e ‘i ai ‘ae aga ‘o
hono tali ‘i Balataisi, ‘ae gaue hake ‘ae kau Bote-
liake, moe kau Balofita, moe kau Ma'oni'oni, ke
fakatagane ki he'ene tau na‘e fai. Kate tau toki
fanogo talanoa ki ai ‘amui. Koe me‘a be ‘oku tau'ilo
ki ai eni, “ Na‘a ne hu ki hono malols‘aga,” bea ne
toki “ ‘alu ‘o malaga ki he g. laumalie nofo bilisone ”
—ka koe taha ia ‘i he g. me‘a fufu ‘oku ‘ae ‘Otua
toko taha hono ‘ilo‘i.
(‘Oku kei toe be.)


KOE VAHE XYIII.
KOE BASIONE.
Koe Toetu'u.
Koe taimi kuo tu‘utu‘uni ki he nofo ‘a Jisu ‘i fa‘itoka
koe ‘aho ‘e tolu. Hei'ilo be koeha na‘e behe ai.
Koe tolu koe fika ‘o lagi; bea na‘a ko hono ‘uhiga ia,
koe behe koe loloa ia ‘o ha bekia fakalagi. Ka ‘oku
te behe kita, koe gata'aga ia ‘oe lava ‘e he ‘aga'aga
ke teke‘i ‘ae ‘auha; bea, ka ne toloi ‘ae toetu'u, kuo
bau ke kovi ‘ae me'afaka'eiki. Ka na‘e ‘ikai koe ‘aho
‘e tolu hage ko ‘etau fa‘a lau, ‘o behe ke kakato ‘ae
houa ‘e 72 : kae hage be koe fa‘a lau ‘ae kuoga mu‘a,
koe ‘aho katoa ‘e taha moe koga ‘oe ‘aho ‘e ua. Ka'e
fakaha‘ele ki fa'itoka ‘oku kei toe ha houa ‘e 6 ‘i he
Faite ; na‘e ‘oji ‘ae Tokonaki katoa mo ‘ene kei toka
aibe : koe houa ia ‘e 30 ; ko hono lahi ‘oe houa ‘i he
Sabate ‘e ‘ikai hulu ‘i he houa ‘e ono. Koia ‘e gata
mei he 36 ‘ae houa o‘ene toka ‘i he fonualoto, bea na‘e
‘ikai fa‘a ji‘i ‘i he 31.
Ko hono gata ia ‘oe me‘a ‘oku tau ‘ilo bau ki ai,
he ‘oku ‘ikai ke fakaha fakababau ‘ae houa na‘e
toetu'u ai ‘ae ‘Eiki. Ka ‘oku gofua ‘etau fakalavelave
ki ai. Koe fakakaukau ‘e taha : Koe mahili leva ‘ae
tu‘uabo ‘i he Tokonaki bea ne tu‘u. Kuo kakato


hono taimi ke ne ‘i fa'itoka ai, ‘ae tolu'i ‘aho na‘e
talaga'i mei mu‘a, bea koe behe ke ne toe nofo atu !
he koe ‘abi manako ki he tagata ‘a Fa‘itoka 1 Bea
‘oku hoa ia moe taibe ‘oe Toetu'u ‘ae hu mai ‘a Isileli
mei Ijibite. ‘Oku ha mai mei he folofola na‘e kakato
‘ae taimi o'enau nofo ‘i Ijibite ‘i he tu'uabo, bea na‘e
‘ikai ke toe houa atu, ka nau ‘atil leva.
Ka ‘oku ai ha fakakaukau ‘e taha. ‘Oku lau ‘e
Maake ki ho'ene fe‘uga, nai, moe hobo ‘ae la‘a na'e
iloa ai ‘ae toetu‘u ‘a Jisu : bea, ne ogo ‘oku ‘ikai ke
fakababau koe taimi ia ‘o hono fai, kae hage ‘oku ai
hona gali ‘oe ‘alu hake ‘ae La‘a Fokalaumalie fe‘uga
moe hobo ‘ae la‘a fakamatelie. Bea 'ajili, he ‘oku
behe ‘e he ni‘ihi koe taimi ia na'e ‘atu ‘i he Temibale
‘ae bolobolo ‘oe ta‘u fo‘ou. Bea ‘oku fakababau mai
‘e Baulo ko Jisu koe fua tabu ‘OO ta‘u ‘ae ‘Otua ; he
ko kitautolu ‘oku tau to ‘ufi, ka koe ‘Otua ‘oku to
‘aga'aga. Bea ‘oku matamata na'e tu‘utu‘uni ‘ae
‘atu ‘oe bolobolo koe jio kia Jisu, bea tau ke na
taimi taha ‘ae taibe mo hono mo'oni. Koe a‘u ia
‘etau fakalavelave, bea taki taha fa'iteliha be koefe
‘oku ne gali'ia ai.
Kuo bau na‘e gatetetu'u ‘a lagi ‘i he Tokonaki
koia, he koe eboke lahi. Talu ‘ae tu‘u ‘a Taimi kuo
bule ‘a Mate, ‘o ne auna ‘ae me‘a kotoa, ka, ‘i he
febaki ‘aneafi ‘ae ogo Mafi ni, na'e ha'aki ‘a Mate ; bea
kuo bau ‘e ai ha fu‘u me‘a ‘e hoko ke kuo liukava.
Tabu mo kitautolu, ‘oku hage ‘oku laga ‘a Natula,
bea galigali fa‘ele‘i ha ‘Alo fo‘ou ‘oe ‘Otua. Koia
‘oku te behe na'e lolofi hifo ha kau agelo ta‘efa‘alaua
ke vakai.
Bea na'e ai, foki, ha gaue ‘i Mamani. Hei'ilo bo
kuo mohe ‘ae Kau Abosetolo be ‘ikai. Kuo mafajia


honau loto ‘i he bekia ji'onau ‘eiki mo takimu'a ; bea,
ne ogo na‘e ai ‘ene lau ki hono tolu ‘oe ‘aho, kae ‘ikai
ha taha ‘e tokaga ki ai. Tala'ehai te nau lava ha
me‘a ta‘e ‘i ai ‘a Jisu. Koe me‘a be ma‘a nau jio ki
ai koe nofo fehi‘anekina, moe ‘ita ‘ae hou'eiki, moe
foki ki ‘abi kuo ‘ikai lava ‘enau me‘a. Na‘e nofo
hoha'a moe kau fefine, ‘o nau faka‘amu be ke ‘aho
ka nau ‘alu ‘o tatafi ji'onau ‘ofa'aga.
‘Oku hage na‘e nofo kehekehe ‘ae kau fefine koia;
bea, ‘i he'ene ofi ke ‘aho, ma‘e kamata laka atu ha
fonoga fefie e ‘ua. Koe taha na‘e taki ai ‘a Jioana,
‘ae ‘eiki fefine mei Kaleli; bea koe fonoga ‘e taha ko
Mele mei Makitala moe Mele ‘e taha, bea mo
Salome. ‘Oku hage koe fonoga ia na‘e mu‘omu‘a.
Lolotoga ‘ae bo koia kuo nofo ‘ae kau sotia Loma
na‘e le‘o, ‘o talanoa be mo lafo —be ha—ke fakanou-
nou ‘ae taimi. Fokifa na‘e to hifo ha fu‘u mo‘a hage
ha afi, bea galulu ‘ae kelekele hage ha mofuike. Bea
nau haga hake —ta koe fu‘u tagata ena hage ha
jiaianiti: na‘e hinaekiaki hono kofu, bea taba tu‘u ‘ae
‘uhila ‘i hono botu kotoabe. Bea uoke ! ‘oku ne ‘alu
atu ki he fa'itoka, ‘o teka‘i atu ‘ae fu‘u maka-kafu,
‘aia na‘e ‘ikai mei lava ‘e ha toko lahi ‘i he ‘aho koe;
‘o ne toki hekeheka ai, hage koe behe kuo te‘eki ‘oji
‘ae me‘a. ‘Oku te behe na‘e toki hu mai ‘a Jisu mei
he fonualoto, ka na‘e ‘ikai jio ki ai ‘ae kau le‘o, he
kuo nau to ki he kelekele hage ha mate.
Fe‘uga moia kuo hu kitu‘a ‘ae fonoga ‘a Mele mo
Mele mo Salome. Na‘e kei tuai ‘ae ‘aho, bea kei
bo'uli ‘ae fonua. Fokifa na‘e behe mai ‘e ha taha,
“ Koe‘uma‘a ‘a ‘etau fu‘u uhu bo'uli mai, he ‘oku
‘ikai ha taha te ne teka‘i ‘ae maka.” Bea laga ai
‘enau haga ki he botu fa'itoka; bea uoke, ‘oku ava I


bea ‘oku tekefili ‘ata ‘ae maka ‘aia na‘e ha mama'o ko
‘ene fu‘u lahi, kae'uma'a hono huhulu ! i he mama ‘oe
agelo na‘e heka ai. Bea hage na‘a nau ofo ‘i he'ene
ha, bea nau behe, “Takuo hobo ‘ae la‘a.” ‘Oku ‘ikai
te tau ofo ‘i he'enau jio ki he mama, kae ‘ikai ke ‘ilo
koe agelo, he koe aga, tokua, ‘oe fa'ahiga fa‘ahikehe
koia ke ha noabe ki he mama'o, kae toki gali tagata
‘oka ofi.
Bea toki behe mai ‘e Salome kia Mele Makitala,
“ Lele, ta‘ahine, ‘o tala kia Bita mo Jione kuo hae ‘ae
fonualoto, bea kuo nau ‘ave ‘ae ‘Eiki.” Bea lele ‘a
Mele kae fai atu ‘ae ogo fmematu‘a. Fokifa be na‘a
nau ‘ilo ki he kau tagata kuo fola ‘i lalo ‘o mate
ilifia. Bea nau haga hake, ta, koe mama ‘oe maka ‘oku
fakatagata hifo ‘o gali fa‘ahikehe ; ‘o nau kamata tete
mo kinautolu foki. Kae lea fakalelu mai ‘ae agelo,
“ ‘E, ‘oua te mo manavaho kimoua; he ‘oku ou ‘ilo
ko bo‘omou kumi ‘a Jisu. ‘Oku ‘ikai te ne ‘i heni;
kuo ne toetu'u hage ko ‘ene me‘a. Mo omi ‘o

kinaua ki he fonualoto; bea ‘i he'enau hu, ta, ‘oku
nofo ai ha taha gali talavou ‘oku kofu hina hage koia
‘itu‘a ; ka na‘e ‘ikai ‘i ai ‘ae me‘a faka'eiki.
Bea toe lea mai ‘ae talavou koe hage koia ‘itu‘a,
“ ‘Oku ou ‘ilo ko ho‘omo kumi ‘a Jisu; ka kua too

kitu'a, ‘o hola ke mama'o ; bea nau toki mo‘utu‘ua
be ‘oku nau tetetete mo tafu'ua—kae fefe ! ‘ikai koe
me‘a fakalele mo‘ui mo'oni ? Kuo fekalei mai moe
kaate, he koe hu leva ‘ae agelo moe ogo fafine, na‘e
hage na‘e mole ‘enau manavahe, ‘o nau tutu'u ‘o hola.


IVuga moia kuo a‘u atu ‘ae fonoga fefine ‘e taha;

Bea tutu‘u leva ‘ae ogo ako, ‘o na ku kitu‘a ‘o lelo,

ha mo ta‘eha ko ‘ene fahteliha. ‘Oku ‘ikai koe
me‘a ia ke tau ofo fau ai, he ‘oku agatolu ‘ae me‘a
kotoabe; bea ko hono aga ‘e taha ‘oku ta'eha.
Vakai ki he g. ‘ao ‘o lagi. Koe ‘ao eni, bea ‘oku ha;
kae ‘anenai koe mao bea ta‘eha, bea te ne toe mao
‘anai ‘o buli. Koia ‘oku ‘ikai te tau tuigata'a ki
he hahamolofia ‘ae jino ‘o Jisu. ‘Oku mahino koe
aga ia ‘oe jino fakalagi, bea ne ogo ‘oku ‘ikai lava
ke behe ‘a hotautolu ni jino, ka —he ‘oku tatau ‘ae
‘unufe moe bebel
Koia na‘e tu‘u ‘a Jisu ‘i honau lotolotoga kae buli
be. Bea hono ‘ikai gaue hono fatu ‘i he/ene fanogo ki
he‘enau lau, moe ha honau ‘ulugaaga kehekehe ‘oku
ne maheni ai. Faifai bea ‘ikai te ne makataki, ‘o ne
tanaki hono aga-ha, ‘o fakabu atu kiate kinautolu, ‘o
ne folofola, “ Ji‘oto‘ofa atu ! ”
‘Oiaue ‘enau ‘oho ‘enau jio ki he‘ene tu‘u mai, he
na‘a nau mahalo kotoabe koe fa'ahikehe ; bea hage
aibe hotau aga, ‘oka ofi mai ha me‘a behe, na‘e vavana
honau jino. Bea jio ki ai ‘a Jisu, ‘o ne lea faka-
lelulelu, kae'uma'ii na‘a ne faka‘ali‘ali hono nima moe
va‘e ke nau ‘ilo ‘ae g. matafa‘o ; bea ne humaki atu
ke nau fafa ‘o ‘ilo koe kakano moe hui.
Bea ala mai ‘a Jione, ‘o fafa ki ji‘ono ‘ofa‘aga. Ta,


ko Jisu be. Bea behe mo Bita, Anitelu, mo Filibe,
nai; ka ko honau toko labi na‘e teki ko ‘enau behe
koe fa‘ahikehe. Bea malimali age ‘e Jisu, ‘o ne kilo
holo ke vakai ha me‘a ke ne fakamo‘oni‘aki ia; ‘o
ne ‘ilo kuo toki fai ‘enau tokoni; bea ne behe leva,
“ ‘Oku ai ha'amou me‘akai henil” Bea nau ‘age ki
ai ha koga ika tunu; bea ne to‘o ‘o kai ‘i honau ‘ao.
Bea na‘e toki mole ‘enau lifujia, ‘o nau tui ko Jisu
mo‘oni ia kuo toetu‘u.
Bea toki fai atu ‘enau talanoa, bea fakamauatu
age ‘e Jisu ‘ene g. kikite mu‘a, ‘o behe te ne toetu‘u
‘i hono ‘aho tolu. Kae‘uma‘a na‘a ne fakamanatu
‘ae g. botutohi ‘oe Fuakava Motu'a na‘e kau ki ho
Misaia. Bea hei‘ilo be koe malie ‘ene fakamatala,
be koe ga e ‘ae Laumalie Ma‘oni‘oni, kae hage na‘e
toki e‘a kiate kinautolu, ta, koe me‘a ia na‘e talaga'i
moi mu‘a, ‘E kai mamahi ‘e he Misaia, bea te ne
bekia mo toetu‘u. Bea toki tala ‘e Jisu ‘enau gaue
‘e fai. Te nau ‘alu ‘i he g. botu kehekehe ‘o
mamani, ‘o malaga‘aki ‘ae fakatomala moe fakamole-
mole; bea koe me‘a te nau fakamo‘oni‘aki ko ‘enau
jio kiate ia, na‘e kalusefai bea toetu‘u. “ Kae ‘ikai
te mou ‘alu leva; ka mou nofo ‘i Kolo kae'oua ke
‘omi ho'omou teu mei ‘oluga. Ko homou faka'iloga
eni —” bea ne ho kiate kinautolu, ‘o ne behe, “ Mou
ma'u Laumalie Ma‘oni‘oni a ! ” —boa ne toki buli;
bea, ‘i he'enau fejiofaki, kuo ‘ikai.
Hei'ilo be na‘a nau mohe ‘i he bo koia be ‘ikai, ka
kuo bau na‘a nau fakataha mai ki he Temibale hegi-
hegi, he koe taimi koia na‘a nau mamafa ki he g.
feigalotu. Bea ha‘u ki ai ‘a Tomasi, foki, bea nau
tala fiefia mai, “Tomasi ni, ‘a ! na‘a ke ‘i fe ‘anebo !
he na‘e ha‘u ‘ae ‘Eiki kiate kimautolu. Koia be


mo'oni; he na‘a mau jio ki ai, mo ala ki ai, bea fai
‘ene taumafa ‘oku mau mamata, bea mau talanoa
fualoa moia.”
“ Bea fefe ai ?ne ne buli 1 ” Ko Tomasi ia.
“ ‘lo, ‘iloage na‘e ‘ikai.”
“ ‘Aua, talaatu, ko hono laumalie be ; kae taumaia
na'aku ‘i ai.” Ko Tomasi ia.
“ Tkai, Tomasi. Ko hono jino mo'oni kuo toetu'u
Na‘a mau jio ki hono matafa'o ‘i hono nima moe
va‘e, bea na‘e ala ki ai ‘a Bita mo Jiono moe toko
lahi. Na‘e ‘ikai te te ala kita he na‘a te manavahe.”
Lau ‘ekita ‘e tui ‘a Tomasi. Tala'ehai koe toko
taha ; na‘e toko lain na‘e fakamatala behe, kae ‘ikai
‘aubito magoi. Kae kalokalo mamahi hono ‘ulu, ‘o
ne behe, “ Ka ‘ikai teu jio ‘i hono ogo nima ki he
matafa'o, mo velo hoku nima ki hono vakavaka ‘e
‘ikai ‘aubito teu tui.”
Bea behe ‘enau nofo ‘o a‘u ki he Sabate ‘e tah.i,
bea fai ‘enau fakataha bo‘uli hage koe ‘aho koe : bea
‘i ai ‘a Tomasi, foki, he hage kuo kamata ogo ki hono
loto ‘ae lau ‘a hono g. kaume'a, bea kuo ne kamata
tui na‘a ‘oku mo'oni, bea na‘a toe ha‘u ‘ae ‘Eiki,
Koe ta'etui ‘a Tomasi na‘e ‘ikai koe ta‘e fie tui; ka
koe lotoji'i moe aga fakatu'atamaki. Fokifa ‘oku
ogo mai ‘ae lea kuo nau maheni ai, “ Ji‘oto‘ofa atu ! "
Bea nau haga hake, ta, koena ia. Bea ne malimali
mai, ‘o ne haga kia Tomasi, ‘o ne behe, “ Tomasi, ‘ai
mai ho tuhu na, ‘o vakai hoku ogo nima ni ; bea ‘ai
mai ho nima na, ‘o velo ki hoku vakavaka: bea ‘oua
te ke hoko koe ta'etui ka koe tui.”
Hono ‘ikai malie ‘ae lea koia ‘a Jisu ! koe hoka
mo'oni ‘o Tomasi; ka na‘e fio ‘ofa foki, ho na‘a ne
vakai ‘ae kukuta hono loto he fie tui, kae bukebuke ‘e


hono aga-tu‘atamaki. ‘Aua ; bea, ‘i he motu ‘ae aga
koia ‘i he mahino koe jino ‘oe ‘Eiki ‘oku ne jio ki ai,
bea buna ‘ene tui, ‘o tu‘u ‘i ha me‘a te'eki ke a‘u ki
ai ha taha. Na‘e ‘ikai te ne ala, ka ne ‘ioho atu,
“Ko hoku ‘Eiki mo hoku ‘Otua !!! ”

KOE YAHE XIX,
KOE BASIONE.
Koe Ha'ele Hake.
Kuo ‘oji eni ‘ae Katoaga ‘oe Basova, bea tutuku ‘ae
g. fu‘u kakai kuo ha‘u ki ai mei he botu kotoabe ‘o
Kenani. Bea o ‘ae Kau Abosetolo ‘i he fonoga na‘e
‘alu ki Kaleli, bea behe foki moe toko lahi ‘oe Kau
Ako, koe'uhi kuo tu‘utu‘uni ‘ae Eiki ke nau fakataha
ki ai. Bea nau a‘u ki ai ‘0 nofo, ‘o talitali ha
faka'iloga o‘ene ha‘u, he kuo ne fakaha ha mo'uga te
ne toki ha ai.
Bea koe ‘aho ‘e taha na‘e behe ‘e Bita, “ Kau
tama, teu ‘alu au ‘abo ‘o toutai, hei'ilo ‘e ma‘u ai
ha me‘a ke tali'aki ‘ae fu‘u kakai ni.” Bea tali mai
leva ‘e he Kau Ako ‘oku nau nonofo, “ Lelei; tau 6
kotoabe.” Bea nau hekavaka, ‘o a'alo ki moana.
Na‘a nau toko fitu : ko Bita aibe mo Tomasi, mo Nata-
niela, mo Semisi mo Jione, boa mo ha toko ua kehe.
Boa nau faifai ‘i he bo koia ‘o ‘aho, kae ‘ikai ma‘u
ha me‘a. Koia, ‘i he‘ene kamata ‘aho mai, na‘a nau
bale ki ‘uta. Bea kuo nau ofi bea nau jio ki ha
tagata ‘oku ta'alo kiate kinautolu, ‘o ne ‘ioho mai,
“ Tamaiki, ‘oku ai ha‘a mo u kiki 1 ” Bea nau kalaga
atu, “ ‘Oku ‘ikai.”


Bea toe ‘ioho mai ‘ae Taha mei ‘uta, “ A‘au ‘ae
kubcga ‘i he mata‘u ‘oe vaka, bea te mou ola.”
Bea nau mahalo, ‘abe, koe taukei, bea ‘oku ne ‘ilo
ha ika ‘oku ‘ikai ha kiate kinautolu, Koia na‘a nau
a‘au ‘ae kubega; bea, ‘i he'enau kamata fuji, uoke, na‘e
‘ikai ke matoho. Bea, ‘i he'enau fakajio hifo, ta, koe g.
fu‘u ika lalahi ena ‘oku ‘oho, hage ka hae ‘ae kubega,
bea nau fiefia. Bea gata ai ‘enau ogo‘i ‘ae toko ono,
kae manatu ‘e Jione ki he me‘a behe na‘e hoko mu‘a,
‘i he fai honau fakanofo ke abosetolo, ‘o ne tuhu ki he
Taha ‘i ‘uta one fanafana kia Bita, “ Koe ‘Eiki be ! ”
Bea fu‘u ‘oho ‘a Bita, ‘o ne ‘ita kiate ia be he ‘ikai te ne
‘ilo leva koia ia. Bea ‘ikai te ne fa‘a tatali ke tui hono
kofu, ka ne nono'o be, ‘o ne hobo ki tahi, ‘o kakau ki
‘uta ki ji‘ono ‘Eiki. Bea malimali ‘a Jione ‘i he'ene
mamata ki ai, ‘o ne behe, “‘A Maka foki! ” Bea ne
toki tala ki hono kaugatoutai ke nau tuku taula, ka
nau ‘alu hifo ki he vakafokotu‘u, ‘o taulani ‘ae
kubega ki ‘uta, he ‘ikai te nau lava ke fakaheka.
Bea fai; bea ne ogo ‘ae lolotu ‘ae fu‘u bota ika, kae
‘ikai ke mahae ‘ae kubega.
Bea, ‘i he'enau hake ki ‘uta ke fakafetaulaki ki he
‘Eiki, uoke, koe afi ena moe mata'i ika ‘oku tunu, bea
tuku ofi ai ha fo‘i nia. Beakuo nau fe‘iloaki mo Jisu,
bea ne fekau, “Mou ‘alu, ‘o ‘omi ha me‘a mei he ika
kuo mou toki ma‘u.” Bea heka ‘a Saimone ki lie
vaka, ‘o buke ‘ae kubega ‘o toho ki ‘uta, ‘o nau tuu‘i
‘ae ika ‘i he ‘one'one, ‘o fokotu'u atu ki he ya‘e ‘o
Jisu. Bea kuo nau lau, ta, koe ika ‘e teau moe ika ‘e
nimagofulu moe ika ‘e tolu : koe ika lalahi kotoa, ‘o
‘ikai ha taha ‘e li‘aki ko ha‘ane tae‘aoga.
Bea toe me‘a mai ‘a Jisu, “ Mou omi ‘o fai ho'omou
belekifasi. Bea ne to‘o ‘ae ma moe mata‘i ika,‘o ne tufa


kiate kinautolu, bea nau tokoni. Kae hage na‘e mo‘uta-
fu‘ua honau loto, ‘o ‘ikai te nau fa‘a lea kiate ia.
Bea kuo ‘oji ‘enau tokoni, bea haga mai ‘ae ‘Eiki
kia Bita, ‘o ne behe, “ Saimone, foha ‘0 Jione, ‘oku
ke ‘ofa kiate au, ‘o lahi hake ‘i ha'anautolu nil ”
Koe fu‘u hoka ia ‘o Bita, he koe fakamanatu ki
he‘ene lea bolebole na‘e fai, ‘o behe, Ne ogo ‘e li'aki
‘ae ‘Eiki ‘e he Kau Ako kotoa, kae ‘ikai te ne li'aki
‘eia —kae, hili ia, kuo ne fu‘u bago'ia ‘iate ia. ‘0
‘ikai'ia, nai, koia, ka na‘e ogo ki he loto ‘o Bita ‘ae
fo‘i lea “ ‘ofa ” na‘e fai‘aki. He na‘e ua ‘ae lea ki
he ‘ofa. Koe taha koe ‘ofa ‘a mama‘o, ‘o taka faka-
‘aba'aba be; ka koe ‘ofa ‘e taha koe ‘ofa ‘a hoto
mo‘oni kia kita. ‘E ‘ikai, nai, loko mama'o ‘etau ui ‘ae
taha, koe ‘ofa momoko, moe taha koe ‘ofa mafana.
Bea kuo gaue'aki ‘e he ‘Eiki, ‘i he fai o‘ene fehu‘i, ‘ae
lea ‘oku jio ki he ‘ofa momoko. Koia ko Bita ‘i
he‘ene tali, na‘a ne fai‘aki ‘ae lea ‘oku jio ki he ‘ofa
mafana—‘ae ‘ofa ‘ae kaiga moe mateaki—he‘ene behe,
“ ‘lo, ‘Eiki; ‘oku ke mea‘i oku ou ‘ofamo‘oni kiate koe.”
Bea folofola mai ‘ae ‘Eiki, “Eafaga ji‘oku faga lami.”
Kuo bau na‘e malie‘ia ‘a Bita ‘i he tali koia, he
na‘e hage ko hono toe fakanofo ia : ka ‘oku ha kiate
kitautolu na‘e takataka tautea be, he koe faga lami
be na‘e tuku ki ai, ‘oji koe taimi mu‘a na‘e a‘ana ‘ae
tauhi ‘oe takaga kotoa, Bea too folofola mai ‘ae
‘Eiki ‘o hage koe fua fai, ka na‘e ‘ikai te ne faka-
manatu ki he‘ene bolebole, he na‘e mahino kuo
tuku. Bea tali ‘a Bita hage koe ‘anenai, ‘o fai aibe
‘aki ‘ae lea ‘oku jio ke he ‘ofa mafana. Bea behe
mai ‘ae ‘Eiki, “ Tauhi ‘eku faga sibi.” Malie ! koe
hiki ia ki ha tu‘uga ‘e taha : ‘oku ‘ikai kei gata eni ‘i
he lami, ka ‘oku ne tauhi ‘ae fu‘u sibi kotoa. Ka


kuo te‘eki ke a‘u ki hono tu‘uga imra, ‘aia koe
taimu‘a ‘i he faga sibi ‘oku taki. Fefe I‘e gata ai ?
Kane behe, ‘e fu‘u fiefia be ‘a Bita. Seuke, ne vai
hono loto ‘i he ‘ofa ‘ae ‘Eiki, ‘o tamate‘i ‘ene faka-
fijiga tu‘o ua ‘aki ‘ene fakamo'oni tu‘o ua.
Bea mea‘i ia ‘e he ‘Eiki Hakule-loto, bea na‘e
ikuna ia ‘e he agavaivai mo fakatomala mo ‘ofa ‘a
‘ene abosetolo. Koia ‘i he‘ene toe me‘a mai, na‘e ne
tuku ‘ae lea ‘oku jio ki he ‘ofa momoko ‘o ne fai‘aki
‘ao ‘ofa mafana, ho‘ene behe, “ Saimone, foha ‘o
Jione, ‘oku ke ‘ofa mo‘oni kiate au 1 ”
Ko loto ke fiefia ‘a Bita ‘i he fehu‘i tu‘o tolu mai,
ho ‘oku mahino koe ‘ai ke tamate‘i ‘aubito ‘ene
fakafijiga na‘e fai —na‘e ‘agatolu ena, koia na‘e ‘ai
ai ke ‘agatolu ‘ene fakamo‘oni. Kae hage na‘e ‘ikai
ke ha behe kia Bita, he na‘a ne mamahi ai, tokua.
Na‘a ko ‘ene behe ‘oku ‘ikai tui ‘ae ‘Eiki ki he‘ene
lau ; bea na‘a ko ‘ene tokaga ki he afi malala, ‘o ne
manatu koe afi malala, foki, na‘a ne tu‘u ai ‘o fai ‘ene
fakafijiga. Kae kehe, na‘a no tali malohi atu, ke ne
hakule hono loto, bea to ne ‘ilo ‘oku n 9 ‘ofa mo‘oni.
‘A, keu mamata mai ki he fofoga ‘oe ‘Eiki ‘i he
fai o‘ene g. lea fakabakohokoho koia ! he, ne ogo ‘ene
hoka ‘oluga, ka ne ‘ofa u‘uu‘u ‘i lalo, bea koe me‘a
koia ‘oku fa‘a ha ‘i he fo‘i fofoga. Bea, ne ogo ‘ae
mamahi ‘a Bita, ka ‘oka ne haga hake kuo ne ‘ilo hono
‘uhiga, moe taba mai ‘ae fu‘u ‘ofa ‘ae ‘Eiki kiate ia.
Bea ne toki folofola mai kiate ia ke ne fafaga ‘ene
faga sibi bele. Ta kuo lava : kuo ne ma‘u kotoa
hono lakaga mu‘a ; kuo tamate‘i ‘ene gauekovi.
‘Oku tau ‘ilo ‘a Bita mo hono aga ‘oho, bea kuo bau
na‘e maifi hono loto ‘o meimei hikijia. Bea vakai ki ai
‘ae ‘Eiki, ‘o ne ‘ai leva hono lolomi, ho‘ene fakaji‘iji‘i


age, ‘e ‘ikai fakabalataha ‘ene taimu'a, ho tene taimu'a
‘i he mamahi, foki, ‘o iku ki he kolosi foki hage koia.
Bea toki behe ‘a Jisu ki he Kau Ako, “Tau o. Mou
muimui mai,” —ko ‘ene taki atu, nai, ki he mo‘uga kuo
ne fekau ke nan katoa ai. Bea tebitebi atu ‘a Bita,
kuo ‘ikai malomi hono loto ‘i he tala kuo fai; he
koeha fua ‘ae mate 1 ‘lloage na‘a ne kilo kitu‘a ke
vakai be ‘oku nau muimui mai, ‘o ne jio ki hono
kaume'a ko Jione, bea ne haga leva ‘o fehu‘i ki he
‘Eiki, “ ‘Oku fefe ‘ae tama koena 1 ” —he kuo toe
Bita ‘oho, foki. Bea bau ke toe lomi ‘e Jisu, koia
na‘a ne folofola mai ki ai, “ Kabau ko hoku loto ke
nofo be ia kae'oua keu ha‘u, ka—he ‘oku ke kau ai ?
Fai be ho‘o muimui ‘au kiate au.” ‘A, ‘oua na‘a tau
lau‘i ‘a Bita ; ko kitaua aibe ia. Ka ki‘i faka‘ataage
‘e he ‘Eiki, kuo bau ke ta ‘oho : bea ko ‘ene gaiie aibe
‘oku fai koe lomia, lomia hono ‘ofa‘aga.
Na‘e tubu mei he me‘a koia ‘ae lau ‘ae ‘uluaki jiaji
‘e ‘ikai bekia ‘a Jione, ka te ne mo‘ui atu be, ‘o a‘u
ki he ha‘ele mai ‘ae ‘Eiki, Bea seuke, na‘e hage ka
behe ; he na‘e ‘oji be ‘ae to‘utagata koia, moe kei nofo
be ‘a Jione ‘o talitali ki hono taimi.
‘Oku ‘ikai mahinobe koe mo‘uga fe na‘a nau ‘alu ki
ai. Na‘a ko Heamoni, ‘aia na‘e fai ai ‘ae fakakehe
hono aga, be ko Teboa, be koe Mo‘uga ‘oe Malaga,
‘Oku hage na‘e toe bull ‘a Jisu ‘i he'enau o, kae ‘alu
atu ‘ae Kau Abosetolo, ‘o fakataha ‘ae Kau Ako ‘i
he botu kuo tala. Kabau koe Mo'uga ‘oe Malaga,
‘oku tau ‘ilo na‘e ai hono lauua, bea toki hobo hake
hono tumutumu. Koe lauua, nai, na‘e tatali mei
ai ‘ae kakai. Fokifa ko Jisu ena ‘oku tu‘u mai
mei he tumutumu ‘oku lagilaghia faufau. Bea
mabe‘e leva ‘ae Kau Abosetolo moe ni'ihi kuo nau


niaheni ai, ‘o nau hu. Bea behe moe toko lalii. Ka
na‘e ai ha ni ‘ihi na‘e kei tala'a, he kuo nau fo'ou
kiate ia. Koia na‘a ne ‘unu‘unu mai ke ofi, ke nau ‘ilo
bau koia. Tokaage ha‘ane g. tu‘utu‘uni na‘e fai, moe g.
boubou; bea ne toki fai ‘ene fu‘u lea fakatu'i koeni—
“ Kuo tuku kiate au ‘ae bule kotoabe ‘i Lagi
mo Mamani. Koia ke mou o, ‘o gaohi ‘ae
kakai kotoabe ko ‘ekukau ako, ‘ihe babitaiso
kinautolu ki be Huafa ‘oe Tamai moe ‘Alo
moe Laumalie Ma‘oni‘oni, moe ako‘i kinautolu
ke taubi ‘ae gahi me‘a kotoabe kuou tu‘utu‘uni
atu. Bea koeni, ‘oku ou ‘late kimoutolu eau,
‘i he gabi ‘aho kotoabe, ‘o a‘u ki he gata'aga
‘o mamani.”
Hono ‘ikai malie ‘ene fai koia ! Ko hono Bule‘aga
e kuo fakataha mai ki honau ‘Eiki, ke ne fai tu'utu-
uni kiate kinautolu te‘eki ke ne ‘alu. Kuo loa
‘enau tui koe Misaia ia, koe Tu‘i Isileli kuo ‘amanaki
ki ai, talu mei tuai, te ne auna ‘a mamani. Kae,
lolotoga ‘ene mo'ui, koe faka'amanakinoa aibe ‘enau
Jio tau'oluga ai. Ka koeni kuo lava ‘enau holi ; kuo
ne tala ‘e a‘u hono Bule'aga ki Mamani katoa, bea ko
‘enau gaiie ke ‘ikuna ‘ae g. fonua. Bea ko ‘ene fono e
kae ‘alu ki Lagi, ‘o hifo ha taba kiate kinautolu.
Talaatu, koe toki fono ia na‘e fijitijimu'a hono lea.
Bea ne buli ai leva, ‘o nau lau kuo ne ‘alu ki Lagi.
Ka na‘e ‘ikai bohe ‘ene Kau Abosetolo, he kuo ne
fekau ke nau foki ki Selusalema, ‘o talitali kiate ia.
Bea na‘e mole, nai, ha g. uike moe ‘ikai ha talanoa ki
ha me‘a na‘a ne fai, gata be ‘ene taka mamani kae
fufii be. ‘Oku kei misiteli ‘ae ‘uhiga kotoa o‘ene
fuoloa belie ‘i lalo ni. Ko hono me‘a be ‘oku mahino
koe ‘aho ‘0 fagofulu, bea koe fagofulu koe fika ia ‘oe


Koe Basione (atbe) —Koe Ha'ele Hake. 27 1
tatali. ‘Oku tau ‘ilo koe hake ‘ae kakai Isileli mei
he Tahi Kulokula koe taibe ia o'ene Toetu'u. Boa
na‘a ko ‘ene kataki ‘i luamani, ‘o ‘aho fagofulu, koe
jio ki he'enau fagofulu'i ta‘u ‘i he Toafa kae toki hu
ki Kenani, bea ko ‘ene ‘ai ke ojiki ‘ae nanuga ‘ae fanau
‘ae ‘Otua? Bea na‘a ko ‘ene fakatata'aki ‘ae tatali
‘ae kakai ‘ae Otua ‘i fa'itoka te‘eki ke nau hu ki lagi ?
Kuo tau vakai kuo ne mavae mo hono Bule'aga;
bea koe aga aibe ‘oe tu‘i ‘oku ‘amanaki hiki ‘oku ne
tu‘utu‘uni hano hoko. Bea hage na‘e belie ‘a Jisu.
Koe hoko totonu ‘i he lau fakaemama ko hano tehina
ko Semisi, he koe hako foki ia ‘o Tevita. Koia na‘a
ne ha ki he toko taha koia, ‘o ne tu‘utu‘uni, nai, ke ne
Sea ‘i he fakataha ‘o bule ki he jiaji ‘i Selusalema.
Kuo ‘oji eni ‘ae ‘aho ‘e fagofulu, talu ‘ae ‘aho
mamafa koia na‘e hae ai ‘ae mataha ‘o Hetesi, ‘o toe
tu‘u mai ‘a Jisu ki Mamani. Kuo ‘oji hono kuoga
tatali; kuo ata hono hala ki Lagi. Na‘e ‘ilo ‘e he Kau
Abosetolo ki he ‘aho koia, ‘o nau fakataha ki Selu-
salema ke tali ia. Ka na‘e ‘ikai te nau ‘ilo ki he'ene
Ha'ele Hake, ka nau mahalo ko ‘ene o‘io‘i ha me‘a
fakabule'aga, ‘o tau mo ‘ene lea ‘i he mo'uga. Fokifa
kuo tu‘u ‘a Jisu ‘i honau lotolotoga, bea nau talanoa
fuoloa moia ‘i he'ene fai ‘ene g tu‘utu‘uni fakarnui.
‘Oiseukeseuke ! ‘ae g. me‘a fakamisiteli na‘a ne a‘au !
Tokua, ke nau nofo ‘i Selusalema kae‘oua ke babitaiso
kinautolu ‘aki ‘ae Laumalie Ma‘oni‘oni. Koeha nai?
Kuo fuoloa ‘enau talanoa moe tu‘u ‘a Jisu, ‘o
kamo atu ke nau muimui mai, ‘o ne taki kinautolu
ki Mo‘uga Olive. ‘Oku tau ‘ilo ko hono lata ‘aga mu‘a
ia ; ka ‘oku te belie na‘e ‘ikai ko hono ‘uhiga ia o‘ene
fili ia ke ha'ele hake mei ai, ka koe‘uhi koe feitu'u ia
na'e hiki mei ia ‘ae Sikaina ‘i he fuofua li‘aki ‘o


Selusalema : bea koia na‘e tiiu ke ne hiki moia mei
ai ‘i hono li'aki koeni. Na‘e laid ‘ae g. balofisai na‘e
kau ki Olive, bea koia, ‘i he'enau hake ai, na‘e mafana
‘ae loto ‘oe abosetolo ni‘ihi, ‘o ‘ikai te nau mata'ofi
‘enau huhu ki he ‘Eiki be te kc fai ni ‘ene fokotu‘u
bule'aga. Bea bau ke ne toe lomia kinautolu ‘enau
jio me‘a fakamama behe, ka na‘a ne toe faka‘atu‘i
leva kinautolu ‘o ne behe, “ Moe fiemalie bo ; he te
mou ma‘u ha fu‘u malohi.” Ko Jisu aibo ia.
Bea nau fai atu ‘enau talanoa, ‘o tuku ki mui ‘ae
tumutumu ‘oe mo‘uga. Koeha ? Lau ‘e kita ‘e fai ai
‘ae ha‘ele hake. Ka ka mole atu be ia kae'oua ke
ha mai ‘a Betaiii, ‘aia na‘e tu‘u ai hono fale lata'aga
‘i mamani. Ta koia. ‘Oku no kei tagata, bea ‘oku
ne fie mavae fakamui ofi ki hono kau ‘ofa'aga. Na‘a
kuo ne tu‘utu‘uni ko nau hu kitu‘a, ‘o jio ki ai.
Fokifa ‘oku ne tu‘u, ‘o ne tafoki ‘o hiki hono nima
‘o tabuakid kinautolu. Bea, lolotoga ‘ene fai, na‘e ‘oho
honau loto ‘enau vakai ‘oku ne mahiki hake date ia
be. Tala‘ehai koe buna kao ‘aulologo hake be ‘ene
‘alu. Na‘a ne fai hake, fai hake, fai hake. Fokifa
na‘e gatolo mai ‘ae Saliote ‘o Lagi koe fu‘u ‘ao gigila,
o tali ia, bea talu ai ‘ene buli meiate kinautolu.
Kane ogo ‘ene buli, ka kuo nau mo‘u haga hake
aibe ka ne tae'oua ‘ao ta‘ofi ‘e ha ogo agelo, bea nau
toki foki ki kolo. Ka ‘oku kei haga hake ‘ae jiaji
koe'uhi koe lea ‘ae ogo agelo koia, hc'ena behe, “ Koe
J'isu koia, ‘aia kuo ‘ohake meiate kimoutolu ki Lagi
to ne toe ha‘u ; bea ‘e hage tofu bo hono aga bea mo
‘ene ha‘ele ki lagi kuo mou mamata ki ai.”
“ Emeni, ‘Eiki Jisu, ke ke ha‘ele mai !”
GATA AI.
